---
name: Gukaza umutekano wawe bwite muvy'ubuhinga bwa none
goal: Gutegura ikibanza c'ubuhinga bwa none gitekanye, gishikamye kandi co vyazwa umusaruro.
objectives:


  - Gutahura ingene sisiteme zigezweko zikora hanyuma uhitemwo ufise amakuru
  - Kuronka ubwigenge bw'ubuhinga muri Linux
  - Gushira mu ngiro imigenzo myiza yo gucungera umutekano ku nyabwonko yawe bwite
  - Gukaza umutekano w'ukuronderera kumbuga n'ugukoresha terefone ngendanwa hifashishijwe ibikoresho vy'isoko yuguruye (open-source) be n'imiterere ibereye
  - Gukingira bikwiriye umuhora wo muhira


---

# Intambwe yegereza k'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none



Mw'isi aho ibikoresho vy'ubuhinga bwa none biri hose ariko bikaba ari gake ababikoreshwa baba batahura uko bikora ijana kw'ijana, kwiga ingene wokingira ikibanza cawe c'ikoranabuhanga ry'amakuru (IT environmnent) ni ngombwa. Yaba ari inyabwonko yawe, mucukumbuzi(browser) yawe, terefone yawe canke umuhora wo muhira, kimwe muri ivyo kirashobora kuba irembo ry'injira m'ubuzimwa bwawe bw'ibanga. Iki cigwa kigufasha gusubirana ububasha kubikoresho vyawe vyubuhinga bwa none.



Si ukumenya gusa imigenzo myiza: ni ugutahura ivyo ukoresha, ingene ubikoresha, n'ico ivyo bisobanura ku mutekano wawe. Iki cigwa ca  SCU202 gitanga intangamarara yimbitse ku vyerekeye ubuhinga bw'ishimikiro bw'ama sisiteme, kikakumenyesha uburyo bwo gukoreshwa Linux, kikakuyobora mu gutegura ikibanza gishikamye, gikora neza, kandi ntayegayezwa.



Mu bice vyose vy'iki cigwa, uzobona ingene wogenzura ubutungane bwa porogarame ushiramwo, kunyegeza neza amakuru yawe, gukoresha neza mucukumbuzi(browse) yawe na terefone yawe ata makuru yawe menshi ashobora kuja ahagaragara, no gukomeza umutekano w'umuhora wawe wo muhira.



Iki cigwa cibanda kubakoresha b'inzobere bashaka kuja kure mu kumenya neza ibikoresho vyabo vy'ubuhinga bwa none. Gishingiye ku buryo bwo gukora, bwibanda ku kwigenga n'ubusegaba, kugira ngo umuntu yubake ingeso nziza kandi zikwiye muvy'ubuhinga bwa none umusi kumusi, hakurikijwe icivugo "*Ntukizere, Suzuma*".



+++

# Intangamarara


<partId>8b696bba-e6f6-47d9-ba30-fe4b75636b88</partId>



## Incamake y'icigwa


<chapterId>7bf90137-7387-462d-884f-fe48e812b739</chapterId>



Murakaze mu cigwa ca SCU202, kibandanyiriza ku cigwa ca SCU101, kizogushikana kure mu kunonosora neza umutekano w'ivy'ikoranabuhanga ry'amakuru (IT) mu gushimika ku busegaba bw'umuntu ku giti ciwe, ku kurinda ubuzima bw'ibanga, no ku gutunganya mu buryo burinzwe amakuru yawe bwite. Dore incamake y'ivyo uzobona muri iki cigwa ca SCU202.



### Igice ca 1 - Intangamarara



Icigwa gitangurana no gusubiramwo muri make ivyo twabonye mu cigwa ca SCU101 bizotuma umenya neza ingingo nyamukuru z'ishimikiro zikenewe kugira ngo ushobore kwegera neza ibikurikira.



### Igice ca 2 - Kuva ku gufyonda gushika kuri porogarame yakira amabwiriza (terminal): kunonosora Linux



Iki gice kikuzanira sisiteme ya GNU/Linux, inkingi y'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none. Uzobona itandukaniro riri hagati ya Linux, Windows na macOS, ubone amateka aryoshe cane ya Linux n'ama porogarame y'ubuntu, kandi utahure igituma Linux akenshi bigaragara ko itanga umutekano n'umwidegemvyo.



Inyuma, uzomenya ingene wohitamwo uburyo bwateguwe bwo gukoresha Linux (Linux Distribution) bujanye n'ivyo ukeneye be n'ikibanza c'ibiro (Desktop environment). Ubwa nyuma, uzotera intambwe yawe ya mbere hamwe na Ubuntu biciye mu mfashanyigisho igaragaza  ido n'ido kukungene woyishiramwo no kuyitunganya.



![Image](assets/fr/064.webp)



### Igice ca 3 - Gukingira inyabwonko yawe


Muri iki gice, uzomenya ingene wokaza umutekano w'inyabwonko yawe. Tuzogenda twegera uburyo bwo kurinda neza aho ushika no gutandukanya uko uyikoresha. Uzotahura akamaro ko gushira sisiteme n'ama porogarame kugihe kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zishobora gushika.



Uzomenyerezwa kandi kugenzura ubutungane n'ukuri kw'ama porogarame uvoma kuri interineti kugira ngo wirinde kwanduzwa umugera nyabwonko canke guhungabanywa, hamwe no gukoresha neza ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru kugirango ukingire amakuru yawe bwite n'ububiko bw'inyongera (backup). Ubwa nyuma, uzobona igituma n'ingene wosukura ubwoko bw'amakuru bwitwa *metadata* bw'amadosiye yawe kugira ngo ukinge ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe kuri interineti.



![Image](assets/fr/235.webp)



### Igice ca 4 - Mucukumbuzi: OS iri muri OS



Muri iki gihe, mucukumbuzi ziri hose mu buzima bwacu bwa misi yose muvy'ubuhinga bwa none, kandi akenshi ni yo ibanza guterwa n'ibitero vyo kuri interineti. Muri iki gisata, dusubiramwo amateka ya mucukumbuzi n'ingene zagiye ziratera imbere.



Uzoheza ubone incamake y'imoteri z'uguhindura (rendering engines) na mucukumbuzi bigezweko, ivyiza n'ibibi vyavyo, hamwe n'imigenzo myiza yo gukingira uko urondera kumbuga uko bishoboka kwose.



![Image](assets/fr/098.webp)



### Igice ca 5 - Gusubirana ububasha kuri terefone yawe



Muri iki gihe, amaterefone smart yacu ni inyongerabushobozi mu buzima bwacu bwite n'ubw'umwuga, ivyo bikaba bituma bihambaye cane ko tugenzura umutekano wayo. Tuzokwihweza mu buryo buziguye sisiteme za terefone ngendanwa, ivyiza vyazo n'aho zigarukira, ari nako tuzobona uburyo bundi bw'isoko yuguruye (open-source) bugufasha kwigarurira ubusegaba bwose ku gikoresho cawe.



Uzoheza wige imigenzo myiza mu gucungera umutekano vya misi yose, kuva ku gushira kugihe amakuru gushika ku gutandukanya amakuru yawe bwite n'ay'umwuga. Ubwa nyuma, uzobona ibikoresho vyo guhanahana amakuru birinzwe be n'utundi duterabwenge (applications) tw'isoko yuguruye (open-source) kugira ngo ushobore kwongereza ibanga n'umutekano wa terefone yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/142.webp)



### Igice ca 6 - Gukingira umuhora wawe wo mu karere(aho hagufi)



Umuhora wawe wo muhira ni ikintu gihambaye cane iyo bije ku bijanye n'umutekano. Tuzotangura turabe ingene umuhuhora wo mu karere ukora, imbere y'uko tuja ku ntambwe zogukora ibijanye no kuwukingira neza.



Uzomenya ingene wohitamwo no gutunganya ruteri (router) irinzwe, gucamwo ibice u umuhora wawe, gukomeza umuhora wawe wa Wi-Fi, no gushiraho ibikoresho vyo kugenzura kugira ngo ubone ningoga ibintu vyose bitameze neza.



![Image](assets/fr/193.webp)



### Igice ca 7 - Igisata ca nyuma



Kugira ngo uheze icigwa, uzoba ushobora gukora ikibazo ca nyuma kugira uronke icemezo cawe no kugenzura ko utahura ingingo zaganiriweko.



![Image](assets/fr/274.webp)



Woba witeguriye gufata bikwiriye ububasha bwo kugenzura umutekano w'ikoranabuhanga ry'amakuru (IT) ryawe, ugakomeza ubusegaba bwawe bwite ukizigira ko ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe bwo kuri interineti? Reka tugende!



*N.B.: Niwahura n'amajambo utamenyereye mw'iki cigwa, usabwe kuraba [urutonde rw'amajambo](https://planb.academy/resources/glossary) kugira ngo ubone insiguro*



## Incamake za ngombwa za SCU101


<chapterId>26cfac35-a3bb-4657-95b3-8508bedfa903</chapterId>



Imbere yo gutangura icigwa ca SCU202, ndashaka gusubiramwo muri make ivyiyumviro shimikiro vyavuzwe mu nyigisho iheruka("SCU101") muri iki gice.



Ikindi kandi, nimba ukiri uwutangura gukoresha inyabwonko kandi utarafata icigwa ca SCU101, ndagusaba nshimitse gutangura n'ico cigwa ca mbere imbere y'uko uja kur'iki. Ivy'ishimikiro vyavuzwe muri SCU101 ntibizosubirwamwo hano. Sinzosubira rero ku migenzo y'ishimikiro y'umutekano, canke ku gukoresha VPN, ubutunganyirizo bw'amajambo y'ibanga, canke ivyemezo bibiri mu kwemeza uwinjira. Kandi naho biri ukwo, ivyo vyiyumviro vyose ni ngombwa kubinonosora neza imbere y'uko tuja ku mikoreshereze yisumbuye, tuzovugako mu bice bikurikira.



Icigwa vya SCU101 cari icigwa c'intango cagenewe gushinga umushinge ukomeye mu bijanye n'isuku muvy'ubuhinga bwa none ku batangura n'abakoresha b'inzobere mw'ikoranabuhanga ry'amakuru (IT). Intumbero yico cigwa yari iyo gukaza umutekano wa misi yose, ubuzima bw'ibanga n'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none.



https://planb.academy/courses/99c46148-7080-4915-a7e0-9df0e145cd47

### Kurondera kuri interineti mu mutekano



Akenshi Kurondera kuri interineti ni co kintu nyamukuru kiba irembo rikurura ibitero vy'iterabwoba vyo kuri interineti. Muri SCU101, twabonye ko ari ngombwa kuguma turi maso cane cane iyo umuntu ariko aravoma amakuru. Voma amadosiye mu bibanza vyizewe gusa, kandi uhitemwo porogarame z'isoko yuguruye (open-source), akenshi zitanga inyungu mu gukorera mu muco cane n'umuryango wagutse uzigenzura.



Ikindi kintu ciza cavuzwe muri ico cigwa cari kijanye n'ama cookies, ni ukuvuga utwo tudosiye dutoduto tubikwa ku nyabwonko yawe iyo ugendereye urubuga. Ukwiye kwama udufuta canke uka tugabanya kugira ngo ukingire ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe.



Muri rusangi, kurondera kuri interineti mu mutekano bisaba ko umuntu yiyubara: wirinde gufyonda ku mahuza utazi, wirinde imbuga ziteye amakenga, kandi ukoreshe mucukumbuzi iri kugihe kandi irinzwe.



![Image](assets/fr/268.webp)



### Gutahura ama VPN no gukingira inzira yawe ya interineti



SCU101 yarakumenyesheje iciyumviro ca VPN (Virtual Private Network). Mu bijanye nuko ikora, VPN inyegeza uruja n'uruza rwawe rwa interineti mu gukora umugende urinzwe hagati y'igikoresho cawe n'urusenge ruri kure (remote server). Ariko rero, VPN zose si zimwe: ushire imbere abazitanga bakorera mukuri, babizigirwa bemera kwiyandikisha ata karanga kawe utanze, nka Mullvad, ProtonVPN canke IVPN. Izo VPN zigufasha kugira ubuzima bw'ibanga ntayegayezwa atagukorakoranya amakuru yawe bwite mu gihe bidakenewe.



Ikindi kandi, twari twabonye ko ku mihora ya Wi-Fi ya rusangi, inzira y'uguhuza iba iri ahagaragara cane. Ni co gituma gukoresha VPN ari ngombwa. Nimba udashobora kuyikoresha, ja gusa ku mbuga za HTTPS kugira ngo ukingire guhanahana amakuru kwawe.



![Image](assets/fr/269.webp)



### Gukoresha wigengesereye inyabwonko yawe



Umutekano kandi bisigura kumenya sisiteme (OS) yawe. Washoboye kuraba OS zitatu nyamukuru: Windows, macOS na Linux, imwe yose ifise ivyiza vyayo vy'umutekano. Kuri Windows cane cane, antivirus iri ku gihe ni ngombwa kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kumenya no guhagarika porogarame mbi.



![Image](assets/fr/270.webp)



SCU101 kandi yarakugabishije ko utokwigera ucomeka ama USB atazwi mu nyabwonko yawe, kuko yoshobora kuba arimwo ibintu bibi bishobora kwanduza sisiteme yawe.



### Gukingira ibitero vyo kuri interineti no gutunganya ububiko bw'inyongera (backup)



Igice nyamukuru c'imenyerezwa rya SCU101 cari ugutahura ibitero vyo kuri interineti. Umugera nyabwonko ntuboneka uko gusa: akenshi bisaba ko ugira ico ukoze utabishaka, nk'ukuvoma dosiye yanduye canke kwugurura ihuza(link) ry'ububeshi muri imeyiri.



Kimwe mu bitero bikunze kuboneka ni phishing(ububeshi buciye mu dutego), aho ubutumwa bw'ububeshi bwoherezwa kugira ngo bakuremeshe gutangaza amakuru y'agaciro. Igihe uhanganye n'ivyo bitero, suzuma mu buryo butunganye uwukurungikiye, kandi wirinde gufyonda ku mahuza canke kwugurura ibintu bifatanijwe na imeyiri bivuye ahantu utazi canke hateye amakenga.



Ikindi kintu gikomeye gitera ubwoba ni ransomware(igitero c'incungu), funga amakuru yawe mu kuyanyegeza ikaca isaba incungu. Kugira ngo ushobore guhangana n'ivyo, ni ngombwa ko uhora ukora backup y'amakuru yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/271.webp)



### Gukingira neza amasandugu yawe y'ubutumwa



SCU101 cane cane yashimikiye ku kamaro ko gucungera imeyiri yawe, irembo ry'izindi konti zawe zose zo kuri interineti. Agasandugu kahungabanijwe gatuma abo bakwinjiriye bashoborra guhindura amajambo y'ibanga y'amakonti yawe hafi ya yose biciye ku buryo busanzwe bwa imeyiri bwo gusubirana konti yawe(recovery).



Rero warabonye akamaro ko kurema aderese imeyiri zirinzwe, zigenewe ibintu bigiye bitanduka. Ni vyiza kugira aderese imeyiri yihariye yagenewe kugira ngo ushobore gusubirana konti yawe, itandukanye na aderese yawe nyamukuru.



![Image](assets/fr/272.webp)



### Akamaro k'ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga



Umutekano mu buhinga bwa none ushingiye cane ahanini ku buryo amajambo y'ibanga yawe ameze. SCU101 yasiguye igituma gukoresha ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga ari ngombwa: ivyo bikoresho bigufasha kurema no kubika amajambo y'ibanga agoranye, yihariye kandi avangitiranye ya buri serivisi yose ukoresha.



Ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga bukworohereza igikorwa cane, kubera ko ubwirizwa kwibuka ijambo ry'ibanga rimwe gusa nyamukuru ry'ayandi yose.



![Image](assets/fr/273.webp)



### Ivyemezo bibiri mu kwemeza uwinjira (2FA)



Ubwa nyuma, SCU101 yakumenyesheje Ivyemezo bibiri mu kwemeza uwinjira (2FA). Iryo hame rigizwe n'ukwemeza uwinjira mu ntambwe zibiri zitandukanye: ijambo ry'ibanga ryawe risanzwe n'ikindi kintu ca kabiri, nka kode y'igihe gito yakozwe n'agaterabwenge(application) nka Google Authenticator canke Authy, canke urufunguzo rw'igikoresho nka YubiKey.



2FA irinda neza cane amakonti yawe: naho ijambo ry'ibanga ryawe ryoba ryarahungabanijwe, ugushika ku makuru ntibishoboka ata kintu kindi kigira kabiri. Menya ko amakode yoherezwa kuri SMS canke kuri imeyiri ata mutekano, kuko ashobora gufatwa canke guhindurwa mbere yuko agushikira.



___



Ibi twiyibukije vy'ishimikiro bizagukora nk'ubumenyi bw'ibanze bw'icigwa cacu ca SCU202, aho tuzoja cane mu kunonosora neza ubuhinga bwo gucungera umutekano wo kuri interineti (cybersecurity), kugira ngo urinde neza ubusegaba bwawe bwite, ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe n'amakuru yawe bwite muri rusangi.



# Kuva ku gufyonda gushika kuri porogarame yakira amabwiriza (terminal): kunonosora Linux


<partId>e28895b3-2b09-4811-8031-5abc1f14fde2</partId>



## Linux, Windows, macOS: ni ikihe kikubereye?


<chapterId>598cdecb-f90c-4382-b13c-0ba5a9dfeede</chapterId>



Reka dutangure iki cigwa ca SCU202 n'ivy'ibanze: sisiteme (OS). Ntigena gusa amahitamwo yawe y'ibikoresho, ariko kandi n'umutekano wawe, ukworoha gukoresha n'ubushobozi bwo guhindura inyabwonko yawe uko ushaka.



Imbere yo kwinjira mu vy'ubuhinga bwa Linux mu bice bikurikira, birahambaye ko dutahura itandukaniro rikomeye riri hagati y'izo sisiteme zitatu zisanzwe: Windows, macOS na GNU/Linux. Muri iki gice, tuzokwiga umuti umwumwe wose, tumenye aho ukora neza n'aho udakora neza, hanyuma uhitemwo neza ufise amakuru ivyo ukeneye.



### Sisiteme yo gukoresha ni iki?



sisiteme ni urutonde rwa porogarame fatizo zikora nk'umuhuza hagati y'uwuzikoresha, uduterabwenge(na two nyene ni porogarame) n'ibikoresho, ni ukuvuga, inyabwonko yawe. Ni akagwi ka porogarame ntoyi zibanze zituma ushoboza gukoresha ibikoresho vy'inyabwonko (processor, memory, disks, peripherals, n'ibindi).



Mu majambo nyayo, sisiteme irakira, igakora hanyuma igatanga ivyo isabwa na porogarame yawe, kandi ibi ibikora ikoresha neza ibikoresho vy'inyabwonko uko bishoboka kwose. Ikurikirana ugukoreshwa kwa porogarame nyinshi icarimwe, igenzura ibihimba vya PC(inyabwonko), igenzura inzira zihuza, iremera kandi gutunganywa kw'amadosiye, kandi ibungabunga umutekano w'amakuru biciye mu buryo bwo kwemerera no kwemeza.



![Image](assets/fr/001.webp)



Ata sisiteme, porogarame imwe imwe yose yobwirizwa kuba ifise uburyo bwayo bwite bwo kuvugana n'ibikoresho vy'inyabwonko, ivyo bikaca bituma gukorana hagati ya porogarame zitandukanye bisa nibidashoboka. Uruhara rwayo rero ni ngirakamaro.



Uko ni ko nyene inyabwonko za kera zakora. sisiteme ya mbere na mbere, GM-NAA I/O, ntiyaribwaboneke gushika mu mwaka w'1956. Yazanye ubuhinga bwo gukora ibintu mu mice, ivyo bikaba vyatuma habaho ukwikoresha mugutunganya ibikorwa ata muntu abigize mo uruhara. Mu myaka y'1960 harabonetse ubuhinga bwo gukora porogarame nyinshi no gusangira igihe hakoreshejwe CTSS (1961) na Multics (1969), ivyo vyatumye abakoresha benshi bashobora gukoresha sisiteme imwe icarimwe. Hanyuma mu myaka y'1970, habayeho uguhingura Unix kwahinduye cane ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko (computing) kubera uburyo bwo gutwarika(portability), uburyo bwo gukora ibikorwa vyinshi icarimwe n'ukoroha.



![Image](assets/fr/004.webp)



### Sisiteme nyamukuru n'imigabane yazo kw'isoko



Ubu, isoko rya sisiteme riganzwa n'imiryango itatu ikomeye: **Windows, MacOS na GNU/Linux**.



Dushingiye ku cegeranyo gihari ubu, Windows iraca fise igice kinini cabay'ishira kunyabwonko z'abo bwite, ikaba ifise umugabane w'isoko ushika ku bice 71%. Ukwo kuganza ni kubera ihuriro ry'ibintu bitandukanye nk'amateka, ubutunzi n'ubuhinga:





- Kuva mu myaka y'1990, Windows yashirwa ku nyabwonko nyinshi zigurishwa, ivyo bikaba vyatumye abantu benshi bayimenya. Microsoft yaciye yihuta gushinga amasezerano menshi ya OEM (amasezerano abahinguzi ba PC bashiramwo Windows imbere y'igihe bariko bazikora), gutyo bituma habaho uwo mukenyuro ugoye guhagarika.





- Naho ivyo bigenda birahinduka buke buke, Windows yabaye nk'umurongo ngenderwako mw'isi y'umwuga kuva kera cane. Uretse imice yihariye nk'iyivy'ikoranabuhanga, murudandazwa hafi ya rwose baracari ku nyabwonko zikoresha Windows.





- Igitigiri kinini c'abakoresha bashishikarije abahingura porogarame gushira imbere guhingura porogarame zabo zijanye na Windows, kugira ngo zishike ku bantu benshi. Bityo rero hanyuma, uko hahingurwa porogarame nyishi bigatuma haboneka abakoresha bashasha, ibi bikaguma bisubirwamwo.





- Ubwa nyuma, uko kuganza bikomezwa kandi n'ishusho ibonwa ya sisteme zindi bihanganye: Linux akenshi ibonwa ko isaba ubuhinga bwinshi cane ku bantu bose muri rusangi (benshi ntayobazi), mu gihe macOS, vy'umwihariko ifatanye gusa n'ibikoresho/porogarame vya Apple, akenshi ibonwa ko izimvye.



macOS, muri ico gihe, ifise umugabane w'isoko ugera kuri 16%, kandi muri rusangi bayihitamwo kubera ko ikorana neza n'ibikoresho vya Apple. Guhitamo iyi sisiteme vyakomejwe mu myaka iheze n'ubushobozi bwogukora bwa Macs, bivuye ku gushiramwo Apple Silicon chips. Iyo mpinduka ikomeye yatumye habaho uguheba processors za Intel x86 bagakoresha ARM architecture, ikora neza cane mu bijanye n'ubushobozi ndetse n'umucanwa zikoresha.



Linux iguma ari ntoyi ku nyabwonko z'abantu kugiti cabo (hafi 4%), ariko iganza ku ma seriveri (hafi 63%) no ku ma supercomputer (100%), kubera ukudahungabana kwayo n'ubushobozi bwayo.



![Image](assets/fr/002.webp)



*Isoko Ndamukiza 2025: [StatCounter Ivyegeranyo kw'Isi Yose - Umugabane w'Isoko rya Sisiteme](https://gs.statcounter.com/os-market-share/desktop/worldwide)*



Linux nayo ihirwa cane mu bikoresho vy'imbere nk'ama router, ama tereviziyo, amaterefone ngendanwa (Android ishingiye ku mutima wa Linux (Linux Kernel)) mbere no mu bijanye n'imiduga. Windows iguma ifise ubushobozi bukomeye mu bucuruzi, mu gihe macOS ikunda cane abanyamwuga mu bice bimwe bimwe.




→ **Igihambaye:** Kernel ni co gice fatizo ca sisitemu: icungera uko ibikoresho (processor, memory, peripherals) vyoshikirwa, ikagena uko hokogwa ibikorwa bitandukanye icarimwe, igashitsa amategeko y'umutekano kandi itanga Igicapo(interface) kimwe kuri porogarame zipfuka ugucangana kw'ibitanda biri mu nyabwonko(electronic circuits). Mu yandi majambo, ikora nk'ikiraro hagati y'ikibanza ca porogarame (libraries, drivers, shells, serivisi, ibikoresho vy'ubuyobozi, igicapo(graphical interface), n'ibindi) n'ibikoresho.



### Windows: koroherwa mugukora be no guhura



Windows ni sisiteme yakozwe na Microsoft. Iri ku nyabwonko nyinshi z'abantu ku giti cabo kw'isi. Mu mateka, yashimiwe kukuba yoroshe gukoresha kandi ikaba ifise igicapo(interface) ciza. Ariko rero, ako karusho gateye amakenga ubu: interface ya macOS na yo nyene woyikoresha vyoroshe, kandi uburyo bwateguwe (distribution) bwinshi bwogukoresha Linux bufise interface ibereye abantu bose (ivyo tuzobisubirako mu bice bikurikira).



Ku bakoresha batabimenyereye canke abafise ivyo bakeneye bike (ibikorwa vyo mu biro, ivyamasanamu, kurondera kumbuga), Windows ishobora kuba uburyo bworoshe bwo gutangurirako, wungukira mu nyandiko nyinshi n'ubu ryo bwo kwiga vyihuse. Ariko mu vy'ukuri, ikintu kimwe gusa Windows ishobora gusumba macOS na Linux ni imikino y'amasanamu(Video games).



![Image](assets/fr/005.webp)



Kimwe mu bintu nyamukuru bikomeye kuri Windows ni ubutunzi bw'ubwinshi bwa porogarame zayikorewe: hafi porogarame zose z'urudandazwa (Office suites, porogarame z'umwuga, imikino y'amasanamu na drivers z'ibikoresho) zihuye na Windows. Ku bakoresha barondera umuti uteguriwe guhita ukoreshwa udasaba guhindura vyinshi mu imiterere, aya ni amahitamo nyayo.



Ariko rero, ukwo gushikira abantu bizanana n'ikiguzi. Windows ni sisteme ifise beneyo,icungerwa itagira kode iri ahagaraga. Nta kugenzura wokwigirira wewe ubwawe gushoboka, ivyo bikaba bigaragaza imipaka igaragara mu bijanye n'ugukorera mu muco n'umutekano. Ikindi kandi, gukorakoranya amakuru (telemetry) birakwiragiye cane muri Windows kandi akenshi bibabisanzwe bikora utarinze kubigiramwo uruhara, atavyo wemeye canke ngo ushobore kubigenzura.



Ku bijanye n'umutekano, Windows ikunda kwibasigwa na malware. Kuba izwi cane be n'utunenge tumwetumwe tw'imiterere yayo muri kahise birasigura neza igituma. Nta gukekeranya ko hariho utwigoro twakozwe mu myaka iheze (cane cane na Windows Defender na UAC), ariko muri rusangi iguma iteguwa cane kugira ngo yorohe gukoreshwa kuruta gukomera no kugenzura kwabayikoresha.


![Image](assets/fr/007.webp)



Mu vyiyumviro vyanje, Windows ifise ikibanza nyamukuru bitavugwa: irashobora kuba itanga umutekano, ariko ikaba itarusha Linux na macOS; iremera ko umuntu ashobora kugira ivyo agenzura, ariko ni bike cane kuruta Linux; nta bubasha bukomeye ifise nk'ubwa macOS, canke ngo ibe yoroshe gukoresha nka Chrome OS canke sisiteme za Linux zishobora gukoreshwa n'abatangura. Iraferageza kuba hagati nahagati mu mice yose, nta kibi cayo muvy'ukuri mu ahantu hamwe canke ahandi (kiretse kukijanye n'ubuzima bw'ibanga, ku buryo busanzwe).



![Image](assets/fr/006.webp)



Ku bijanye n'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none be n'ukunonosora ivy'ubuhinga, Windows ica yerekana ningoga aho igarukira. Uko ikoze bishingiye ku mubano utagira uburinganire hagati y'uwukoresha n'abanyeneyo, ku nyungu yaba nyeneyo. Ku bashaka cane gutahura, guhindura no gukingira inyabwonko yabo, si sisitemu ibereye cane. Ni co gituma tutazoguma tuvuga cane kuri Windows muri SCU202.



### macOS: ubufatanye n'ugutuma ibintu bigenda neza



macOS ni sisiteme yakozwe na Apple ikoregwa inyabwonko zabo za Mac.Ni sisiteme ifise iragi rikomoka kuri Unix, biciye mu ri sisiteme ya NeXTSTEP, Apple ikaba yara buronse mu 1997.



![Image](assets/fr/008.webp)



Uwo mushinge ukomeye utanga ukudahungabana, gucunga neza ibikoresho na n'uko yubatse bitanga umutekano. Ivyongeweko n'igicapo(graphical interface) giteye igomwe cane, cakozwe kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kugikoresha neza.



![Image](assets/fr/003.webp)



Kimwe mu bintu bikomeye vya macOS ni ugushiramwo mu buryo buhagaze ibikoresho na porogarame. Apple ni yo igenzura uruhererekane rwose, kuva ku guhingura processor gushika ku bintu bitobito vya interface. Ico bivamwo ni sisiteme yo kwizigirwa muri rusangi, ifise ibibazo bikeyi vyerekeye ibikoresho vy'inyabwonko kandi butunganijwe neza kugira ngo bukore neza.



Ariko rero, iyo nzira yo gukorana irafise akaga ko gukomeza kuba yugariye kubikoregwa muri Apple gusa. macOS ni sisitemu ifise banyeneyo(ifise ahanini kode y'isoko yugaye) ikoreshwa gusa ku bikoresho vyakozwe na Apple. Abakoresha bafise uburyo buke bwo kugenzura uko sisiteme ishigwa ku gihe, guhitamo imiterere ihambaye ya sisiteme canke amahitamwo y'ibihimba vy'ibikoresho. Ibikoresho biragoye guhindura canke gusanura, kandi akenshi vyugariye kuri porogarame.



![Image](assets/fr/009.webp)



Ku bijanye n'ubuzima bw'ibanga, naho macOS idaterwa cane nka Windows, iguma igaruka kugukorakoranya amakuru, gusanisha n'igicu(cloud) no kwizigira serivisi zicungerwa ziri hamwe. Ivyinshi mu bikorwa bihambaye vy'a sisiteme bishingiye ku guhuzwa kwamako na Apple (iCloud, App Store, Siri...), ivyo bikaba bigabanya ubwigenge bw'uwukoresha.



macOS ishobora gushimisha abakoresha baha agaciro ubushobozi, ukudahungabanwa n'ugutekanirwa gutangwa na sisiteme yubatse neza, bidasavye ko baja kwisuka mu bintu vy'ubuhinga ido n'ido. Ku rundi ruhande, ku bijanye n'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none no kugenzura ikibanza cawe c'ikoranabuhanga ry'amakuru, birafunze cane, bishingiye cane kw'ishirahamwe rimwe, kandi ntivyoroshe kugira ico uhindura uko uvyumva. Ni co gituma tutazobivugako cane muri iri shure rya SCU202.



### GNU/Linux: umwidegemvyo, ubugenzuzi n'umutekano



GNU/Linux itandukanye cane n'izindi zibiri zabanje kubera uburyo yubatsemwo bwo gukoreshwa kubuntu ikaba ari sisiteme y'isoko yuguruye (open-source). Bitandukanye na Windows canke macOS, Linux ntihingurwa n'ishirahamwe rimwe, ahubwo ihingurwa n'umuryango wabahinguzi bama sisiteme bo kw'isi yose. Ubwo buryo y'ubatsemwo bw'umuryango wagutse butuma habaho gukorera mu muco, umutekano n'uguhinduranya vyoroshe. Linux itanga ububasha bwose ku bakoresha bayo, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora guhindura neza aho akorera. Ivyo biraryoshe cane cane ku bakoresha binzobere, abahinguzi canke abashaka kunonosora neza ikibanza cabo c'ubuhinga bwa none.



Ivyiza vya Linux ni ugukomera no kwaguka kwayo, ukudahungabana kwayo n'umutekano wayo wo hejuru. Kubera ko ari iy'isoko yuguruye (open-source), kode yayo irashobora gusuzumwa n'uwuyikoresha canke ishirahamwe, ivyo bikaba bigabanya cane ingorane zo gukoresha porogarame mbi(malware) canke backdoors. Linux irakomeye cane, muri rusangi ikoresha ibikoresho bike kuruta Windows, kandi irabereye cane cane mu gukoresha ibikoresho bitari vyinshi canke gukoresha inyabwonko cane nk'ivy'ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko (computing), uburongozi bwa seriveri canke umutekano wo kuri interineti (cybersecurity).



![Image](assets/fr/010.webp)



Ariko rero, Linux nayo irafise ibintu bimwe bimwe bigoranye ku batangura. Igitigiri kinini c'uburyo bwateguwe bwo gukoresha linux bushobora gutera amadidane ku bakoresha bayibonye ubwa mbere. Co kimwe kandi, nokuyikoresha ubwambere, naho uburyo bwokuyikoresha bumwe bumwe bworoshe, vyoshobora gusaba ko umuntu yiga imbere y'igihe kugira ngo ayi nonosore neza, canecane iyo umuntu yihweje ukuntu bisaba ko ukoresha ubudasiba porogarame yakira ama kode (umurongo w'amabwirizwa canke mucongereza: command line). Kandi ivyo nivyo gusa iki gice ca mbere c'icigwa ca SCU202 kivuga!



### Ni sisiteme iyihe ukwiye guhitamwo?



Amahitamwo yawe azovana ahanini n'ivyo ukeneye n'ivyo witega:




- Nimba uriko urarondera ukworoherwa, ibikoresho bishobora kwongerezwa ubushobozi n'uguhura kwa porogarame (na cane cane ku mikino y'amasanamu), hamwe n'ugukora ibintu rusangi, Windows yoshobora kuba ari uburyo bwiza. Ariko rero, urakeneye kumenya aho igarukira mu bijanye n'ingene ikora, umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga;
- Nimba uriko urarondera ubufatanye bwiza hagati y'ibikoresho vyawe na sisiteme yawe, interface itunganijwe neza kandi yoroshe gukoresha n'umutekano ukwiye udakeneye guhindura imiterere mu buryo bw'isumbuye, kandi ukaba usanzwe ufise canke wipfuza gutunga ibikorerwa muri Apple, macOS ni yo ukeneye;
- Ubwanyuma, nimba uriko urarondera umutekano, ukudahungabana ubushobozi bwo gukora neza hejuru ya vyose kandi ushaka no kugenzura vyimbitse ikibanza cawe c'ubuhinga bwa none, kandi mu gihe witeguye gushira inguvu mu kwiga uko ukoresha sisiteme yawe, Linux ni uburyo bwiza cane, cane cane mu gihe ubwigenge bw'ubuhinga n'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none ari vyo uhaye agaciro.



Mu bice bikurikira vy'iki gisata ku bijanye na sisiteme, nzoba ndiko ndagutwara cane muri Linux, kubera ko ishobora gutuma ushobora kugenzura cane ikibanza cawe bwite c'ubuhinga bwa none.



## Inkomoko ya GNU/Linux

<chapterId>9dbf749d-daae-493b-ab96-93a322df011d</chapterId>



Imbere yo kuraba ivyerekeye uburyo bwa teguwe bwogukoresha GNU/Linux n'ikibanza iyo sisiteme ifise mu buhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko, birahambaye ko umuntu akurikirana inkomoko yayo kugira ngo atahure ico ihagarariye. Muri iki gice, turasubira kuraba imizi ya GNU/Linux mu mateka, mu vya firozofiya no mu vy'ubuhinga, biciye mu iragi rya Unix, Genesis y'umugambi wa GNU, iremwa rya umutima wa Linux(kernel)n'uguseruka kw'umuhari w'ama porogaram y'ubuntu.



### Iragi rya Unix



Ivuka rya Linux ntirishobora gutahurwa tutavuze umukurambere wayo: Unix. Unix yaremwe mu mpera z'imyaka y'1960 no mu ntango z'imyaka y'1970 na Ken Thompson, Dennis Ritchie na bagenzi babo bo muri AT&T Bell Labs, Unix yatumye habaho ihinduka rikomeye mu mateka y'ama sisiteme. Mu ntango yateguwe muri *Assembler*, hanyuma isubirwamwo muri *C* na Dennis Ritchie mu 1973, Unix yashizeho umushinge w'umurongo mushasha wa OS (sisiteme) ushingiye ku guhinduranya n'ukworohereza.



![Image](assets/fr/011.webp)



Ubwo buryo buboneka mu ngingo ngenderwako y'ishimikiro yashizwe ahabona na Doug McIlroy:



> Kora ikintu kimwe kandi ugikore neza.

Unix ishobora kubonwa nk'iterambere rya, n'inyishu ku, sisiteme ya Multics, ukoyubatse ninako Unix yubatse. Multics yari umugambi watangujwe mu 1964, icamwa c'ubufatanye hagati ya MIT, General Electric na AT&T Bell Laboratories. Ken Thompson na Dennis Ritchie (abaremye UNIX) bagumye bacungera cane umugambi wa Multics gushika mu 1969, igihe ishirahamwe ryabo ryava mu mambi.



Ni muri ico gihe Unix yaseruka, mu ntango yitwa "*UNICS*" mu majambo yose "*UNiplexed Information and Computing Service*", bihushanye cane na "*MULTiplexed Information and Computing Service*", biva mw'ijambo Multics. Ubu buryo bushasha bwaje bushigikira ukworoha, uguhinduranya n'ugukora neza. bitandukanye n'ugucangana birenze urugero kwa Multics.



Kuva mu myaka y'1970 ubandanya, Unix yategurwa mu buryo bw'ubushakashatsi, imbere y'uko ikwiragizwa cane muri za kaminuza kuva mu 1975 kubandanya, ntivyari bibi kubera amategeko ntarengwa ya porograme igwanya umugera yashizwe kuri AT&T. Ivyo vyatumye yemerwa mu bibanza vy'ubushakashatsi vyinshi nka, nka Berkeley, aho ishami rya BSD (*Berkeley Software Distribution*) ryavukiye. Muri ico gihe nyene, AT&T yatanguye kumenyekanisha Unix mu myaka y'1980, bituma habaho ukwiyongera kw'ubundi bwoko bufise banyebwo budahuye nayo (System V, Xenix, SunOS, AIX, Solaris, HP-UX, n'ibindi).



![Image](assets/fr/012.webp)



*Isoko: Amateka-yoroshe ya Unix, na Eraserhead1, Infinity0 na Sav_vas, ishusho yavuye ku kigereranyo c'amateka ya Unix cakozwe na Éric Lévenez, [Wikimedia Commons](https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/File:Unix_history-simple.svg).*



Ugucika ibice hagati y'ayo mashami (BSD ku ruhande rw'ivyo kwishuri, na System V cane cane ku ruhande rw'inganda) kwatumye habaho amadidane menshi kandi uburyo bwo gukorana hagati ya sisiteme buragabanuka. Kugira ngo barondere sisiteme isa nka Unix idahuungabanywa, ishobora gutwarika, bidasaba kugira uwo wizera kugira uyikoreshe, umuryango wagutse waratanguje ibikorwa vyinshi, harimwo umugambi wa GNU mu 1983, hanyuma hakurikiraho ugutegura umutima wa Linux(kernel) mu 1991, ivyo bikaba vyaratumye huzuzwa ikinogo caje kubera ata kernel y'ubuntu mu mugambi wa GNU. Ivyo ni vyo vyabaye intango ya sisiteme ya GNU/Linux.



### Umugambi wa GNU



Umugambi wa GNU (ijambo risobanura "*GNU's Not Unix*") watangajwe ku mugaragaro na Richard Stallman kw'igenekerezo rya 27 Nyakanga 1983, mu mice yihariye y'amakuru. Ico gihe, Stallman yari agikora mu kigo ca MIT kijejwe ivy'ubwenge bw'ubukorano. Ku wa 5 Nzero 1984, yarahevye inshingano ze ku bushake kugira ngo kode yaragira yandike ntize yitirirwe umukoresha wiwe. Yaciye atangura gutegura GNU, afise intumbero yo guhingura sisiteme yu buntu, ni ukuvuga nk'akarorero sisiteme yubahiriza ingingo fatizo zine z'umwidegemvyo: gukora ku buntu, kwiga ku buntu, guhindura ku buntu no gusubira gutanga ku buntu.


![Image](assets/fr/013.webp)



Uretse imice yawo y'ubuhinga, umugambi wa GNU uri muri firozofiya yarazwe n'umuco w'aba hacker(abatwinjirira) bo mu myaka y'1970: umuco ushingiye ku gusangira ubumenyi, gukorana n'urunganwe no kuronka ku buntu kode y'isoko (source code). Richard Stallman yipfuje kuzigama impwemu yo gukorana n'abandi yari ihambaye mu misi ya mbere y'ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko, igihe abahinguzi bari bagitanga kubuntu kode z'inkomoko z'ama sisiteme yabo. Umugambi wa GNU ntugamije gusa gutanga sisiteme y'ubuntu, ariko kandi ni ukugwanira intumbero ya politike n'inyifato runtu y'ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko: ubumenyi bushikira bose, ata kwigungirako canke kwiharira ibintu. Intumbero ni ukubuza abakoresha kuba imbohe z'ama porogarame badashobora gutahura canke guhindura, no guteza imbere ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko mukwidegemvya.



Hamwe nibi vyiyumviro, Stallman yashinze *Free Software Foundation* (FSF) mu mwaka w'1985, ishirahamwe ryihaye guhimiriza no guteza imbere gukoresha no kurema porogarame z'ubuntu.



![Image](assets/fr/014.webp)



GNU itanga vyihuse urutonde rw'ibikoresho vya ngombwa kuri sisiteme yayo:




- GCC (compiler ya C)
- glibc (ububiko(library) bwa C busanzwe)
- coreutils (amabwirizwa y'ishimikiro)
- Emacs (umuryango wa text editor)
- bash (umusemuzi w'amabwiriwa (command-line interpreter))
- GDB (Debugger)



![Image](assets/fr/018.webp)



Hongewe mwo nibindi, nka sisiteme ya X Window, moteri y'uguhingura TeX na microkernel ya Mach, ikoreshwa na package ya seriveri ya GNU Hurd (hamwe, Mach na Hurd zirangura uruhara rumwe n'urw'ukuba umutima(kernel) wa Unix wa kera, ariko mu myubakire ya microkernel + server). Uwo mugambi wo gusubiriza kernel wari uhambaye cane ariko wari ugoye cane. Ntizokwigera ikora neza, ivyo rero bituma hasigara umwanya wa kernel ya Linux.



![Image](assets/fr/019.webp)



Ivyinshi muri GNU vyateguwe n'abakorerabushake mu bihe vyabo vyo kuruhuka, abandi baterwa inkunga n'ibigo, za kaminuza, canke amashirahamwe. Mu mpera z'imyaka y'1980, FSF yatanguye guha akazi abahinnga mu guhingura ama porogarame kugira ngo igikorwa cihute. Ibigo bimwe bimwe, nka Cygnus Solutions (mu nyuma yaje kuba igice ca Red Hat), yaragize uruhara runini mu kubungabunga no kumenyekanisha porogarame za GNU zitangwa k'ubuntu.



Igihe Linus Torvalds yasohora kernel yiwe ya Linux mu 1991, yari ihuye neza n'ikibanza GNU yari maze kurema, kandi yerekanye ko ari yo yo koreshwa neza kuruta kernel ya Mach + Hurd.Uguhuzwa kwa GNU na Linux vyatumye bishoboka ku ncuro ya mbere kugira sisiteme yuzuye, k'ubuntu kandi ikora neza: **GNU/Linux**, ni ukuvuga ugushirwa mu ngiro kw'umugambi watangujwe na Stallman hafi imyaka cumi imbere y'aho.



### Ivuka rya kernel ya Linux



Inkuru ya kernel ya Linux itangura mu mwaka w'1991, na Linus Torvalds, mw'ico gihe yari umunyeshure mu vya siyanse y'inyabwonko muri kaminuza ya Helsinki muri Finilande. Kubera ko Torvalds atashimishijwe n'ivyo Minix itabasha gukora, sisiteme ya Unix yakozwe na Andrew S. Tanenbaum ku bw'intumbero y'inyigisho, yaciye atangura gukora kernel yiwe bwite yo gukoresha ku nyabwonko yiwe bwite, afise intumbero gusa yo kwiga biciye mu gukora. Kw'igenekerezo rya 25 Myandagaro 1991, yaratangaje ku mugaragaro umugambi wiwe ku rubuga rwa Usenet, avuga yifata ko ukiri umugambi w'intango kandi ko uri mwigeragezwa. Mu ntango z'umwaka w'1992, verisiyo 0.12 y'uwo mugambi yarasohotse hakoreshejwe uruhusha rwa GNU GPL ku buntu.



![Image](assets/fr/016.webp)



Iyi kernel, mu ntango yitwa Freax, hanyuma ihindurirwa izina yitwa Linux (bisunze "Linus" na "Unix"), ntiyatevye gukundwa n'abandi bahinga muguhinguea ama porogarame ba banyamwete. Umuryango mpuzamakungu wahagurukiye kugira ngo ushireko umusanzu kuri iyo kode y'isoko yuguruye (open-source). bitandukanye na GNU, Linux mu ntango ni kernel gusa: igice ca porogarame gijejwe gucunga ibikoresho vy'inyabwonko. Ifatanijwe n'ibikoresho na porogarame amaze gutegurwa n'umugambi wa GNU, iyo kernel iraheza igatanga sisiteme y'ubuntu kandi ikora neza. Uku guhuzwa vyitwa "GNU/Linux" kugira ngo vyemezwe ugukorana hagati y'iyo migambi ibiri. Mu rurimi rusangi, ariko, iyi sisiteme muri bisanzwe twayitwa "Linux".



![Image](assets/fr/017.webp)



→ ***Tux***: ikimenyetso na logo ya kernel ya Linux, vyakozwe mu 1996 na Larry Ewing akoresheje porogarame ya GIMP.



### Isoko yuguruye (open-source) na firozofiya ya porogarame y'ubuntu



Uko Linux yagenda irakundwa cane mu myaka y'1990, haradutse impaka z'ingengabitekerezo ku majambo "porogarame y'ubuntu" n' "isoko yuguruye (open-source)", vyari vyo kubera insiguro igaruka kabiri y'ijambo "*ubuntu*".



Naho Richard Stallman na FSF bashigikira cane iciyumviro ca porogarame y'ubuntu bashingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako z'inyifato runtu ("*free as in freedom*"), abandi bo bashigikira uburyo bushingiye ku vy'ukuri, bushingiye ku buhinga bwibanda kugukorera mumuco no kubuhinga bwihagiijie bw'ikigereranyo c'isoko yuguruye (open-source). Mu mwaka w'1998, harashizweho umugambi w'isoko yuguruye (open-source) (OSI) canke Open Source Initiative mu congereza, ushizeho ijambo "open source" kugira ngo bibere vyiza cane urwego rw'amashirahamwe, ivyo bishimika ku nyungu z'ubutunzi n'ubuhinga aho gushimika ku vyiyumviro vy'ingengabitekerezo.



Richard Stallman yaraneguye ku mugaragaro ikoreshwa ry'ijambo "isoko yuguruye (open-source)", abona ko ritagira aho ribogamiye cane, mbere ko ritagiramwo poritike. Ashimika ku ijambo "porogarame y'ubuntu" kugira ashimike ku vy'uko ikibazo nyamukuru atari ic'ubuhinga, ahubwo ari ic'imibano: ic'umwidegemvyo w'abakoresha.



![Image](assets/fr/015.webp)



**Isoko: Nathaniel Welch**



Itandukaniro hagati y'ayo majambo abiri rero riri mu ntumbero nyamukuru iyari inyuma: umuhari w'ama porogarame y'ubuntu ushira imbere mbere na mbere firozofiya y'umwidegemvyo w'umuntu ku giti ciwe n'uw'abantu bose ku bijanye n'ama porogarame, mu gihe isoko yuguruye (open-source) ahanini iha agaciro ubuhinga bukwiye, ugukorera mu muco n'ugukorana nk'uburyo bwo kuronka umwimbu mwiza.



Naho hari itandukaniro muri firizofiya zizo nzira, izo nzira zibiri zisangiye agaciro nko gukorera mu muco, gusuzuma kode y'isoko, ubwigenge bw'abagurisha, n'ubushobozi bw'abakoresha bwo gutahura, guhindura no kunoza ibikoresho vyabo vya porogarame. Na n'ubu, uko gutandukana gutuma habaho impaka n'uguzirikana mu miryango y'abahinga, cane cane Bitcoin.



### Ingaruka ku muco no ku mibano



GNU na Linux si inkuru y'uguterimbere gusa mu vy'ubuhinga: ingaruka zavyo ku mico no ku mibano ni ngirakamaro nk'uko nyene. Ugukwiragira kwazo kwa mbere  ahanini kwari guciye kuri interineti, biciye mu mahuriro y'ubuhinga n'urutonde rw'abarungika ubutumwa, hanyuma vyihuta biciye mu buryo bwateguwe bwogukoresha linuz (Linux distributions), akarorero, ni ukuvuga amakoraniro y'ama porogarame yari yaratunganijwe imbere y'igihe akikuje kernel ya Linux. Kera mu mwaka w'1993, hariho distributions nka Slackware na Debian kugira ngo sisiteme ya GNU/Linux ishobore gushikirwa n'abantu benshi.



Ubu buryo bushingiye ku miryango, bw'uguruye korana no gukorana kwatuma Linux itera imbere ningoga, mu buryo bwo gukwiragiza(decentralizing) kandi buriwese agira uruhara rwiwe. Uwukoresha wese arashobora gutanga umusanzu mu mugambi, haba mu kwandika amakode, mu gukora inyandiko canke mu kugerageza. Ivyo bikorwa vyinshi vy'ugukorana bigaragaza uguhanga udusha mw'isi y'ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko.



Nk'uko twabibonye mu gice ca banje, iragi rya Linux uno musi rirarenga kure cane inyabwonko z'abantu bwite zisanzwe: riraganza isoko ry'ama seriveri ya interineti, itanga ububasha ku nyabwonko zikomeye cane(supercomputers), ni yo mushinge wa sisiteme ya Android itanaga ububasha ku ma miriyaridi y'amaterefone y'ubuhinga bwa none kw'isi hose, kandi mbere iri mu mutima w'ibikoresho vya eregitoronike bidaharurika (routers, smart TVs, connected objects, etc.).




GNU/Linux irengeye kuba ari sisiteme gusa: ni firozofiya, ikoranabuhanga, ni umukenyuro w'umuco n'imibano bishingiye ku bw'uguruke, gukorana n'umwidegemvyo mu vy'ubuhinga bwa none. Ivyo vyiza bibandanya bihindura cane uburyo twakira, dukoresha kandi dusangizanya ivy'ikoranabuhanga muri iki gihe.



Mu rumuri rw'iri ragi ry'ubuhinga, ubu birashoboka gusuzuma mu buryo nyabwo ingene izo ngingo ngenderwako zishirwa mu ngiro mu bijanye n'ubuhinga bwa inyabwonko y'umuntu bwite. Kugeza aha, turaza  kwihweza neza cagutse ca ama distribitions ya Linux (canke GNU/Linux), kugira ngo dutahure uko yateye imbere n'ingene akoreshwa, no kugira ngo tugufashe guhitamwo iyo ihuye neza n'ivyo ukeneye.



## Incamake ya distributions za Linux


<chapterId>868f44d7-69ce-4493-b65e-daff00f3eb54</chapterId>



Distribution ya Linux (canke kenshi bakunze kwandika "*distro*") ni sisiteme ishitse yubakiye kuri kernel ya Linux (kandi kenshi irikumwe na nibigize GNU), hamwe n'umugwi wa porogarame, amasomero(libraries), inyandiko(scripts) zo gutanguza n'ibikoresho vyo gutunganya, kugira ngo haboneke ikibanza giteguriwe gukoreshwa. Distribution ya linux rero ntigarukira kuri kernel gusa, ahubwo itanga uguhuza ibihimba vya porogarame vyose bikenewe kugira ngo inyabwonko ikoreshe (canke ikindi gikoresho cose co gukoresha ibijanye n'inyabwonko).



Buri distribution ya Linux irimwo :




- **kernel ya Linux**, ivugana n'ibikoresho(hardware) kandi igacungera ibindi bikoresho vya sisiteme nka (CPU, memory, disks, n'ibindi)
- **bootloader**, nka *GRUB*, kugira ngo sisiteme itangure
- **sisiteme yo gutanguza** ituma serivisi zitanguzwa mu gihe co gutangura: *systemd*, *OpenRC*, *SysV init*, canke *runit* bivanye na amahitamo ya firozofiya ya distribution
- **sisteme itunganya ama package**, igufasha gushiramwo, gushira kugihe no gukuramwo porogarame. Iyizwi cane ni *APT* (Debian, Ubuntu), *RPM/DNF* (Fedora, RHEL), *Pacman* (Arch), *Zypper* (openSUSE) canke *APK* (Alpine)
- kuri interineti **ububiko bwa porogarame(software repositories)**, bushira hamwe verisiyo zihari zemejwe za ma porogarame
- **umugwi w'ibikoresho vya sisiteme** (shell, editors, compilers, interfaces z'umuhora, n'ibindi) kandi kenshi n'ikibanza c'ibiro vyatunganijwe imbere (*GNOME*, *KDE Plasma*, *XFCE*, n'ibindi)
- inyandiko z'imiterere, inyandiko kuri sisiteme no, mu bihe bimwe bimwe, serivice zo gutanga ubufasha



![Image](assets/fr/050.webp)



Ico gikorwa co gukoranya kirihariye bivanye na distribution, yo ihitamwo ivyo ishiramwo vyayo bivanye na firozofiya ifise (ukworoha, kuremuruka, umutekano, ukudahungabana, uguhanga udusha, n'ibindi), abantu igenewe (abatangura, abacuruzi, ama seriveri, ama workstations, inyabwonko z'imbere(embedded), n'ibindi.) n'urugendo rwayo yo mugutegura (*rolling release* canke *stable*). Nk'akarorero, Arch Linux yibanda ku kworosha imiterere n'ubuhinga buciye mu muco, mu gihe Ubuntu yibanda ku kukungene abakoresha bakoresha sisiteme n'uguhuza na mainstream (ariko ivyo tuzobigarukako mu gisata ca nyuma c'iki gice).



→ **Iciyumviro:** Distribution ya *rolling release* ishiramwo ama verisiyo ya porogarame nshasha ako kanya akiboneka, bikaba bituma habaho sisiteme ihora iri kugihe ariko ishobora kuba idashikamye. Ku rundi ruhande, distribution ya *stable* irungika ama verisiyo ya porogarame iyo verisiyo nini isohotse, bikaba vyemeza ko hariho ukwizigirwa kwinshi kugusha ibishasha.



Kuba hariho distribution bituma abakoresha bashobora kwungukira mukuba bafise sisiteme ya Linux iteguriwe gukoreshwa, bidasavye gusubira kwubaka igice cose ca porogarame. Ivyo bitanga inyungu nini cane mu bijanye n'umwanya, ugushikama n'umutekano. na none Kandi, ku bijanye n'imyubakire, distribution ikoresha igice ca siseteme gikorana n'ibikoresho gitangwa na kernel ya Linux. Iki gice gituma sisiteme ishobora gukorana n'ibikoresho vyinshi bitandukanye, ata nkenerwa yo guhindura porogarame zijanye n'igice kimwe kimwe cose. Ukwo guhinduranya bituma vyoroha guhindura canke gusubiriza ibihimba vya sisiteme bidasavye gusubira kwubaka sisiteme yose.



Gutahura itandukaniro riri hagati ya distiributions za Linux rero ni intambwe ihambaye mu guhitamwo iyibereye ivyo ukeneye, ubuhinga bwawe n'ivyo ukeneye. Ivyo ni vyo tuzoba turiko turaraba muri iki gice.



### Inkomoko ya kahise ya distributions za linux



Distributions za mbere linux zagaragaye inyuma y'aho Linus Torvalds asohoye kernel ya Linux muri nyakanga 1991. Ico gihe, Linux yari kernel gusa: kugira ngo umuntu aronke sisitem ikwiye, abakoresha bategerezwa gukoranya bo nyene ibice bitandukanye bisabwa (kenshi bikurwa mu mugambi wa GNU), ivyo bikaba vyasaba urugero rwo hejuru rwo kuba utahura ibintu uko bikorwa. Gushiramwo sisiteme vyasigura gukoranya(compile) kernel wewe nyene, gutunganya imigabane (partitions), guhitamwo ibikoresho, gutunganya dependencies za porogarame... Muri make, igikorwa kigoye, kibikiwe ababizobereye.



Kugira ngo Linux ishobore gukoreshwa cane, imigambi myinshi iriko iraseruka vuba, hamwe n'iciyumviro co gukoranya sisiteme iteguriwe gukoreshwa iva kuri kernel ya Linux n'umugwi w'ibikoresho bikwiye.



Izo ngufu vyasaba aho hambere ni vyo vyatumye distributions za Linux zivuka:





- **Ruhuhuma 1992: MCC Interim Linux**



Yateguriwe muri kaminuza ya Manchester, MCC Interim Linux ifatwa nka distribution ya linux ya mbere cane. Intumbero yayo yari iyo kworohereza gushiramwo sisiteme kuri PC isanzwe. Iza mu buryo bw'ama disquette makeyi kandi irimwo ibikoresho bikeyi vyo gutuma Linux ikora ningoga.





- **Rusama 1992: Softlanding Linux System (SLS)**



Distribution ya SLS ni yo ya mbere yatanze ugushiramo sisiteme gukwiye ifise ubuhinga bwo gukoresha idirisha (X Window), shell, igikoresho co gukoranya(compiler) n'ibindi bikoresho vyatunganijwe imbere y'igihe. Intumbero yayo ni ugutanga sisitem imeze nka Unix ishobora gukoreshwa na bose.




![Image](assets/fr/049.webp)



Mu misi yayo ya mbere, SLS yari iteye imbere cane, ariko abayikoresha ntibatevye gutangaza amajambo y'ukunegura ukudashikama kwayo be n'ingingo zimwe zimwe zo kuyibungabunga. Ivyo vyatumye abahinguzi benshi batangura imigambi isa n'iyo, haba mu gutuma SLS itera imbere canke mu kuyisubirira. Gutyo niho hatanguye igiti kinini ca distributions za Linux n'ukuzicamwo imiryango.



SLS ntay'ikiriho. Verisiyo yayo ya nyuma izwi ni iyo mu mpera za 1994.





- **Mukakaro 1993: **Slackware**



Patrick Volkerding yatanguje Slackware mu buryo bw'isanganyabumwe, akosora no kunoza ibibazo muri SLS nk'igice c'umugambi wo kwishure muri kaminuza ya leta ya Minnesota. Biciye mu guhindura vyinshi no gutuma ibintu bigenda neza, verisiyo yiwe yahinduwe ya SLS yaje kuba distribution ya Linux yigenga vy'ukuri, yashobora gushimisha abantu bose bavunitse umutima kubera imipaka ya SLS. Amaze kwemererwa na kaminuza yiwe, yarasohoye verisiyo ya mbere yasohoye mw'izina rya Slackware kw'igenekerezo rya 17 Mukakaro 1993.



![Image](assets/fr/048.webp)



Slackware niho yaciye ihinduka distribution ya Linux ikoreshwa cane mu myaka y'1990. Umyubakire yayo yoroshe, inyandiko z'imiterere ya shell, kwubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako za Unix n'ukubura ibintu bikozwe ibice vyatumye iba ikigereranyo ku bakoresha binzobere barondera sisiteme yoroheje kandi ikorera mu muco.



Slackware iracabungabungwa n'uyu musi, bikaba bituma iba ari yo distribution ya Linux ikuze kurusha izindi igikoreshwa. Ni n'inkomoko kandi y'izindi distributions zavuye muri yo, bituma habaho umuryango munini wa distribution za Linux: Slackware.





- **Myandagaro 1993: **Debian**



Muri ico gihe nyene, Ian Murdock yatanguje distribution ya Debian, mu mpwemu itandukanye cane n'imigenzo y'ico gihe, cane cane iya koreshwa na distribution nka SLS, akenshi ibungabungwa n'umuntu umwe. Murdock yafata Debian ko ari umugambi w'abanyagihugu, uteguwe mu buryo bwuguruye, mu mpwemu ya porogarame z'ubuntu be n'umugambi wa GNU. Bitandukanya n'izindi distribution nyinshi za Linux, Debian ni distribution idaharanira inyungu.


![Image](assets/fr/047.webp)



*Ian Murdoki. Isoko: [Ilya Schurov CC BY-SA 2.0](https://www.flickr.com/photos/ivoyager/2398462112/).*



Ku bijanye n'ubuhinga, Debian yagaragaje itandukaniro muzindi kuva mu ntango biciye muri sisiteme yo gupakira(packaging system), uburyo bwo gukurikirana udusha, kandi ikiruta vyose n'ugushiraho ubutunganyirizo bw'ama packet buhambaye, *dpkg*, yuzuzwa ningoga na *APT* mu 1998, bishobora gutuma habaho ugutunganywa kw'amapaki kwizewe.




![Image](assets/fr/046.webp)



*Debiani 1.3 (1997). Isoko: Ububiko bwa distribution ya linux*



Mu ntango, uwo mugambi warashize mu ngiro ivyemezo vyawo vy'inyifato runtu mu gusohora *Debian Social Contract* n'ingingo ngenderwako z'i koreshwa rya porogarame z'Ubuntu za Debian mucongereza Debian Free Software Guidelines (DFSG) , kugira ngo hashingwe itegeko ritomoye ryerekeye umwidegemvyo ku makode n'ugukorera mu muco. Yatewe inkunga n'ishirahamwe ry'ama porogarame y'ubuntu, Debian yaciye yigenga mu gushinga ishirahamwe ridaharanira  inyungu ry'ama porogarame mu nyungu za bose canke mucongereza Software in the Public Interest (SPI) mu 1997.



Debian rero yabaye imwe mu nkingi z'ubuhinga n'ingengabitekerezo mw'isi ya GNU/Linux, umushinge wavukiyemwo amajana y'ibikoresho bikomeye, harimwo Ubuntu, Linux Mint, Kali Linux na Raspberry Pi OS.





- **1994: Red Hat Linux**



Marc Ewing yasohoye verisiyo ya mbere ya Red Hat Linux mu 1994. Ivyo vyatumye havuka distribution zizogira uruhara runini mu gutuma Linux ikomeza gukoreshwa kinyamwuga. Ewing yashimishijwe n'isi ya Unix, yararemye verisiyo ya Linux itunganijwe, ishobora gukoreshwa, ashiramwo igikoresho gihambaye: *Red Hat Package Manager* (RPM), cashizeko umurongo ngenderwa ko w'uko amapaki y'ama porogarame agomba kuba ameze kandi kuyashiramwo bikoroha, gushira kugihe no kuya kuramwo, cane cane mu bibanza vy'umwuga. Ubwo buryo bwabaye umurongo ngenderwa ko ukoreshwa cane.



Mu mwaka w'1995, Bob Young, uwashinze ishirahamwe ryitwa AAC Corporation ryitaho cane ibikoresho vya porogarame za Linux, yaraguze ishirahamwe rya Marc Ewing. Ivyo bigo bibiri bihuriye hamwe vyatumye havuka Red Hat Software. Bompi hamwe, barateguye uburyo bwo gukora urudandazwa rwo: ugukwiragiza porogarame z'isoko yuguruye (open-source) zifatanijwe n'ugufasha no gutanga serivisi y'icemezo ku bucuruzi. Uwo murongo w'urudandazwa wacitse ikigereranyo, kandi ushobora kuwusanga mu migambi myinshi iri mw'isi ya Bitcoin.



![Image](assets/fr/045.webp)



*Bob Young na Marc Ewing. Umufotozi: Candice C Cusic/AP*



Mu mwaka w'2003, Red Hat yaracitse mwo imice: ishami ry'abanyagihugu ryacitse Fedora, Ahagiye gukorerwa ubushakashatsi bwa guhanga udusha hamwe nuburyo bwo guhingura ivyobakora mu mwanya muto, mu gihe ishami ry'urudandazwa ryahinduwe Red Hat Enterprise Linux (RHEL), distribution yemewe, ishikamye,  y'igihe kirekire yagenewe ibikorwa vy'urudandazwa. Kuva ico gihe, Fedora yarakoreshejwe nk'ikibanza co kugeragezako ikoranabuhanga rizoheza rigashirwa muri RHEL. Iryo shirahamwe, Red Hat yarashoboye guhuza ubuhinga bwo gukorana n'abanyagihugu n'ubuhinga bwo gukorana n'inganda.



Izo distribution za zashinze imiryango ikomeye ya Linux y'ubu, imwe yose muri yo ikaba yarateguye uburyo bwayo bwite bw'ubuhinga n'umukenyuro wa firozofiya.



### Imiryango ikomeye ya distribution za Linux uyu musi 



#### Umuryango wa Debian



Uyu muryango wubakiwe hirya no hino y'ubutunganyirizo bw'amapaki ya APT hamwe n'uburyo bw'amapaki bwa `.deb`. Debian igaragara kubera uburyo bwayo bukomeye bwo gukoresha porogarame z'ubuntu n'uburyo bukomeye bwo gutunganya dependency.



![Image](assets/fr/044.webp)



Ubuntu, ikomoka kuri Debian, imenyekanisha Linux biciye mu buryo bworoshe bwo kuyishira mu nyabwonko no kuyikoresha. Ubuntu ifise izo bisa nyinshi zizwi, nka Kubuntu (ikibanza ca KDE) na Xubuntu (XFCE). Izindi distribution zihambaye zishingiye kuri Debian ni Linux Mint (nayo iva kuri Ubuntu), Kali Linux (umutekano w'inyabwonko), na Raspberry Pi OS ku nyabwonko ntoya za Raspberry Pi.



Uyu muryango ni wo tuzokwibandako cane mu nyuma, kuko ukusanyiriza hamwe zimwe muri distributions za Linux zikoze neza kandi zikunzwe cane zikoreshwe ku nyabwonko z'abantu ku giti cabo.



#### Umuryango wa Red Hat



Ishingiye ku buryo bwa RPM (*Red Hat Package Manager*), uwo muryango rero urimwo Fedora, distribution y'umuryango uhanga udusha ihari nk'ishimikiro ry'ubuhinga rya Red Hat Enterprise Linux (RHEL), distribution y'urudandazwa igenewe amashirahamwe kandi izwi cane kubera ukudahungabana kwayo kw'igihe kirekire.



![Image](assets/fr/043.webp)



Disribution ny'inshi zikomeye ziva ata guca ku ruhande kuri RHEL, mu ntumbero yo gutanga ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha ku buntu kandi buhuye, ata n'amahera y'ubufasha utanze. Murizo, CentOS yaramaze igihe kirekire ifise ikibanza gihambaye nk'ikigereranyo c'abanyagihugu ca RHEL, gushika Red Hat ihinduye kamere yayo mu 2020 ikaba CentOS Stream, verisiyo iri hagati ya Fedora na RHEL. Ico cemezo catumye habaho ama forks mashasha nka AlmaLinux na Rocky Linux.



Izindi distribution zihambaye ziva muri uwo muryango harimwo Oracle Linux, ifise ivyiza vyihariye mu bibanza vya cloud, na ClearOS, distribution yihariye kuri SMB ifise seriveri y'urufunguzo n'uburyo bwa firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro).



#### Umuryango wa Arch Linux



Umuryango wa Arch Linux utandukanywa nizindi kuri firozofiya itandukanye cane n'iya distributions za off-the-shelf. Ni zikozwe kukigero cohejuru, kandi zakozwe hakurikijwe ingingo ngenderwako ya "*KISS*" ("*Keep It Simple, Stupid*"). Arch Linux itanga sisiteme y'ishimikiro, itagiramwo ibintu vyinshi, uwuyikoresha ategerezwa kuyi yubakira n'amaboko bivanye n'ivyo akeneye.



![Image](assets/fr/041.webp)



Ubu buryo bushingiye ku kukigereranyo ca *rolling release*, aho amapaki aguma ashigwa kugihe, bidasavye ko usubira gushiramwo sisiteme buri uko haje verisiyo nshasha. Ubutunganizo bw'amapaki bwa Pacman burihuta kandi ntiburemereye, bituma vyoroha gushiramwo no guhindura porogarame, kandi AUR (*Arch User Repository*), ububiko bw'abanyagihugu, buratanga uburyo bwo gukoresha amapaki menshi cane atareremerwa n'aya kiriko arategurwa.


Arch Linux igenewe cane cane abakoresha b'inzobere bashaka kugira ububasha bwo gucungera ibibanza vyabo, mu gihe bemera kugorwa n'ibintu bimwe bimwe bigoranye mu kuyishiramwo no kuyibungabunga. Ico gisabwa mu buryo bw'ubuhinga catumye habaho izindi distributions zivuye kuri yo hagambiriwe gutuma ikoreshwa na bose.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/arch-linux-7a3dc8a8-629b-4971-bb0d-4eab94f93973

Iyizwi cane ni Manjaro, igumya ishingiro ry'ubuhinga rya Arch mu gihe itanga uburyo bwo kuyishiramwo byoroshe, ibibanza vy'ibiro vyatunganijwe imbere na gutevya gatoyi gushira kugihe kugira ngo ntihabeho guhagabana kwa sisiteme.


![Image](assets/fr/042.webp)



#### Umuryango wa Slackware



Slackware iguma ari intahemuka ku ngingo ngenderwako za Unix za kera, ishimikiye cane ku kworoha, ugukorera mu muco no kudahungabana. Bitandukanya na distributions zigezweko zituma habaho gutunganywa kw'ama porogarame bidasavye ko umuntu agira ico akoze, Slackware yizigira sisiteme y'ama paki ya `.tgz` itagira umuti wo kutunganya  dependency mu buryo bw'ikoresha, bisaba rero ubumenyi bwinshi ku bibanza vyayo n'ama porogarame yayo.



Ubu buryo budahanitse cane, bufatanijwe n'ugushikama kwinshi, butuma Slackware iba distribution ikunzwe n'abakoresha bazi utuntu n'utundi canke abahinga mu vy'ubuhinga bwa Unix, cane cane aho ubushobozi bwo kumenya imbere y'igihe no kugenzura ari ngirakamaro (seriveri, sisiteme z'imbere, ibibanza bihambaye cane, n'ibindi).



![Image](assets/fr/040.webp)



Slackware yavyaye distribution nyinshi, zimwe muri zo zishaka guhindura ikoreshwa ryayo mu gihe zigumya impwemu yayo: Salix, Porteus, Slackel...



Naho umuryango wayo uri muto kuruta Debian canke Red Hat, umuryango wa Slackware uguma ari ikigereranyo c'amateka n'ubuhinga mu gisata ca GNU/Linux.



#### Umuryango wa Gentoo



Ishami ry'umugambi wa Enoch Linux waremwe mu 1999, Gentoo yaremwe na Daniel Robbins afise intumbero yo guhingura distributions ishobora guhindurwa ku kigero kiri hejuru cane, bidasavye binaries zateguwe mbere, kandi ibereye ibikoresho vy'uwuyikoresha. Yahinduriwe izina yitwa Gentoo (iryo zina ryavuye kunyoni yo mubwoko bwa Papuan penguin,imwe mu nyoni zo mu bwoko bwa penguin ziruka cane), distribution ishingiye ku gukoranya(compile) amapaki kuva ku ntango, bikaba bituma ushobora gukora neza cane bivuye ku gukoresha *Portage*, ubutunganyirizo bw'amapaki buva kuri BSD ports. Gentoo igenewe abakoresha bazi utuntu n'utundi barondera ubushobozi, ubugenzuzi n'a sisiteme iremurutse, kukiguzi c'umwanya muremure ufata uyishiramwo no kuyi bungabunga.



![Image](assets/fr/038.webp)



Kugirango yaguke yavyaye izindi nyinshi nka: Funtoo, Redcore Linux (Sabayon), Calculate Linux, Pentoo, n'ibindi.



Ubwa nyuma, ChromeOS, sisiteme yateguwe na Google ikoregwa ama Chromebooks, yakomotse mu ntango kuri Gentoo, gusa rero kuva ico gihe yaciye itandukanwa na yo bigaragara.



![Image](assets/fr/039.webp)



Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi ku miryango ya distribution za linux no kubona neza amashami ya burumwe, ndagusaba kuraba iki kigereranyo ciza cane kandi gitomoye cane kuri Wikimedia: [*Ingenga bihe ya distributions za Linux*](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/1b/Linux_Distribution_Timeline.svg).



### Ni iyihe distribution ya Linux wohitamwo?



Guhitamwo distribution ya Linux bivana n'ivyo ukeneye, urugero rwawe rw'ubuhinga n'ivyo ushaka kuyikoresha. Akira urutonde rwa distribution zikoreshwa cane canke zihariye, be n'ivyiza n'ibibi nyamukuru vyazo.



#### Distribution rusangi kandi zoroshe kuronka





- **Ubuntu**:



Yateguwe na Canonical itanguzwa mu 2004, Ubuntu ni imwe muri distributions zizwi cane kw'isi. Ishingiye kuri Debian, yama isohora verisiyo nshasha mu buryo bwamako, ika gira n'amaverisiyo ya LTS (*Long Term Support*) abungabungwa mu gihe c'imyaka itanu. Ubuntu iratandukanye n'izindi kubere uburyo ikorana neza n'ibikoresho vy'inyabwonko, umuryango munini n'inyandiko nyinshi, bikaba bituma iba amahitamo meza cane ku batangura. Mbere, tuzokoresha Ubuntu mu gihe gisigaye turiko twiga ikicigwa c'imenyerezwa ca SCU202, kuko ni inzira nayo yo kwinjira mw'isi ya GNU/Linux. Ubuntu iza ifise ikibanza c'ibiro ca GNOME, n'ibintu bikeyi vyo guhindura.



![Image](assets/fr/020.webp)



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/ubuntu-78a3be56-5d51-4ec3-8629-0dd27c352ab5



- **Linux mint**:



Yatangujwe mu mwaka w'2006, Linux Mint ni distribution ikomoka kuri Ubuntu, yakozwe kuburyo itanga ubundi buryo bwiza, bwegereye uko windows ikozwe. Itanga ibibanza vyinshi vy'ibiro, harimwo Cinnamon, Fork ya GNOME yakozwe vy'umwihariko n'umugwi wa Mint, itanga interface igaragara, isanzwe kandi imenyerewe



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/linux-mint-da44852e-513f-4004-949a-8fde60c1bca5

Mint igaragara kubera ukworoha kwayo, ukuba izanana na codecs za multimedia be n'igikoresho co gushira kugihe gitunganijwe neza. Ku rundi ruhande, yizigira cane kubikorwa n'ibikoresho (infrastructure) vya Ubuntu, bikaba bituma ikorana na amahitamwo y'ubuhinga ya Ubuntu (cane cane ku rugero rwa kernel n'ububiko). Mint ibereye cane cane abakoresha batari abahinga, canke abashaka ubuhinga buteguriwe gukoreshwa budasaba kwiga cane.



![Image](assets/fr/021.webp)





- **Zorin OS**:



Zorin OS yaremwe mu mwaka w'2008 n'umugwi w'abanya Irelande, ikaba yibanda cane ku bakoresha Windows na macOS barondera guhindura bakaja kuri Linux bitabagoye. Ishingiye kuri Ubuntu LTS kandi itanga interface ishobora kwigana Windows canke macOS bivanye n'ivyo ukunda.



Kuyishiramwo bigenda neza, porogarame za nkenerwa uzisangamwo, kandi verisiyo ya "Lite" iratuma ukoresha iyo sisiteme ku mashini za kera. Hariho integuro zimwe zimwe, nka "Pro", zitari ku buntu (hafi €50), ariko verisiyo y'ubuntu iracakora neza. Zorin OS ni amahitamo meza ku barondera interface bamenyereye, ikibanza gitunganijwe neza ata bisaba guhindurwa.



![Image](assets/fr/022.webp)





- **elementary OS**:


Yatangujwe mu 2011, elementary OS ni distribution ishingiye kuri Ubuntu yibanda cane cane ku gicapo n'ugusanisha interface. Ikibanza cayo c'ibiro ca Pantheon, bisunze macOS, ntiri kurwego ruhanitse, imeze neza kandi igenda neza. Ariko rero, sisiteme iguma uko iri idashobora guhindurwa nk'izindi distributions, kandi abakoresha bamwe bamwe b'inzobere boshobora kwumva ko harivyo babujijwe kubijanye n'amahitamwo ya interface be n'imiterere yayo utogira ico uhinduye. Ibereye abakoresha bakunda ivy'ubwiza barondera sisiteme yoroshe kandi ihura nivyo bakeneye gukora umusi ku musi ku musi.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/elementary-os-757a20be-22b5-484c-a032-2bdd909860ac


![Image](assets/fr/023.webp)





- **Pop!OS**:



Pop!OS yakozwe n'ishirahamwe ry'Abanyamerika ryitwa System76, na yo nyene ishingiye kuri Ubuntu. Igenewe abakoresha inyabwonko bisanzwe n'abahingura ama porogarame, ifise interface GNOME yahinduwe (kandi ubu hakaba hariho ikibanza co mu nzu indani citwa COSMIC). Pop!OS izanana uburyo bwogutuma ama GPU ya NVIDIA akora neza, kandi ifise uburyo bwo gutunganya idirisha bwa mosaic. Sisiteme iguma yoroshe gukoresha, ariko kandi itanga uburyo bwokuyikoresha buteye imbere ugiheza kuyishiramwo. Igenewe abakoresha b'iinzobere, abanyeshure canke abanyamwuga bashaka sisiteme ikora neza batabwirizwa gutunganya ikibanza cabo n'amaboko.



![Image](assets/fr/024.webp)



*Isoko: [Na Allman - Igikorwa kiwe bwite, CC BY-SA 4.0](https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?curid=114760696).*



#### Distributions z'inzobere kandi z'ubushobozi bwinshi





- **Fedora** (Workstation canke KDE Plasma):



Fedora ni distribution ishigikiwe na Red Hat, ishingiye kw'ikoranabuhanga rigezweko (Wayland, PipeWire, Flatpak...). Ikoresha uburyo bwa RPM n'ubutuganirizo bw'amapaki bwa `dnf`. Uburyo isohora vyihuse ama verisiyo mashasha bisigura ko sisiteme yawe yama iri kugihe, ariko uzoguma ukeneye kuguma ushira kugihe. Ni distribution nziza ku bahingura ama porogarame canke abakoresha ubuhinga barondera sisiteme igezweko.



![Image](assets/fr/025.webp)


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/fedora-8c17b6ca-5acb-4825-a069-4474375534b0


- **openSUSE** (Tumbleweed canke Leap):



openSUSE iboneka nka rolling release canke distribution ishikamye. Irafise igikoresho ca YaST co gutunganya sisiteme, kandi ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bwinshi be n'ibibanza vyinshi vy'ibicapo. Bisaba gato ubumenyi bwinshi, ariko iguma ishoboye kuba yakoreshwe ku musi ku musi.



![Image](assets/fr/026.webp)





- **Debian**:



Debian iboneka mu mashami menshi, harimwo *Stable* (yizewe cane, ariko ni porogarame ya kera) na *Testing* (iyigezweko, ariko ntiremezwa cane). Ikoresha `apt` kandi izwi kubera uburindutsi bwayo, firozofiya y'ubuntu n'uguhuza cane. Debian ni amahitamo meza ku bakoresha barondera ugushikama, abayobozi ba sisiteme...



![Image](assets/fr/027.webp)


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/debian-d09a57ec-8372-40ca-bcff-499415209e1f


- **Manjaro**:



Ishingiye kuri Arch, Manjaro ituma Arch Linux ishobora gukoreshwa. Iyi distribution itanga uburyo bw'ibicapo bwokuyishira mu nyabwonko,ibikoresho vya in-house n'ubufasha bwiza bw'ibikoresho. Ugushira ku gihe sisiteme bishobora gukorwa mukindi gihe uhisemo kugira ngo wirinde guhungabanya sisiteme. Manjaro ibereye abakoresha b'inzobere barondera distribution igezweko ya Arch Linux, bidasavye ko batunganya vyose n'amaboko.



![Image](assets/fr/028.webp)





- **Arch Linux**:



Arch Linux ntiri ku rwego ruhanitse, ni distribution ushobora gukomeza ushira kugihe, iza idafise interface canke porogarame zidakenewe. Bisaba gushiramwo burikimwe n'amaboko, ariko itanga ububasha bwo kugenzura burikimwe be n'inyandiko nziza cane (Arch Wiki). Ninziza ku bakoresha binzobere bashaka kumenya neza buri kimwe.



![Image](assets/fr/029.webp)



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/arch-linux-7a3dc8a8-629b-4971-bb0d-4eab94f93973

#### Distribution zidasanzwe



- **Kali Linux**:


Kali Linux ni distribution ishingiye kuri Debian yagenewe kugerageza kwinjira muma sisiteme no kugenzura umutekano. Harimwo amajana y'ibikoresho vya pentest. iyi distribution ntibereye vy'ukuri kuba sisiteme nyamukuru ukoresha ku musi ku musi.



![Image](assets/fr/030.webp)





- **Parrot OS**:



Parrot OS nayo ikomoka kuri Debian. Itanga ikibanza co gukora pentesting, umutekano w'ibitero n'ukurinda ubuzima bw'ibanga. Ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bwinshi kuruta Kali, iyo distribution irabereye kandi gukoreshwa mu buryo busanzwe ku musi ku musi, hamwe n'ibikoresho ifise vy'umutekano bizanana.



![Image](assets/fr/031.webp)





- **Tails**:



Tails ni distribution ya live  ishingiye kuri Debian, yibanda ku buzima bw'ibanga. Ivyo vyose bica mu rubuga rwa Tor, kandi nta kintu na kimwe kibikwa hagati y'ibihe vy'abakoresha. Ni ugukwiragiza kwiza ku gukoresha rimwe gusa (itangazamakuru, ubukangurambaga, uruvyaro rwa seed Bitcoin...).



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/tails-15108901-f15d-4f7f-a001-b02b1dcd60c8

→ **Iciyumviro:** Distribution ya live ni sisiteme ya Linux ishobora gukoreshwa ako kanya atakindi bisavye kuri USB canke kuri CD, utabwirizwa kuyishira kuri hard disk.



![Image](assets/fr/032.webp)





- **Qubes OS**:



Qubes OS ishingiye kuri Fedora kandi ni sisiteme ikoresha ubuhinga bwa virtualization bwa Xen kugira ngo ikoreshwe mu bice. porogarame yose ikoreshwa mu nyabwonko mpimbano (virtual machine) iri ukwayo. Ni imyubakire irinzwe cane, ariko ikoresha cane ibikoresho vy'inyabwonkokandi iragoye kuyikoresha.



![Image](assets/fr/033.webp)





- **BlackArch**:



BlackArch n'inyongera bushobozi ya Arch Linux yagenewe pentest (nka Kali kuri Debian). Itanga ibikoresho vy'umutekano birenga 2800. Ni distribution ikwiye cane, ariko yagenewe abakoresha binzobere bamaze kumenya isi ya Arch, kandi bakeneye ivyo bikoresho vyihariye (abashakashatsi muvy'umutekano, aba pentesters...).



![Image](assets/fr/034.webp)





- **PureOS**:



PureOS ni distribution ikomoka kuri Debian yateguwe na Purism, ku buntu (vyemejwe na FSF). Yibanda cane ku buzima bw'ibanga, ifise porogarame z'ubuntu gusa kandi ntanakimwe kirimwo kiyihuza nabanyeneyo.



![Image](assets/fr/035.webp)




https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/pureos-2b6d5fe8-62f8-4a62-b898-4e0530ed408a


- **Raspberry Pi OS**:


Raspberry Pi OS (yahora yitwa Raspbian) ni distribution yatunganirijwe inyabwonko ntoya za Raspberry Pi. Ishingiye kuri Debian, n'amapaki yasubiwemwo ku bwa ARM architecture. Ishobora gukoreshwa mu migambi y'inyigisho, mu bijanye no gupima ivya eregitoronike canke seriveri ntoya z'umuntu ku giti ciwe.



![Image](assets/fr/036.webp)





- **Whonix**:



Whonix ifatanya Debian n'umuhora wa Tor mu myububakire y'ama VM abiri canke mucongereza two-VM architecture (gateway + workstation). Ni distribution ishingiye ku mutekano, ariko bihagaze ahanini kuri virtualization. Ni vyiza kuri abo bose bakeneye vy'ukuri kwiherera canke ubuzima bw'ibanga.



![Image](assets/fr/037.webp)



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/whonix-06f9172c-2962-412e-9487-b665d8ca9f59

Iyi panorama iraguha icegeranyo ca distribution za linux zihari uyu musi, biragufasha guhitamwo distribustion ihuye neza n'ubuhinga bwawe n'intumbero zawe.


Mu gice gikurikira ca SCU202, tuzokwihweza neza ikibanza ca Linux tuyikoresha, dutangurane n'ikibanza c'ibicapo arico kigize ibintu vy'ishimikiro mu migenderanire yawe ya misi yose na sisiteme.


## Ikibanza c'ibiro ca linux


<chapterId>ecfac353-a31b-48fb-b2af-2abbeeac5f2b</chapterId>


Muri sisiteme ya GNU/Linux, ikibanza c'biro kirafise uruhara ruhambaye cane mu bumenyi bwawe bwo gukoresha sisiteme. Ni igice ca sisiteme c'ibicapo kigushoboza gukorana na sisiteme, bishingiye ku bimenyetso n'amashusho bimenyerewe: amadirisha, menus, icons, panels na porogarame zizanana na sisiteme.


Muri iki gice, nzoba ndiko ndatohoza imiterere n'uruhara rw'ikibanza c'ibiro, ibice vyaco bisanzwe, imiryango nyamukuru iriho, ibigenderwako mu guhitamwo n'ukuntu gishirwa muri distribution za Linux zikunzwe cane.


### Ikibanza c'ibiro ni ikiki?


Ikibanza c'ibiro (canke "*DE*" bisigura *Desktop Environment*) ni umugwi wa porogarame zigize interface y'ibicapo yuzuye ya sisiteme. Kuri Windows na macOS, uronka ikibanza kimwe c'ibiro kizanana na sisiteme, kandi nta bushobozi bwo kugihindura cose (hariho gusa shells zimwe zimwe zo guhindura igice ca interface). Ku rundi ruhande, sisiteme za Linux z'ubutse mu buryo buri gice kiba kigenga, nukuvuga ikibanza c'ibiro ni igice cigenga gishobora gusubirizwa ata nkomyi.


Mu Linux, birahambaye ko umenya gutandukanya neza ibice vyose: kernel (icungera imigenderanire n'ibikoresho), seriveri yerekana amashusho (ikora nk'umuhuza hagati y'porogarame, ama drivers y'amashusho, be n'ibikoresho biciye kuri kernel), hanyuma ubwa nyuma ikibanza c'ibiro ubwaco,  gikenera ubu buryo bw'imikoranire kugira gitange interface y'ibicapo imeze neza kuwukoresha sisiteme. iritandukaniro riri hagati yi bi bice rishobora rimwe na rimwe kutagaragara neza, kuko ama distributions menshi ya Linux azana n'ikibanza c'ibiro cashizweho imbere y'igihe rimwe na rimwe kikaba cifitiye Wayland compositor yaco, ikaca ikora nka seriveri yerekana amashusho (display server).


![Image](assets/fr/052.webp)



### Ibice bisanzwe vy'ikibanza c'ibiro



ikibanza c'ibiro muri distribution ya Linux si porogarame imwe, ahubwo ni urutonde rw'ibice vya porogarame bihuye bitanga interface y'ibicapo yuzuye igufasha gukorana na sisiteme. Ivyo bice usanga biri ku nzego zigiye zitandukanye za porogarame porogarame, vyubatse kuburyo bukurikira:





- **Igice kijejwe gutunganya idirisha**: gicapa imirongo kumuzunguruko w'idirisha, gicungera aho rishirwa, kugabanya ingano yaryo, nuko rihinduka... Nk'akarorero: Mutter (GNOME), KWin (KDE Plasma), Xfwm (Xfce).





- **Igice kijejwe gutunganya dosiye**: kigufasha kubona urutonde rw'ububiko, kugira kopi, kwimura, canke gufuta amadosiye mu buryo bugaragara. Uturorero: Nautilus (GNOME), Dolphin (KDE), Thunar (Xfce).





- **Aho guhindurira imiterere**: aka ni akagwi k'ibikoresho bishoboza umukoresha guhindura ama parametere ya sisiteme atagomvye guca ku murongo w'amabwirizwa: uko sisiteme igaragara, wallpaper, gucundera ivy'umukoresha, umuhora, ibikoresho vy'inyongera...





- **Applets za sisiteme**: utu ni uducapo duto duto be nibindi bintu wo fyondako biri kuri kumurongo w'ibiriko birakogwa(taskbar) canke panel, nk'ahagufasha gucungera ama jwi, urugero rwa bateri, kuraba umuhora uriko, isaha...





- **Panel canke dashboard**: igice kiboneka, gikunze kuba kenshi hejuru canke hasi, harimo menu nyamukuru, Applets za sisiteme, inzira zabugufi, ahari ibijanye n'imenyekanisha, n'ibindi.





- **Igice gicungera ikiganiro**: gitangura gukora igihe sisiteme itanguye, kika kwereka aho winjirira ukoresheje umwidondoro wawe hanyuma kigatanguza ikiganiro cawe n'inyabwonko. Akarorero: GDM (GNOME), SDDM (KDE), LightDM (Xfce).





- **Igice kijejwe imenyekanisha**: gicungera ibijanye nokwerekana amatangazo ya sisiteme (ubutumwa, imburi, amakuru mashasha, n'ibindi). Nk'akarorero: dunst, Plasma-notifier, xfce4-notifyd.





- **X11 compositor (si mpaka ibe ihari)**: yongerako (ibitutu, kubonerana, n'ibindi) mu kibanza aho igice kijejwe gutunganya idirisha bidakunda ko habaho compositing. Nk'akarorero: kompton, pikom.





- **Seriveri yerekana amashusho**: iyi ni porogarame ijejwe gutunganya ivy'uguhanahana amakuru hagati ya sisiteme (biciye kuri kernel n'ama drivers y'amashusho) na porogarame z'amashusho. Igaragaza amadirisha kandi igacungera ivyo winjiza kuri keyboard n'imbeba. Seriveri yerekana amashusho akenshi usanga ari igice gitandukanye c'ikibanza c'ibiro, ariko sisiteme nyinshi ziriko zikoresha Wayland, uburyo bugezweko aho uruhara rwa seriveri yerekana amashusho rushobora gufatwa n'igice kijejwe gutunganya idirisha (nk'akarorero Mutter ya GNOME canke KWin ya KDE). Ivyo rero bica vyitwa "Wayland compositing".



Ivyo vyose bishingiye ku mugwi w'bikoresho vy'amashusho, ni ukuvuga, isomero (library) rya porogarame ritanga ivyangombwa kugira ngo habeho interface z'amashusho: aho bafyonda, za menus, ahaja ivyandiko... hariho imigwi y'ibikoresho ibiri nyamukuru ya Linux ariyo:




- GTK (*Umugwi w'ibikoresho wa GIMP*): ukoreshwa na GNOME, XFCE, Cinnamon, MATE...
- Qt: ikoreshwa na KDE Plasma, LXQt...



![Image](assets/fr/054.webp)



### Incamake y'ibibanza vy'ibiro vya Linux



![Image](assets/fr/053.webp)



#### GNOME



Yatangujwe mu 1997, isohoka ubwa mbere mu 1999, GNOME ("*GNU Network Object Model Environment*") ishingiye kuri GTK library kandi igamije kugabanya guta umutwe uronderera kure ivyo ukeneye kuri interface biciye mu gupanga ibintu mu buryo bworoheje. Kuva kuri GNOME 3, umushinge wayo, GNOME Shell, yarahevye imvugo ngereranyo ya kera y'ibiro vyuzuye ibicapo: aho gukoreshereza icarimwe ibibanza vyinshi vy'akazi, abakoresha bashobora gukoresha uburyo bumwe bwo guhitamo ibikorwa vyabo aho ba cungera amadirisho, ibiro mpimbano, nuko porogarame zitangura



![Image](assets/fr/051.webp)



Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, Mutter compositor ifatanya igice kijejwe gutunganya idirisha na Wayland stack, kandi ari nako ishobora gukorana na X11 kubera XWayland. Mubisanzwe, ikibanza kiba gifise Nautilus ikagufasha kurondera ama dosiye, Terminal ya GNOME ika gufasha ku murongo w'amabwirizwa, na panel y'imiterere irimwo vyose. Amahitamwo yo guhindura GNOME arafise aho agarukira.



Iki nico kibanza Fedora Workstation ikoresha, Ubuntu be n'izindi distribution nyinshi zikoreshwa ku nyabwonko.



#### KDE  Plasma



Umugambi wa KDE watangujwe mu 1996, verisiyo yabo yambere y'ikibanza c'ibiro yasohotse mu 1998. Mu 2014, harabayeho gutandukanya ikibanza c'ibiro n'ibindi bice vy'umugambi. Ikibanza c'ibiro giherako citwa "Plasma".



KDE Plasma ishingiye kuri Qt 6, uburyo bw'imikorere canke framework mucongereza bwa C++ bukorera kuri sisiteme zose, ishingiye kandi no kuri KDE Frameworks, urutonde rw'amasomero(libraries) agabuye mubice bifasha gutegura porogarame ziri kumwe na sisiteme. Igice kijejwe gutunganya idirisha ca plasma, KWin, naco nyene gikora nka Wayland compositor: gikora  ibijanye no kwongera ko (ugupfukiranya, kubonerana, guhinduranya), kugabura mwo kabiri canke kenshi ivyo ubona kumashusho ubifashwa mwo na GPU acceleration, n'ibimenyetso vya multi-touch vyinshi biciye kuri libinput.



![Image](assets/fr/055.webp)



Kimwe mu bintu bitandukanya KDE Plasma nibindi ni ikibanza cayo ahahindurirwa ibijanye n'imiterere, kigaragaza interface y'ibicapo ku miterere hafi ya yose: inyifato y'ibiro, inzira zangufi zose, uburyo bwo gukora neza, uburongozi bw'ububasha, imiterere y'umuhora, ukugaragara kw'idirisha... Nta dosiye za guhindura imiterere mu buryo bw'inyandiko zoguhindura, bigatuma rero vyoroha guhindura uko ushaka ikibanza c'ibiro.



KDE Plasma ikoreshwa muri distributions nyinshi, harimwo Kubuntu, OpenSUSE Tumbleweed, Fedora KDE Spin na Manjaro KDE.



#### Xfce



Xfce ni ikibanza c'ibiro c'ubuntu, kandi c'isoko yuguruye, cakozwe mu 1996 na Olivier Fourdan. Intumbero yayo ya mbere, ikiriho n'ubu, yari iyo gutanga ubundi buryo bworoshe, buremurutse kandi bwihuta butanduka nye n'ibibanza vy'ibiro biremereye nka GNOME canke KDE. mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, Xfce ishingiye ku mugwi w'ibikoresho vya GTK, ivyo bikaba bituma ishaka gusa na GNOME mu buryo bumwe bumwe, ariko kandi bigatandukanira mu vya firozofiya.



Xfce ifata uburyo bwa kera bwa interface y'ibicapo, bufise ibiro bikoreshwa n'uducapo(icon-driven desktop), menu y'ama porogarame, umurongo w'ibiriko birakogwa, n'ibipande bishobora guhindurwa. Ivyo vyose vyakozwe kuburyo bitonona ibikoresho, haba mu bijanye n'ubushobozi bwa RAM be n'ubushobozi bwa processor. Ivyo bituma ari umuti mwiza ku nyabwonko za kera, zidakomeye cane, canke gusa ku bakoresha barondera uburyo bugenda neza, bushikamye kandi bukora neza.



![Image](assets/fr/056.webp)



#### LXQt



LXQt ni ikibanza c'ibiro kiremurutse kigenewe gutanga interface y'ibicapo yuzuye mu gihe gikoresha ibikoresho bikeyi vya sisiteme. Ni vyiza cane cane ku nyabwonko za kera canke zidakomeye cane.



LXQt yaje nk'icamwa kivuye mu guhuza imigambi ibiri itandukanye mu 2013: LXDE (yateguwe mu ntango na GTK+ library) na Razor-qt (ikibanza bisa n'ivyo bishingiye kuri Qt). Ukwo guhuza kwavyaye LXQt, mu ntumbero yo guhuza utwigoro mu gihe wungukira ku bubasha n'ubuhinga bwa none bwa framework ya Qt, ihuye neza n'iterambere rya sisiteme za Linux kuruta GTK+ 2, ikoreshwa na LXDE.



![Image](assets/fr/057.webp)



#### Cinnamon



Cinnamon ni ikibanza c'ibiro kigezweko categuwe kandi kibungabungwa n'umugwi wa distribution ya Linux Mint. Catangujwe mu 2011 nk'inyishu ku mpinduka zikomeye zazanywe na GNOME 3, zibonwa ko ari uguhungabanya cane na bamwe mu banyagihugu.



Mu ntango, Cinnamon yari Fork yoroshe ya GNOME Shell, ariko buhoro buhoro yikuye muri GNOME kugira ngo ibe ikibanza c'ibiro cuzuye, aho ni mu gihe yariko irabandanya ikoresha GTK libraries (cane cane GTK 3).



Intumbero yayo nyamukuru ni ugutanga interface ya isanzwe, ishobora gutahurwa, mu kubandanyiriza aho GNOME 2 yarigeze na Windows: urutonde rwa porogarame ruri hasi ibubafu, umurongo w'ibiriko birakogwa, ahantu h'imenyekanisha, n'ibiro bishobora gukoreshwa. Ubu buryo buraryoshe cane cane ku bakoresha bashasha canke abava kuri Windows, bazoca babona ningoga ivyo bakoresha.



![Image](assets/fr/058.webp)



#### MATE



MATE ni Fork ya GNOME 2, yatangujwe mu 2011, inyuma y'ukuza kwa GNOME 3 na interface yayo itandukanye cane (GNOME Shell). MATE yavutse ku cipfuzo co kugumiza ko uburyo bwa kera bw'ikibanza ca GNOME 2, mu gihe ibungabungwa kandi ikajana nibigezweko.



Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, MATE ishingiye kuri GTK 3 libraries (inyuma yo gukoresha GTK 2 igihe kirekire), kandi igumya imiterere y'ibice: ubutunganyirizo bwa dosiye (Caja), panel y'ubugenzuzi, terminal, texteditor... Ivyo bice vyose ni ama fork y'ibikoresho vya GNOME 2, biguma bisanugwa kugira ngo bigume bihura n;ama sisiteme agezweko.



Interface yayo ishingiye ku nzira y'ubuhinga bwa kera: panel imwe canke zibiri (menu, ahantu ho gutangurira ningoga, isaha, ahantu h'imenyekanisha), ibiro bifise uducapo, n'imitunganirize y'idirisha rireremba.



![Image](assets/fr/059.webp)



### Ivyangombwa kugira uhitembo



Guhitamwo ikibanza c'ibiro cawe ca GNU/Linux si ikintu gisanzwe: bigena uburyo ukoresha sisiteme, ubushobozi bwa sisiteme, n'ugukorana neza na porogarame. Buri DE(Desktop environment) ishingiye ku mahitamwo y'ubuhinga (libraries, imyubakire, igice gitunganya idirisha...) bigize ico bikoze ku kuntu igaragara, inyifato, ubushobozi, n'ibikoresho bisabwa. Ngibi ivyangombwa nyamukuru umuntu akwiye kwitwararika igihe ahitamwo neza afise amakuru.



#### Ubushobozi bw'ibikoresho



ikibanza cose c'ibiro gifise uburyo gisaba butandukanye kugira gikore. Ivyo wobipima urabiye kuri RAM ikoreshwa, CPU ikoreshwa, n'igihe bisaba kugira sisiteme itangura:




- Ku mashini za kera canke zidakomeye cane (CPU ya core imwe, RAM iri munsi ya 2 GB...), ndabagira inama yo gukoresha ikibanza kiremurutse nka LXQt, LXDE canke Xfce. bitanga interface y'ibicapo ikwiye, ariko ata bindi vyiyongereyeko vy' udusha canke ibindi vy'inyongera bituma iremera;
- Ikibanza c'isumbuye ho gato, nka MATE canke Cinnamon, bisaba ibikoresho bishasha gatoyi (RAM ya 4 gushika kuri 6 GB ni yo ubwirizwa kuba ufise), ariko ubiravye birakwiye;
- Ikibanza kigezweko, gihambaye nka GNOME canke KDE Plasma birikwije, ariko bisaba uburyo bwinshi, cane cane iyo wemejemwo udukoryo tw'amashusho. Birabereye ku mashini nshasha za vuba.



#### Ubwiza(Aesthetic) n'ivyo ukunda bikorohereza



Buri DE itanga firozofiya yihariye ya interface:




- GNOME ishira imbere kworosha imikoreshereze, ifise interface itunganye, ata biro canke uducapo bimenyerewe vya kera, n'uburyo bwo gukora bushobora gutera ubwoba abatangura
- KDE Plasma irashobora guhindurwa cane, gushika no ku bintu bitobito. Irafise ukuntu igaragara mu buryo bugezweko, ibicapo bigendagenda, n'iyindi interface ishaka gusa ni ya Windows.
