- Cinnamon na MATE bitanga uburyo bwa busanzwe bwa kera: menu iri hasi ibubafu, umurongo w'ibiriko birakogwa (taskbar), uducapo two ku biro. Cinnamon iboneka nka sisiteme igezweko, MATE ira remurutse
- Xfce na LXQt zigamije kworosha n'ubushobozi bwo gukora neza, n'ubwiza buzigamye ariko bushobora guhindurwa



#### Ikigambiriwe gukogwa



Ikintu nyamukuru ugambiriye gukoreshwa inyabwonko naco nyene kizogira ico gihinduye ku mahitamwo yawe:




- Ku bijanye n'ibiro na multimedia, ikibanza ico ari co cose cokoreshwa
- Kuri workstation yo guhingura amaporogarame, ivyo wohitamwo biravana: abahinguzi bamwe bamwe bashima ubukerebutsi bwa Xfce, abandi bakunda ibikoresho bizanana na KDE.
- Ku ma porogarame ya seriveri canke yo kwinjiza(embedded) ada kenera interface iri kurwego rwo hejuru, canke ku mashini za kera cane, LXQt, LXDE canke Xfce ni zo zonyene woshobora guhitamwo .



#### Gukorana neza na distribution wihitiyemwo



Distribution yose ya GNU/Linux ishira imbere ikibanza c'ibiro gisanzwe, akenshi usanga carashizwemo neza atankomyi, kikaba cara geragejwe neza, kizanana n'ibikoresho vyihariye, kandi gishirwamo ku buryo busanzwe. Bizo kwama bishoboka ko ushiramwo ikindi kibanza c'ibiro, ariko ivyo bishobora gutuma habaho gushiramwo porogarame zibiri zisa, amakimbirane mubijanye no gutunganya, canke uburyo bwo gukoresha butagenda neza. Amahitamwo yawe y'ikibanza c'ibiro rero ashobora guterwa na distribution ya Linux, canke, bitandukanye n'ivyo, amahitamo yawe y'ikibanza c'ibiro ashobora kuba ariyo agena amahitamwo yawe ya distribution.



Usabwe kumenya ko distributions zimwe na zimwe, zaba zicungegwa n'umugwi w'umugambi canke n'abatanga intererano bo hanze, ziba zirimwo ikibanza c'ibiro gitandukanye n'ikiba gisanzwe kirimwoe (nk'akarorero Kubuntu, Lubuntu, Xubuntu...).



Ngibi ibibanza vy'ibiro vya distribution nyamukuru:





- Ubuntu → GNOME





- Kubuntu → Plasma ya KDE





- Xubuntu → Xfce





- Lubuntu → LXQt





- Linux Mint → Cinnamon (integuro nyamukuru), ariko kandi na MATE be na Xfce





- Fedora → GNOME (integuro y'ingenzi), ariko itanga ama Spins menshi yemewe:
 - Fedora KDE Spin → KDE igicapo
 - Fedora Xfce Spin→ Xfce
 - Fedora LXQt Spin → LXQt
 - Fedora Cinnamon Spin → Cinnamon
 - Fedora MATE-Compliz Spin → MATE
 - Fedora SoaS, i3, n'ibindi → ibibanza vy'ihariye





- Debian → GNOME (isanzwe irimwo), amahitamo ya KDE, Xfce, LXQt, Cinnamon, MATE mu gihe co kuyishiramwo





- Manjaro → KDE Plasma, GNOME canke Xfce bivanye n'integuro; Integuro z'abanyagihuga zirahari zizanana na Cinnamon, MATE, LXQt, i3, n'ibindi.





- Zorin OS → Zorin Destop, ishingiye kuri GNOME (Verisiyo y'Ibanze) na Xfce (Verisiyo y'yoroheje)





- elementary OS → Pantheon, elementary ifise ikibanza gishingiye kuri GTK





- Pop! OS → GNOME yaje guhindurwa na interface ya COSMIC, vuba izosubirizwa na verisiyo ya Rust





- openSUSE → uhabwa amahitamwo yo guhitamo hagati ya KDE Plasma (integuro ikunzwe kba irimwo), GNOME, Xfce, MATE, n'ibindi.





- Arch Linux → mubisanzwe ntitanga ikibanza, rero ukeneye gushiramwo ico uhisemwo





- Kali Linux → Xfce (isanzwe ikoreshwa kuva muri 2019), kandi itanga KDE, GNOME, i3, MATE, n'ibindi.





- Parrot OS → MATE (isanzwe irimwo), iyindi verisiyo na KDE Plasma





- Tails → GNOME





- Qubes OS → Xfce





- BlackArch → igice kijejwe gutunganya idirisha ca i3 (ntabwo ari ikibanza c'ibiro gikwiye)





- PureOS → GNOME





- Whonix → KDE Plasma (verisiyo nyamukuru), ubundi buryo buboneka na Xfce



Mu gusozera, nta kibanza kimwe ciza kuruta ibindi vyose c'ibiro gihari, ahubwo ni kimwe gusa gihuye neza n'ibikoresho vyawe, ivyo ukora be n'ivyo ukunda. Ni ibisanzwe mbere kugerageza DEs nyinshi imbere yo kuronka iy' itanga uburyo nyabwo buhuza y'ubwiza, ubuhinga, n'ubushobozi.



Iki gice kizoba caraguhaye ugutahura neza ico ari co ikibanza c'ibiro, ibice nyamukuru bikigize, itandukaniro riri hagati y'imiti nyamukuru iriho, n'ivyangombwa ngenderwako bihambaye kugira uhitemwo. Mu gice gikurikira, uzoshobora gutera intambwe zawe za mbere ukoresheje Ubuntu, distribution ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bwinshi ku bantu bose.



## Gutangura na Ubuntu: vyose ukeneye kumenya


<chapterId>7cea476d-f759-4c7e-8ca5-8b35bc79c682</chapterId>



Uyu musi, Ubuntu ni imwe mu nzira zishobora gutuma ushika kuri GNU/Linux: ikibanza ca GNOME ciza, ububiko bwinshi, amakuru masha y'umutekano n'umuryango munini. Ni co gituma nahisemwo gushikiriza iyi distribution.



Ariko rero, kugira ngo umenye neza gushiramwo ikibanza c'ibiro cawe bisaba gutahura uburyo shimikiro bwo gukoresha iyo sisiteme: gucunga amapaki, umurongo w'amabwirizwa, umutekano w'ishimikiro, n'imigenzo myiza yo ku musi ku musi. Muri iki gice, nzogutwara intambwe ku yindi, kuva ku gutunganya ivy'intango gushika ku gushiramwo ibikoresho vyo kugwiza umwimbu ni vyo guhingura, kugira ngo umenye neza ko ufise ibiro vyuzuye, bitekanye kandi bikora neza.



### Gushiramwo distribution ya Ubuntu



Imbere y'uko ukoresha Ubuntu, ukeneye kuyishira ku mashini yawe. Iyi ntambwe yoshobora gusa n'iyiteye ubwoba nimba utarigeze ubikora nambere, ariko muri iyi misi biroroshe cane kubikora.



Ibintu vyinshi birashoboka, bivanye n'ingene inyabwonko yawe imeze:




- Nimba ufise inyabwonko isanzwe irimwo Windows, urashobora gushiramwo Ubuntu iruhande ya Windows (*"dual boot"*), canke ugasubirira sisiteme yawe yose. Nimba uhisemwo *dual boot*, urashobora guhitamwo sisiteme uzotangura igihe cose ufunguye imashini. Uyu ni umuti wo guhitamwo nimba ushaka gusa kugerageza Ubuntu mu gihe uguma ufise uburenganzira bwo gukoresha Windows .
- Nimba ufise inyabwonko nshasha idafise sisiteme, ushobora gushiramwo Ubuntu nka sisiteme nyamukuru.



Mu bihe vyose, uburyo bwo gushiramwo bukurikiza izo ngingo ngenderwako z'ubuhinga, izo tugira turabona.



#### Kuvoma Ubuntu



Dosiye yo gushiramwo Ubuntu iza mu buryo bw'ishusho ya ISO, dosiye irimwo vyose ukeneye kugira ngo utangure no gushiramwo sisiteme. Kugira ngo uyironke, [genda ku rubuga rwemewe](https://ubuntu.com/download/desktop).



![Image](assets/fr/060.webp)



Hariho verisiyo 2 za Ubuntu:




- LTS (*Ubufasha bw'igihe kirekire*)
- Verisiyo igezweko



Itandukaniro rikomeye hagati ya verisiyo ya LTS na verisiyo itari LTS ya Ubuntu ni ikiringo co guhabwa ubufasha n'ukudahungabana. Verisiyo ya LTS ihabwa ubufasha mukiringo c'imyaka 5. Ku rundi ruhande, verisiyo itari LTS ihabwa ubufasha gusa mukiringo c'amezi 9, rero urakeneye kuza urahindura sisiteme yawe ubudasiba. Ku rundi ruhande, verisiyo nshasha itari LTS irimwo ibintu vyose bishasha. Ndabagira inama yo gukoresha verisiyo ya LTS nimba uriko uratangura, kuko igumaho kandi isaba guhindura bike cane. Ariko rero, urashobora guhitamwo verisiyo nshasha itari LTS niwabishaka: ntaco izokonona kuri gahunda yacu isigaye.



Fyonda gusa kuri buto ya "*Download*" kugira ngo ubone ishusho ya Ubuntu ISO.



#### Rema urufunguzo rwa USB sisiteme ishobora gutangurirako



Kugira ngo ushire Ubuntu ku nyabwonko yawe, ukeneye gutuma ishusho ya ISO ishobora gufunguka ukoresheje urufunguzo rwa USB. Urufunguzo ruzokora nk'uburyo bwo gushiramwo sisiteme.



Shiremwo USB ifise nimiburiburi 8 GB (wirinde, ibirimwo biza kuvako), hanyuma ukoreshe igikoresho nka [BalenaEtcher](https://www.balena.io/etcher) kugira ngo ukore ukore uburyo bwo gutangurirako sisiteme ukoresheje ishusho ya ISO. Hitamwo gusa dosiye ya ISO, urufunguzo rwa USB, hanyuma fyonde kuri "*Flash*".



![Image](assets/fr/061.webp)



#### Gutangurira ku rufunguzo rwa USB



Ubu rero ukeneye gutangura inyabwonko yawe atari kuri hard disk, ahubwo kur'urufunguzo rwa USB. Tanguza inyabwonko yawe maze winjire muri menu y'ugutangura canke BIOS/UEFI. Ivyo bikorwa kenshi mu gufyonda buto umaze Kwugurura inyabwonko yawe (kenshi `F2`, `F10`, `F12`, `DEL`, `ESC`). Suzuma ingene ushobora gushika kuri iyi menu ku mashini yawe.



Muri menu y'ugutangura, hitamwo urufunguzo rwa USB (rushobora kuboneka yanditse ko izina ry'umuhinguzi w'urufunguzo canke nka "USB"). Hanyuma uhitemwo "*Try or Install Ubuntu*". inyabwonko izoca itangurira muri Ubuntu mu buryo bwa "live": ivyo bigufasha kugerageza sisiteme ataco uhinduye, canke utanguza installer ako kanya.



#### Imiterere y'intango



installer izo kwereke ivyo uhitamwo:




- Hitamwo ururimi rwawe n'isaha yawe
- Ja k'umuhora wa Wi-Fi
- Hitamwo ubwoko bw'ugushiramwo sisiteme (busanzwe canke bwagutse) bivanye n'uko ushaka sisiteme ntoyi canke ifise porogarame nyinshi zashizwemwo mbere zizanana na sisiteme
- nimba woshiramwo canke ntushiremwo porogarame y'zindi (drivers z'amashusho, ama codecs, n'ibindi)



#### Hitamwo ubwoko bwo gushiramwo sisiteme



Umaze gutanguza Ubuntu, porogarame igufasha gushiramwo Ubuntu irakuyobora intambwe ku yindi. Kurikiza intambwe yose maze uhitemwo uburyo bukubereye. Intambwe ihambaye kuruta izindi zose ni yerekeye ubwoko bwo gushiramo sisiteme. Bivanye n'uko uhageze, hari uburyo butatu bushoboka:





- **Gushiramwo sisiteme iruhande ya Windows (*dual boot*)**



Nimba inyabwonko yawe isanzwe irimwo Windows, Ubuntu izoca imenya ubwo nyene iyo installation maze iguhe iciyumviro co gukoresha dual-boot kuri izo sisiteme 2:




- installer izogabanya partition ya Windows kugira ngo haboneke ikibanza
- Ubuntu izoshirwa muri ico kibanza kizoba kibonetse, na partion zayo bwite
- Hazoshirwamwo boot manager (GRUB), izogufasha guhitamwo hagati ya Windows na Ubuntu igihe cose inyabwonko iriko iraka .



Hitamwo iyi nzira nimba ushaka kuguma ukoresha Windows ku bikorwa bimwe bimwe (nk'imikino y'amashusho) mu gihe uriko uriga gukoresha Linux.



Kugira ngo ivyo ubikore neza, vyiza wobanza kurema igice kitagira partion kuri disk uhisemwo muri Windows, hanyuma ukaza kuba arico uhitamwo igihe ushiramwo Ubuntu. Kugira ngo ubikore, fungura Disk Manager muri Windows, utumbereze imbeba kuri disk ushaka gukoresha hanyuma ufyonde buto y'iburyo uhitemwo "*Shrink Volume*". Hanyuma utange ubunini bw'ikibanza wipfuza kubikira Ubuntu (vyiza wo koresha 80 GB kugira ngo uzoyikoreshe neza atankomyi).





- **Gusubirira Windows**



Nimba ushaka gukoresha Ubuntu gusa, ushobora guhitamwo gufuta ibiri kuri disk vyose:




- Ubu buryo bufuta amakuru yose asanzweko, harimwo na Windows .
- Ubuntu izoca iba sisiteme yonyene iriku mashini .



Hitamwo ubu buryo nimba wipfuza guhindura 100% ukaja kuri GNU/Linux. Ibuka gukora ubu biko bw'inyongera bw'amakuru ya we ari kuri Windows imbere y'uko uyafuta burundu.





- **Gushira sisiteme ku nyabwonko itariko ikintu nakimwe**



Nimba inyabwonko yawe ata sisiteme irimwo, canke nimba warahanaguye disk imbere y'igihe, gushiramwo bikorwa nkuko twabibonye mbere. Ubuntu izokwishiramwo nka sisiteme nyamukuru maze ice itunganye partition zikenewe.



Uzoca usabwa gushinga konti y'uwukoresha (izina, ijambo ry'ibanga, izina ry'inyabwonko). Hitamwo ijambo ry'ibanga rikomeye: rizogufasha kwinjira muri sisiteme, gushiramwo porogarame canke guhindura imiterere ihambaye



Ku bindi bisobanuro ku bijanye n'ivyo gushiramwo Ubuntu, ushobora kandi kuraba iyi nyigisho:



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/ubuntu-78a3be56-5d51-4ec3-8629-0dd27c352ab5

Igihe gushiramwo birangiye, kuramwo urufunguzo rwa USB igihe usabwe kubikora, hanyuma wongere utanguze. Ubu Ubuntu izoba imaze gushirwamo kandi yiteguye gukoreshwa ku mashini yawe.



Urakejwe ubu ufise sisiteme ishitse ya GNU/Linux!



![Image](assets/fr/062.webp)



### Imiterere ya sisiteme y'intango



Igihe porogarame igufasha gushiramwo sisiteme ihejeje, winjire na konti nshasha hanyuma w'ugurure terminal:



```bash
Ctrl+Alt+T
```



![Image](assets/fr/063.webp)



#### Shira kugihe



Amashusho ya ISO arimwo amapaki yahagaritswe amayinga menshi imbere y'uko asohoka, rero urokwama uhuza urutonde(synchonize indexes) hanyuma ukoreshe patches mbere:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt full-upgrade
sudo apt autoremove --purge
```



Ibwirizwa rya mbere rishira kugihe urutonde rw'amapaki ari muri sisiteme, rikavoma amaverisiyo mashasha maze rikayashiramwo; irya kabiri rifuta ibintu vyose bitagikenewe.



→ Ibwirizwa rya `sudo` rikora igikorwa gisaba uburenganzira bw'umuyobozi kandi risaba ijambo ry'ibanga ryawe kugira ngo wemeze ibigomba gukorwa.



![Image](assets/fr/064.webp)



Ubu rero urashobora gusubira gutanguza inyabwonko yawe:



```bash
sudo reboot
```



#### Ububiko bwa porogarame be n'imihora: gutahura aho porogarame ikomoka



Muri Ubuntu, porogarame ishirwa muri sisiteme kandi igashirwa kugihe biciye muri sisiteme ya ububiko bwemewe. Ububiko ni seriveri irimwo ibihumbi vy'amapaki y'amaporogarame (porogarame, amasomero, drivers...), vyose bitunganijwe hakurikijwe amategeko atomoye. Ayo mapaki agenzurwa, agashirwako umukono hanyuma agakwiragizwa ubwo nyene biciye mu buryo bwo gutunganya ama paki bwa `apt`.



Ububiko bwose bugabanywamwo ibisata. Kubisanzwe, Ubuntu ikoresha ibisata bine nyamukuru:




- **main**: porogarame z'ubuntu zibungabungwa ku mugaragaro na Canonical. Uturorero: Firefox, LibreOffice, bash
- **restricted**: porogarame zitari iza gusa zangombwa kugira ngo ibikoresho bikore neza. Akarorero: Drivers za NVIDIA, sisiteme ya Wi-Fi, codecs zifise banyenezo
- **universe**: porogarame z'ubuntu zibungabungwa n'abanyagihugu. Uturorero: GIMP, Inkscape, Audacity
- **multiverse**: porogarame zitegekanijwe n'amategeko (zisaba uburenganzira kugira zikoresha, zifise uruhusha kandi zitari iz'ubuntu). Uko zishobora kuboneka bivana n'igihugu. Uturorero: codecs zimwe zimwe z'amajwi/amasanamu, Steam



Burikimwe mur'ivyo bisata gishobora guca mu mihora canke amashami menshi: `versiyo`, `umutekano`, `gushira kugihe`, `backports`, n'ibindi, bihuye n'ingene ivyo bishigwa kugihe bimeze.



### Intambwe zambere ku murongo w'amabwirizwa



Interface y'ibicapo ituma gukoresha Ubuntu bishoboka, ariko ku bikorwa bimwe bimwe vy'uburongozi, terminal iguma ari igikoresho gikora neza kandi gikomeye kuruta ibindi vyose. Muri Ubuntu, shell ikoreshwa ni **Bash** (*Bourne Again SHell*), shell y'ubuntu ikomoka kuri Unix.



Gukoresha terminal bigufasha gukorana n'amadosiye mu buryo bwako kanya udaciye kure, gutunganya neza sisiteme, gucunga amapaki, ibikorwa vy'ikora ataruhara ubigizemwo canke gusuzuma ingorane. Aha niho hari amabwirizwa y'ingenzi uzokenera kugira ngo utangure.





- Erekana ububiko uriko ukoreramwo:



```bash
pwd
```



Iri bwirizwa ryerekana inzira y'ububiko uriko ukoreramwo. Ni ngirakamaro cane nimba ushaka kuguma ukurikirana aho uri mu giti c'ububiko.



![Image](assets/fr/065.webp)





- Urutonde rw'ibirimwo mu bubiko



```bash
ls -lah
```



Iri bwirizwa ritanga urutonde rw'amadosiye n'ububiko biri mububiko uriko ukoreramwo mu buryo buziguye:




- `-l`: uburyo bwa "*long*", bugaragaza uruhusha, ubunini, umukoresha, itariki...
- `-a`: nayo yerekana amadosiye anyegejwe (ayo atanguzwa n'akaburungu).
- `-h`: "*mu buryo umuntu ashobora gusoma*", yerekana ubunini mu buryo bushobora gusomwa (KB, MB...).



![Image](assets/fr/066.webp)



Ico bija gusa:



```bash
lsblk
```



Igaragaza igiti c'imiterere y'amadisk n'imigabane (partition) iri kuri sisiteme yawe. Nk'akarorero ivyo ni ingirakamaro cane mu kumenya USB sisiteme isoma, .





- Guhindura ububiko urimwo:



```bash
cd /inzira/iganisha/k'ububiko
```



`cd` nukuvuga "*Change directory*" canke mukirundi hindura ububiko. Ivyo bituma ushobora kuja hirya no hino muri giti c'amadosiye. Nk'akarorero, utanze ibwirizwa `cd Music`, uzoba uri mu bubiko `/Music`.



![Image](assets/fr/067.webp)





- `cd ~`: rigaruka ku bubiko utangurirako.
- `cd -`: rigaruka ku bubiko bwabanje.





- Rema ububiko



Kugira ngo ureme ububiko bushasha imbere mubwo urimwo, koresha ibwirizwa:



```bash
mkdir izina
```



Hindura gusa "izina" wandike ko izina ry'ububiko bwawe bushasha.


![Image](assets/fr/068.webp)





- kopiya dosiye:



Kugira ngo ukopiye dosiye, koresha ibwirizwa `cp`, ukurikizeko izina rya dosiye (utegerezwa kuba uri mu bubiko aho dosiye iri), hanyuma hakurikire inzira ija ku bubiko ushaka ko ijamwo.



```bash
cp dosiye.txt aho itegerezwa kuja
```



![Image](assets/fr/069.webp)





- Kwimura canke guhindura izina rya dosiye:



```bash
mv dosiye.txt /ububiko/bushasha/
```



Ibwirizwa `mv` rigufasha kwimura canke guhindura izina rya dosiye canke ububiko. Niwatanga inzira ija mu bundi bubiko inyuma y'izina rya dosiye, dosiye izokwimurirwa muri ubwo bubiko. Niwatanga izina rishasha mu bubiko urimwo, dosiye izohindurirwa izina.



![Image](assets/fr/070.webp)





- Gufuta dosiye canke ububiko:



```bash
rm dosiye.txt
```



Imburi: iri bwirizwa ntirijana amadosiye mw'iyarara.



![Image](assets/fr/071.webp)





- `-r`: gufuta vy'isubiramwo (ku bubiko).
- `-f`: gufuta kunguvu utabanje kwemeza (nivyo kwitondera).



Kugira ngo wirinde amakosa n'iri bw'irizwa, nivyiza kwongerako ubutumwa bwo kwemeza. Emeze muri terminal yawe:



```bash
echo "alias rm='rm -i'" >> ~/.bashrc
source ~/.bashrc
```



Uzosabwa kwemeza igihe cose imbere y'uko ufuta.





- Guhanagura terminal



Kugira ngo uhanagure terminal maze utangure na terminal itarimwo ikintu na kimwe, andika:



```bash
clear
```





- Emeza ibwirizwa nk'umuyobozi:



```bash
sudo ibwirizwa
```



Ijambo ry'urufunguzo `sudo` (*superuser do*) rikwemerera kwemeza ibwirizwa vyakanya gato n'uburenganzira bwa *root* (umuyobozi wa sisiteme). Uzosabwa ijambo ry'ibanga ryawe kugira ngo wemeze iki gikorwa. Urabe maso: ntuze wigere ukoresha `sudo` utatahuye ico ibwirizwa rikora.



Impanuro: guhindura ugakorera muri shell ya root (ikiganiro c'umuyobozi), andike:



```bash
sudo -i
```



Ivyo biguha terminal ikwiye n'uburenganzira bwa root. Uyikoresha wiyubara kandi ntuzokwigere uyikoresha igihe kirekire.





- Raba ubufasha kw'ibwirizwa:



```bash
man izina_ry'ibwirizwa
```



Ibwirizwa `man` (*igitabu canke manual mucongereza*) ry'ugurura inyandiko zose zijanye n'iryo bwirizwa. Kugendagenda koresha amabuto y'ivyerekezo (acafyeko umwampi) gusohoka ufyonde `q`.



Akarorero:



```bash
man cp
```



Kugira ngo ubone incamake yihuse, koresha:



```bash
cp --help
```



Aya mabwirizwa y'intango ni yo ukeneye kugira ngo ukore ibikorwa vyinshi vy'ishimikiro muri terminal yawe. Iyo wimenyereje gatoyi, uzoronka ubwigenge n'umuvuduko.



Mu bice bikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza ingene twokoresha terminal kugira ngo ducungere sisiteme, amapaki, n'ibikoresho vy'umutekano.



### Ugutunganywa kw'amapaki: APT, Snap na Flatpak



Kur sisiteme ya GNU/Linux nka Ubuntu, gushiramwo porogarame, gushira kugihe no gukuramwo bikorerwa hamwe biciye muri sisiteme yo gutunganya amapaki. Bitandukanye no muri Windows, aho uvoma amadosiye nka `.exe` canke `.msi`, Ubuntu ikoresha ibikoresho nka APT, Snap canke Flatpak kugira ngo ivyo bikorwa bikorwe, bikaba bituma sisiteme ikora neza.



#### APT: Uburyo bw'umwimerere bwa Debian



APT (*Advanced Package Tool*) ni ubutunganyirizo bw'amapaki ya Ubuntu. bufata amapaki mu buryo bwa `.deb`, avuye mu bubiko buzwi bwemewe. Buri paki irimwo porogarame, ivyo bikoranao n'amakuru y'imbere. Reka turabe amwe mu mabwirizwa y'ishimikiro, dukoresheje GIMP porogarame ikora amashusho nk'akarorero.



Kugira ngo urondere mu bubiko amapaki ahari (utegerezwa, vy'ukuri, gusubiriza "gimp" n'izina rya porogarame wipfuza):



```bash
apt search gimp
```



![Image](assets/fr/072.webp)



Kugira ngo ushiremwo porogarame n'ibindi vyose bishingiye kuriyo:



```bash
sudo apt install gimp
```



![Image](assets/fr/073.webp)



Igihe gushiramwo birangiye, uzosanga porogarame ushobora kwugurura mu rutonde rwa porogarame za Ubuntu, ruri hasi ibubafu bwa interface.



![Image](assets/fr/074.webp)



N'ikiruta ivyo: urashobora kandi kwandika izina rya porogarame ukeneye muri terminal (nka karorero, "gimp") kugira ngo uyugurure.



![Image](assets/fr/075.webp)



Kugira ngo ukuremwo porogarame, ushobora gukoresha ibwirizwa rikurikira (urashobora gusubiriza "gimp" n'izina rya porogarame wipfuza gukuramwo):



```bash
sudo apt remove gimp
```



Ushobora kandi kwongerako `--purge` kw'ibwirizwa ryawe kugira ngo ufute amadosiye y'imiterere ajanye niyo porogarame:



```bash
sudo apt remove --purge gimp
```



![Image](assets/fr/076.webp)



Kugira ngo ushire kugihe urutonde rw'amapaki ahari (`update`) no gushiramwo verisiyo nshasha (`upgrade`), ushobora gukoresha aya mabwirizwa abiri akurikira:



```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade
```



![Image](assets/fr/077.webp)



→ APT iranyaruka, iraremurutse, kandi ikorana neza cane na Ubuntu. Ku maporogarame yose ari mu bubiko buzwi, ubu ni bwo buryo bwiza.



#### Snap: amapaki yugaranye(containerized) ava muri Canonical



Snap ni uburyo bw'amapaki bwateguwe na Canonical, bwateguwe kugira ngo bube bwakoreshwa hose, butandukanijwe na sisiteme nyamukuru kandi bwigenga. Ivyo bisigura ko snap iba yifitiye ivyo ikenera kandi ikorera mu kibanza c'igerageza(sandbox).



Ivyo bituma bishoboka ko porogarame ishigwa kugihe yubwayo itari kumwe na sisiteme, kandi igakora kuri distribution za linux zose zemera gukorana na Snap. Ku rundi ruhande, bifata igihe kirekire kugira ngo utangure, bishobora gutuma umuntu yongeramwo ibintu bimwe bimwe bidakenewe, kandi gukorana n'ikibanza c'ibiro usanga bitagenda neza.



Kugira uronde ipaki ya Snap mu bubiko bwa Snap (akarorero kuri porogarame ya Spotify):



```bash
snap find spotify
```



![Image](assets/fr/078.webp)



Kugira ngo ushiremwo iyo paki:



```bash
sudo snap install spotify
```



Gushiramwo birangiye, uzosanga porogarame ushobora kwugurura mu rutonde rwa porogarame za Ubuntu, ruri hasi ibubafu bwa interface. Canke, n''ikiruta ivyo: urashobora kandi kwandika izina rya porogarame ukeneye muri terminal (nk'akarorero, "spotify") kugira ngo uyugurure.



![Image](assets/fr/079.webp)



Kugira ngo ushire kugihe amapaki yose ya Snap yashizwemwo:



```bash
sudo snap refresh
```



Kugira ngo ufute porogarame:



```bash
sudo snap remove spotify
```



![Image](assets/fr/080.webp)



→ porogarame za Snap zishirwa mu bubiko bwa `/var/snap` zigashirwako nk'sisiteme y'amadosiye iri ukwayo.



#### Flatpak: ubundi buryo bw'impine



Flatpak ni ubundi buryo bw'amapaki bwa rusangi, bwateguwe n'abanyagihugu bashigikiye (Red Hat, GNOME...). Bugamije gukuraho imipaka y'imiterere ya kera, mu gihe itanga uburyo bwiza bwo gucunga ivy'impusha kurusha Snap. Porogarame yose ikorera mu kibanza c'igerageza (sandbox), ariko gifise uburyo bwiza bwo gutanga ububasha bwo kugenzura.



Kugira ngo ushiremwo Flatpak na interface y'ibicapo bifatanye:



```bash
sudo apt install flatpak gnome-software-plugin-flatpak
```



Gushiramwo ububiko nyamukuru bw'abanyagihugu (Flathub) muri sisiteme:



```bash
flatpak remote-add --if-not-exists flathub https://flathub.org/repo/flathub.flatpakrepo
```



Kugira ngo ushiremwo porogarame biciye kuri Flatpak, koresha ibwirizwa rikurikira (muri aka karorero, kugira ngo ushiremwo porogarame ya VLC):



```bash
flatpak install flathub org.videolan.VLC
```



![Image](assets/fr/081.webp)



Muri make:



| Ubwoko       | Inkomoko  | ukwitandukanya | Ingano | Ubushobozi | Ububasha bw'impusha |
| ------------ | --------- | -------------- | ------ | ---------- | ------------------- |
| APT / `.deb` | Debian    | ❌            | ✅     | ✅        | 🟡                  |
| Snap         | Canonical | 🟡            | ❌     | ❌        | 🟡                  |
| Flatpak      | Community | ✅            | 🟡     | 🟡        | ✅                  |

#### App Center: installer ifise interface y'ibicapo



Ubuntu irimwo porogarame yitwa *App Center*, ikora nka interface y'ibicapo ifasha kurondera, gushiramwo no gukuramwo porogarame mu buryo bworoshe, ata gukoresha imirongo y'amabwirizwa nk'uko twabibonye. mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, App Center ikora nk'ishisho y'ubutunganyirizo bw'amapaki. Nukuvuga rero ko ishobora:




- Gushiramwo amapaki ya .deb ikoresheje APT
- Gushiramwo amapaki ya Snap avuye mu bubiko bwa Snap



Rero App Center store si uburyo bwo gushiramwo sivyo yagenewe gukora, ahubwo ni interface ihuriza hamwe kandi igahuza amasoko menshi ya porogarame, ikaba ifise ubuhinga bwo kurondera, amakuru y'ido n'ido amabuto yo gushiramwo ashobora gukoreshwa n'abatangura batabimenyereye.


![Image](assets/fr/082.webp)



### Kubungabunga no gushira kugihe


Kugira ngo ubone ko sisiteme yawe ari ntayegayezwa kandi ifise umutekano, Ubuntu ihita ishiramwo ibisha bihambaye vyabonetse biciye ku gikorwa citwa `unattended-upgrades`. Iyi serivisi ikorera aho utabona kandi igashiramwo ibishasha vy'umutekano vyasohowe na distribution, ataco urinda gukora.



#### Suzuma serivisi zihita zitanguza atabigizemwo uruhara



Kugira ngo umenye neza ko ubu buryo bukora:



```bash
sudo systemctl status unattended-upgrades
```



Ushobora kubona inyishu igaragaza ko serivisi ikora (iriko irakora) `active (running)`.



![Image](assets/fr/083.webp)



Nimba atari uko bimeze, ushobora kuvyikorera:



```bash
sudo systemctl enable --now unattended-upgrades
```



Iyi serivisi ikingira sisiteme yawe kugira integenye, bidasavye ko uza urashira kugihe sisiteme buri musi. Ni ngirakamaro cane cane kuri workstation zitagenzurwa cane, nk'inyabwonko z'abantu, kuko bitanga umurongo ngendegrwa ko wokugenzura umutekano.



→ **Ibuka:** `unattended-upgrades` igarukira ku mapaki y'umutekano ava mu bubiko bwa `umutekano`. Nukuvuga rero ko idashira kugihe porogarame zisanzwe, ivyo uzobwirizwa kuvyikorera.



#### Kw'ishirira sisiteme yose kugihe



Naho patches zihambaye zokwishiramwo ubwazo, birahambaye ko wo kwama wishirira kugihe sisiteme kugira uronke verisiyo nshasha za porogarame n'ibindi bitari muvyo `unattended-upgrades` itunganyiriza. Kugira ngo ubikore, koresha iri bwirizwa:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt full-upgrade
```





- `apt update` ihuza urutonde rw'amapaki ahari 
- `apt full-upgrade` ishiraho verisiyo nshasha, naho ivyo vyoba bisobanura guhindura ibintu bimwe bimwe (bitandukanye n'ivyo `upgrade`, ikora kuko yo harivyo idahindura)



![Image](assets/fr/084.webp)



Inyuma yo gushira kugihe, ushobora gufuta amadosiye adakenewe ukoresheje:



```bash
sudo apt autoremove --purge
```



Iri bwirizwa rikurako amapaki ya kera n'amadosiye y'imiterere bijanye.



Nimba warashizemwo porogarame biciye kuri Snap canke Flatpak, ushobora gukoresha aya mabwirizwa abiri kugira ngo uzishire kugihe nazo nyene:



```bash
sudo snap refresh
flatpak update
```



#### Gusubira gutanguza sisiteme inyuma yo gushira kugihe



Harigihe gushira kugihe bigira icobihinduye aruko usubiye gutanguza sisiteme cane cane nkigihe ushize kugihe kernel canke libc (library ya C ikoreshwa na porogarame hafi yazose). Kugira ngo umenye nimba gusubira gutanguza bikenewe, shiramwo igikoresho ca `needrestart`:



```bash
sudo apt install needrestart
```



Hanyuma wandike:



```bash
sudo needrestart
```



Iyi porogarame izo sesengura serivisi canke ibikorwa ivyarivyo vyose bikiriko birakoresha verisiyo za kera z'amasomero (libraries) canke kernels, maze ikubwire nimba bisabwa gusubira gutanguza kugira ngo ukoreshe ivyo bishasha.



![Image](assets/fr/085.webp)



Kwama ushira sisiteme yawe kugihe ningombwa cane iyo bigeze ku mutekano w'inyabwonko. Kugira sisiteme ya Linux iri kugihe bitanga gushikama, umutekano n'ubushobozi.



### firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro) be no gukomeza umuhora



firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro) n'igikoresho co gucungera umutekano kigenzura uruja n'uruza k'umuhora inyabwonko iriko. Kuri Ubuntu, uzoyikoresha mu kuyungurura uruja n'uruza kugira ngo wemerere gusa amakuru yemewe no guhagarika ayashobora kuba ari mabi. Ivyo bibuza abantu bo hanze kukwinjirira, nk'akarorero, kugira ngo urushirize gukingira amakuru yawe na sisiteme yawe.



Ukimara gushiramwo Ubuntu, kurinda uburyo bwo guhanahana amakuru bw'umuhora w'inyabwonko yawe ni intambwe ihambaye. Ubuntu irimwo firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro) isanzwe: UFW (*Uncomplicated firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro)*). Iragufasha gucunga uruja nuruza mububasha iguha, bidasavye ko urinda kwandika n'amaboko amategeko ngenderwako agoranye.



#### Gukoresha firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro)



Kubisanzwe, UFW isanzwe irimwo, ariko ntikora. Kugira ngo uyikoreshe:



```bash
sudo ufw enable
```



![Image](assets/fr/086.webp)



Iyo imaze gutangura gukora, ushobora kugenzura uko imeze n'amategeko ariho ukoresheje:



```bash
sudo ufw status verbose
```



![Image](assets/fr/087.webp)



Kubisanzwe, UFW ifata umukenyuro wo kwanka amahuzu ashaka kwinjira adakenewe mu gihe yemera amahuza uruja nuruza rusohoka, ivyo bikaba ari uburyo bwiza bw'umutekano canke imikorere ku nyabwonko yagenewe ibikorwa rusangi y'umuntu kugiti ce.



#### Kwemerera serivisi



Nimba ukeneye gutuma serivisi yokoreshwa mu buryo bwa remote kure y'inyabwonko (nka seriveri ya SSH), utegerezwa kuyiha uburenganzira:



```bash
sudo ufw allow 22/tcp comment 'SSH'
```





- `22` ni port isanzwe ya serivisi ya SSH
- `tcp` n'itegeko rikoreshwa
- igice ca `comment` kigufasha kwongerako insiguro isomeka kugira ngo vyorohe gusobanura amategeko mu nyuma



Ushobora kugenzura itegeko na:



```bash
sudo ufw status numbered
```



![Image](assets/fr/088.webp)



#### Gusigura amategeko hakurikijwe urutonde rwa IP (bikoreshwa mu karere)



Birashoboka ko ushobora kurekurira uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ama serivisi amwe amwe gusa ku urutonde rw'ama aderesi IP yemewe, bishobora kugira umumaro mu muhora wo mu karere w'aho hantu (LAN) Local Area Network:



```bash
sudo ufw allow from 192.168.1.0/24 to any port 6881 proto tcp
```



Ibi vyemerera TCP kuganirira kuri port 6881 gusa ku muhora wa `192.168.1.0/24` (mu bisanzwe uba ari umuhora wa Wi-Fi yo muhira iwawe).



#### Interface y'ibicapo: GUFW



Nimba udakunda cane terminal, hariho interface y'ibicapo yitwa GUFW, ituma vyoroha gucunga amategeko ya firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro) ukoresheje amabuto, urutonde rumanuka, n'ibisandugu vy'ibiganiro. Ku y'ishiramwo:



```bash
sudo apt install gufw
```



Imaze kujamwo, yugurure uciye ku rutonde rwa porogarame. Uzoba ushobora gukoresha firewall, kwemerera canke guhagarika serivisi no kubona ibiganiro vyayunguruwe muri ako kanya.



![Image](assets/fr/089.webp)



→ **Imigenzo myiza:** Naho woba utashize ahabona serivices izo arizo zose z'umuhorora, firewall izokwama ikenewe mu guhagarika ubwoko bumwe bumwe bw'ukurondeza canke bwo kwinjira. Kandi wibuke guhagarika serivisi zidakenewe kandi wame ushira kugihe porogarame yawe y'umuhora. Ukwo gukomera kw'umuhora wo mu karere ni umukenyuro wa mbere wo kwikingira mu nzira yagutse y'umutekano, ariko ivyo tuzobigarukako mu nyuma muri iki cigwa.



### Inzira ya interineti n'ugucungera umuhora



Hamwe na Ubuntu, gucungera umuhora bikorwa na *NetworkManager*, serivisi ishira hamwe amahuzu y'intsinga, Wi-Fi, VPNs, modems, n'ibindi. Ikorana hafi nahafi na *netplan*, igikoresho gitunganya imiterere y'umuhora hifashishijwe ivyanditwe mu ma dosiye yo mubwoko bwa YAML. Ivyo bikoresho vyose hamwe, bituma habaho uburyo bworoshe bwo gukoreshwa buri musi kandi bikaba ari umuti ukomeye mugi he duhaganye nibigoranye nka (amaserveri, guhindura imiterere n'amaboko, n'ibindi).



#### Gucungera hifashishijwe interface y'ibicapo



Ku bakoresha benshi, interface y'ibicapo iriri muri GNOME (System settings → Network/Wi-Fi) irahagije cane. iguha uburenganzira bwo:




- Kwihuza n'umuhora wa Wi-Fi urihafi
- Gucungera amahuzwa y'intsinga (wired connections), proxie canke VPNs
- Kuraba uko uko buri interface y'umuhora ihagaze



Ubu buryo bwo gucunga busanzwe burimwo vyinshi mu bikenewe ku nyabwonko y'umuntu ku giti ciwe.



![Image](assets/fr/090.webp)



#### Gukoresha teriminal na nmcli



Ku bijanye no gutorera umuti ingorane canke kwinjira urikure(remote access), ibwirizwa `nmcli` rigufasha gukoresha *NetworkManager* ku murongo w'amabwirizwa.





- Kugaragaza interface y'umuhora yabonetse:



```bash
nmcli device status
```





-  Kurondera imihora ya Wi-Fi iri hafi



```bash
nmcli device wifi list
```





- Kwihuze n'umuhora wa Wi-Fi



```bash
nmcli device wifi connect "wifi_name" password "password"
```



### Gushiramwo porogarame za ngombwa



Igihe sisiteme yawe imaze gukora, intambwe ikurikira ni ugushiramwo porogarame ukeneye. Ubuntu itanga uburyo bwinshi bwo gushiramwo (APT, Snap, Flatpak), ivyo twabivuze mu buryo buziguye haruguru. Aha, dukoresha APT igihe cose bishoboka kugira ngo tuzigame  uguhuza kw'umwwimerere hagati y'ama paki na sisiteme.



#### Mucukumbuzi



Mubisanzwe, Ubuntu irimwo verisiyo ya Snap ya Firefox. Ubu buryo butanga ukwitandukanya gukwiye(bi bikaba ari vyiza mu bijanye n'umutekano), ariko bituma igihe co gutangura kigenda buhoro, habaho gukoresha uburyo bwinshi bw'ibikoresho, n'imipaka imwe imwe kuri sisiteme (ugucungera amadosiye, insasanuro...).



Nimba ukunda verisiyo z'umwimerere za `.deb`, ushobora kuyishiramwo ukoresheje PPA yemewe ya Mozilla:



```bash
sudo add-apt-repository ppa:mozillateam/ppa
sudo apt update
sudo apt install firefox
```



Hanyuma, kugira ngo ubuze sisiteme gusubira kuri verisiyo ya Snap mu gihe uyishize kugihe:



```bash
sudo apt-mark hold firefox
```



Ibi bihagarika verisiyo ya `.deb` yashizwemwo. Izobandanya gushirwa kugihe, ariko izoguma ihagaritswe.



![Image](assets/fr/091.webp)



Turaza kuraba mu buryo buziguye ibijanye na mucukumbuzi mu gice gikurira, kugira ngo bigufashe guhitamwo iyo ukwiye gukoresha ivyo ukeneye, no kuyitunganya neza.



#### Emeyiri



Thunderbird ni porogarame  open-source yo kuruhande rw'umukiriya ya e-mail, na yo nyene yateguwe na Mozilla. Ikorana n'ama konti ya IMAP/POP, ingengabihe, inyongera bushobozi, kunyegeza na OpenPGP.



```bash
sudo apt install thunderbird
```



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/thunderbird-91d02325-0361-4641-b152-8975890284a8
#### Office suite



LibreOffice ni Office suite y'ikwije cane. Itanga ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha Word, Excel na PowerPoint, ikaba ihuye neza cane n'amoko yama dosiye ya Microsoft Office (.docx, .xlsx, .pptx).



```bash
sudo apt install libreoffice
```



Nimba wipfuza gushiramwo ibintu bimwe bimwe:



```bash
sudo apt install libreoffice-writer libreoffice-calc libreoffice-impress
```



Izo paki zitatu nizo zangombwa: Gukorana n'amajambo, Gukorana n'impapuro z'ibiharuro n'ugushikiriza.



![Image](assets/fr/092.webp)



Hariho n'ubundi buryo, nka OnlyOffice (ishaka gusa na Microsoft office), WPS office (bifise banyenevyo, ariko bigenda neza cane), canke Calligra Suite (umugambi wa KDE). Ivyo ushobora kubishiramwo uciye kuri Flatpak, Snap canke bikavomwa ku mbuga zavyo.



#### Multimedia



VLC ni igikoresho co gukina amashusho, imiziki n'ibindi, gishobora gukina amajwi/amasanamu menshi bidasavye codecs z'inyongera:



```bash
sudo apt install vlc
```



Ubuntu ntitanga ama codecs amwe amwe (MP3, H.264...) ku buryo busanzwe, kubera imvo zijanye n'amategeko. Iyi paki ikurikira yongeramwo ibikenewe vyibanze:



```bash
sudo apt install ubuntu-restricted-extras
```



#### Ibicapo n'ugucapura



Ku bijanye no gukora amafoto no gucapa, hariho uburyo bubiri bwa open-source:



```bash
sudo apt install gimp inkscape
```



GIMP ni porogarame iteye imbere yo gukora amafoto, igereranywa na Adobe Photoshop, Inkscape na yo ni porogarame y'ibicapo, igereranywa na Adobe Illustrator.



Ku bijanye no gukora amashusho, urashobora gushiramwo Kdenlive, ikaba ari nziza, ishobora gutahurwa kandi ibereye abatangura n'inzobere:



```bash
sudo apt install kdenlive
```



Ku bijanye no gukora amajwi, hariho Audacity



```bash
sudo apt install audacity
```



Ku bijanye no gufata amashusho ya interface(screen recording), streaming canke gukora amashusho, hariho OBS Studio



```bash
sudo apt install obs-studio
```



#### Ibikoresho vyo guhingura ama porogarame



Nimba uri umuhinguzi, ushobora gushiramwo ikibanza c'ishimikiro ca C/C++, Git, n'ibindi bikoresho wifashishije iri bwirizwa:



```bash
sudo apt install build-essential git curl
```



Gushiramwo VSCode



```bash
sudo snap install code --classic
```



Uretse ibi bikoresho bikeyi vy'ishimikiro, ndagusaba kandi gushiramwo ibikoresho vy'umutekano vyangombwa bihuye n'ingene ukoresha sisiteme, cane cane ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga na VPN:



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

Ubwa nyuma, kugira ngo dusozere iki gice, ng'iyi imwe mu m'imigenzo mvyiza umuntu yokurikiza ku musi ku musi:





- Koresha ibwirizwa rya `sudo` gusa igihe bikenewe cane. Iri bwirizwa riduza uburenganzira bwawe bwo gukora igikorwa nk'umuyobozi. Ikosa rya `sudo` (nk'akarorero `rm -rf`) rishobora gutera ingaruka kuri sisiteme yose. Ugomba kandi kwirinda guhindura ukaja mu buryo bwa root (`sudo -i`) umwanya munini, kiretse iyo bikenewe cane;





- Naho Ubuntu ihita ishiramwo ubwayo patches zimwe zimwe z'umutekano biciye kuri service ya `unattended-upgrades`, ivyo ntibikora kuri porogarame zose. Ugomba kw'ishirira kugihe sisiteme wewe nyene umusi kumusi:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade
```



N'iki gice ku vy'ishimikiro vya Ubuntu, ubu ufise ikibanza ca Linux gikora, gipanze neza kibereye gukoreshwa buri musi. Urazi gushiramwo porogarame, gutunganya umuhora wawe, kwama ushira kugihe sisiteme yawe, no kugira ico ukora uciye kumurongo w'amabwiriza.



Ukwo kwigenga mu buryo bw'ubuhinga ni wo mushinge w'umumaro warukeneye kugira ubandanye n'ibice bisigaye vy'iyi nyigisho ushize amanga. Mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano w'aho ukorera maze dushire mu ngiro ingingo za mbere zitomoye zo gukomeza ubushobozi bwaho bwo guhangana n'ibiza.






# Gukingira inyabwonko yawe


<partId>7fda3e41-ff0e-4fa0-8bd5-350d9ad5bbec</partId>



### Kwemeza uwinjira n'ukugabura


<chapterId>c8350e86-5581-4d51-8207-fd4ee48502a7</chapterId>



Umutekano w'inyabwonko yawe utangura n'ivyiyumviro bibiri bihambaye mu mutekano wo kuri interineti: kwemeza uwinjira n'ukugabura. Izo nzira zibiri ni zo shingiro mu gukingira neza inyabwonko yawe, kuzigama ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe no kugira ubusegaba bwawe muvy'ubuhinga bwa none. Muri iki gice, tuzokwihweza mu buryo bwimbitse ingene wocungera ivyo bintu ku nyabwonko yawe.



### Gukingira inyabwonko yawe



Gukingira inzira zigaragara niza porogarame zokwinjira mu nyabwonko yawe ni vyo bintu shingiro ry'umutekano wayo. Inyabwonko idakingiye irashobora guhinduka bitagoranye inzira uwukwinjirira yocamwo canke igatuma amakuru y'agaciro asohoka, mbere n'aho woba utari kuri interineti. Waba ukoresha Windows, macOS canke Linux, hariho ingingo nyinshi z'ishimikiro ukeneye gushira mungiro kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zo kwinjirirwa.



#### ijambo ry'ibanga rya sisiteme



Ijambo ry'ibanga ry'ikiganiro (iryo usabwa igihe wakije canke igihe imashini ivuye muka ruhuko) ni ryo mbogamizi ya mbere ku wugerageza kukwinjirira. Bibuza uwundi muntu gushika ku makuru yawe canke gukoresha nabi sisiteme yawe iyo inyabwonko yawe yibwe canke isigaye ata wuyicunga.



Iri jambo ry'ibanga ritegerezwa kuba rikomeye:




- Ritegerezwa kuba ari rirerire bihagije. Muri iki gihe (ruheshi 2025), nivyiza ko ukoresha n'imiburiburi indome 20;
- Ritegerezwa kugira indome nini n'into, ibiharuro, ibimenyetso bidasanzwe;
- Rikwiye kuba rigizwe n'indome zivangitiranije kuburyo bwose bushoboka, kandi ntiribemwo ikintu gifise aho gihuriye n'ikibanza cawe mu buryo bumwe canke ubundi, nk'izina, itariki canke ahantu.



![Image](assets/fr/201.webp)



*Isoko: [Hive Systems](https://www.hivesystems.com/)*



Ijambo ry'ibanga rigoye nta gukekeranya kuryibuka biragoye. Ndabahimiriza rero gukoresha ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga nka Bitwarden canke KeePass.



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

Ubwa nyuma, nuhindure iryo jambo ry'ibanga ubudasiba inyuma y'amezi 3 canke 6 na canecane nimba inyabwonko yawe ikoreshwa mukibanza gihuriramwo abantu benshi canke uyigendana



#### Gukingira inzira ishika kuri BIOS/UEFI



Umutekano w'inyabwonko yawe ntutangura iyo sisiteme itanguye, ahubwo utangura kuva mu ntango. Imbere y'uko Windows, Linux canke macOS itangura gukora, porogarame iri mu gitanda c'inyabwonko (motherboard), yitwa BIOS canke UEFI, bivanye n'umuryango w'inyabwonko yawe, ifata ububasha ku mashini kugira ngo itanguze ibikoresha hanyma itanguze igikorwa co kwaka.



BIOS (*Basic Input/Output System*) ni yo yabanjirije UEFI (*Unified Extensible Firmware Interface*). Muri iki gihe, UEFI ni wo murongo ngenderwako w'inyabwonko zose zo muri iki gihe.



Mubisanzwe, inzira yinjira muri iyo mitererer ntirinzwe. Uwugutera ashoboye gushikira imashini yawe (mu kibanza rusangi, mu gihe wibwe canke vy'akanya gato ataco ubiziko) yoshobora kwinjira muri interface UEFI aka gira ivyo ahindura bihambaye. Yashobora, nk'akarorero:




- Guhindura boot order kugira ngo inyabwonko itangurire kuri sisiteme yindi iri ku rufunguzo rwa USB
- Guhagarika uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano nka Secure Boot
- Gushiramwo porogarame mbi muri firmware y'inyabwonko yawe...



Kugira ngo wikingire ivyo bitero bidasaba ko uba uri kuri interineti, birahambaye ko w'ugara uburenganzira bwo kwinjira muri BIOS/UEFI ukoresheje ijambo ry'ibanga. Iryo jambo ry'ibanga ritandukanye n'ijambo ry'ibanga rya sisiteme yawe kandi ribuza umuntu ata vyemerewe kwinjira muri BIOS/UEFI.



Kugira ngo ibi bikunda, bizovana n'ubwoko bwa motherboard yawe, ariko muri rusangi ukeneye:




- Gutanguza inyabwonko yawe
- Ubwo nyene inyuma y'ukwaka, fyonda ningoga buto yo gushika kuri BIOS/UEFI yihariye ku mashini yawe (`Del`, `F2`, `F10`, `Esc`...)
- Muri interface ubona, nurondere ahanditse ijambo ry'ibanga ry'umutekano canke ry'umuyobozi (security canke administrator password).
- Andika ijambo ry'ibanga rirerire, ryihariye mundome zivangitiranije, hanyuma wemeze
- Emeza ivyo wahinduye hanyuma wongere utangure inyabwonko



![Image](assets/fr/203.webp)



**Imburi:** iyo utakaje iri jambo ry'ibanga, uzobuzwa gukomeza kandi uzobwirizwa kugira ivyo uhindura kuri motherboard. Rero, nubika iryo jambo ry'ibanga mu butunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga canke ahantu harinzwe.



Ikindi kandi, emeza "Secure Boot" nimba irimwo kandi itariko irakora. Ubu buryo burabuza kode itashizweko umukono canke ihinduwe gukora igihe imashini itangura. Ikoreshwa mu guhagarika bootkits na rootkits, ubwoko bwa porogarame mbi ishobora kwanduza boot y'inyabwonko, mbere n'imbere y'uko OS(sisiteme) itangura gukora.



Gukingira UEFI ni ikintu gikunda kwirengagizwa ariko gihambaye cane mu kugira ukingire inyabwonko yawe ibitero bikomeye. Ni kimwe mu bikorwa vyoguhagarika ibitero mu gihe inyabwonko yawe yafashwe.



#### Kurinda inzira igaragara yo kwinjira mu nyabwonko



Gukingira workstation ntibigarukira ku gukingira porogarame gusa: iyo umuntu w'umunyaruyeri aronse uburenganzira bwo gushika ku mashini yawe, arashobora guca ku nzitizi nyinshi canke agahungabanya sisiteme yawe ataco ubiziko. Ivyo ni ko biri canecane ku ma laptops (inyabwonko ngendanwa), yoroshe gutwara, ariko kandi ku gikoresho cose gisigaye mu kibanza gisangiwe nabantu benshi, cugururiwe bose 



Kimwe mu bitera ingorane (ariko bikaba bifatwa nk'ibidahambaye) ni ugusiga inyabwonko ata wuyicungera, mbere n'iminota mikeyi, mu bibanza vya bose nk'amasomero, amakoraniro, ahantu hafunguye no mu bibanza vy'amahoteli. Ivyo si ingorane gusa yo kwiba: mu masegonda makeyi, umuntu w'umunyaruyeri arashobora gucomekako USB mbi, agashiramwo porogarame y'ubutasi, agahindura imiterere ya boot kugira ngo agerageze kugira book kuri USB, canke agafata amakuru yawe yo kwinjira akoresheje igikoresho ca keylogger.



Muri iyo nzira nyene, ndabagira inama yo kudakoresha ibikoresho vyo hanze canke udashobora kugenzura. Irinde kwinjiza mu nyabwonko yawe USB, ama hard drives, ama chargeur canke ama dongle mu nyabwonko yawe nimba utazi inkomoko y'ivyo bintu (mu gihe atari bishasha canke ari ivy'umuntu wizigira). Ibikoresho bimwe bimwe bisa n'ibitagira akamaro bishobora kuba birimwo ama circuits ashobora gutanguza amabwirizwa mabi igihe nyene uyinjije mu nyabwonko. Ku rundi ruhande, ntutize ibikoresho vyawe bwite canke ngo ubisige ata wubicungera ahantu umuntu ashobora kubironka: vyoshobora gusubirizwa nibindi bisobora kukwononera.



Kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zo kwibwa, urashobora gushira kuri PC yo ku biro ubuhinga bwo kwugara. PC nyinshi z'abahinga zifise port ya Kensington security, kikaba gituma umuntu ashobora gufatisha umugozi w'icuma ku kintu kitava aho kiri. Vyinshi bisanivyo biraboneka kandi ku ma laptops (inyabwonko ngendanwa). Birumvikana ko ivyo bikoresho bidatanga uburinzi bukwiye ku busuma, mugabo birahagije kugira ngo umuntu ahagarike ibitero vy'akaryo.


![Image](assets/fr/202.webp)



Vyongeye, wama uzimy'inyabwonko yawe iyo uri kure yayo, canecane iyo uri ahantu hatagira umutekano. Bitandukanye na standby isanzwe, kwugara burundu bibuza OS gukora, kandi bikarinda ibitero bimwe bimwe bitera RAM. Biratuma kandi umutekano wawe wa BIOS/UEFI ujako.



Ubwa nyuma, imwe mu ngingo zihambaye cane ushobora gufata kugira ngo wikingire ubusuma ni ugukoresha ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru yose kuri disk. Ivyo bikingira amakuru yawe mu gutuma adashobora gushikwako ata jambo ry'ibanga, naho iyo disk yoba yakuwemwo hanyuma igashirwa mu yindi mashini. Kuri sisiteme zimwe zimwe, ubu bubiko bukoreshwa mu buryo busanzwe:




- macOS ikoresha FileVault
- Windows ikoresha BitLocker, ariko gukoreshwa kwayo bivana n'inyabwonko na verisiyo ya OS .
- Distributions ya Linux ntitera inyegeza ibiri kuri disk, kiretse iyo ubwi buryo bwahiswemo mu gihe co kuyishiramwo. Ushobora gukoresha LUKS kugira ngo unyegeze ibiri kuri disk


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/luks-13d9928b-08b1-478c-a1b4-67617978584a

Mu bihe vyose, ijambo ry'ibanga ryo kugarura amakuru yanyegejwe ritegerezwa kuba rikomeye, ritandukanye n'ijambo ry'ibanga rya sisiteme, kandi rikabikwa mu butunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga burinzwe. Nimba uriko urakoresha disk yo hanzeinyuma canke urufunguzo rwa USB rurimwo amakuru y'agaciro, nuzirikane kandi kuyanyegezaka ukwayo n'ibikoresho nka VeraCrypt.



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/veracrypt-d5ed4c83-7c1c-4181-95ea-963fdf2d83c5

### Ihame ry'uburenganzira buke



Ihame ry'uburenganzira buke ni itegeko ry'ishimikiro mu mutekano wo kuri interineti, rivuga ko ico ari co cose (uwukoresha, porogarame, igikorwa ca sisiteme, n'ibindi) gikwiye gusa kugira uburenganzira bukenewe cane kugira ngo gishobore gukora ibikorwa vyaco. Mu yandi majambo, ntukigere utanga uburenganzira bwinshi kuruta uko bikenewe, kuko uburenganzira bwose bwongereweko bwongera amahirwe yo gutegwa.



Mu majambo nyayo, ku nyabwonko yawe bwite, ivyo bisigura ko konti yawe nyamukuru ukoresha idategerezwa kuba ifise uburenganzira bw'umuyobozi ku bikorwa vya misi yose: kuronderera kumbuga  gusuzuma imeyiri, gukora ibikorwa vyo mu biro, n'ibindi. Porogarame mbi yugururiwe kuyindi konti ifise uburenganzira buri hejuru, ishobora kuba yohindura amadosiye ya sisiteme, igashiramwo ama servise yandi, canke igakurako uburinzi. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo ikorera mu kibanza kizitiwe, ubushobozi bwayo bwo gutera akaga buzoba buke.



Kuri Windows, benshi mu bakoresha barafise konti y'umuyobozi ku buryo busanzwe, naho ivyo ari umugenzo mubi. ndagusaba gukora konti y'ukoresha isanzwe yo gukoresha buri musi, maze ugasiga konti y'umuyobozi ku bikorwa biyikeneye vy'ukuri. Iyo ugerageje gukora igikorwa gisaba uburenganzira bwo hejuru, Windows izogusaba gusa kwinjiza ijambo ry'ibanga ry'umuyobozi aho gufyonda gusa ku buto "*YES*".



![Image](assets/fr/204.webp)



Muri Linux, iryo hame ry'uburenganzira buke rakoreshwa mu buryo bukwiye. Mubisanzwe, uba ufise konti y'uwukoresha ifise uburenganzira buke, kandi ushobora kuduza uburenganzira bwawe mu gihe gito ukoresheje ibwirizwa `sudo`. Birashoboka kandi gutunganya `sudo` kugira ngo yemere amabwirizwa amwe amwe gusa bivanye n'uwukoresha (biciye muri `/etc/sudoers`).



![Image](assets/fr/064.webp)



Kuri macOS, naho konti ya mbere iremwa ifise uburenganzira bw'umuyobozi, sisiteme ikoresha uburyo busa na `sudo`: ukeneye kwemeza ibikorwa vyawe ukoresheje ijambo ry'ibanga kuri buri gikorwa cose gihambaye ushaka gukora. Naho biri ukwo, birashoboka cane gukora konti yindi isanzwe hanyuma konti y'umuyobozi igakoreshe rimwe na rimwe, ivyo bibavyiza mu gihe inyabwonko ikoreshwa n'abantu benshi.



Uko kuntu vyubatse ntikugarukira ku bantu bakoresha inyabwonko gusa. Porogarame nyinshi zisaba uburenganzira bwo hejuru igihe uzishiramwo, hanyuma zikabandanya zikorana n'ubwo burenganzira kugeza aho bitagikenewe. Ndaguhanura rero, aho bishoboka hose, guhitamwo porogarame zidasaba uburenganzira bwo hejuru, gukuramwo izo utagikoresha no kuba maso ku bijanye n'ugusaba guhabwa uburenganzira bwo hejuru.



### Ibiganiro vy'inshi(Multisession): ibibanza bitandukanye



Uretse gutandukanya amakonti y'abarongozi n'amakonti asanzwe, uburyo bwiza bukwiye ni ukurema ibiganiro(sessions) bitandukanye ku nyabwonko imwe kugira ngo buri kiganiro gikoreshwe ibintu kanaka nikindi gutyo. ubwo buryo bushingiye ku nsiguro yoroshe: mu kugabura ibikorwa vyawe mubibanza bitandukanye, ugabanura amahirwe ya buri kibanza yo gutegwa kandi bikagabanya ingaruka zitewe n'isanganya ribaye muvy'umutekano.



Sisiteme zose zigezweko zikwemerera gukora amakonti menshi ku mashini imwe. Izo konti imwe yose irafise ikibanza cayo bwite: amadosiye, ama porogarame, imiterere n'ikiganiro ku muhora ntibisangiwe hagati yayo makonti, kiretse mu gihe vyemejwe mu buryo butomoye.



Nk'akarorero, woshobora gutunganya ibiganiro vyawe gutya:




- Konti yihariye y'ibikorwa vyawe kinyamwuga, aho ushiramwo gusa porogarame ukeneye cane (office suite, ibikoresho vyo gukorana, guhanahana ubutumwa kinyamwuga...). Iki kiganiro ntigitegerezwa gukoreshwa mu kurondera kumbuga canke mu kugerageza porogarame;
- Konti yo gukoresha bisanzwe, ikoreshwa mu kurondera kumbuga, ku mbugankoranyambaga, streaming canke mu gushiramwo porogarame z'consumer. Iki nico kiganiro kenshi gikunda guterwa cane n'ibitero vya mucukumbuzi canke amadosiye ateye amakenga;
- Konti yagenewe ibikorwa bihambaye, nkukugenzura amakonti ya banki, gucunga amakete yawe ya Bitcoin, canke ikindi gikorwa cose gisaba umutekano ukwiye. Iyi konti ikwiye gukoreshwa gusa muri ivyo bikorwa, hakaba harimwo porogarame zashizwemwo zikoreshwa ibikenewe gusa, kandi hakaba harimwo n'imiterere y'umuhora ikomeye gusumvya;
- Konti y'umushyitsi canke ifise uburenganzira buke cane, igenewe gusa gukoreshwa rimwe na rimwe n'abagize umuryango, nk'akarorero. Iyi konti itegerezwa kuba idafise uburenganzira bw'umuyobozi kandi ikaba ifise uburenganzira kubintu bike.



Hariho ivyiza vyinshi vyo gukoresha ubwo buryo. Ica mbere, ama porogarame ashizwe mw'ikonti imwe ntashobora kugira aho ahurira nay'abandi (kiretse iyo ubwoburenganzira ubufise). Ica kabiri, iyo ikonti ihungabanijwe, nk'akarorero biciye ku maporogarame afise umugera nyabwonko yavomwe kuri interineti, ingaruka muri rusangi zigarukira kwiyo konti gusa. Ivyo bisigura ko inyandiko zawe z'urudandazwa canke amakete yawe ya Bitcoin bizoguma bidashobora gushikirwa n'uwo mugera igihe bibitswe muyindi konti.



Kuri Linux, ukwo gutandukanya amakonti gushobora gukomezwa n'uburyo nka AppArmor canke SELinux, bushobora gukoreshwa mu kurushirizaho kugabanya uburenganzira bwa buri konti.



![Image](assets/fr/205.webp)



Ni ngombwa kumenya ko multisession idasubirira gukoresha konti itari umuyobozi, canke gukoresha ihame ry'uburenganzira buke. Ahubwo iza kwongerako ubundi bushobozi bwo gutandukanya amakonti wisunze ibizokorerwamo, biroroshe gukora kandi biragira umumaro mumikoreshereze kinyamwuga canke mumuryango.



Ubwa nyuma, ubundi buryo, bukomeye kuruta ariko bukora neza cane, ni ugutanga inyabwonko zitandukanye imwe imwe nico yagenewe, nk'akarorero: laptop (inyabwonko ngendanwa) imwe ikoreshwa gusa mu bikorwa vy'umwuga, iyindi ikoreshwa ku giti cawe, n'iya gatatu yoroheje kandi icungizwe neza igenewe ibikorwa bihambaye.



### Inyabwonko mpimbano (Virtual machines)



Inyabwonko mpimbano (canke "VMs") zigufasha gukora ikibanza cihariye mu nyabwonko yawe. VM yigan'inyabwonko yigenga ifise sisiteme yayo, porogarame zayo n'imiterere yayo, ariko mu vy'ukuri iba ari porogarame ikorera ku mashini yawe nyamukuru.



Iri koranabuhanga rishingiye kuri hypervisor, ni porogarame icungera uguhingura no gushirwa mu ngiro kwa VMs. Umuti uzwi cane ni VirtualBox, ni porogarame ya open-source, ikorana na sisiteme zose. Ituma vyoroha gukora VM mu gufyonda inshuro nke, mu kuyiha uburyo bw'ibikoresho yihariye.



![Image](assets/fr/206.webp)


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/virtualbox-6472f5be-10ce-4a07-8b24-097bfbcedd65

Ku bijanye n'umutekano w'ivy'ikoranabuhanga ry'amakuru, kimwe mu vyiza bikomeye vya VMs ni ubushobozi bwo gukora ikibanza cihariye. VM ntisangira amadosiye yayo, ibikorwa canke uburyo bwo gushika ku muhora na sisiteme irimwo, kiretse uvyemeje kubushake. Rero iyo VM ifashwe n'umugera, canke iyo ugerageje porogarame z'amabanga akomeye ziri muri yo, ingaruka ziguma muri VM: sisiteme yawe nyamukuru iguma uko yariri, igihe cose imiterere y'ukwitandukanya yubahirijwe (nta bubiko busangiwe, nta bikoresho vya USB bica kuri VM...).



VM irashobora kugufasha kugerageza porogarame ziteye amakenga: iyo uvomye porogarame kw'isoko itizewe canke ku rubuga ruteye amakenga, urashobora kubanza kuyikoresherza muri VM kugira ngo ubone inyifato yayo mu mutekano wose. Ivyo bifise umumaro kandi mu gihe uriko uronderera amakuru kumbuga zishobora gutera ingorane: urashobora kugena VM uzohora urakoresha ku bijanye no kuraba ibintu utazi vy'amabanga akomeye kumbuga, ivyo bikaba bigabanya amahirwe y'ibitero vya mucukumbuzi. Muri make: gukoresha VM bigufasha gutandukanya mu buryo bworoshe ikoreshwa ry'ibintu bimwe bimwe na sisiteme yawe.



Ubwa nyuma, birahambaye ko utahura ko umutekano utangwa na VMs uvana n'ingene zitunganijwe neza. Mubisanzwe, hypervisors zimwe zimwe zitanga uburenganzira bwo guhana amadosiye hagati ya sisiteme nyamukuru na VM, canke zikemerera kwakira ibikoresho vyo kuruhande vya USB. Ubwo bushobozi bukwiye guhagarara kugira ngo VM ishobore kwitandukanya birushijeko.



### Igikorwa ca Sandboxing



Sandboxing ni uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano w'inyabwonko bujanye n'ugukoresha porogarame canke igikorwa mu kibanza kiri ukwaco, gifise uburenganzira buke cane. Intumbero ni ukugabanya cane uburyo porogarame ikorana n'ibindi bice vyo muri sisiteme. Iyo habaye ikintu cokonona, ingaruka bigize ziguma aho nyenera.



Aho bitandukaniye na VMs, yigana sisiteme ikwiye n'uburyo bw'ibikoresho vyayo bwite, sandboxing iraremurutse, iranyaruka gukoreshwa kandi ntikoresha uburyo bw'ibikoresho bwinshi. Ishingiye ku buryo bwo kugabanya uburenganzira bwo kugira ico porogarame ironka: kuri RAM, ku madosiye, kumihora, ku bikoresho vyo ku ruhande... porogarame iri muri sandbox ishobora, nk'akarorero, gusoma dosiye imara igihe gito ariko ntiyigere yinjira mu bubiko bwawe bwite canke muri sisiteme y'amadosiye.



Akira inyishu zitomoye za sandboxing, bivanye na OS yawe ukoresha:



**Windows**




- Windows Sandbox (iboneka gusa muri Windows 10/11 Pro na Enterprise);
- Sandboxie Plus (open source).



**Linux**




- Firejail: igikoresho gikomeye, gifise kiremurutse gishira porogarame ukwayo hakoreshejwe uburyo bwategekanijwe imbere. Ikorana neza na porogarame zitari  nke, harimwo Firefox, VLC na Telegram;
- Flatpak: nk'uko twamaze kubibona, iyi si porogarame ya sanboxing ubwayo, ahubwo ni ubutunganyirizo bw'ama paki bufatanye na sandboxing: porogarame yose ishizwemwo biciye kuri Flatpak mu busanzwe ica yitandukanya na sisiteme, ifise uburyo bwiza bwo kugenzura uburenganzira nko (gukoresha mikoro, kamera, umuhora, n'ibindi).



**MacOS**




- Kuri macOS, sandboxing ni uburyo bw'umwimerere bwubakiye muri kernel, ariko bukora gusa iyo vyategekanijwe nuwakoze porogarame. porogarame za App Store zihita zishirwa muri sandbox, ariko nk'izavuye k'urubuga (canke zivuye ku murongo w'amabwirizwa) mu bisanzwe ntizishirwa muri sandbox.



Ubwa nyuma, naho sandboxing itanga ubundi bushobozi bwo kwikingira, birahambaye gutahura ko itaje gusubirira VM canke uburyo bwo kugabura  sisiteme mubice.



Ubu ko twamaze kuvuga ibijanye n'umutekano w'inyabwonko yawe biciye mu kwemeza uwinjira no gukora ikibanza cihariye, mu gice gikurikira tuzora kubijanye n'uburyo bwiza bwo kuyibungabunga kugira ngo urushirizeho gukaza umutekano wayo.



## Kugabanya amakosa biciye mu kubungabunga


<chapterId>71d7fd95-ce1d-43d8-9a66-be7b425857fc</chapterId>



Abantu benshi biyumvira ko gushiramwo porogarame zikingira umugera canke guhitamwo ijambo ry'ibanga ryiza bihagije kugira ngo bakingire inyabwonko zabo. Ariko hariho vyinshi ku mutekano w'inyabwonko kuruta gutunganya ibintu rimwe gusa bikitwa ko bihagije. Ukuri kurengeye kure ivyo twibwira: ibitero vyinshi vyo kuri interineti bikoresha integenye za sisiteme idashirwa kugihe. Mu yandi majambo, umutekano w'inyabwonko na wo nyene usaba ko udasiba kubungabunga imachine yawe.



Muri iki gice, nzogutwara intambwe ku yindi mu buryo bwo kubungabunga neza inyabwonko yawe, no kugabanya ingorane zo guhungabanywa.



### Ibishigwa kugihe vya sisiteme



Nk'uko twabibonye mu ntango y'iki cigwa, sisiteme icungera ibikoresho (processor, memory, disks, ibikoresho vyo kuruhande ibikoresho vyo kuruhande, n'ibindi), igatanguza ama porogarame, igaratunganya amadosiye kandi igacungera amahuzu y'umuhora. Ni co gituma ari ikintu gihambaye cane kiri ku mashini yawe.



#### Ni kuki woshira OS yawe kugihe?



Kubera ari urusobe rw'ibintu vyinshi, nta verisiyo ya OS wovuga ko itoshobora guhunganywa canke ngo ibure integenke. Aha turiko tuvuga ivy'imirongo y'amakode igera ku ma miriyoni. Izo ntegenye zirashobora gukoreshwa n'abatera kugira ngo barungike kode mbi, baronke uburenganzira batemerewe canke ngo bashire mu kaga sisiteme yose. Zimwe muri izo ntegenke zivumburwa n'abashakashatsi mu vy'umutekano wo kuri interineti mu buryo bubereye biciye mumuco, mu gihe izindi ziriko ziravumburwa nabandi mu buryo butazwi muri rusangi: izo zizwi kw'izina rya zero-day vulnerabilities.


Abadandaza sisiteme basohora ubudasiba amakuru mashasha y'umutekano agenewe gukosora izo ntegenke. Kudashiramwo izo patches ni nk'ugusiga ibigirankana umuryango wugururiwe ibitero, naho woba wibaza ko atavyinshi ukoreshe canke ko amakuru yawe ata co amaze.



Si ikibazo co gukosora ibibazo bigaragara gusa, ariko ni ukugira ico ukoze ku bishobobora kuba imvo y'ibitero kuri sisiteme yawe. Uko imvo ziba nke, niko n'abatera inyabwonko yawe bagabanuka.



Mu buryo bwihariye, ndagusaba ko wokwemeza ko sisiteme iza irishira kugihe utabigizemwo uruhara. Uburyo n'umwimerere kuri sisiteme zose zigezweko muri iki gihe. Nk'akarorero, Windows Update ijejwe gutunganya ivyo gushira kugihe ku mashini za Windows 10 na 11. Kuri macOS, amakuru masha y'umutekano ashigwa muri sisiteme yo gushira kugihe. Kuri Linux, bivanye na distribution ukoresha, ibikoresho nka `unattended-upgrades` (Debian/Ubuntu) canke `dnf-automatic` (Fedora) bigufasha gutegura igihe co gushira kugihe.



Ubwa nyuma, nuzirikane yuko kenshi, ibintu bimwe bimwe bihambaye bishirwa kugihe aruko usubiye gutanguza sisiteme. Ni ngombwa rero ko uza uratanguza imachine yawe ubudasiba, cane cane inyuma y'ugushira sisiteme kugihe. Gushira kugihe sisiteme yawe kenshi bifata iminota mikeyi gusa, ariko ni kimwe mu bintu bifasha cane gukingira ibitero vyinshi.



#### None OS yanje noyishira kugihe gute?



Naho nyene sisiteme yawe ishobora kwishira kugihe, birahambaye ko usuzuma n'amaboko, mu bihe bitandukanye, ko ata makuru ategereje gushirwa kugihe. Reka turabe ingene ivyo wobikora, bivanye na sisiteme yawe:





- Sisiteme ya *Windows*



Windows ifise porogarama ituganya ivyo gushira kugihe yitwa "Windows Update". Ivoma amakuru mashasha ikaca iyashiramwo, patches z'umutekano, drivers z'ibikoresho, rimwe na rimwe mbere nza microcode za processor.



Kugira ngo ugenzure n'amaboko ko sisiteme yayizwe kugihe :



```txt
Settings → Windows Update → Check for updates
```



Ntiwibagire kuraba ko hariho amakuru mashasha yandi muri iyo menu nyene.





- Sisiteme ya *Linux*



Distribution za Linux zishingiye kuri sisiteme y'amapaki abungabungwa n'abanyagihugu n'abacungera distribution ukoresha. Amakuru masha uyaronka biciye kubutunganyirizo bw'amapaki.



Kuri Debian (Ubuntu nk'akarorero) :



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade -y
```



![Image](assets/fr/213.webp)



Nimba ushaka gukoresha interface y'ibicapo, kuri Ubuntu hariho igikoresho ca *Software Updater* kigufasha gushira kugihe mu buryo bworoshe udaciye muri terminal.



![Image](assets/fr/214.webp)



Kuri Red Hat (Fedora) :



```bash
sudo dnf upgrade
```



Kuri Arch Linux :



```bash
sudo pacman -Syu
```






- Sisiteme ya *MacOS*



Apple ishira hamwe ibijanye no gushira kugihe muri interface y'imiterere. Kugira usuzume ko hariho amakuru mashasha:



```txt
Apple menu → System Settings → General → Software Update
```



macOS ihita ivoma bishasha vy'umutekano, vya sisiteme na porogarame biciye ku nzira ya "*Automatic Updates*" iri muri iyo menu nyene.



![Image](assets/fr/212.webp)



### Gushira kugihe porogarame



Umutekano w'inyabwonko yawe ntuvana gusa na sisiteme ukoresha. Porogarame yose ushiramwo ishobora kuba inzira yo kwinjirirwa nibitero. porogarame ikimara kuba ifise utugorane tw'umutekano tutakosowe, irashobora gukoreshwa kugira ngo ihungabanye sisiteme yawe canke yibe amakuru yawe.



Hariho porogarame zimwe zimwe zihambaye kuruta izindishobora, kuko zikorana n'isi yo hanze canke zigakoresha amadosiye yawe. Muri zo porogame zihambaye harimwo :





- *Mucukumbuzi*: ni zo zibanza guterwa, kuko zikorera ku makuru atagenzuwe mu gihe nyaco kandi zifise uburyo bwinshi zishobora gutegwamo. Ikindi kandi, zifise uruhara runini mu kurinda amakuru yawe bwite. Kandi, ikiruta vyose, zishaka gusubirira porogarame nyinshi zahora zikoreshwa bidasavye interineti (e-mail clients, office suites, media players...). Ariko tuzogaruka kuri iyo ngingo mu gice gikurikira c'iy'inyigisho ya SCU202;





- *Mail clients*: zironka ivyobifatanijwe na imeyiri (attachement) canke amahuza (links) ava hanze adashobora kugenzurwa rero akaba yoteza akaga gakomeye;





- Ibikoresho vyo guhanahana amakuru (TeamViewer, Zoom, Signal, Teams...): kubera uburyo bikoramo, ni vyo vyibasigwa n'ibitero vy'ubutasi canke muku gerageza kubikoreshereza kure(remote control). mu buryo bumwe n'ubwa e-mail clients, ibikoresho vyo guhanahana amakuru birashobora kuba imvo y'ububeshi buciye mu dutego (phishing) canke bigakoreshwa mugukwiragiza attachements mbi;





- Antivirus, firewall n'ibindi bikoresho vyo gushira ahagaragara ingorane: ivyo bikoresho muri rusangi birafise uburenganzira bwo hejuru, kuko biguma bipima amadosiye yawe, ibikorwa n'imigenderanire ya we kumuhora. Signature base itari kugihe, ugutunganya nabi imiterere canke intege nke za porogarame ubwayo birashobora gutuma porogarame mbi zitamenyekana, canke mbere zikaronka uburenganzira bwo hejuru.



Ego kandi, izo ngorane ntiziva gusa ku bijanye no kutabungabunga, mugabo birahambaye ko umuntu yitwararika cane cane gushira kugihe izo porogarame zihambaye cane. Ndiko ngerageza kworosha hano, ariko rero nyene, n'izindi porogarame zawe zose na zo nyene zikeneye gushirwa kugihe ubudasiba. Reka turabe ingene wobikora navyo, bivanye na sisiteme ukoresha.



#### Kuri Windows



Kuri Windows 11, igikoresho ca *Winget* gisanzwe kiri muri sisiteme. kiragufasha kuronka urutonde no gushira kugihe porogarame nyinshi ziri ku nyabwonko yawe, uciye muri terminal. Tanguza Windows PowerShell:



```CMD
winget upgrade --all
```



Iri bwirizwa rironderera mububiko bwa rusangi ku bijanye n'ama verisiyo mashasha ya porogarame ufise, maze rikazishira kugihe utabigizemwo uruhara.



![Image](assets/fr/211.webp)



Ikibabaje, iri bwirizwa ntirikora kuri porogarame zose. Ni co gituma ndagusaba ko wobika urutonde rw'ama porogarame yawe yose kandi ukagenzura n'amaboko ko woyashira kugihe ibi ukabigira umusi ku musi, cane cane porogarme z'amabanga akomeye. Ku bijanye na porogarame zihambaye cane, nka antivirus, canke mucukumbuzi, ndaguhanura ko woza urasuzuma umusi ku musi.



#### Kuri Linux (Debiani/Ubuntu)



Inkomezi za distribution ya Linux ziri mu butunganirizo bwa porogarama zayo zihuriwe hamwe. ubutunganyirizo bw'amapaki (`APT` mu gihe ari Debian) bushira kugihe sisiteme na porogarame zose biciye mu bubiko bwemewe buzwi.



Mu buryo bumwe no gushira OS kugihe, kugira ngo ushire porogarame zawe kugihe, andika gusa:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade
```



Iri bwirizwa ry'ishimikiro rishira kugihe urutonde rw'amapaki ahari (`apt update`) hanyuma rikemeza ivyashizwe kugihe (`apt upgrade`).



Kugira ngo ubone ushire kugihe mu buryo bwuzuye, ushobora gukoresha iri bwirizwa:



```bash
sudo apt update \
&& sudo apt full-upgrade -y \
&& sudo apt autoremove -y \
&& sudo apt autoclean
```





- `sudo apt full-upgrade` ishira kugihe amapaki yose yashizweho, harimwo n'ibindi bishingi kuri yo bikenewe kongerwako canke gukurwako. `-y` iguha uburenganzira bwo kwishura "ego" ku kwemeza kwose ubutunganizo bw'amapaki bwoshobora kugusaba;
- `sudo apt autoremove -y`: gukuraho ibidakenewe ;
- `sudo apt autoclean`: isukura ububiko bw'amapaki yataye igihe/ya kera.



![Image](assets/fr/215.webp)



Nimba ufise porogarame washizemwo ukoresheje amapaki ya Flatpak canke Snap, zimwe zishira kugihe zonyene, ariko ushobora kuzishira kugihe zose icarimwe n'amaboko ukoresheje ibwirizwa:



```bash
flatpak update sudo snap refresh
```



#### Kuri macOS



porogarame zishizwemwo biciye kuri App Store zishobora gushirwa kugihe bitagoranye muri menu ikurikira:



```txt
Apple menu → App Store → Update All
```



Ushobora kandi gukoresha ubuhinga bwokwishira kugihe mu miterere ya App Store.



Ariko rero, si porogarame zose zishirwa muri Mac yawe ziva muri App Store. Ku zindi porogarame, uzobwirizwa kuvyikorera n'amaboko. Rero, nk'uko bigenda ku bakoresha Windows, ndagusaba ko wobika urutonde rwa porogarame yawe yose kandi ukaguma usuzuma ko hariho verisiyo nshasha, cane cane izo zihambaye nka mucukumbuzi yawe.



### Gukuramwo porogarame



Uvuye ku bijanye n'umutekano w'ikoranbuhanga ry'amakuru, uko ushiramwo porogarame nke, ni ko n'aho n'amahirwe yo guterwa aba make. porogarame yose ishizwe kuri sisiteme yawe yoshobora kuba irimwo utubazo tw'umutekano, naho woba utazokwigera uyikoresha. Ivyo bizwi kw'izina rya attack surface: uko attack surface iba nini ni ko n'ingorane zirushiriza kuba nyinshi. Kugabanya iyo attack surface kuramwo porogarame zidakenewe ni uburyo bworoshe ariko bukora neza bwo kwirinda.



Porogarame zimwe zimwe zizanana na sisiteme canke izo wishiriyemwo zikoreshwa rimwe gusa, zirashobora kuguma ku nyabwonko yawe amezi menshi zidakoreshwa, kandi ziguma zishirwa kugihe canke zikorana na sisiteme yawe. Ikibi kuruta, ni mu gihe  izo porogarame zitagikurikiranwa, zishobora kuba zifise intege nke zo tuma uhura n'ingorane.



#### Kuri Windows



Kugira ngo ubone urutonde rwa porogarame zirimwo:



```txt
Settings → Apps → Installed apps
```



Suzuma uru rutonde rwa porogarame ukuremwo ikintu cose utagikoresha, canke utazi ico gikoreshwa (inyuma yo gusuzuma vyihuse kuri interineti mu gihe bikenewe). Urabe maso ku bijanye na porogarame za sisiteme, ariko ntukekeranye gukuramwo inkino zizanana na sisiteme, ibikoresho vyo kubungabunga sisiteme biteye amakenga canke porogarame zo kwamamaza.



#### Kuri Linux (Debiyani/Ubuntu)



Fungura terminal maze ukoreshe iri bwirizwa kugira ngo ufute porogarame:



```bash
sudo apt remove izina_rya_porogarame
```


![Image](assets/fr/216.webp)



Hanyuma uc'ukoreshe iri tegeko kugira ngo ukureho ubwawe ibintu vyose bitagikenewe:



```bash
sudo apt autoremove
```



#### Kuri macOS



Kuri macOS, hari uburyo 2 nyamukuru: biciye kuri *Launchpad* canke biciye kuri *Finder*. Nimba iyo porogarame yaravuye muri App Store, ugurura *Launchpad* (uciye kuri Dock canke mu bubiko bwa `/Applications`), urondere iyo porogarame, hanyuma ufyonde buto ya Option ugumizeko canke ukore igikorwa co gufyonda igihe kirekire gushika agacapo ka porogarame gatanguye kujugumira. Hanyuma ufyonde kukamenyetso ko kugwiza kari iruhande yiyo porogarame, maze wemeze ko ifuswe.



![Image](assets/fr/210.webp)



Iyo buto yo gufuta itabonetse, iyo porogarame izoba itaravuye kuri App Store. Ico gihe, ucukoresha *Finder*. Ubanza kwugara porogarame, nimba iriko irakora. Ugurure *Finder*, uje mu bubiko bwa `/Applications`, uhitemwo porogarame wipfuza gukuramwo, hanyuma uyishire mu gitereko c'ubucafu. Ubwa nyuma, n'ufute ibiri mu gitereko c'ubucafu vyose gugira ube uhejeje kuyikuramwo.



#### Ntiwibagira inyongera bushobozi za mucukumbuzi (browser extensions)



Inyongera bushobozi be n'ivyongegwako kuri mucukumbuzi yawe akenshi birirengagizwa, ariko na vyo nyene vyoba imvo y'ibitero. extension mbi canke yataye igihe, ishobora kwitambika amakuru yawe mu gihe uriko urarondera ikarungika amakode canke ikagutata mu buryo bwibanga.



Genda mu miterere ya mucukumbuzi yawe maze uhagarike canke ufute extensions zose udakoresha canke utazi. Gumizayo gusa izo zikenewe, ziva ahantu wizeye kandi zikibungabungwa.



### Gukurikirana no kugenzura sisiteme



Umutekano wo kuri interineti kandi urimwo no kugenzura ibikorwa vya sisiteme. Ubwo buryo buratuma umuntu ashobora kubona inyifato idasanzwe (inzira ziteye ama kenga, ibikorwa bidasanzwe, ukugerageza kwinjira mu buryo butemewe, n'ibindi) hakiri kare no kugira ico akoze imbere y'uko hagira ikiba.



Iyo ushizeho umurongo ngenderwako w'igenzura (naho biba ari ibintu bisanzwe) urashobora kumenya ko hariho porogarame mbi, ama Trojans asinziriye canke porogarame z'ubutasi hakiri kare. Mwene ukwo kugenzura gushobora gukorwa hakoreshejwe ibikoresho vyihariye.



#### Kuri Windows



Nk'uko twabibonye mu gisata ca mbere, Windows mu mateka yashikiriwe cane n'ibitero vy'inyabwonko, kubera ukuntu ikoreshwa cane muvy'ubuhinga no mubindi vyihariye. Ni ngombwa rero ko inyuma yo kwikingira bisanzwe wongerako ibikoresho vy'ugupima biteye imbere:





- *Microsoft Defender*: kuri Windows, kugira porogarame ikingira umugera nyabwonko nziza ni ikintu gikenewe cane. Mu myaka myinshi, Microsoft Defender (yahora yitwa Windows Defender), antivirus y'ubakiye muri sisiteme, yabonwa ko idashobora kwizigirwa, kandi vyabonwa ko hokoreshwa izindi antivirus mu kibanza cayo. Ariko iyo porogarame yarateye imbere cane uko igihe cagenda kirarenga, kandi ubu, mu vyiyumviro vyanje, irahagije kugira ngo itange uburinzi bw'ishimikiro kumikorere y'umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ivyo biravuzwe, ntidukwiye guha agaciro cane uruhara rwa porogarame zikingira umugera: ni hejuru y'imigenzo yawe bwite y'ubuhinga bwa none ari yo ituma ugira umutekano. Kimwe mu vyiza vya Defender ni uko ikorana na Windows mu buryo bw'umwimerere. Uretse uburinzi mu gihe nyaco, itanga uburyo bwiza bwo kurondera ibibazo vya sisiteme mu gihe ushaka kuza urabikora kundwi kundwi canke wewe uvyikoreye muhihe bihoraho



![Image](assets/fr/007.webp)





- *Sysinternals Suite*: uyu ni umugwi w'ibikoresho biteye imbere bitangwa na Microsoft vyo gupima, gukurikirana no gutorera umuti ingorane za Windows. Ehe ibikoresho nyamukuru biri muri iyi suite:
- **Process Monitor**: ishobora kugufasha kwihweza ibikorwa biriko birakora, uburenganzira bwo kwinjira muri dosiye, ama registers, n'ibindi mu gihe nyaco;
- **Autoruns**: yerekana porogarame zose zatangujwe mu gihe co gutangura sisiteme, igufasha kumenya ningoga porogarame mbi ziguma zikora canke porogarame zidakwiye kuba ziriko zirakora;
- **Process Explorer**: ikurikirana ibiriko birakogwa kandi ikamenya inyifato iteye amakenga;
- **TCPView**: igaragaza inzira z'umuhora zikora (kumenya inzira zidasanzwe) ;
- **Sigcheck**: isuzuma imikono y'ubuhinga bwa none (digital signatures) ku madosiye kugira ngo ibone kode mbi.



![Image](assets/fr/207.webp)





- *GlassWire*: igikoresho co gukurikirana umuhora. Ikurikirana inzira zinjira n'izisohoka mu gihe nyaco, kandi ikakumenyesha igihe hari ibikorwa bidasanzwe.



![Image](assets/fr/208.webp)



#### Kuri Linux



Ku mashini ya Linux ibungabungwa neza ikoreshwa ku bintu vy'umuntu ku giti ciwe, ingorane ziba nke. Nyamaze, ng'ibi ibikoresho bimwe bimwe vyisumbuye bigufasha gukurikirana sisiteme yawe :





- *Fail2ban*: ikurikiran'inyandiko za sisiteme(system logs) ku kugerageza kwinjira kutakunze (nk'ukugerageza kwinjira muri SSH kungu). Iyo inyifato iteye amakenga ibonetse, irabuza vy'igihe gito aderese IP biturutse ko yifashishije `iptables`;



![Image](assets/fr/217.webp)





- *Lynis*: igikoresho co kugenzura umutekano gisesengura sisiteme yawe kugira ngo ubone imiterere itameze neza, ko hariho integenke zizwi canke ko hariho ukunyuranya n'imigenzo myiza. Itanga icegeranyo coroshe gusoma, gitanga kandi amanota y'umutekano n'impanuro.



![Image](assets/fr/218.webp)


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/lynis-1cf865b3-a352-4dd2-94d2-f17fa65547af

#### Kuri macOS



macOS izwi cane kubera umutekano wayo, cane cane kubera amategeko ajanye n'umukono wa porogarame n'imyubakire yugaranye yayo. Ku bijanye n'ukuyikoresha bisanzwe kugiti cawe, inyabwonko isanzwe iri kugihe n'imiterere yayo kandi itanga umutekano ukwiriye. Kugira ngo utere intambwe yindi mu gukurikirana sisiteme yawe, ndagusaba kuraba :





- **KnockKnock**: isuzuma burikimwe cose gitegerezwa gukora mu gihe sisiteme itangura (agents, daemons, modules za kernel...) maze ikamenya izo zishobora kuba ziteye amakenga, zitashizweko umukono canke zitazwi. Bigufasha kumenya ningoga ibishobora konona sisiteme yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/209.webp)



### Gusozera: gutekanirwa nivya misi yose



Umutekano ukwiye w'inyabwonko ntushobora kuwushikako mu gushiramwo ibikoresho vyihariye rimwe, ahubwo uwushikako mu gucungera ubudasiba, mu buryo bukomeye kandi mu buryo bubereye. Kuguma ushira sisiteme yawe kugihe, kwongerereza ububasha porogarame zihambaye, gukuraho porogarame zidakenewe no gukurikirana neza sisiteme nibwo buryo bufadika bwo kuyibubungabunga neza. Muri rusangi, iyi migenzo myiza uzokwama uyigira kubikoresho vyawe vyose vy'ubuhinga bwa none: ibintu bihuye, ama seriveri, amaterefone ngendanwa...



Mu gice gikurikira, turaza kuraba mubikorwa ingene wokwirinda gushiramwo porogarame mbi, mu kwiga ingene wosuzuma ubutungane n'ukuri kw'amadosiye uvoma kuri aja kunyabwonko yawe.




## Ubutungane n'ukuri vya porogarame


<chapterId>ffa06aeb-0b90-4271-a385-9a752c1bb5ed</chapterId>



Gushiramwo porogarame ku nyabwonko yawe vyoshobora gusa n'ikintu gisanzwe, mugabo mu vy'ukuri bishobora gutuma inyabwonko yawe igira ingorane zikomeye cane. Vy'ukuri, porogarame zishobora guhindurwa canke zikanduzwa umugera n'abatera, bagakoresha ako karyo kugira ngo bashiremwo umugera, ama Trojans n'ubundi bwoko bwa porogame mbi muri sisiteme yawe.



Gusuzuma ubutungane n'ukuri kw'ama porogarame imbere y'uko ashirwamwo rero ni umugenzo uhambaye cane wo kubungabunga umutekano, cane cane iyo bishitse ku maporogarame y'agaciro gakomeye  nk'ingodo ya Bitcoin canke ubutunganyirizo bw'amajambo y'ibanga. Ivyo bituma porogarame zikuwe kuri interineti ubona neza na neza ko zihuye n'izo zasohowe n'uwazikoze, ata co zihinduweko.



Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba ingene wosuzuma ubutungane n'ukuri kw'idosiye, n'ingene woyikora kuri sisiteme yawe.



### Ni kubera iki wosuzuma ubutungane n'ukuri kwa porogarame?



Iyo ukuye porogarame kuri interineti, uba wizigiye udakekeranya ko izagukora ku mashini yawe. Ariko ukwo kwizigira ntukwiye kubigira nk'impumyi. Ni ngombwa rero gutahura ivyiyumviro bibiri vy'ishimikiro: ubutungane n'ukuri vya dosiye.



#### Ubutungane: kumenya neza ko ata mpinduka zabaye



Ubutungane bwa dosiye buratanga icemezo c'uko itahinduwe, n'ibigirankana canke bitagambiriwe, hagati y'igihe yasohowe n'uwayikoze n'igihe wayikuye kuri interineti. N'uguhindura gatoyi gusa birashobora kuba bihagije kugira ngo umuntu yinjize kode mbi muri porogarame.



Ivyo bihinduka ntibiboneka n'ijisho ry'umuntu: dosiye yavomwe kuri interineti ishobora gufunguka kandi igakora neza, mu gihe nyene ikora akaba ari nako yonona. Ni co gituma bihambaye kugenzura ubutungane bwayo hakoreshejwe ubuhinga bwa cryptographic fingerprints (Hash).



#### : Ukuri kw'ibintu (Authenticity): gutanga icemezo c'uko porogarame ifise inkomoko yanyayo



Dosiye ishobora kuba ataco ibaye (itahinduwe), ariko ikaba yasohowe n'ikigo kitarico kinyaga akaranga k'uwayiteguye yemewe. Authenticity rero igamije kwemeza ko iyo dosiye vy'ukuri ikomoka ku ahantu h'ukuri hemewe, atari ku munyaruyeri, ku rubuga rw'indorerwamo rutagenzuwe, canke ku winjiriye seriveri ijejwe gukwiragiza akayihungabanya



Ukwo kugenzura inkomoko bishoboka biciye ku mukono w'ubuhinga bwa none, uburyo bwo kunyegeza amakuru buhuza dosiye n'urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa nyeneyo. Iyo usuzumye uwo mukono ukoresheje urufunguzo rwa rusangi rwa nyeneyo (rukwiragizwa biciye ku nzira zitekanye), urashobora kwemera udakekeranya ko iyo dosiye mu vy'ukuri ikomoka kuri uwo muntu.



Mu kugenzura ukuri (ni ukuvuga ko dosiye yo gushiramwo iva kw'isoko yizewe) n'ubutungane (ni ukuvuga ko itahinduwe kuva yasohorwa na nyeneyo), urashobora kumenya neza ko uriko urashiramwo porogarame ya nyayo.



#### Inyishu z'ubuhinga: Hash n'umukono w'ubuhinga bwa none



Kugira ivyo tubishikeko, tuzokoresha ibikoresho 2 vya cryptography(ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru). Ica mbere ni hashing. Hash ni iryugane rigizwe n'indome ntoyi riboneka hakoresheje uburyo buzwi kandi ataho rihuriye nibiri muri dosiye, hakoreshejwe ubuhinga bwa Hash nka SHA-256. Dosiye zibiri zisa zizogira Hash imwe, ariko guhindura gatoyi gusa ikintu muri dosiye bizotuma Hash ihinduka burundu.



Uwukora iyo porogarame yemewe akenshi atangaza Hash ya dosiye y'umwimerere ku rubuga rwiwe rwemewe. Ku ruhande rwawe, uzoharura Hash ya dosiye wavomye, kugira ngo ugereranye ivyo bibiri. Iyo ivyo bimenyetso bibiri vy'intoke bihuye, urashobora kwemera udakekeranya ko iyo dosiye wavomye kuri interineti ari iyukuri kandi ko ata co yahinduweko.



Igikoresho ca kabiri ni umukono w'ubuhinga bwa none. Ivyo bigenzura ko porogarame yo gushiramwo ari iyukuri. Uwukora iyo porogarame ashira umukono kuri dosiye irimwo Hash n'urufunguzo rwiwe rw'ibanga, kandi urashobora kugenzura uwo mukono ukoresheje urufunguzo rwa rusangi rujanye. Ivyo vyerekana ko iyo dosiye yasohowe n'umuntu wanyawe.



Iyi sisiteme ishingiye ku buhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru budahuye (asymmetric cryptography) n'ibikoresho nka GnuPG (umurongo w'amabwirizwa) canke Kleopatra (interface y'ibicapo ya Windows). Ivyo bikoresho bitegerezwa kuba vyatunganijwe neza, kandi urufunguzo rwa rusangi rw'umuhinguzi rutegerezwa gusuzumwa biciye ku nzira itekanye (urubuga rwemewe, fingerprint kuri Twitter...). Reka turabe ibishobora gukorwa.



Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi ku bikorwa vya cryptographic hash be n'imikono y'ubuhinga bwa none, ndagutumiye ngo ufate inyigisho ya CYP 201 ku buntu itangwa kuri Plan ₿ Academy:


https://planb.academy/courses/46b0ced2-9028-4a61-8fbc-3b005ee8d70f

### Genzura ubutungane bwa porogarame n'ukuri



#### Ibisabwa



Nimba ukoresha Linux, GPG isanzwe irimwo mu ma distribution menshi. Nimba atayirimwo, ushobora kuyishiramwo ukoresheje iri bwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
sudo apt install gnupg
```



![Image](assets/fr/232.webp)



Kuri macOS, nimba utarashiramwo ubutunganyirizo bw'amapaki ya Homebrew, ubikore ukoresheje aya mabwirizwa akurikira:
