```bash
/bin/bash -c "$(curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Homebrew/install/HEAD/install.sh)"

echo 'eval "$(/opt/homebrew/bin/brew shellenv)"' >> ~/.zprofile

eval "$(/opt/homebrew/bin/brew shellenv)"
```



Hanyuma ushiremwo GPG n'iri bwirizwa:



```bash
brew install gnupg
```



Ku bijanye na Windows, iyo udafise GPG, urashobora gushiramwo [Gpg4win](https://www.gpg4win.org/).



![Image](assets/fr/219.webp)



#### Kuvoma inyandiko



Kugira ngo utangure, uzokenera inyandiko nyinshi zijanye na porogarame wipfuza gushiramwo. Muri aka karorero, tuzoba turiko turasuzuma *Sparrow wallet*, ubutunganyirizo bw'ibikorwa vya Bitcoin. Ivyo biguma aruko bikorwa no kuyandi ma porogarame yose: ico ukeneye gukora n'ukurondera amadosiye yanyayo yo kugenzura.



Genderera urubuga rwemewe rwa [Sparrow wallet mu gice ca "_Download_"](https://sparrowwallet.com/download/). Nimba wifuza kuraba iyindi porogarame, genda ku rubuga rw'iyo porogarame.



![Image](assets/fr/220.webp)



Ushobora kandi kuja [ku bubiko bwa GitHub bw'umugambi](https://github.com/sparrowwallet/Sparrow/releases).



![Image](assets/fr/221.webp)



Kuvoma porogarame igufasha gushiramwo ihuye na sisiteme yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/222.webp)



Uzokenera kandi Hash ya dosiye, akenshi yitwa "_SHA256SUMS_" canke "_MANIFEST_".



![Image](assets/fr/223.webp)



Kandi n'uvome umukono wa PGP wa dosiye. Iyi ni inyandiko ya `.asc`.



![Image](assets/fr/224.webp)



Raba neza ko izo dosiye zose uzishira mu bubiko bumwe kugira ngo ushobore gukora neza intambwe zikurikira.



Ubwa nyuma, uzokenera urufunguzo rwa rusangi rw'umuhinguzi kugira ngo ugenzure umukono wa PGP. Urufunguzo muri rusangi ruboneka ku rubuga rwemewe rwa porogarame, ku bubiko bwa GitHub bw'umugambi, rimwe na rimwe ku mbuga z'umuhinguzi, canke ku mbuga zidasanzwe nka Keybase.



Ku bijanye na *Sparrow wallet*, ushobora kubona urufunguzo rwa rusangi rw'umuhinguzi [Craig Raw kuri Keybase](https://keybase.io/craigraw). Kugira ngo uyivome ukoresheje terminal, koresha iribwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
curl https://keybase.io/craigraw/pgp_keys.asc | gpg --import
```



![Image](assets/fr/225.webp)



![Image](assets/fr/233.webp)



Kugira ngo umenye neza ko uriko ukoresha urufunguzo rwa rusangi nyarwo rw'umuhinguzi, atari urwakozwe umunyaruyeri, ndagusaba gusuzuma amasoko ruvako: usuzume ko fingerprint y'urufunguzo ihuye kuri Keybase, ku rubuga rwemewe rw'umugambi, no ku mbuga zose zo guhanahana amakuru canke imihora y'itumanako y'umuhinguzi.



#### Gusuzuma umukono



Uburyo bwo kugenzura umukono burasa haba kuri Windows, macOS canke Linux. Wabwirizwa kuba wamaze kuronka urufunguzo rwa rusangi mu ntambwe yambere duhejeje, ariko nimba utarabikora, ushobora kuruzana ukoresheje iri bwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
gpg --import [key_path]
```



Subiriza `[key_path]` n'aho dosiye y'urufunguzo rusangi y'umuhinguzi iri.



![Image](assets/fr/226.webp)



Suzuma umukono ukoresheje iri bwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
gpg --verify [dosiye.asc]
```



Subiriza `[dosiye.asc]` n'inzira yaho dosiye y'umukono iri. Ku bijanye na Sparrow, iyi dosiye yitwa "_sparrow-2.0.0-manifest.txt.asc_" ku verisiyo 2.0.0.



![Image](assets/fr/227.webp)



![Image](assets/fr/234.webp)



Nimba umukono ari uwanyawo, GPG izovyemeza mu buryo butomoye. Ushobora rero gutera intambwe ikurikira, kuko iri suzuma ryemeza ko iyo dosiye ari iy'ukuri.



![Image](assets/fr/228.webp)



![Image](assets/fr/235.webp)



#### Gusuzuma Hash



Ubu ko ukuri kwa dosiye irimwo ama hashes kwemejwe, ni igihe co kugenzura ubutungane bwa dosiye, bishingiye kuri iyi dosiye yemejwe. Intumbero ni ukugereranya Hash ya dosiye ufise n'iyo yerekanwa muri dosiye ya `.asc`. Iyo ivyo bibiri bihuye, ivyo biremeza ko kode ya porogarame itahinduwe mu buryo bumwe canke ubundi.



Kuri Windows, fungura terminal maze ukoreshe ibwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
CertUtil -hashfile [file_path] SHA256 | findstr /v "hash"
```



Subiriza `[file_path]` n'inzira ija kuri dosiye canke porogarame wa vomye.


![Image](assets/fr/229.webp)



Teriminal ikuzanira Hash iri kumwe na porogarame wa vomye kuri interineti.



![Image](assets/fr/230.webp)



Hanyuma ugereranye inyishu n'ibiri muri dosiye ya "_sparrow-2.0.0-manifest.txt_".



![Image](assets/fr/231.webp)



Ku ruhande rwanje, izo hatchings zirahuye neza cane.



kuri macOS na Linux, uburyo bwo kugenzura Hash usanga vy'ikora utabigizemwo uruhara, rero nta nkenerwa yo kugereranya n'amaboko izo fingerprints zibiri, nk'uko bishobora kuba mu gihe ca Windows.



Gusa gukoresha iri bwirizwa kuri macOS:



```bash
shasum --check [file_name] --ignore-missing
```



Subiriza `[file_name]` n'izina ija kuri dosiye yemejwe irimwo ama hashes. Nk'akarorero, kuri Sparrow wallet verisiyo 2.0.0:



```bash
shasum --check sparrow-2.0.0-manifest.txt --ignore-missing
```



Nimba hashes zihuye, inyishu ikwiye kuba:



```bash
Sparrow-2.0.0.dmg: OK
```



kuri Linux, ibwirizwa nico kimwe n'iryo:



```bash
sha256sum --check [file_name] --ignore-missing
```



Kandi iyo hashes zihuye, ushobora kuronka:



```bash
sparrow_2.0.0-1_amd64.deb: OK
```



![Image](assets/fr/236.webp)



Ubu urashobora kwizigira ko porogarame waronse ari iyukuri kandi ko ari iyo kwizigirwa. Ubu urashobora kuyishira mu mashini yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/237.webp)



Gusuzuma ubutungane n'ukuri ni umugenzo urasa ku ntego cane, mugabo uratanga uburinzi nyabwo kandi bubereye ku bibazo vyinshi cane bijanye no kuvoma kuri interineti no gushiramwo porogarame.



Mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza ingene amakuru atunganywa. Turaza kuraba ingene wokwikingira ingorane zibiri zikomeye: gutakaza amakuru n'ukwibwa amakuru.




## Kunyegeza (encryption) no gukingira amakuru


<chapterId>bcba9b26-72d2-446b-b23c-89927a2e857c</chapterId>



Gukingira amakuru yawe bwite ni igice gihambaye co guhagarara k'ubusegaba bwawe muvy'ubuhinga bwa none, ubuzima bw'ibanga n'umutekano. Ivyago ku makuru yawe ni vyinshi: kwiinjirirwa, gutakaza ibikoresho canke mbere no gufatirwa amakuru yawe. Mu gushira mu ngiro umukenyuro mwiza wo kurema ububiko bw'inyongera bw'amakuru yawe no kuyanyegeza, urashobora kwirinda vyinshi muri ivyo bintu bishobora kugutera ingorane.



Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba mu buryo buziguye ingene woshobora kurema ubu biko bw'inyongera bw'amakuru yawe no ku ya nyegeza(encryption), hamwe no gusukura amakuru y'agaciro ari mu nyandiko zawe.



### Kurema ububiko bw'inyongera bw'amakuru yawe (backup)



#### Kubera iki ukora backup y'amakuru yawe?



Kugira backup y'amakuru yawe bwite canke y'akazi ni ingingo ihambaye y'umutekano, bikunze kw'irengangizwa kugeza igihe bikugizeko ingaruka. mu buryo butandukanye n'ivyo abantu benshi bemera, kugira backup y'amakuru si igikorwa co guhitamwo ushatse canke c'ishirahamwe gusa: kiraraba umuntu wese akoresha inyabwonko. Waba ufise ivyangombwa vy'akazi, amafoto y'umuryango, ivyangombwa vy'umuntu ku giti ciwe canke ibindi vyose bihambaye, ayo makuru arashobora kuzimangana bukwi na bukwi kubera imvo zitari nke:





- Kudakora neza kw'ibikoresho: HDDs na SSDs zifise ubuzima bw'igihe gito. Ata nteguza, birashobora kwononekara, bigatuma amakuru adashobora gushikwako.





- Igitero c'inyabwonko: hariho porogarame mbi, cane cane ransomware, zinyegeza amadosiye yawe kandi zigasaba incungu muri kugira uhabwe urufunguruzo rwokugarura amakuru yawe yanyegejwe. Ata backup yigenga, uri ku mbabazi zabo.





- Ikosa ry'umuntu: gukoresha nabi, isanganya ryongufuta canke gukuraho burundu bishobora gutuma umuntu atakaza ibintu bidashobora kugaruka.





- Isanganya: umuriro, amazi, ubusuma canke mbere n'umuyagankuba bishobora gutuma ibikoresho vyawe bidashobora gukoreshwa mu kanya nk'ako gukubita urugohe.



Ni co gituma ukeneye umukenyuro, wizwe neza kandi ukomeye wo gukora backup.



#### Uburyo bwa 3-2-1: urugero rukomeye rw'umutekano



Uburyo bwa "3-2-1" ni urugero rwemewe mu mutekano w'ikoranabuhanga ry'amakuru. Bushingiye kuma hame yoroshe ariko akora cane atuma habaho kwihanganira amakosa n'impanuka zishobora gushika. Nguku uko bikora:





- Kopi 3 z'amakuru yawe: aha nukuvuga amadosiye y'umwimerere (amadosiye ari ku nyabwonko yawe) n'izindi kopi zibiri z'inyongera za backup.





- Ububiko 2 butandukanye: intumbero ni ukwirinda ingorane y'ibikoresho ishobora gutera ububiko bwawe bwose icarimwe. Nk'akarorero, hard disk yindi + cloud; canke NAS + inyabwonko yawe.





- Kopi ya 1 off-site: iyo kopi itegerezwa kuba iri kure y'aho uba nyamukuru (mu nzu y'incuti yawe, kuri seriveri iri kure, muri cloud irinzwe...). Bikurinda ibintu nk'umuriro canke ubusuma.



Reka dufate akarorero nk'uwukoresha yiwe, Alice, ashaka gukingira amakuru yiwe bwite.



Alice abika verisiyo y'amadosiye yiwe kuri laptop yiwe, aho ayakoresha ku musi ku musi. Kugira ngo agire n'imiburiburi aho abika amakuru habiri hatandukanye, arakunda (nk'akarorero, buri wa mbere) gukopiya amakuru yiwe yose akayashira ku kuri USB, abika muhira. Kugira ngo Alice yikingire ubusuma bw'amadosiye yiwe mu gihe yoba atakaje igikoresho ciwe canke yibwe, ashiramwo ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru kuri USB akoresheje porogarame zabigenewe (tuzobona ingene twobikora mu nyuma muri iki gice).



Hamwe niyo ntunganyo, Alice aba arinzwe ibitero bimwe na bimwe. Ariko rero, hariho ingorane imwe: mu gihe hateye umuriro canke ubusuma mu nzu yiwe, amakopi yiwe abiri (inyabwonko na USB) yoshobora kuzimangana icarimwe. Kugira ngo yirindi ako kaga, afata ingingo yo gukoresha serivice yo kubika amadosiye mu gicu(cloud storage services), kandi akibuka kuza arasanisha amakuru ye nayari kugicu umusi ku musi.



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/proton-drive-03cbe49f-6ddc-491f-8786-bc20d98ebb16

Alice rero yubaha itegeko rya 3-2-1: nukuvuga afise kopi 3 z'amadosiye yiwe (inyabwonko, urufunguzo rwa USB, cloud), ibitswe n'imiburiburi ku bikoresho 2 bitandukanye (disk y'indani munyabwonko, urufunguzo rwa USB, seriveri ya kure), ifise n'imiburiburi kopi 1 iri hanze y'aho akorere mucongereza bakunze kwita 1 off-site (server ya cloud).



Uwo mukenyuro utuma agira inkomezi cane: mu gihe inyabwonko yiwe ipfuye, arashobora kugarura amadosiye yiwe akoresheje USB canke cloud; mu gihe ububiko bwa cloud bugize ikibazo gikomeye, nubundi aguma afise amadosiye yiwe hafi; kandi mbere n'igihe habaye ubusuma akibwa laptop yiwe na USB, arashobora kugarura amakuru yiwe biciye kuri serivisi ya cloud.



![Image](assets/fr/255.webp)



#### Ukwikoresha nk'inzira yo kwirinda kwibagirwa



Uburyo bumwe bwiza bwo gushiraho isuku ryiza rya backup ni uburyo bw'ikoresha(automation). Gutunganya ibikoresho vyawe kugira ngo ama backups yikore ubwayo mukiringo kanaka wateguye (buri joro, buri ndwi...). Ivyo bikingira kwibagira kandi bigatuma ntakibuza ko vyokogwa no mugihe woba utarihafi.



Mu bishobora gukorwa, hari uburyo bwinshi bwo gukora ama backups yawe bidasavye ko uvyikorera n'amaboko. Ushobora, nk'akarorero, gukora inyandiko yanditswe mu rurimi rwa Python yikoresha ubwayo kugira ngo iko re kopi y'amakuru yawe ku kindi gikoresho. Ni umuti woroshe, ushobora kwikorera.



Nimba ufise NAS, ibikoresho nka *Syncthing* canke *Rclone* bigufasha gukora backups mu muhora wawe utabigizemwo uruhara, udakoresheje interineti.



![Image](assets/fr/253.webp)



Kugira ngo ukoreshe ubwo buryo bwa backups zikora kuri serivisi ya cloud, urashobora gukoresha porogarame itangwa nabanyene iyo serivisi. akarorero ni *Proton Drive*, itanga porogarame ihuhuza amadosiye yawe nayari mu gicu (cloud). Ushobora kandi guhitamwo porogarame zishobora ziguha ubushobozi burenze nka *Duplicati*, igufasha gutegura umwanya wokugira backups zinyegejwe kuri serivices ziri kuri interinet (Dropbox, Google Drive, Proton Drive, FTP, WebDAV...).



![Image](assets/fr/254.webp)



Ibuka kandi kugerageza ama backups yawe ubudasiba, ni ukuvuga ko ushobora kuyagarura. Backup ntaco imaze iyo yononekaye, idatunganye canke idashobora gusomwa.



Uretse no kuba amakuru yawe afise ubukomezi, birahambaye cane ko ukingira inzira yo kuyashikira. Mu vyukuri, inkomezi n'umutekano akenshi birajana: uko ukora kopi nyinshi z'amadosiye yawe, ni ko urushiriza kwongera attack surface yazo, bigatuma uja mukaga kuko woterwa. Ni co gituma kunyegeza amakuru yawe ari intambwe ihambaye. Reka turabe ingene twobishira mu ngiro.



### kunyegeza bikwiye amakuru ari kuri disks zo hanze no kubindi bikoresho vy'ububiko



Imwe mu nkingi z'umutekano w'inyabwonko y'umuntu ku giti ciwe ni ukunyegeza amakuru yabitswe. Cane cane, kunyegeza bikwiye amakuru ari kubikoresho vy'ububiko nka hard drive y'indani munyabwonko, za USB canke amadisk yo hanze bituma, mbere n'igihe habaye ubusuma, kubura canke uguhungabana kw'ibikoresho, ata makuru ashobora gusomwa ata rufunguzo rwo kwugurura.



#### Ni kubera iki ari ngirakamaro?



Iyo igikoresho cy'ububiko kita nyegeza amakuru, ushobora gusa kugishira mu nyabwonko iyariyo yose kugira ngo ushobore guca ubona ibirimwo. Nta nzitizi zihari zo kurinda amadosiye. Ivyo bisigura ko iyo laptop yawe yibwe, canke iyo utakaje urufunguzo rwa USB, umuntu afise umugambi mubi yoshobora gushika ku nyandiko zawe bwite.



Uretse ibibazo vy'ubuzima bw'ibanga buzoba bugiye mu kaga, amadosiye yawe arashobora kandi kugukwegera ingorane nyayo y'umutekano. Reka dufate akarorero nyako: nimba ama backups yawe arimwo kopi y'inyandiko zawe z'akaranga, uwugutera yoshobora kuyakoresha kugira ngo akwiyitirire, akugurura amakonti ya banki canke amakonti ya crypto mw'izina ryawe, canke mbere agasaba inguzanyo muri banki mw'izina ryawe. Ubwo bwoko bw'ukuja ahagaragara kw'amakuru burashobora kugira ingaruka zikomeye, ku muntu ku giti ciwe no mu kazi.



Kunyegeza amakuru mu buryo bukwiye ni nk'ukwugara n'igufuri: igihe cose ijambo ry'ibanga ritatanzwe, amakuru aguma atakimazi. N'uwoza kugutera afise ibikoresho vyihariye vyo kugaruza amakuru yazimiye ntaco azoshobora gukuramwo ata rufunguzo afise.



#### Ni inyishu izihe z'ubuhinga sisiteme yawe itanga?





- *Linx (Debiyani)*



muri Linux, umuti umuti uhari ni LUKS (*Linux Unified Key Setup*). LUKS ni sisiteme yo gutunganya ibibanza biriko amakuru anyegejwe izanana na distribution nyinshi za linux. Igihe uriko ushiramwo sisiteme, muri rusangi uzosabwa kwemeza ko amakuru yose ari kuri disk y'inyabwonko yawe anyegezwa. Ego cane, ndagusaba cane kwemera. Igihe wemeje encryption, sisiteme izokwama igusaba ijambo ry'ibanga igihe cose wuguruye inyabwonko, mbere n'imbere y'uko OS itangnura. Ivyo bituma naho uba washikiriye iyo disk udashobora kurenga ingingo z'umutekano zashizweko.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/luks-13d9928b-08b1-478c-a1b4-67617978584a

Nimba wipfuza kunyegeza amakuru ari kuri disk yo hanze canke kuri USB, ivyo bishobora gukorwa kandi ukoresheje umurongo w'amabwirizwa canke ukoresheje interface y'ibicapo. disk izobwirizwa gufutwa ibiriko vyose biveko, rero amakuru yose ariho azozimangana mugihe atabanje gushirwa ahandi.



**Biciye kuri terminal**



Raba neza ko ufise ipaki ya *cryptsetup*:



```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt install cryptsetup
```



Tangura uraba ko ubona USB yawe ukoresheje iri bwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
lsblk
```



Ushobora kubona igikoresho nka `/dev/sdb` gifise igice bikurikirana, nk'akarorero `/dev/sdb1`. Urabe maso uhitemwo disk y'ukuri, kuko itegerezwa gufutwa!



Kugira ngo wemeze uburyo bwokunyegeza amakuru kuri USB, koresha iri bwirizwa kugira ngo utanguze encryption:



```bash
sudo cryptsetup luksFormat /dev/sdb
```



Andika "YES" mu ndome nini kugira ngo wemeze igikorwa, hanyuma uhitemwo kandi wemeze passphrase ikomeye. Iri jambo ry'ibanga rizotuma ushobora gushika ku makuru yawe: wibuke gukora ububiko bw'inyongera, kuko udafise iyo backup, gushika ku makuru urufunguzo rwugurura azo bura vy'iteka.


![Image](assets/fr/238.webp)



Kwugurura no gushikira ikibanza c'amakuru(volume):



```bash
sudo cryptsetup open /dev/sdb encrypted_usb
```



Uzokenera kwandika passphrase yawe kugira ngo wugurure volume. `encrypted_usb` ni izina rya volume y'uguruwe (decrypted volume).



![Image](assets/fr/239.webp)



Hanyuma uyihe ubwoko(format). Ubwoko bwa Linux kavukire/bw'umwimerere:



```bash
sudo mkfs.ext4 /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb
```



Canke, nimba ushaka guhuza na Windows:



```bash
sudo mkfs.vfat /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb
```



![Image](assets/fr/240.webp)



Gukora mount kugira urufunguzo rukoreshwe:



```bash
sudo mkdir -p /mnt/usb
sudo mount /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb /mnt/usb
```



Ubu ushobora gushika ku rufunguzo rwawe biciye mu bubiko bwa `/mnt/usb`, no gusoma no kwandika amadosiye nk'uko biri ku yandi ma volume.



Kugira ngo ushobore kuyikura muri sisiteme no gusubira kunyegeza ibiri ku rufunguzo:



```bash
sudo umount /mnt/usb
sudo cryptsetup close encrypted_usb
```



Ushobora rero gukuramwo urufunguzo rwawe rwa USB ata nkomanzi.



Kugira ngo ukoreshe muri kazoza USB yawe uzokora ibi:



```bash
sudo cryptsetup open /dev/sdb encrypted_usb
sudo mount /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb /mnt/usb
#### … you work on the usb …
sudo umount /mnt/usb
sudo cryptsetup close encrypted_usb
```


![Image](assets/fr/241.webp)



Nimba ushaka, ushobora kandi gukoresha uru rukurikirane rw'amabwiriza ukoresheje inyandiko za Python canke Bash.




**Biciye kuri GNOME Disks:**



Uwundi muti ni ugukoresha porogarame ya GNOME Disks biciye kuri interface yayo y'ibicapo, akenshi usanga vyoroshe kuruta gukoresha terminal. Mu bisanzwe, iki gikoresho gisanzwe kiri muri sisiteme ya Ubuntu. Nimba ataco ubona, urashobora kugishiramwo n'amaboko ukoresheje iri bwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt install -y gnome-disk-utility
```



Kugira ngo wugurure iyo porogarame, genda kuri menu ya application za Ubuntu maze urondere "*Disks*". Mu bisanzwe iboneka ku buryo busanzwe mu bubiko bwa "*Utilities*".



Mu gice c'ibubafu, nurondere urufunguzo rwawe rwa USB. Nimba hariho ikibanza gisanzwe kiriho, gihitemwo; nimba atari uko, rema ikindi gisha: fyonda ku buto "+" iri munsi y'urutonde rw'imigabane/ibibanza(partitions).



![Image](assets/fr/242.webp)



Hanyuma uhitemwo igice uzoshiramwo amakuru anyegejwe. Fyonda ku kimenyetso c'umuzingi, hanyuma uhitemwo "Format Partition...".



![Image](assets/fr/243.webp)



Ahari:




- "Volume name", shiramwo izina (nk'akarorero `usb`);
- Hitamwo uburyo bwa "Internal disk for use with Linux systems only (Ext4)";
- Emeza mu kazu "Password protected volume (LUKS)".



![Image](assets/fr/244.webp)



Andika kandi wemeze passphrase ikomeye.



![Image](assets/fr/245.webp)



Emeze kandi urindire ko igice gihindurwa neza (amakuru yose azokurwaho).



![Image](assets/fr/246.webp)



Iyo icogikorwa kirangiye, ico gice kigaragara kiriko agacapo gato k'igufuri. Hitamwo, hanyuma ufyonde ku gufuri kugira ngo uyugurure.



![Image](assets/fr/247.webp)



Andika ijambo ry'ibanga, hanyuma ufyonde kuri "Unlock".



![Image](assets/fr/248.webp)



Volume izoca yemezwa muri sisiteme kandi igaragare muri porogarame icungera amadosiye yawe, kenshi mu bubiko bwa `/media/izina_rya_nyene_konti/usb`.



![Image](assets/fr/249.webp)



Kugira ngo ukuremwo(unmount) urufunguzo rwa USB maze wongere ukore encryption, ongere ufyonde ku gacapo k'igufuri muri GNOME Disks.



Ubwa nyuma, fyonda ku buto icapye ko umwampi iri hejuru bukaboko kiburyo kugira ngo ukure urufunguzo muri PC yawe neza. Igihe kindi winjiye, Ubuntu izoca ibona urufunguzo rwawe ruri encrypted hanyuma ice igusaba ijambo ry'ibanga, bidasavye ko ufungura GNOME Disks.



![Image](assets/fr/250.webp)





- **Windows:**



Kuri Windows, umuti kavukire/w'umwimerere ugufasha kunyegeza amakuru aja kuri disk yawe. Biroroshe kuw'ukoresha: genda gusa muri "*Privacy & Security*", hanyuma wemeze mugasandugu kari kuri "*Device encryption*" mu gice kindi kirimwo ibijanye nivyo nyene. Imfunguruzo zo gusubirana ububasha zizoca zibikwa muri konti yawe ya Microsoft.



![Image](assets/fr/251.webp)



Nimba ukoresha konti isanzwe idafatanye na konti ya microsoft, canke nimba inyabwonko yawe itemera ubwo buryo, urashobora gushiraho uburyo bwa *BitLocker* uvyigiriye (porogarame ya Microsoft inyegeza amakuru). Ariko kandi hariho n'ubundi buryo bwa open-source nka *VeraCrypt*.



*VeraCrypt* ni porogarame y'ubuntu, ikoreshwa kuri Windows, Linux na macOS. Ishobora gukoreshwa mukunyegeza amakuru ari kuri disk yose canke ku gice, canke kurema dosiye ya container ikora nka disk mpimbano irinzwe. interface ya VeraCrypt iremeza ko iyo volume ishobora gushirwako nka disk isanzwe, ishobora gushikwako gusa inyuma yo kwemeza uwinjira.



Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi kuri uwo muti, usabwe kuraba iyi nyigisho yuzuye :



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/veracrypt-d5ed4c83-7c1c-4181-95ea-963fdf2d83c5




- **macOS :**



Kuri macOS, sisiteme yo kunyegeza amakuru ari kuri disk ishingiye kuri *FileVault*, uburyi bw'umwimerere ushobora gushikako winjiye mu miterere y'umutekano. Nimba Mac yawe ifise cip ya Apple Silicon (M1, M2...) canke chip ya T2, kunyegeza amakuru y'ibikoresho bisanzwe bikora kuburyo bwa burundu. Ariko rero, gukoresha FileVault birongereza ubundi bushobozi bw'umutekano mu kunegeza volume ya sisiteme yose.



![Image](assets/fr/252.webp)



FileVault imaze kuba ikora, uzokenera guhitamwo uburyo bwo kuyigarura mu gihe ijambo ry'ibanga ryatakaye: canke ukoreshe konti yawe ya *iCloud*, canke ureme urufunguzo rwihariye rwa backup. Urufunguzo rutegerezwa kubikwa ahantu hatekanye, kuko iyo rwatakaye vyotuma amakuru yawe adashobora gushikwako burundu.


Ku bikoresho vyo hanze vyo kubika (ama hard disks, USB sticks, n'ibindi), encryption ikorwa hakoreshejwe disk utility. Uzokenera guhindura burundu volume:



- Hitamwo igikoresho, ufyonde kuri "*Delete*".
- Hitamwo sceme ya "GUID Partition Table" scheme
- Hanyuma uhitemwo uburyo bwa dosiye (*APFS* canke *Mac OS extended*)
- Hitamwo ijambo ry'ibanga rikomeye
- Fyonda kuri "*Delete*" hanyuma "*OK*" encryption izoba irangiye.


Iyo encryption imaze gushirwaho, drive yo hanze ishobora gusomwa muri sisiteme mugihe ubanje gushira mwo ijambo ry'ibanga. Iyo sisiteme izoheza iyugurure ako kanya.


#### Impanuro nke ku bijanye n'ububiko bwawe bw'amakuru anyegejwe


Imbere yo kunyegeza amakuru ari kububiko, ukeneye gukora ububiko bw'inyongera bw'amakuru yawe yose (kiretse iyo atakiriho, birumvikana), kuko uburyo bwo kunyegeza anakuru muri rusangi bufuta ibisanzwe biriko.


Guhitamwo ijambo ry'ibanga na vyo nyene ni ngirakamaro cane: ritegerezwa kuba rirerire, rikomeye kandi ryihariye, kuko ari ryo ryonyene ririnda amakuru yawe uwundi muntu w'umunyaruyeri. Ukeneye kandi gukora backup, nk'akarorero mu butunganirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga, kuko aho bitandukanye n'izindi serivisie zitangwa kuri interineti, nta buryo bwo kugarura ivyatakaye buriho. Iyo wibagiwe ijambo ry'ibanga ryawe, amakuru arazimangana burundu


### Guhitamwo  dosiye za kunyegeza


Mu bihe bimwe bimwe, harigiihe usanga bidakenewe canke ugasanga bitanashoboka ko unyegeza hard disk canke idindi bikoresho vyo hanze. Muri ivyo bihe, urashobora guhitamwo gukoresha uburyo bwo kunyegeza amadosiye ca ububiko wihitiyemwo, ivyo bikaba birimwo gukingira gusa amadosiye canke ububiko bumwe bumwe burimwo amakuru y'agaciro.


Uburyo bumwe buzwi cane bwo kunyegeza amadosiye ni ugukoresha GPG. Ico gikoresho gishingiye ku buhinga bwo gukingira amakuru budahuye(asymmetric cryptography): ufise imfunguruzo zibiri, rumwe ni urwa rusangi, ushobora gutanga atakibazo, urundi na rwo rw'ibanga, rutegerezwa kuguma ari ibanga rikomeye. Amadosiye aranyegezwa hakoreshejwe urufunguzo rwa rusangi rw'uwuyakira, ariko ashobora kwugurugwa gusa hakoreshejwe urufunguzo rwiwe rw'ibanga.


Iyi tegeko ngendegwako ni ryiza cane mu guhana amadosiye y'agaciro n'abandi ata nkomanzi, ata jambo ry'ibanga utanze. Mugihe harivyo ukora ku giti cawe canke rimwe na rimwe, GPG ikoresha kandi ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru buhuye(synnetrical encryption): dosiye iraheza igakingirwa n'ijambo ry'ibanga ry'ihariye rizwi na wewe gusa.


Iyindi nzira nziza cane ni Cryptomator. Iyi porogarame ya open source iragufasha gukora ububiko burinzwe(safe): ububiko budasanzwe aho amadosiye yose ashizwemwo ahita anyegezwa. Iyi safe ishobora guhuzwa na serivisi za cloud nka Dropbox, Google Drive canke Nextcloud ata nimwe ironse uburenganzira kumakuru atanyegejwe. Iyo porogarame iraboneka kuri sisiteme zose, harimwo Android na iOS, kandi ntibisaba ubuhinga budasanzwe kugira ngo umuntu ayikoreshe.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/cryptomator-84e52c76-2253-49fe-81da-e05e90c28d0d


![Image](assets/fr/256.webp)



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/picocrypt-98c213bd-9ace-425b-b012-bea71ce6b38f

Ubwa nyuma, birashoboka kandi gukoresha VeraCrypt mu buryo bwa disk mpimbano, Ituma ushobora kurema dosiye ikora nka disk mpimbano inyegeza amakuru, ishobora kwemezwa muri sisiteme nka disk isanzwe.


Ubu ko umaze kwiga ingene wokingira amakuru yawe bwite ubusuma canke ivyago vyokuyatakaza, igice gikurikira kivuga kukindi kintu gihambaye: ingene wokingira amadosiye yawe bwite ngo ntabe imvo y'ibitero biciye ku makuru yayo yitwa metadata.


## Gusukura amakuru ya metadata


<chapterId>0869e92e-5488-4e8a-90e6-9b9d1c58a19b</chapterId>


Igihe cose ukoze dosiye ya ubuhinga bwa none, yaba ifoto, inyandiko y'ibiro, dosiye y'amajwi canke y'amasanamu, iba irimwo metadata. Aya makuru ntaboneka iyo w'uguruye dosiye, ariko aba ahari, kandi arimwo ibintu by'ingirakamoro cane kurwego rwo hejuru.


### Ni kuki metadata yo gushira mu kaga?


Metadata ni amakuru afatanye na dosiye, uruhara rwayo ni ugutanga amakuru yerekeye ibirimwo. Mw'ishusho, ayo makuru ni itariki n'isaha iyo shusho yafashweko, amakuru nyayo ya GPS, ubwoko bw kamera canke terefone ngendanwa yakoreshejwe, rimwe na rimwe mbere n'imiterere y'ubuhinga. Muri dosiye y'inyandiko, ayo makuru ashobora kuba izina ry'umwanditsi, izina ry'ishirahamwe, ID y'ikiganiro (session ID), ibimenyetso vy'igihe ya remwa canke yahinduriwe, canke mbere ivyiyumviro vyatanzwe mugihe yahindurwa.


Izo metadata zoshobora gusa n'ibitagira akamaro, ariko arashobora gukoreshwa n'abanyaruyeri kugira ngo bamenye uwanditse dosiye, bamenye aho umuntu ari, ingeso, canke mbere bakoreshe ibibibazo vya verisiyo ya porogarame wakoresheje bisanzwe bizwi nkinzira yo kukwinjirira.


Reka dufate akarorero nyako: ushize ifoto bivugwa ko ata muntu ayizi ku rubuga. Nimba utakuyeho metadata ya EXIF, gufyonda rimwe gusa birashobora kwerekana ama coordinates nyayo ya GPS y'inzu yawe, ubwoko bwa terefone yawe n'itariki nyayo iyo foto yafashweko. Cokimwe, n'inyandiko ya PDF yoherejwe ata wuzi uwayirungitse yoshobora kuba irimwo izina ryawe ryose muri metadata zayo.


Ni co gituma imbuga zimwe zimwe zisohora ibinyamakuru be n'izi tumatumanako zica zikurako metadata y'amafoto yawe. Izo ninka X (Twitter), Instagram, Signal na Session. Ku rundi ruhande, izindi mbuga ntizikurako metadata na gato: ivyo ni ko bigenda ku forumu menshi kuri interineti, kuri mbuga nyinshi za imeyiri, canke mbere iyo ushize ahabona dosiye iyariyo yose k'urubuga.


Ni ikintu gihambaye co kwimenyereza: dosiye ikimara kuva mu maboko yawe, urakeneye kwiyumvira gusukura metadata zayo kugira ngo wirinde gutangaza amakuru y'ibanga canke y'agaciro utabizi. Reka turabe ingene ivyo wobikora, bivanye na sisiteme ukoresha.


### Kuri Linux (Debian)


#### Gukoresha ExifTool


Uburyo bushitse kandi bwizewe bwo gucunga no gufuta metadata ni ExifTool, bwateguwe na Phil Harvey. Ihuye n'igitigiri kinini c'ubwoko bw'amadosiye y'amafoto (JPG, PNG, PDF, MP3, DOCX...) ubasha kandi nokubona kandi ugashobora gufuta izo metadata.



- Intambwe ya 1: Shiramwo ExifTool


Kugira ngo uyishire muri distribution ya Debian (Ubuntu), ugurura terminal wandike ibwirizwa:


```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt install libimage-exiftool-perl
```


Iyi paki ishiramwo `exiftool`, ushobora kuca ukoresha ku murongo w'amabwirizwa.



![Image](assets/fr/259.webp)





- Intambwe ya 2: **Kubona metadata za dosiye** (mu gifaransa)



Kugira ngo ubone metadata zose ziri muri dosiye, koresha ibwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
exiftool name.webp
```



Subiriza `name.webp` n'izina ry'ukuri rya dosiye yawe. Kandi urabe neza ko uri mu bubiko burimwo iyi foto. Nk'akarorero, nimba mfise ifoto y'igicapo ca Satoshi Nakamoto mu bubiko bwa `/Downloads`, ndashobora kwerekana amakuru yaco nkoresheje iri bwirizwa rikurikira:



```bash
cd Downloads
exiftool Satoshi-Nakamoto-Lugano.webp
```



![Image](assets/fr/260.webp)



Uzoca ubona urutonde rurerure rw'ibiranga, bishobora kubamwo:




- Itariki n'isaha y'iremwa
- Amakuru ya GPS 
- Uwakoze kamera n'ubwoko
- porogarame yakoreshejwe mu gu kuyikora
- Amakuru yerekeye uwayikoze...



Ivyo biguha inyishu yuzuye y'ivyo ugiye gutangaza canke gutanga.





- Intambwe ya 3: Gufuta metadata



Kugira ngo ufute metadata zose zidakenewe muri dosiye, koresha ibwirizwa:



```bash
exiftool -all= name.webp
```


![Image](assets/fr/261.webp)



Iri bwirizwa rihita rikora kopi ya dosiye y'umwimerere na metadata zigira zifutwe. Dosiye y'umwimerere ibikwa kw'izina ryayo rigaherezwa na `_original`.



![Image](assets/fr/262.webp)



Nimba udashaka kugumana dosiye y'umwimerere, ushobora kuyifuta ukoresheje iri bwirizwa:



```bash
exiftool -all= -overwrite_original name.webp
```



Nitwasubira kuraba metadata za dosiye yacu, turashobora kubona ko metadata zose zidakenewe canke y'ibanga zakuweho.



![Image](assets/fr/263.webp)





- Intambwe ya 4: Sukura ububiko bwose



Nimba ufise amadosiye menshi yo gukora mu bubiko bumwe, ushobora gukoresha ibwirizwa rusangi nka:



```bash
exiftool -all= *.jpg
```



Rizo futa metadata z'amadosiye yose ya JPEG ari mwubwo bubiko. Ushobora guhindura iyo nzira kugira ngo ihure n'ivyo ukeneye (`*.webp`, `*.pdf`...).



![Image](assets/fr/264.webp)



#### Gukoresha MAT2.



Nk'uburyo bundi busa no gukoresha ExifTool, ushobora gukoresha MAT2 (*Metadata Anonymization Toolkit v2*).





- Gushiramwo MAT2:



```bash
sudo apt install mat2
```



![Image](assets/fr/265.webp)



Iyo umaze kuyishiramwo, ushobora kuyikoresha uciye ku murongo w'amabwirizwa nk'uku:



```bash
mat2 fichier.pdf
```



![Image](assets/fr/266.webp)



Mu bisanzwe, MAT2 ntihindura dosiye y'umwimerere: irema verisiyo yasukuwe mu bubiko uriko ukoreramwo mugihe `-clean` yongeweko.



![Image](assets/fr/267.webp)



Kugira ngo usukure ububiko bwose, nk'ububiko bwa `/Downloads`:



```bash
mat2 ~/Downloads/*
```



### Izindi sisiteme (Windows na macOS)



Kuri Windows na macOS, hari uburyo bwinshi bwo gukuraho metadata mu nyandiko zawe. Njye mbona, ikintu coroshe ni ugukoresha porogarame ya open-source [ExifCleaner](https://exifcleaner.com/). Ico gikoresho kira remurutse kandi gifise interface y'ibicapo gikorana n'ubwoko bwinshi bw'amadosiye mu guterura no gutereka gusa (drag and drop). Mu gutereka dosiye imwe canke nyinshi muri interface, iyo porogarame ica ifuta metadata zidakenewe igasubirira dosiye y'umwimerere n'iyahinduwe mubwo bubiko nyene. ExifCleaner iraboneka kuri Windows, macOS na Linux.



Biroroshe cane kuyi koresha: ico usabwa gusa nukwugurura porogarame, hanyuma uterure dosiye imwe canke nyinshi utereke muri interface.


![Image](assets/fr/257.webp)



Rindira umwanya mutoyi mu gihe igikoresho gisukura metadata. Igihe ivyo birangiye, uzobona incamake yerekana igitigiri ca metadata z'arizihasanzwe n'izisigaye. Amakuru yose atari ngombwa azoba yamaze kuvako.



![Image](assets/fr/258.webp)



Gusukura metadata y'amadosiye usangiza abandi rero ni akamenyero keza ko gukurikiza iyo bije ku bijanye n'umutekano w'ikoranabahanga ry'amakuru. Kubw'ibikoresho vyoroshe vyashikirijwe muri iki gice, ni akamenyero ushobora kugira mu buryo bworoshe ku musi ku musi.



Twashitse ku mpera y'iki gisata ku bijanye no gukingira inyabwonko yawe. Mu gice gikurikira, tuzoba turiko turihweza mu buryo bwimbitse imwe muri porogarame zihambaye cane z'inyabwonko yawe: mucukumbuzi. Ni yo yonyene ihuriza hamwe igice kinini c'ibikorwa vyawe vy'ubuhinga bwa none, bikaba biyigira intumbero nyamukuru mu bijanye n'umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga.




# Mucukumbuzi: OS iri muri OS


<partId>125c3d99-6aba-4050-bc7c-8543ef8587e4</partId>



## Incamake y'amateka ya mucukumbuzi


<chapterId>ac6d2c23-5883-4564-b6a9-bc109b47f92c</chapterId>



Mucukumbuzi ni porogarame igufasha gushika ku mbuga n'ibiri kuri *World Wide Web*. Uruhara rwayo ni ugusobanura indimi zikoreshwa mu guhingura amapaji y'urubuga, cane cane HTML, CSS na JavaScript, kugira ngo bigaragaze ivyo tubona ku rubuga mu buryo busomeka kandi ukaba wabikoresha. Ikora nka interface hagati y'uwukoresha na seriveri y'imbuga, habaho kurungika ubusaba no kwakira inyishu biciye kw'itegeko rya HTTP canke HTTPS.



Ariko muri iki gihe, mucukumbuzi yaracitse ikintu kirenze kuba ari porogarame gusa: ahubwo kenshi iba ari interface nyamukuru mu vy'ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko, cane cane ku bakoresha bashasha. Ni co gituma rimwe na rimwe ifatwa nka "sisiteme igira kabiri" kuyisanzwe muri nyabwonko (Twamaze kubona mu gisata ca mbere ca SCU202). Vy'ukuri, ibikorwa vyinshi vyahora bikorwa hakoreshejwe porogarame zihariye ku nyabwonko ubu bikorerwa kuri interineti biciye kuri mucukumbuzi: ivyo kwisamaza (entertaimebt), ibikorwa vyo mu biro (Gukorana n'amajambo, Gukorana n'impapuro z'ibiharuro n'ugushikiriza), gucunga ubutumwa bwa imeyiri, gutanga ubutumwa bugufi, kubika amadosiye no gukorana n'abandi.



Nyamaze rero ntiyamye ifise urwo ruhara nyamukuru. Amateka ya mucukumbuzi yaranzwe n'urugendo rw'udusha twagiye tugaragara, uguhiganwa mu vy'ikoranabuhanga, rimwe na rimwe n'ukugira umuntu umwe yiharira isoko. Gukurikirana ivy'iyi nkuru bizodufasha gutahura ingene mucukumbuzi zacitse ikintu gikomeye cane, n'igituma umutekano wazo ari ikibazo gihambaye cane muri iki gihe.



→ Akenshi mucukumbuzi bayitiranya na moteri y'ukurondera. Nyamaze ivyo bibiri biratandukanye cane. Mucukumbuzi ikoreshwa mu kugaragaza imbuga, mu gihe moteri y'ukurondera (ishobora gushikwako biciye kuri mucukumbuzi) ikoreshwa mu kurondera amakuru kuri interineti biciye mu gukora urutonde no gupanga neza amapaji y'imbuga.



### Ivuka na mucukumbuzi ya mbere



Amateka ya mucukumbuzi atangurira kw'ivuka rya *World Wide Web*, yavumbuwe na Tim Berners-Lee mu 1989-1990. Ni uburyo bwo gushika ku mapaji arimwo inyandiko, amashusho, amasanamu canke amahuzu biciye kuri interineti, ukoresheje mucukumbuzi. Kugira ngo iyi sisiteme nshasha ishobore gukoreshwa, mu mpera z'umwaka w'1990 yarakoze mucukumbuzi yambere yo gukoresha, yitwa "WorldWideWeb", yashizeho umushinge w'ukuronderera kumbuga nk'uko tubizi uyu musi. Itwemerera  kuraba no gukora amapaji y'urubuga, harimwo editor ya HTML bikoranye. Kugira ngo ntihabeho kw'itiranya mucukumbuzi n'urubuga ubwarwo, izina ryayo ryahinduwe mu nyuma riba "Nexus".



![Image](assets/fr/093.webp)



Mu 1992, harabonetse izindi mucukumbuzi nyinshi zigeragezwa. Imwe mu za menyekanye cane ni Erwise, yateguwe n'abanyeshure bane bo muri Finlande bayikorera sisiteme ya X Window ishingiye kuri Unix. Ni yo yari mucukumbuzi ya mbere ifise interface y'igicapo ya korewe ubu bwoko bw'ikibanza. Naho yari ifise akamaro mu vy'ubuhinga, yarashikiwe n'ingorane z'ukubura amahera kandi ntiyabungabungwa inyuma y'aho isohokeye ubwa mbere. Iyindi migambi, nka ViolaWWW, na yo nyene yarabonetse muri ico kiringo.



![Image](assets/fr/094.webp)



1992 kandi niho haremwa Lynx, mucukumbuzi ikuze kurusha izindi iki bungabungwa kandi ikoreshwa n'ubu. Yateguwe n'umugwi w'abanyeshure bo muri kaminuza ya Kansas.



Ariko mu mwaka w'1993 niho vy'ukuri urubuga rwinjiye mu gihe c'iterambere ryihuse hamwe n'ugushika kwa NCSA Mosaic. Iyi browser yakozwe na Marc Andreessen na Eric Bina bo muri NCSA (*National Center for Supercomputing Applications*) muri leta z'unze ubumwe z'amerika. Mosaic ni mucukumbuzi yambere yashobora gufatanya neza inyandiko n'amashusho mw'idirisha rimwe. Ishobora kwerekana amashusho neza kuri paji z'urubuga (yo mu bwoko bwa GIF na XBM), iza nk'iterambere k'uburyo bwari buhasanzwe bwa mucukumbuzi zigaragaza inyandiko gusa nka Lynx. Mosaic kandi yarashizeho uburyo bwo kwemera amafomu, bica bifungura inzira y'ugukorana nyakuri hagati y'uwukoresha na seriveri y'urubuga. Mosaic yaciye yihuta gushirwa muri sisiteme nyinshi (Windows, Mac, Unix), bituma vyoroha gukwiragiza. Mu mwaka umwe, yacitse igikoresho cemewe co kuronderera kumbuga.



![Image](assets/fr/095.webp)



Mu mwaka w'1994, Marc Andreessen yaravuye muri NCSA, ashinga ikigo ca Netscape Communications arikumwe na Jim Clark. Igice kinini c'umugwi mubari barakoze kuri Mosaïque barifatanije nawe. Haciye igihe gito, ico kigo cashize hanze mucukumbuzi yitwa Netscape Navigator, mucukumbuzi ishingiye ku mishinge ya Mosaic, ariko ikora neza kandi yongererejwe ubuhinga bwo gukora neza. Mu mwaka w'1995, Netscape yazanye agasha kogushiramwo ururimi rwa JavaScript, rwateguwe na Brendan Eich, rwatuma amapaji y'urubuga agira ubushobozi bundi, ni ukuvuga ko yaca agira ubushobozi bwo kw'ishura kubikorwa vy'abakoresha bidasavye ko barinda gutanguza urubuga.



![Image](assets/fr/096.webp)



Kubera ko Netscape Navigator yari yoroshe gukoresha, ikaba ishobora gukorera kuri sisiteme zose kandi ikagira umuvuduko udasanzwe, yaciye yihuta kwishingira intahe nk'ikigereranyo c'urubuga ruriko rurakura. Mu mwaka w'1995, yari ifise ibice 90% vy'isoko, ivyo bikaba ari intango y'igihe ca mbere ca mucukumbuzi. Ivyo vyatumye Microsoft igira ico ikoze, bituma haba intambara ya za mucukumbuzi.



### Kuva ku ntambara za mucukumbuzi gushika ku myaka y'ukwiharira isoko



Ivyo Netscape Navigator yaronse hagati mu myaka y'1990 ntitwo vugako Microsoft harico yatakaje, kuko yaciye itahura ningoga akamaro ka mucukumbuzi muri kazoza k'ubuhinga bwo gukoresha inyabwonko. Muri Myandagaro 1995, haciye imisi mikeyi Windows 95 isohotse, Microsoft yarasohoye verisiyo ya mbere ya Internet Explorer, mu ntango yari ishingiye ku ruhusha rw'ubudandaji rwa kode y'isoko ya Spyglass Mosaic (iyindi verisiyo y'ubudandaji ya Mosaic itandukanye n'iyakozwe na NCSA).



Verisiyo ya mbere ya Internet Explorer yari igitegugwa, ariko Microsoft yatanguye politike ikaze y'ukuyitegura. Mu mwaka w'1996, hamwe na Internet Explorer 3.0, Microsoft yatanguye kuza irashiramwo mucukumbuzi yayo muri sisiteme ya windows, ivyo bikaba vyatumye abakoresha batagikenera kuvoma mucukumbuzi z'abandi. Uko guyishira muri sisiteme za windows kwa komejwe na Internet Explorer 4.0 mu 1997, iyo na yo ikaba yarazanye imoteri nshasha y'uguhindura amapage yitwa Trident. Iyi moteri yongereza umuvuduko wo kubonesha neza ama paji kandi ikorana neza cane na interface ya Windows.



![Image](assets/fr/097.webp)



Umukenyuro wa Microsoft ushingiye ku buhinga n'urudandazwa:




- gufatanywa kwa Internet Explorer na Windows (isanzwe irimwo kandi yokugwamwo igihe cose bikenewe);
- mucukumbuzi y'ubuntu, ugereranyije na Netscape, yagumye idandazwa gushika n'ubu;
- kugenzura APIs na sisiteme kugira ngo bahimirize gukoresha mucukumbuzi yabo mu kibanza ca Windows.



Mu gihe c'iryo higanwa, Netscape yaciye itakaza ikibanza vyihuse. Mu gihe c'imyaka irimunsi y'itatu, umugabane wayo kw'isoko waragabanutse cane. Mu ntango z'imyaka ya 2000, Internet Explorer yari ifise umugabane urenga 95% mw'isoko, ivyo bikaba vyatumye izindi mucukumbuzi bisankuko zidahari.



![Image](assets/fr/098.webp)



Uko kwiharira isoko kwatumye habaho igabanuka ryo guhanga udusha. Kubera ko ata n'umwe yari asigaye mw'ihiganwa, Microsoft yasa niyaretse iterambere rya Internet Explorer risa nirihagaza. Hagati ya IE6 (yasohotse muri 2001 na Windows XP) na verisiyo yayo yakurikiye IE7 (mu 2006), nta verisiyo nini yasohotse, naho hariho ubugoyagoye mu vy'umutekano, kudashobora kwakira CSS be nokudahuza nibisabwa na W3C. Ukwo guhagarara kwatumye iterambere ry'urubuga rihagarara imyaka itari mike, bica bituma abahingura bandika kode zihariye zikosora amakosa yari muri Trident canke inyifato idasanzwe.



Kubera ko Netscape yari izi ko itazosubira kuja mw'ihiganwa ry'urudandazwa, yahisemwo gutanga kode yayo y'kubantu bose mu 1998. Ivyo ni vyo vyatumye havuka umugambi wa Mozilla, ivyo bikaba vyatumye habaho ihinduka rikomeye: ugutegura mucukumbuzi y'ubuntu, yubahiriza ibisabwa, ishigikiwe n'ishirahamwe ryigenga.



Intumbero y'uyu mugambi ni ugusubira kwubaka gushasha mucukumbuzi ku mishinge mishasha, na moteri nshasha yo guhindura izo kwubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako z'urubuga rwuguruye(open web standards). Intumbero yari igaragara: gusubizaho ukwuguruka n'ugukorana n'urubuga, mu gihe Internet Explorer yariko iranyiganyiga. Ni muri uwo mugambi, haciye imyaka mikeyi, Mozilla Firefox yavutse.



### Isanurwa mw'ikorana buhanga: Mozilla Firefox na Safari



Inyuma y'imyaka myinshi urubuga ruhagaze kubera ukwiharira isoko kwa Internet Explorer, urubuga rwinjiye mu gihe co gusubira kwisanura mu ntango z'imyaka ya 2000. Iryo hinduka ryatangujwe n'abakinyi babiri bakuru: Mozilla na Apple.



Mu mwaka w'2002, umugambi wa Mozilla, wavutse mu gusohora kode y'isoko ya Netscape, waratanguje mucukumbuzi nshasha: Phoenix, ica ihindurirwa izina yitwa Firebird, hanyuma amaherezo ica yitwa Firefox mu mwaka w'2004 kugira ngo ntihagire amakimbirane abaho yamazina. Firefox yari ishingiye kuri moteri nshasha yo guhindura, yitwa Gecko, yagenewe kwihuta, kwaguka kandi, ikiruta vyose, kuba intahemuka ku ngingo ngenderwako z'urubuga zasobanuwe na W3C (*World Wide Web Consortium*). Bitandukanye na Trident, Gecko ishigikira ubuhinga bwa none nka CSS 2.1, DOM na SVG (*Scalable Vector Graphics*), hamwe n'ugucungera umutekano gukomeye.



![Image](assets/fr/099.webp)



Firefox kandi yashizeho udusha twinshi tuzogira ingaruka ziramvye ku kuronderera kumbuga:




- uburyo bwo kwagura bushingiye ku bice, butuma abakoresha bashobora kwongerako ibintu bishasha bitagoranye badakoze ku mutima wa mucukumbuzi;
- tabbed browsing, izwi cane mu bantu bose, naho nyene isanzwe iriho muri mucukumbuzi za kera nka Opera;
- ibikoresho vy'ubuzima bw'ibanga nk'uguhagarika pop-up, ubutunganiriizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga, n'uburyo bwo gutunganya neza amakuki(cookies) na JavaScript.



Ukwuremuruka kwayo, ubushobozi bw'uguhinduranya no kwubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako vyakwegereye ningoga abakoresha binzobere, abahingura imbuga n'umuntu wese arondera ubundi buryo bw'uguruye kuruta Internet Explorer. Mu mwaka w'2005, Firefox yari yararengeye 10% vy'isoko, ivyo bikaba ari ikintu ciza cane ugereranije na mucukumbuzi yari yarashizwe muri buri PC zose zikoresha Windows.



Hagati aho, Apple yariko irategura mucukumbuzi yayo y'umwimerere ikorana na macOS. Muri Nzero 2003, Safari yarasohotse ku mugaragaro. Ishingiye kuri WebKit, moteri y'uguhindura ya open source ikomoka kuri KHTML, yateguwe mbere n'umugambi wa KDE kuri mucukumbuzi yawo Konqueror. WebKit irashimwa cane kubera uburyo iremurutse mwo, yihuta kandi yoroshe gutwarika. Apple yashizeho ubuhinga bwinshi bwo gutuma ibintu bigenda neza, cane cane mu bijanye no gutunganya JavaScript, ivyo bikaba vyariko biraba ikibazo nyamukuru kubera ukuntu hariko haza porogarame zo kurubuga z'ikorana n'abakoresha.



![Image](assets/fr/100.webp)



Safari yabaye mucukumbuzi ikoreshwa kuri Mac zose guhera kuri Mac OS X Panther (10.3), buhoro buhoro isubirira Internet Explorer ya Mac, iyo Microsoft yahevye mu 2005. WebKit na yo izokoreshwa mu nyuma mu zindi mucukumbuzi nyinshi.



Ivyo bikorwa vyatumye habaho amahiganwa mu vy'ubuhinga, vyagiye gutuma Internet Explorer igarukana ububasha bwayo buhoro buhoro, kandi bica bituma habaho gucira inzira uruvyaro rushasha rwa mucukumbuzi zihuta, zubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako, kandi zibanda ku bwuzuzanye, umutekano n'ubushobozi. Hagati y'umwaka wa 2006 n'uwa 2008, Internet Explorer yaratakaje buhoro buhoro umugabane w'isoko, mu gihe Firefox yishizeho nk'ubundi buryo nyamukuru. Ivyo vyatumye habaho ukuza kw'umukinyi mushasha: Google Chrome.



### Ihinduka ry'isoko: ukuza kwa Google Chrome



Kw'itariki ya 2 nyakanga 2008, Google yatangaje ko isohoye mucukumbuzi yayo bwite: Google Chrome. Ico gihe, Firefox yariko iratera imbere kandi Internet Explorer yari igifashe imitima yabenshi, ariko yariko iranegurwa cane kubera ko igenda buhoro, idashikamye kandi isigaye inyuma y'ingingo ngenderwako zari zigezweko. Google, yizigira cane urubuga ku bikorwa vyayo (kurondera, Gmail, Maps...), yashaka mucukumbuzi ibereye igihe twariko kiza ca porogarame zigoye z'urubuga.



![Image](assets/fr/101.webp)



Chrome mu ntango yari ishingiye ku nkingi zibiri z'ubuhinga:




- moteri yo guhindura ya WebKit, kw'iragi rya Safari na KHTML, yo kwerekana HTML/CSS;
- moteri nshasha ya JavaScript, yitwa V8, yanditswe muri C++ ikoranya kode ya JavaScript mu mabwirizwa y'inyabwonko akokanya (JIT, mu majambo yose *Just-In-Time*), igatuma ibikorwa vy'urubuga bikora neza cane.



Ariko icari kidasanzwe na Chrome ni ubuhinga bwayo bwo gukora ibintu vyinshi. Buri tab ikora mu buryo bwihariye, ikoresheje ubuhinga bwa sandboxing burinda paji yoteza ingorane guhungabanya mucukumbuzi yose. Ukwo kwitandukanya na kwo nyene kuratuma habaho ugushikama: iyo tab yononekaye, izindi ziguma zikora. Ikindi kuri ivyo ni interface iriko ibintu bikeyi, ishingiye ku kugaragaza neza amapaji, ikaba ita umurongo wa menu, Aderese n'umurongo w'aho barondere biza birihamwe (*Omnibox*), kandi ikishira kugihe bikaba ata ruhara ubigizemwo.



Ishigikiwe k'ukumenyekana kwa Google hamwe n'isekeza ryiza cane ryo kwamamaza, Chrome yararonse umugabane w'isoko ningoga. Ukwihuta kwayo n'uko yoroshe gukoresha vyatumye abayikoresha bayikunda. Mu mwaka w'2012, Chrome yararengeye Internet Explorer kw'isoko ry'isi yose ku ncuro ya mbere.



![Image](assets/fr/102.webp)



Mu mwaka w'2013, Google yatangaje ihinduka rikomeye ry'ingene yokora: yagomba kuzokoresha fork ya WebKit kugira ngo ireme moteri nshasha yigenga yo guhindura, yitwa Blink. Iyi fork isigurwa n'itandukaniro ry'ubuhinga n'imitunganirize bitandukanye na Apple, cane cane ku bijanye n'uko moteri yubatse n'ugushiramwo ibintu vy'igerageza. Blink yabaye moteri yihariye ya Chrome kuva kuri verisiyo ya 28 gushika ubu, hanyuma iraheza ikoreshwa n'izindi mucukumubuzi nyinshi: Opera (yahevye Presto mu 2013), Vivaldi, Brave, Microsoft Edge (kuva muri 2020), n'izindi.



Kuva mu mwaka w'2025, Google Chrome ifise ibice 66% vy'isoko ry'isi yose ku bikoresho vyose (inyabwonko, amaterefone ngendanwa, tablet), nk'uko bigaragara mu makuru ya StatCounter. Ikurikirwa cane na Safari (ahanini kuri iOS/macOS), Microsoft Edge, na Firefox, zisanzwa ziriko zirakoroka kumigabane yazo y'isoko. Kwiharira isoko kwa Chrome kwarashitse kandi no mu mamaterefone ngendanwa biciye kuri Android WebView (igice ca sisiteme gikoreshwa n'ibihumbi vyama porogarame), na co nyene kikaba cizigiye Blink.



Chrome yarahinduye cane ubushobozi, umutekano n'ingingo ngenderwako z'ubuhinga bwa none bwa mucukumbuzi, mu gihe ivyura ikibazo gishasha co guhuriza hamwe nokugena ikoranabuhanga ry'urubuga.



### Uguhinduka kw'moteri zo guhindura: kuva kuri Trident gushika kuri Blink



Moteri y'uguhindura ni co gice nyamukuru ca mucukumbuzi. Uruhara rwayo nyamukuru ni ugusobanura amadosiye yakiriwe kuri seriveri (HTML, CSS, JavaScript, amashusho, imyandikire...) ku girango ireme interface y'igicapo. Moteri y'uguhindura ni nk'umusemuzi hagati y'indimi z'urubuga n'imboneshamashusho yawe, ihindura imirongo ya kode mwo paji ikora neza kandi ihuye.



Mu majambo nyayo, iyo winjije URL mu murongo wa aderese:




- Mucukumbuzi yohereza ubusabe bwa HTTP kuri seriveri iri kure;
- Serveri yishura n'inyandiko ya HTML;
- Moteri y'uguhindura isesangura iyo HTML, ikavoma amadosiye bifatanye (CSS, JavaScript, amashusho...);
- Yubaka "DOM" (*Document Object Model*) igaragaza imiterere y'inyandiko;
- Ikoresha amategeko ya CSS kugira ngo iharure ukuntu ikintu cose kigaragazwa (*layout*);
- Ihindura ibicapo ikoresheje ikarata y'ibicapo n'uburyo bwo gukoresha idirisha(graphics card and windowing system.).



Iyi nzira yose ikeneye kwihuta kandi igenda neza kugira ngo itange uburyo bwiza bw'abakoresha, mbere no ku mapaji atoroshe usanga agoye. Ivyo ni vyo vy'ukuri uruhara rwa moteri y'uguhindura.



Akira insiguro y'amateka ya moteri zo guhindura nyamukuru zahinduye iterambere ry'urubuga:



#### Trident (kuva mu 1997 gushika mu 2015)



Trident yakozwe na Microsoft ikorerwa mucukumbuzi ya Internet Explorer 4, ni moteri yari iganje ku rubuga mu ntango z'imyaka y'2000, hagati mu ntambara za mucukumbuzi. Naho mu misi yayo ya mbere yari ifise ubuhinga bushasha, yaciye yihuta gusubira inyuma mu bijanye no kwubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako za W3C, ivyo bica bituma habaho imbuga nyinshi zatunganijwe gusa kugira zibasha kugaragara kuri Internet Explorer.



Trident kandi yarerekanye ingorane z'umutekano be na moteri igenda gahoro ya JavaScript. Abahinguzi b'imbuga benshi bategerezwa kwandika kode yihariye kugira ngo bashobore gukora baciye k'uruhande ibibazo vyayo. Microsoft yarayisubirije mu 2015 na EdgeHTML, moteri y'ubuhinga bwa none cane yananiwe guhindura iyo nzira. Trident iguma ari ikigereranyo c'igihe moteri yashobora gushinga amategeko yayo bwite ku rubuga.



![Image](assets/fr/103.webp)



*Isoko : pcworld.com*



#### Gecko (1998)



Gecko yakozwe na Netscape, hanyuma ikabungabungwa n'ishirahamwe Mozilla, itanga ubushobozi kuri mucukumbuzi ya Firefox. Kuva mu ntango, Gecko yarabaye ntahangagwa mu bijanye no kwubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako. Yanditswe mu rurimi rwa C++ kandi igakorera kuma sisiteme menshi.



Gecko ni yo yatumye habaho udusha twinshi. Ariko rero, ishingiro ryayo ry'amakode rigoye kandi ry'akahise rituma ubwihindurize bumwe bumwe bugenda buhoro.



Ku bijanye n'umugabane w'isoko, Gecko ubu iri inyuma cane ya Blink, kuko Firefox ariyo yonyene ikoresha iyikoresha. Ikoreshwa kandi ku ruhande na mucukumbuzi nke zikoreshwa gake kandi zitazwi kenshi usanga ari forks za Firefox: Tor Browser, LibreWolf, Zen Browser, GNU IceCat, Waterfox... Ivyo bituma Gecko iba umushingantahe w'ubudasa ku rubuga, mu gihe Blink ari yo itwara.



![Image](assets/fr/104.webp)



#### KHTML (kuva mu 1998 gushika mu 2005)



Yateguwe n'umugambi wa KDE ikoreshwa na mucukumbuzi ya Konqueror, KHTML ni moteri iremurutse, itunganyijwe mu bice kandi inyaruka. Yanditswe mu rurimi rwa C++, yubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako kandi itanga ishingiro risukuye kandi rifise inyandiko nziza. Iyi moteri ni yo Apple yahisemwo mu 2001 kugira ngo ikore WebKit. KHTML rero ni umukurambere w'ubuhinga bwa Chrome na Safari.



![Image](assets/fr/105.webp)



#### WebKit (2003)



WebKit ni Fork ya KHTML yatangujwe na Apple kugira ngo ikore mucukumbuzi yabo bwite: Safari. Yabanje gutunganywa neza kugira ngo ikore neza kandi ikoreshwe muri macOS, hanyuma ikoreshwa na Google Chrome igihe yasohoka mu 2008. WebKit ishingiye ku bice bibiri:




- WebCore ku guhindura HTML/CSS ;
- JavaScriptCore (izwi kandi nka "Nitro") y'ugushitsa kode ya JavaScript.



WebKit igaragara cane kubera umuvuduko wayo n'ikirenge gitoyi (footprint). Ku bijanye na iOS, Apple yategetse ko ikoreshwa kuri mucukumbuzi zose kubera umutekano n'ugukoresha neza inguvu: mbere na Firefox canke Chrome kuri iPhone zikoresha WebKit.



![Image](assets/fr/106.webp)



#### Blink (2013)



Blink ni Fork ya WebKit yatangujwe na Google kugira ngo ikoreshwe na Chrome (na Chromium), hanyuma ifatwa vuba cane na Opera, Brave, Vivaldi, mbere na Microsoft Edge kuva mu 2020. Blink yazanye intwaro ibereye kurusha iya Apple, bituma Google ishobora kugerageza vuba cane APIs nshasha z'urubuga



![Image](assets/fr/107.webp)



Muri iki gihe, Blink ni moteri ikoreshwa cane mu guhindura kw'isi yose. Ariko rero, ubwo busumbasumbane buravyura ikibazo c'ubuhinga bumwe bumwe ku rubuga, ariko ivyo tuzobigarukako mu nyuma.



#### EdgeHTML (kuva mu 2015 gushika mu 2020)



Samuragwa wa Trident, EdgeHTML yakozwe na Microsoft kugira ngo Edge ijane nibigezwe ho, ifise ubushobozi bwo gukora neza kandi ihuye neza nibisabwa. Irimwo amwe mu ma kode ya Trident, ariko ikaba ifise moteri ya JavaScript yahinduwe. Naho ivyo bikorwa vyakozwe, EdgeHTML yarananiwe kwemeza abakoresha n'abakora urubuga. Muri 2020, Microsoft yahisemwo guheba EdgeHTML kugira ngo ikoreshe Blink, itanguza Edge Chromium, yacitse mucukumbuzi ya Blink ifise igice ca interface ya Microsoft.



![Image](assets/fr/108.webp)



Ugutera imbere kw'ama moteri yo guhindura kwerekana amateka y'urubuga: uguhuzagurika hagati y'uguhingura udusha n'ugushinga imirongo ngenderwako, ukuganza kw'abakinyi bakuru, ukugerageza uburyo bundi bwo guhindura ibintu bushingiye ku nyifato runtu canke ubuhinga. Ubu, hafi mucukumbuzi zose zishingiye kuri Blink, uretse Firefox (Gecko) na Safari (WebKit).



### Blink mugihe iganza, Gecko iriko igwana



Kuva Blink yaremwa muri 2013 no kwemerwa kwayo cane muri mucukumbuzi zose zikoreshwa na Chromium, iyo moteri yo guhindura ni yo yabaye igihambaye. Mu mwaka w'2025, ntizotanga gusa ubushobozi kuri Google Chrome, ariko kandi izotanga ubushobozi kuri Microsoft Edge (kuva mu mwaka w'2020), Opera, Brave, Vivaldi n'izindi mucukumbuzi nyinshi zitazwi cane. Ubukuru bwayo burenze 80% vy'isoko ku bikoresho vy'ibiro, na cane cane kuri Android, aho Chrome iza imbere y'igihe.



Ivyo bizana inyungu zimwe zimwe: Blink irakomeye kandi ishigikiwe n'imigwi ikomeye y'abahinga (Google, ariko kandi na Microsoft n'abandi), kandi iratera imbere cane. Blink kandi irafasha mu gutuma habaho uguhuza ibintu bimwe bimwe: abahinguzi b'imbuga barashobora gushimikira ku rubuga rumwe kugira ngo bashikire hafi abakoresha bose. Ariko kandi, ukwo kwibanda ku kintu kurafise ingorane zikomeye mu bijanye n'imiterere.



Ku ruhande rumwe, ishira ku ruhande izindi moteri, cane cane Gecko, ikoreshwa hafi gusa na Firefox. Mu mwaka w'2025, Firefox izogira umugabane w'isoko uri munsi ya 6%, ivyo bikaba bigabanya cane ubushobozi bwayo bwo gutuma ijwi ryayo ryumvikana mu biganiro ku bijanye n'iterambere ry'ingingo ngenderwako z'urubuga (W3C, WHATWG). Gecko itunganywa na Mozilla, ishirahamwe ridaharanira inyungu rifise uburyo buke cane kuruta Google. Moteri iguma ishobora guhangana kubindi bijanye n'ubuhinga bumwe bumwe (cane cane ugukingira ubuzima bw'ibanga), ariko irashikirwa n'ugusubira inyuma mu gushira mu ngiro API zimwe zimwe zo muri iki gihe. Kandi iki kintu kiri mu nzinguzingu y'ububisha: Gecko ntikora neza cane, ivyo bikaba bituma igitigiri c'abayikoresha kibanuka, ivyo bikaba bitera intege abahinguzi b'imbuga gutungunya imbugaza batitaye cane kuri Gecko, rero Gecko ntikora neza cane... n'ibindi.


![Image](assets/fr/109.webp)



Ku rundi ruhande, ukwo guhuriza hamwe ibintu vyose kuri Blink bisigura ko Google igenzura umuvuduko w'iterambere n'ivyoshigwa imbere mu buhinga bw'imbuga. Ariko rero, inyungu zayo mu rudandazwa (kwamamaza, gukurikirana inyifato, uburyo bw'abanyagihugu, n'ibindi) zishobora guhushanya n'ingingo ngenderwako z'ukutagira aho zibogamira, ugukorana n'abandi n'ubuzima bw'ibanga arivyo abakinyi nka Mozilla barwanirira.



Ikindi, kwizigira moteri imwe gusa biratuma habaho ingorane ku bijanye n'urubuga. Iyo Blink igize ikibazo, canke hakaba ikosa, ingaruka zishikira abakoresha bose. Ubutandukane bw'ubuhinga burafise uruhara rukomeye cane hano, nk'uko nyene bugira uruhara mu bijanye n'imyubakira ya sisiteme be na porogarame.



Ubu, Mozilla irabandanya kugira uruhara runini mu kurwanira urubuga rwuguruye, rwubahiriza ubuzima bw'ibanga kandi rushobora gushikwako ata nkomanzi. Firefox iguma ari imwe muri mucukumbuzi nke zikomeye zidashingiye kuri Chromium, kandi zitanga ubuhinga bushasha bwigenga. Ariko ukurokoka kwayo kuva ku bushobozi bwayo bwo kuguma ifise abayikoresha bahagije be n'amahera aramba.



Ubutegetsi bwa Blink rero si ikintu c'ubuhinga gusa: bujanye n'ivya politike, ubutunzi n'imibano mu bijanye n'uburongozi bw'urubuga. Muri ivyo, guteza imbere moteri y'uguhindura vyinshi biguma ari akamenyero keza mu gushigikira urubuga rudafise aho rugarukira, rutekanye kandi rukomeye.



Mu myaka mirongo itatu, mucukumbuzi yarahindutse kuva ku gikoresho coroshe co kuraba gushika ku rubuga rwa porogarame rukomeye, rwinjijwe mu mutima w'ubumenyi bwacu bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none ku musi ku musi. Gutahura iyo nzira y'iterambere ry'amateka biratomora akamaro k'ingene mucukumbuzi ikora mu bibazo vy'umutekano n'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none.



Mu gice gikurikira, Tuzotanga icegeranyo ca mucukumbuzi ziriho ubu, kuva kuza kera gushika ku kuzo muri kazoza, tugereranye ivyiza n'ibibi vyazo kugira ngo bigufashe guhitamwo neza.



## Incamake ya mucukumbuzi



<chapterId>4a9f71bc-8d76-4ce3-b983-2df1d6e47fb5</chapterId>



Tumaze gutohoza amateka n'iterambere rya mucukumbuzi, ubu turaza kuraba mucukumbuzi nyamukuru iriho uno musi. Guhitamwo mucukumbuzi si ikintu kidahambaye cane cane iyo, nk'uko biri kuri twebwe, ikintu ca mbere ari umutekano, ubuzima bw'ibanga n'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none. Buri mucukumbuzi irafise ivyiza vyihariye, ariko kandi irafise intege nke, akenshi bifitaniye isano n'uburyo bw'ubucuruzi bwaba nyenezo canke amahitamwo yabo y'ubuhinga.



Intumbero y'iki gice ni ukugufasha guhitamwo mucukumbuzi ikwiye neza ivyo ukeneye. Nazitunganije nisunze moteri y'uguhindura, ariko urutonde ntirugaragaza ubwoko ubwo ari bwo bwose bw'amanota.



### Mucukumbuzi zishingiye kuri Blink



#### Google Chrome



[Chrome](https://www.google.com/chrome/) inyungu iri mu gutera imbere vyihuta kandi bikomeza, ahanini birongowe na Google. Imenyekana kubera ubushobozi bwayo bwinshi, umuvuduko, ukuntu ihuye cane n'ingingo ngenderwako z'urubuga rwa none be n'ugushiramwo neza ibikorwa vya Google.



![Image](assets/fr/110.webp)



Ariko rero, mu bijanye n'umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga, Chrome iravyura ivyiyumviro bikomeye. Ku buryo busanzwe, mucukumbuzi ikorakoranya amakuru menshi ku bakoresha bayo (ivyobarondera, amateka...), aca akoreshwa cane cane mu kwamamaza na Google. Ubushobozi bwo gutandukanya cookies na trackers burafise aho bugarukira, kandi guhagarika burundu ugukurikirana biracagoye. Kandi, naho Chrome yoba itekanye mu buryo bw'ubuhinga (sandbox ikora neza, guhindura vyihuse...), iguma igenzurwa n'umukinyi akomeye inyungu ziwe z'ubucuruzi zidahuye n'ubusegaba nyakuri bw'ubuhinga bwa none.



Ikindi co kwitwararika ni kubera iyo nzira y'umuvuduko n'ugusobanuka, Chrome ikoresha uburyo bwinshi cane bwa sisiteme, cane cane RAM.



Google Chrome ishingiye ku mugambi wa Chromium, ikaba ari open source, Ariko rero, Google yongerako kode nyinshi z'uburenganzira. Rero ntifatwa nka open source bikwiye.



Rero sinzogusaba gukoresha Google Chrome, haba ku giti cawe canke ku kazi (kiretse, vy'ukuri, ubucuruzi bwawe bukorana na Google suite). Nkako, hariho uburyo bundi bwiza cane busa na serivisi za Google, haba mu karere no mu gicu. Cane cane, ndabatumiye kumenya ibikorwa bitangwa na Proton :



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/proton-mail-c3b010ce-254d-4546-b382-19ab9261c6a2

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/proton-drive-03cbe49f-6ddc-491f-8786-bc20d98ebb16

#### Brave



[Brave](https://brave.com/) ishingiye kuri Blink (nka Chrome), ariko itandukanye cane n'uburyo bwayo bushingiye ku buzima bw'ibanga. Ku bisanzwe, Brave ihagarika amatangazo n'ibikurikirana (ads and trackers), igashiramwo *HTTPS Everywhere*, kandi itanga uburinzi buteye imbere kuri fingerprinting n'inyandiko z'abandi. Uburyo bwayo bwo gukora ubucuruzi bushingiye ku kwamamaza kujanye no kwubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga, ariko ivyo biguma ari ivy'uguhitamwo kandi bishobora guhagarara bitagoranye.



Brave ishingiye kuri Chromium kandi kode yayo yose iraboneka kuri GitHub. Ibice bitobito vyonyene ni vyo bifise igice c'uburenganzira. Muri rusangi, Brave iri hafi cane ya mucukumbuzi iri open source.



![Image](assets/fr/111.webp)



Brave ni uburyo bukomeye bwo gusubirira Chrome, bufatanya umuvuduko, umutekano ukagije, ubuzima bw'ibanga bwiza ku buryo busanzwe na interface yoroshe. Ariko rero, sinoyiguhanurira, kubera gusa ko ishingiye kuri Chromium.



Naho mucukumbuzi nyinshi (harimwo na Brave) zishingiye kuri Chromium mu gihe zivuga ko zifise uburyo bwo gucungera ubuzima bw'ibanga, itohoza ryakozwe muri 2024 ryerekanye ko hariho ubufatanye, ku buryo busanzwe, bwa API yemerera Google kuronka amakuru y'agaciro yerekeye ibikoresho vy'ukoresha (CPU, GPU, RAM), na cane cane ibikorwa akore bijanye na serivisi za Google, nk'uko. Iyi API, yinjijwe nk'iyindi nzira idashobora gukurwaho muri Chrome, yariho kandi mu bikoresho vyinshi bikomoka kuri Edge, Opera... mbere na Brave.



Naho Brave kuva ico gihe yaciye ihagarika iyi API, iki kibazo kirerekana neza ukuntu izo mucukumbuzi zi z'ubakiye kuri Chromium, iguma ari umugambi uboshe cane ku bikorwa vya Google. Nk'inyishu, mbere n'ibindi bikoresho vy'ubuzima bw'ibanga vya Chromium ntibishobora gutanga ubwigenge bwose canke uburinzi bwose bw'amakuru y'abakoresha.



→ "***fingerprinting***" mu bijanye no kuronderera kuri interineti bisigura ubuhinga bujanye n'ugukorakoranya no gusuzuma amakuru kandi rimwe na rimwe yihariye yerekeye mucukumbuzi ukoresha, kugira ngo ushobore kumenyekana kandi ukurikiranwe ku mbuga zitandukanye, ata gukoresha ibimenyetso bigaragara nka cookies. Aya makuru ashobora kubamwo:




- Aderese IP yawe,
- Uwuguha interineti,
- Aho uri,
- Mucukumbuzi yawe n'imiterere yayo,
- sisiteme yawe ukoresha,
- Verisiyo ya porogarame yawe,
- Imyandikire yashizweho,
- Ingano y'imboneshamashusho yawe,
- Ubujakuzimu bw'ibara,
- Isaha yawe n'ururimi rwawe,
- HTML5 canvas,
- Isesengura ry'ibicapo,
- Inyongera bushobozi za mucukumbuzi yawe,
- n'ibindi...



Kugira ngo umenye nimba fingerprint ya mucukumbuzi yawe yihariye canke ko isa n'izabandi, urashobora gukoresha urubuga rukurikira: https://amiunique.org/


#### Vivaldi



[Vivaldi](https://vivaldi.com/), yashinzwe n'uwahoze ari umuyobozi mukuru wa Opera, iriko yibanda cane kubakoresha binzobere barondera ubuhinga bwo guhindura ibintu bwimbitse n'ibintu vy'ubuhinga nk'ibipande vyo ku ruhande(side panel), ubutunganyirizo bw'ama tab be n'uburyo bikoranye bwo kw'imura ivyandikwa.



Ku bijanye n'umutekano, Vivaldi irimwo uburyo bwinshi bwo guhagarika trackers na ads, ariko ubwo buryo bwo kurinda burihasi cane ya Brave. Kandi nayo ntikorera mu muco mu buryo buziguye, kuko ibice bimwe vya kode yayo si open source. Naho biri ukwo, itanga ubundi buryo bwiza, butashimikiye cane ku buzima bw'ibanga bukomeye kuruta Brave, ariko bushimikiye cane kuri Chrome canke Opera.



![Image](assets/fr/112.webp)



#### Opera



[Opera](https://www.opera.com/) ni urubuga rwa kera, rwamaze igihe kirekire ruriho kuva mu 1995. Ubu rukoresha Blink inyuma yo guheba moteri yarwo (*Presto*). Ifise interface igezwe ho n'ibintu bimwe bimwe bishasha.



Ariko rero, ku bijanye n'ubuzima bw'ibanga, Opera irateza impaka cane: yari ifiswe n'ishirahamwe ry'Abashinwa kuva mu 2016, ivyo bikaba vyatumye haba ibibazo ku bijanye n'ukuntu amakuru y'abakoresha yoshobora gukoreshwa nabi. Opera irimwo VPN bifatanye (proxy aho kuba VPN y'ukuri), ariko amategeko y'ubuzima bw'ibanga ntasobanutse neza ku bijanye n'ugucungera inyandiko zivyabaye(log). Opera na yo ni mucukumbuzi y'umuntu. sivyiza rero, cane cane igihe ubuzima bw'ibanga ari bwo buhambaye.



![Image](assets/fr/113.webp)



#### Mucukumbuzi zihariye



Muzishingiye kuri Blink harimwo n'izindi mucukumbuzi zo ku ruhande, akenshi zigenewe ibintu kanaka vyihariye:





- **Arc**:



Yateguwe n'ishirahamwe rya mucukumbuzi, [Arc](https://arc.net/) itanga uburyo butandukanye cane bwa interface. Isubirira ama tabs ya kera n'uburyo bwa "*ibibanza*", umurongo wo kuruhande wihariye, kandi igashiramwo ibikoresho vy'ubuhinga nko gufata ifoto y'ivyo ubona n'uburyo bwo guhindura urubug bworoshe. Ico gishimikiyeko ni ugukoresha vyoroshe, n'uguhindura amashusho, ivyo bikaba bituma iki gikoresho gikundwa n'abahinga bamwebamwe.



Mu bijanye n'ubuhinga, Arc ishingiye kuri Chromium, ariko iguma ari porogarame y'umuntu ku giti ciwe. Nta buryo buciye mu muco ikoresha mubijanye no gukorakoranya amakuru, kandi ingingo ngenderwako zayo z'ubuzima bw'ibanga ziguma zidatomoye, cane cane iyo bije ku bijanye n'ugupima amakuru n'uguhuza amakuru mu gicu. Bikwiye rero kwirindwa mu buryo bw'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none.



![Image](assets/fr/114.webp)





- **Polypane** :



[Polypane](https://polypane.app/) igenewe cane cane abahinguzi ba front-end n'abahinguzi ba UX. Igikorwa cayo nyamukuru ni ugushira ahabona icarimwe ingero nyinshi z'urubuga rumwe ku ngano zitandukanye z'imboneshamashusho, kugira ngo igerageze inyifato ya *responsive* ya interface mu gihe nyaco. Itanga kandi ibikoresho vya accessibility, ibikoresho vyo kugenzura HTML/CSS, ibikoresho vy'ugupima amabara n'ibipimo vy'imikorere.



Polypane ni mucukumbuzi y'umuntu, irihishwa, ishingiye kuri Chromium, ivyo bikaba bituma ari nziza mugukoreshwa kinyamwuga rimwe na rimwe. Ntibereye gukoreshwa urondera buri musi, kandi amategeko yayo yerekeye ubuzima bw'ibanga arahuye n'ama porogarame y'ubucuruzi, nta nakimwe cizewe.



![Image](assets/fr/116.webp)



### Mucukumbuzi zishingiye kuri Gecko



#### Mozila Firefox



[Firefox](https://www.mozilla.org/firefox/new/) ni mucukumbuzi izwi cane ikoresha moteri y'uguhindura Gecko. Yateguwe na Mozilla Foundation, Firefox iratandukanye  kubers ingingo ngenderwako zayo zitomoye z'ubuzima bw'ibanga: uburinzi bukajije bwo gukurikirana(tracking), uburyo buteye imbere bwo guhagarika ama cookies y'abandi nantu, tab zihariye, n'ugushiramwo inyongera bushobozi zuzuje ibisabwa vyerekeye umutekano.



Mozilla ni ishirahamwe ridaharanira inyungu, ivyo bikaba biyiha ubwigenge ku bijanye n'inyungu z'ubucuruzi gusa, naho yoba iguma yizigiye cane mu vy'amahera ubufatanye na Google. Iyi ya nyuma ahanini itanga amahera kuri Mozilla Foundation, ku mugaragaro kugira ngo moteri yayo y'ubushakashatsi igume ari yo ikoreshwa muri Firefox, gutyo igume ifise umugabane wayo kw'isoko. mu buryo butazwi, iyo nzira ituma Google iguma ifise uburyo bwo guhiganwa bugenzurwa: mu gushigikira Mozilla, Google iguma ifise abahiganwa bakeyi, ivyo bikaba bigabanya ibirego vyo gukoresha nabi ikibanza c'ubukuru kandi bikagabanya ingorane zo guhanwa n'amategeko.



![Image](assets/fr/117.webp)



Firefox ni mucukumbuzi ya open source, ikwiragizwa hakurikijwe MPL (*Mozilla Public License*). Kode yayo ni ubuntu rwose, irashobora guhindurwa kandi igasubira gukwiragizwa, kandi igizwe n'umusada w'abandi bantu bo hanze batanga.



Firefox iguma ari ikigereranyo c'umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga, naho nyene isigaye inyuma gatoyi ya mucukumbuzi zikoresha Blink mu bijanye n'ibikorwa bimwe bimwe. Ishobora kuba mucukumbuzi nziza cane, igihe cose itunganijwe neza.



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/firefox-11814cec-3415-4ed9-a06e-f6fda5c9510f
#### Mucukumbuzi ya Tor



[Mucukumbuzi yaTor](https://www.torproject.org/download/) ni mucukumbuzi Ishingiye kuri Firefox ESR. Ni kimwe mu nyishu zikomeye cane zo kutamenyekana kuri interineti. Ihindura inzira y'uruja n'uruza biciye ku muhora wa Tor, gutyo ikabuza isano ryose ryoba hagati y'uwukoresha n'aho urubuga ruja.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/tor-browser-a847e83c-31ef-4439-9eac-742b255129bb

Ikibi ni ukugabanya cane ubushobozi (high latency) n'uguhuza n'imbuga zimwe zimwe. Tor Browser ni nziza cane ku bikorwa vy'amabanga akomeye (itangazamakuru, ubukangurambaga...), ariko ntibereye cane gukoreshwa mu buryo busanzwe bwa misi yose.



![Image](assets/fr/118.webp)



#### Mucukumbuzi ya Mullvad


[Mucukumbuzi ya Mullvad](https://mullvad.net/en/browser) ni icamwa c'ubufatanye hagati ya Tor Foundation na Mullvad VPN. Ishingiye kuri mucukumbuzi ya Tor, iyo ubwyo ikaba ikomoka kuri Firefox ESR. Mullvad Browser yakozwe kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gushika kukugira ubuzima bwiwe bwibanga. Ku bisanzwe, harimwo uburinzi buteye imbere kuri fingerprinting (ibimenyetso vy'intoke), inkurikizi(trackers) n'inyandiko z'abandi.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-browser-a16c13d6-8bf9-4cb5-9aa0-85411a9cda0e

Ifise vyinshi mu bijanye n'umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga bitangwa na Tor Browser, hariho itandukaniro rimwe: ntihindura inzira y'uruja n'uruza biciye ku rubuga rwa Tor. Kugira ngo wirinde gusohoka kwa aderese IP, ushobora kuyikoresha hamwe na VPN (vyiza cane, Mullvad VPN).


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

Mullvad Browser ni umuti mwiza cane nimba uhangayikishijwe n'ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe, waba uri uwutangura canke uwubizobereyemwo.



![Image](assets/fr/119.webp)



#### Librewolf



[LibreWolf](https://librewolf.net/) ni mucukumbuzi ishingiye kuri Firefox yagenewe gutanga urugero rwo hejuru rw'ubuzima bw'ibanga. Ikuraho ibintu vyose bishobora guhungabanya ubuzima bw'ibanga, nka telemetry, gukorana na serivisi za Mozilla be n'iza Pocket.



Ku bisanzwe, LibreWolf ikoresha imiterere y'umutekano ya Firefox (nk'uburyo bwo kurinda bwisumbuye ibijanye no gukurikiranwa bukomeye) kandi igahagarika ubufasha bwa DRM. Uwo mugambi wose ni open source, ushingiye ku muryango wagutse, kandi ntushingiye ku mahera iyo ari yo yose ava mu bigo vyigenga. Ndagusaba nimba uriko urarondera Firefox "ikomeye", iguha ububasha bwinshi ku makuru yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/115.webp)



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/librewolf-1783e9dc-9d41-4449-a3cf-ed116849057c

#### Mucukumbuzi ya Zen


[Zen Browser](https://zen-browser.app/) ni mucukumbuzi y'ubuntu kandi yuguruye ishingiye kuri Firefox (moteri ya Gecko), yatangujwe mu 2024. Intumbero yayo ni ugutanga ubuhinga bwo kurondeza bugezweko, buteye igomwe, bushobora guhindurwa cane kandi hejuru ya vyose bushingiye ku buzima bw'ibanga, bidasavye kwisunga Chromium.


Zen igaragara kubera uburyo bwayo bukomeye bwo gukoresha interface n'ubushobozi bwo kuyikoresha, ahanini yisunze mucukumbuzi ya Arc, ariko ikabohorwa kuri yo kubera kamere yayo y'isoko yuguruye na moteri ya Gecko. Birimwo :



- Interface y'ibintu bikeyi y'ubatse mubice, ifise umurongo uhagaze w'amatab, ivyerekanwa bigabuye, na sisiteme ya *workspace* YO gushiramwo imigwi y'ibice hakurikijwe umugambi;
- Uburyo bw'ibigereranyo vya interface bishobora guhindurwa (*Zen Mods*) bishobora gukoreshwa mu guhindura cane ukuntu mucukumbuzi isa;
- Umurimo w'umwimerere witwa *Glance*, wugurura ihuza mw'idirisha ry'igihe gito riremurutse, wirinda uruja n'uruza rw'ama tab...


Zen kandi irashigikira inyongera bushobozi za Firefox, hamwe n'uguhuza biciye kuri konti ya Mozilla.


Ku bijanye n'umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga, Zen irafise uburinzi buhagarika trackers z'abandi. Mucukumbuzi ubwayo nta makuru yegeranya, kandi yemerera ko telemetry ya Mozilla idakora. Ica kandi ihita yanka ivyemezo vya SSL vya kera canke bitajanye n'amategeko.


Zen Browser ni uburyo bubereye nimba uriko urarondera ahantu ho gukoresha Gecko ku buntu, harimwo ubuhinga bushasha, hatagiramwo ibintu vyinshi kandi bubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/zen-browser-f1afc500-1933-409a-a2b7-b6c1c43ec285

### Mucukumbuzi ishingiye kuri WebKit 


#### Safari


Mucukumbuzi nyamukuru ikoresha moteri yo guhindura WebKit (itari Fork nka Blink) ni Safari. [Safari](https://www.apple.com/safari/) ni mucukumbuzi ya Apple yihariye kuri macOS. Itanga ubufatanye bwiza cane n'ikibanza ca Apple, ikora neza cane, ubu ikaba irimwo uburinzi bukomeye bwo guhagarika gukurikiranwa na fingerprinting.


Ariko Safari iguma yugaye, igarukira kuri macOS kubera verisiyo yayo y'ibiro, kandi ikorera mw'isi y'ibikoresho vya Apple. Naho Apple ifise politike ikomeye y'ubuzima bw'ibanga, n'uburyo bwayo bwo gukora ubucuruzi bushingiye ahanini ku kudandaza ibikoresho vy'ubuhinga bwa none aho gushingira ku kwamamaza, biraguma bitamenyekana ku bijanye n'imigenzo imwe imwe y'indani.


Aha, turiko twibanda ku bikoresho vyo ku biro, ariko birahambaye kumenya ko kuri iOS, Apple isaba ko mucukumbuzi zose zikoresha moteri y'uguhindura ya WebKit (ikintu gishobora guhinduka vuba, ariko, kubera amategeko amwamwe y'i Buraya). Ivyo bisigura ko mucukumbuzi nka Chrome, Firefox canke Brave zitegerezwa, kuri iOS, gutanga porogarame ishingiye kuri WebKit, atari kuri moteri yabo isanzwe yo guhindura.



![Image](assets/fr/120.webp)



#### Orion



Ubundi buryo bwiza bworoshe cane busa na Safari ni [Orion](https://kagi.com/orion/), mucukumbuzi y'ubuhinga bwa none yagenewe gusa ikibanza ca Apple, kandi na yo ishingiye kuri WebKit. Intumbero yayo ni ugutanga uburyo bwihuta, buremurutsebbb v kandi bubaha cane ubuzima bw'ibanga, ataco buhinduye ku bintu biteye imbere.



Orion itandukanye na Safari mu buryo bwinshi bw'ubuhinga:




- Ifata politike ikomeye y'ubuhinga bwa zero telemetry: nta makuru yegeranywa canke arungikwa ku buryo busanzwe, harimwo n'igihe co gushiramwo ubwa mbere;
- Harimwo igikoresho co kubuza kwamamaza n'ugukurikirana gisanzwe kirimwo ku buryo busanzwe, kigereranywa mu bushobozi na *uBlock Origin* mu buryo bwinshi;
- Ishigikira mu buryo bw'umwimerere gushiramwo no gukoresha inyongera bushobozi za Chrome na Firefox mu buryo bw'umwimerere kuri macOS;
- Ibikoresho vy'ingirakamaro birimwo uburyo bwa *Focus*(Interface-free navigation), uburyo bw'inguvu nke n'ugutunganya tab zihagaze.



Orion yose yakozwe n'umugwi wa Kagi (uzwi cane kubera moteri yo ukurondera yabo itagira amatangazo). Iterambere ryayo riterwa inkunga n'abayikoresha gusa biciye ku nzira ya *Orion+*, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kuronka inyungu zitari nke.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/orion-browser-a5f225d4-946f-425a-8d8e-3a3ec0174a76
### Mucukumbuzi zitagira moteri zo guhindura



bwa nyuma, ndashaka gusozera iyi nsiguro n'ubundi buryo butazwi cane kandi bwo kuruhande: ubuhinga bwo gukoresha amajambo, ubuzwi cane muri bwo ni [Mucukumbuzi ya Lynx](https://lynx.invisible-island.net/).



Lynx ni urubuga rwa kera cane rukiriho (1992). Ikora gusa mu buryo bw'inyandiko kandi ikoreshwa ukwonyene muri terminal, ata interface y'igicapo. mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, Lynx ntishigikira JavaScript, CSS canke amashusho, ivyo bikaba bikuraho ugushitsa kwa kode yose ikora kuri paji z'urubuga. Isobanura gusa kode ya HTML mbisi, ika zihindura nk'inyandiko itunganijwe.



Ubu buryo bworoheje buyigira imwe muri mucukumbuzi zitekanye cane: nta nyandiko mbi ishobora gukora, nta kwamamaza kwoza mwo ngo kugaragazwe, kandi nta makuru ashobora gusohoka biciye ku buryo bwa none (canvas fingerprinting, gukurikirana kwa JavaScript, n'ibindi) bishoboka.



![Image](assets/fr/121.webp)



Ubu buryo bigaragara ko bufise aho bugarukira: ukubura kwo guhindura ibicapo n'amashusho, ukudashobora gukoresha imbuga nyinshi zo muri iki gihe (vyinshi muri vyo usanga bikoresha JavaScript) n'ubuhinga busanzwe bugenewe abakoresha bazi utuntu n'utundi.



Lynx irashobora kuba iryoshe mu bihe bimwe bimwe vyihariye:




- Gusuzuma amapaji y'urubuga ya HTML atagiramwo JavaScript canke CSS;
- Kurondeza mu bibanza vyoroheje;
- Kurondeza mu bibanza bitekanye cane;
- Kurondeza ku muhora ugenda buhoro cane canke udashikamye;
- Ivy'ukwikoresha canke scraping.



### Ni iyihe mucukumbuzi wohitamwo?



Ku bakoresha bashira imbere umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga ku buryo busanzwe, batabwirizwa guhindura n'amaboko ibintu vyinshi mu miterere, kandi barondera mucukumbuzi y'ibikorwa vya rusangi ku musi ku musi, amahitamwo meza cane mu vyiyumviro vyanje ni LibreWolf na Mullvad Browser. Mu rwego rumwe, nimba udafise ikibazo co gukoresha urufatiro rwa Chromium (naho hari ingorane zirimwo na firozofiya itandukanye), woshobora kandi kwiyumvira Brave. Nk'uko mubibona, ndakunda moteri y'uguhindura Gecko kubera imvo nyinshi, naho ubu iri inyuma ya Blink mu bijanye n'ubushobozi.



Firefox nayo ni uburyo bwiza cane nka mucukumbuzi y'ibikorwa rusangi rusangi, igihe cose itunganijwe neza kugira ngo yongere ubuzima bw'ibanga.



Ku rugero rwo hejuru rwo kutamenyekana, ku giciro co kugabanya ubushobozi, Tor Browser iguma ari umuti mwiza.



Chrome, naho izwi cane, ntishobora kwemerwa nk'igice c'uburyo bwo guharanira ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none, kuko Google ishira inyungu zayo z'ubucuruzi hejuru y'ukurinda ubuzima bw'ibanga. Ni co gituma ntabagira inama yo kuyikoresha.



Muri iki gihe, uguhitamwo kwawe mucukumbuzi kurafise uruhara runini mu mutekano wawe wo kuri interineti no mu buzima bw'ibanga bwawe. Rero fata umwanya wo kumenya iyo ihuye cane n'ubuzima bwawe be n'ivyo ushira imbere.



Ehe incamake yihuta kugira ngo igufashe guhitamwo (ariko rero, wibuke ko iki kigereranyo gishobora kuba carahindutse kuva igihe iki cigwa SCU202 candikwa, kandi isuzuma rya interface n'ibiyiranga ni ikibazo c'ugukenguruka kw'umuntu ku giti ciwe):



| Mucukumbuzi     | Ubuzima bw'ibanga | Umuvuduko | Ibiyigize | interface | Open source | Uburyo bw'ibikoreshoion |
| --------------- | ----------------- | --------- | --------- | --------- | ----------- | ----------------------- |
| Google Chrome   | 🔴               | 🟢        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🔴         | 🔴                      |
| Brave           | 🟡               | 🟢        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🟢         | 🟡                      |
| Vivaldi         | 🟡               | 🟢        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🔴         | 🟡                      |
| Opera           | 🔴               | 🟢        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🔴         | 🔴                      |
| Arc             | 🔴               | 🟢        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🔴         | 🟡                      |
| Polypane        | 🟡               | 🟡        | 🟢       | 🟡        | 🔴         | 🔴                      |
| Mozilla Firefox | 🟡               | 🟡        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🟢         | 🟡                      |
| Tor Browser     | 🟢               | 🔴        | 🟢       | 🟡        | 🟢         | 🔴                      |
| Mullvad Browser | 🟢               | 🟡        | 🟢       | 🟡        | 🟢         | 🟡                      |
| Safari          | 🟡               | 🟢        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🔴         | 🟡                      |
| Lynx            | 🟢               | 🟢        | 🔴       | 🔴        | 🟢         | 🟢                      |
| LibreWolf       | 🟢               | 🟡        | 🟢       | 🟡        | 🟢         | 🟡                      |
| Orion           | 🟡               | 🟢        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🔴         | 🟢                      |
| Zen Browser     | 🟢               | 🟡        | 🟢       | 🟢        | 🟢         | 🟡                      |

Mu gice gikurikira, turaza kuraba uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha urubuga ata nkomanzi, mu gihe ugabanya ukuntu ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe buja ahagaragara.



## Imigenzo myiza mu gukoresha urubuga


<chapterId>ded47ada-0569-4e63-b668-0da042e691d5</chapterId>



Mu gice giheruka, twaciye mw'ido n'ido rya mucukumbuzi nyamukuru ziriko ubu, hamwe n'ivyiza n'ibibi vyazo mu bijanye n'umutekano n'ubuzima bw'ibanga.



Ariko rero, mbere naho mucukumbuzi yoba ifise umutekano mwinshi cane ntibihagije: ingene uyikoresha biguma ari ngirakamaro mu kurinda umutekano wawe w'ubuhinga bwa none. Muri iki gice, turaraba mu buryo bwimbitse imigenzo myiza yo kugabanya ingorane zijanye n'ugukoresha urubuga ku musi ku musi.



### Kwama ushira kugihe mucukumbuzi yawe



Mucukumbuzi ni kimwe mu bihimba vya porogarame bigaragara cane muri sisiteme y'inyabwonko. mu buryo butandukanye n'izindi porogarame nyinshi, ikora ibintu bihinduka biva kuri interineti mu gihe nyaco, ivyo bikaba ari ibintu bidashobora kwizigirwa. Iyo urubuga rwamaze kuguruka, mucukumbuzi ishitsa kode iri kure, iyo kode ikaba ikorana na sisiteme yawe biciye kuri moteri y'uguhindura.



Ubwo budahangagwa bw'ubuhinga, hamwe na attack surface yagutse cane, bituma mucukumbuzi iza kumwanya wambere muvyo aba tera baza barondera.
