Amakosa akomeye mu ma moteri yo guhindura (nka Blink canke Gecko), amasomero y'isesengura ry'amashusho canke ubutunganyirizo bw'uburyo bwa memory bushobora gutuma haba ibitero vyitwa "zero-click" (ronderera gusa urubuga rwa booby-trapped maze inyabwonko yawe ice ihungabana), canke ibitero vya "zero-day" (integenke zitazwi na banyeneyo).



Kugira ngo ivyo bibazo bigabanuke, banyene mucukumbuzi basohorora vya hato na hato, kenshi buri ndwi, ibintu bishasha bikosora izo ntege nke iyo zimaze kumenyekana. Izo patches nizigarukira kuri interface canke ku gutera imbere kw'imikoreshereze: birazibira n'inzira ziriho z'anditswe zoba imvo y'igitero


![Image](assets/fr/129.webp)



Ni ngombwa rero:




- kwemerera mucukumbuzi yawe kw'ishira kugihe kandi ukama usuzuma n'amaboko ubudasiba ko ata bishasha vyabonetse;
- canke, nimba ukoresha verisiyo ikoreshwa n'amaboko (nk'akarorero biciye kuri `apt`, `flatpak` canke `snap` kuri Linux), ujye uhindura ubudasiba sisiteme yose biciye ku butunganirizo bw'a mapaki.



Kugira ngo usuzume n'amaboko verisiyo maze utangure gushira kugihe:




- muri Firefox: `Menu > Settings > Firefox Updates`;
- umurongo w'amabwirizwa muri Linux, (amapaki ya `apt`):



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade firefox
```



Gushira kugihe mucukumbuzi yawe, porogarame yawe na sisiteme yawe ni intambwe ya mbere nyayo ushobora gutera mu bijanye n'umutekano wo kuri interineti.



### Koresha amajambo y'ibanga akomeye kandi yihariye



Ku bijanye n'umutekano w'urubuga, rimwe mu makosa asanzwe (kandi ateye akaga) ni ugusubira gukoresha amajambo y'ibanga ku mbuga nyinshi. Ivyo bitera ingaruka ziteye akaga: iyo serivisi imwe gusa ihungabanijwe (ugusohoka kw'amakuru, phishing, igitero c'inguvu z'agahomerabunwa...), uwutera ashobora rero kugerageza iryo jambo ry'ibanga nyene ku zindi mbuga, akaronka uburenganzira bwo gushika ku makonti ahambaye nk'ivyo ukoresha kuri imeyiri yawe, amakonti ya banki canke ahantu ukora.



Ingingo ya mbere ku bijanye n'amajambo y'ibanga ni ukudasubira kuyakoresha. Konti yose yo kuri interineti ikwiye kurindwa n'ijambo ry'ibanga ry'umwihariko, ritandukanye rwose n'izindi. Kugira ijambo ry'ibanga ry'umwihariko kuri konti imwe imwe biratandukanya ibitero bishobora gutera kandi bikagabanya ingaruka zavyo.



Nk'akarorero, niwakoresha ijambo ry'ibanga rimwe ku rubuga rw'imikino ya videwo no kuri konti yawe ya imeyiri, kandi iryo jambo ry'ibanga rikagira ingorane biciye ku rubuga rw'ububeshi (phishing) ruhuye n'urubuga rw'inkino, uwoba ategura kugutera yoshobora rero kwinjira muri konti yawe ya imeyiri bitamugoye maze akagenzura izindi konti zawe zose zo kuri interineti.



Ingingo ngenderwako ya kabiri ihambaye ni ukugira ijambo ry'ibanga rikomeye. ijambo ry'ibanga rifatwa nk'irikomeye iyo rigoye gukoresha inguvu ngo urimenye(brute force), ni ukuvuga kurironka mu kugerageza no gukosa. Ivyo bisigura ko amajambo y'ibanga yawe akwiye kuba agizwe n'indome zivangitanije uko bishoboka kwose, maremare, kandi arimwo indome zitandukanye (indome nto, indome nini, ibiharuro n'ibimenyetso).



Gushira mu ngiro izo ngingo ngenderwako zibiri z'umutekano w'ijambo ry'ibanga (ubudasa n'inkomezi) birashobora kugorana ku musi ku musi, kuko bidashoboka gufata mu mutwe ijambo ry'ibanga ry'umwihariko, ry'indome zivangitiranije kandi rikomeye ry'amakonti yacu yose. Aho niho ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga bwinjira mukibuga.



Igikoresho co gucungera amajambo y'ibanga kiratanga amajambo y'ibanga akomeye kandi kikabika mu buryo butekanye, ivyo bikaba bigufasha gushika ku makonti yawe yose yo kuri interineti ataco ukeneye gufata ku mutwe. Ukeneye kwibuka ijambo ry'ibanga rimwe gusa, ijambo ry'ibanga nyamukuru, riguha uburenganzira bwo gukoresha amajambo y'ibanga yawe yose abitswe m'ubutunganyirizo. Gukoresha ubutunganyirizo bw'amajambo y'ibanga birakomeza umutekano wawe wo kuri interineti, kuko bibuza gusubira gukoresha amajambo y'ibanga amwe kandi bukaguha amajambo y'ibanga atagira aho asa asaniye.



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

Gukoresha ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga bitanga ivyiza vyinshi: birorosha ubuzima bwawe bwa misi yose mu gukuraho ivy'ugufata mu mutwe amajambo y'ibanga menshi, kandi bikagabanya intege nke nyamukuru yo kwemeza uwinjira: abakoresha ubwabo.



Ku bijanye no kwemeza uwinjira, gukoresha ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga bitegerezwa kwuzuzwa n'umuti w'ivyemezo bibiri (2FA), kugira ngo ukoreshwe ku makonti yose awushigikira. Ivyiza ni uko wokoresha porogarame y'ihariye, canke mbere n'ikiruta, igikoresho gifadika nka Yubikey.



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/authy-a76ab26b-71b0-473c-aa7c-c49153705eb7

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/trezor-u2f-fido2-41d2939e-69b9-4c2e-b836-a2b09de58051

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/ledger-fido-u2f-59f8105b-a0cc-4aff-bc56-048a6a42d39f

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/security-key-61438267-74db-4f1a-87e4-97c8e673533e

### Gukoresha VPN



VPN (*Virtual Private Network*) ni igikoresho gikora inzira inyegeza uruja n'uruza rw'umuhora hagati y'igikoresho cawe na seriveri y'umuhuza. Uwo murongo ukora nk'irembo, rihindukiza amakuru yose ukoresha kuri interineti. Ivyo bituma abaguha serivisi za interinet ISP (Internet Service Provider) babona gusa amakuru anyegeje aja kuri VPN, kandi imbuga ugenderera zibona gusa aderese IP ya server ya VPN, atari iyawe.



Hariho ivyiza vyinshi vyo gukoresha VPN. Irinda ukuntu ukoresha amakuru yawe ku mbuga zidatekanye (nk'akarorero, Wi-Fi ya rusangi ku bibuga vy'indege canke mu mahoteri), mu kubuza abandi bantu gufata amakuru yawe. Ihisha kandi aderese IP yawe nyayo, bishobora kuba ngirakamaro mu kwirinda gukurikiranwa, canke kwigana uruja n'uruza ruva mu kindi gihugu. Ivya nyuma ariko bitari bike, VPN ni igikoresho co gukingira ubugenzuzi. Mu turere aho amakuru amwe namwe y'ugariwe kurugero rwa ISP, guhindura uruja n'uruza rwawe kuri server ya VPN iri mu gihugu kidayungurura bigufasha gusubira kuronka ku buntu uburenganzira bwo kugira ico ushitse ko.



![Image](assets/fr/128.webp)



Ku rundi ruhande, bitandukanye n'ivyo abantu benshi bemera, VPN ntitanga ukutamenyekana. Uwutanga VPN arazi aderese IP yawe nyayo, arashobora kwandika inzira zawe, kandi akaba umuntu agira gatatu yizigirwa. Ubashinga igikorwa cawe cose co kuri interineti. Iyo uwuguha VPN ari umunyaruyeri, afise inshingano zitegekanijwe n'amategeko canke afise ubujuju mu vy'ubuhinga, amakuru yawe arashobora gushirwa ahagaragara.



Ikindi, VPN nta n'uburinzi itanga kuri malware, gukurikirana JavaScript canke cookies z'abandi. Iyo winjiye muri konti yawe ya Google canke Facebook, ukoresha VPN ntibizobuza izo mbuga kukumenya neza. VPNs nazo nyene ntizicungera ibirimwo, kandi ntizizobuza urubuga rwa booby-trapped kugutera biciye ku ntegenke za mucukumbuzi.



Kandi, ibikoresho vya VPN ntibikwiye kwitiranywa n'umuhora wa Tor, ari wo muhora usanzagiye amakuru acaho anyegejwe kugira ngo wizere ko utamenyekana. Tor igenda buhoro, ariko irakomeye cane ku bijanye n'ugucungera kw'isi yose kuruta VPN.



VPN nziza ikwiye kugira politike itomoye yo kudakorakoranya amakuru, itanga ubuhinga bwa none (cane cane WireGuard), yemera gukoresha iyo serivisi ata mazina utanze kandi itanga urufatiro rw'ubuhinga rwa open source canke rwogenzurwa abantu bose. Ivyo ndabifise ku muzirikanyi, ndabagira inama y'ibikoresho nka Mullvad canke IVPN.



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mozilla-vpn-f55903d4-aece-4d59-b193-2eb073e59b67

VPN zihambaye cane zikwiye kwirindwa. Uretse no kuba z'amamaza cane, ziguma ari serivisi z'ubucuruzi zigenzurirwa ahantu hamwe, akenshi zishingiye ku mategeko atarinzwe cane, kandi ntabwo zigaragaza neza ingene zikora.



### Gusukura amateka n'ama cookies



Urubuga rwose ugenderera rurandika amakuru y'ikiganiro yaho mu karere kawe ku nyabwonko yawe, ayo makuru akaba ari ubwoko bubiri nyamukuru: amateka y'ibironderwa n'ama cookies.



Amateka ni urutonde rw'amakuru rworoshe rugaragaza imbuga zose wa rondeye, n'itariki zazo, izina ryazo rimwe na rimwe n'igihe zagenderewe. Bituma vyoroha kuronka paji wari w'uguruye mbere. Ariko ku rundi ruhande, bigaragaza ivyo urondera vyose kuri interineti ku muntu wese afise uburenganzira bwo gushika ku kiganiro cawe (harimwo na porogarame mbi, canke incuti yawe ishaka kumenya vyinshi).



Ku rundi ruhande, ama cookies ni utudosiye dutoduto tubikwa na mucukumbuzi ku busabe bw'imbuga. akoreshwa mu kwibuka igihe cawe (nk'akarorero kuguma inzira y'urubuga yuguruye), kubika ivyo ukunda, canke gukurikirana inyifato yawe ku ntumbero yo gukora icegeranyo. Ama cookies amwe amwe arakora (ni ukuvuga ngo ni ngombwa kugira ngo urubuga rukore neza), mu gihe ayandi ari ay'abandi (ashirwaho n'amashirahamwe y'iyamamaza canke abakurikirana kuri paji zarondewe). Ivyo vya nyuma bishoboza gukurikirana urubuga rwose, rimwe na rimwe mu myaka, mu gukurikirana ingeso zawe zo kuronderaa kugira ngo habeho urutonde rw'ivyo kwamamaza.



Gusukura ubudasiba aya makuru yo mu karere ni uburyo bworoshe ariko bukora neza bwo kugabanya ugukurikiranwa no kuzigama ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe. Mucukumbuzi zitanga amahitamwo yo:




- gufuta aya makuru uvyikoreye  (mu miterere);
- gufuta aya makuru igihe cose wugaye mucukumbuzi, canke mu kiganiro kinaka (ndagusaba ko ukora ivyo);
- gutanguza ikiganiro c'igihe gito biciye ku buryo bwo kuronderera mu buryo bwibanga (ibindi kuri ivyo mu gice gikurikira).



Muri Firefox, nk'akarorero, urashobora gushiraho uburyo bwo gufuta bw'ikoresha biciye muri Settings > Privacy & Security.



Ariko rero, uzirikane ko gufuta ama cookies gusa bidahagije kugira ngo ubone ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe: hariho ubundi buryo buteye imbere bwo gukurikirana, nka fingerprinting (fingerprint yihariye ya mucukumbuzi yawe, ibikoresho vyawe, IP yawe, uko ukoresha...), bisaba izindi ngingo zo gukingira:




- Koresha mucukumbuzi itanga ubushobozi bwo guhangana na fingerprinting: Tor Browser na Mullvad Browser ni vyo vyiza kuri ivyo, ahandi ho, ubundi buryo bwiza cane ni LibreWolf, Brave canke Firefox ugaca uhindura ubukomeza ukabushira kuyindi ntambwe;
- Kudaha uburenganzira bukwiye canke guhagarika burundu JavaScript igihe cose bishoboka;
- Irinde inyongeranushobozi zidakenewe;
- Muri rusangi, nufate urutonde rusanzwe, rudahinduka, kugira ngo wisange kandi ugabanye amahirwe yo kumenyekana.



### Gutahura uko worondera mu buryo bw'ibanga



Uburyo bwo kurondera mu buryo bwibanga, buboneka muri mucukumbuzi zose zigezweko (Firefox, Chrome, Brave, Safari...), ntabwo ari igikoresha gituma utamenyekana, canke ngo kigukingire gukurikiranwa kuri interineti. Ubu buryo buragabanya gusa kwandika amakuru ku nyabwonko yawe mu gihe c'ikiganiro.



Mu majambo nyayo, iyo w'uguruye idirisha uriko urondera mu buryo bw'ibanga:




- amateka y'ivyo waronderye ntazobikwa aho hantu ku gikoresho cawe;
- ama cookies yashizweho mu gihe c'ikiganiro azoca afutwa igihe igihe idirisha rizoba ryugawe;
- amakuru y'ifomu (ibibanza vyuzuye, amajambo y'ibanga) ntazobikwa;
- dosiye z'igihe gito zihujwe na paji z'urubuga zizokurwaho inyuma yo gufungwa.



Ariko rero, ubu buryo ntibunyegeza igikorwa cawe kuri interineti: imbuga ugenderera ziguma zibona aderese IP yawe, zirashobora gukoresha ubuhinga bwa fingerprinting, kandi ISP yawe, canke umuntu wese ari ku muhora wawe wo mu karere, arashobora kubona imbuga ugenderera.



Ni ngombwa rero ko utagomba kwitiranya kurondera mu buryo bwibanga n'ukutamenyekana. Kugira ngo ukingire neza ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe bwo kuri interineti, ukeneye gukoresha ibikoresho vy'inyongera nka Tor canke VPN nziza, bivanye n'urugero rw'ibiguhangayikishije.



![Image](assets/fr/127.webp)



### Kumenya no kwirinda phishing na social engineering(ububeshi)



Phishing ni uburyo bwo guhenda abakoresha kugira ngo bashire ahagaragara amakuru y'agaciro ataco babiziko: amakuru yo kwinjira, inomero z'ikarata y'inguzanyo, amakode yo kwinjira, inyandiko z'ibanga. Iki kibazo ntigishingiye ku kibazo c'ikosa muvy'ubuhinga, ahubwo gishingiye ku guhenda abantu, gukoresha icizere cabo, uguhuzagurika canke ukubura ubwenge.



Akenshi, igitero gishingiye ku kwigana ukuntu urubuga rwemewe rusa (banki, serivisi z'ubutumwa, ubuyobozi, iduka ryo kuri interineti, n'ibindi) biciye ku rubuga rw'ikinyoma rufise URL yiyoberanije. Abakoresha bararonka ihuza ry'ububeshi biciye kuri imeyiri, SMS canke porogarame zo gutumatumanako, hanyuma rero mukwizera ko bariko barakorana n'urubuga nyarwo, bakinjiza amakuru yabo yo kwinjira.



Kugira ngo wirinde ivyo bitero igihe uriko urarondera kuri interineti, birahambaye ko ukurikiza ibintu bimwe bimwe vy'ishimikiro:





- **Sesangura URL**: abatera kenshi bakoresha aderesi zishaka gusa cane niz'umwimerere (nk'akarorero `micr0soft-support.com`, `paypal-verif.net`, n'ibindi). Hari n'abasubiriza indome zisa n'izo, bagakoresha indome za Unicode. Suzuma ko aderese ihuye neza na neza n'aho witeze kuja, atakintu giteye amkenga imbere canke inyuma ya URL.





- **Irinde amahuzu magufi**: serivisi nka `bit.ly` canke `t.co` birashobora gupfuka aderese ya nyuma. Niwaronka ihuza rigufi, ugire amakenga canke ukoreshe serivisi yo kwagura URL kugira ngo umenye aho ija.





- **Iyubare ubutumwa bukwibutsa**: igeragezwa rya phishing kenshi hakoreshwa amarangamutima akomeye (ivy'ihutigwa, ugutera ubwoba, agahembo, amatsiko...). Imeyiri ivuga ko konti yawe igiye guhagarikwa canke ko umuzigo udashobora gushika, birasanzwe ko ari ikintu giteye amakenga.





- **Ntukigere urungika amakuru y'agaciro biciye kw'ihuza waronse**: Ikigo cemewe ntikizokwigera kigusaba ijambo ry'ibanga, kode y'ukwemeza canke kopi ya karangamuntu yawe wafotoye biciye ku butumwa bwo kuri imeyiri canke SMS isanzwe.



Kandi ng'izi ingingo nkeyi zo kwirinda ushobora gushiramwo muri mucukumbuzi yawe kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zo gushikirwa na phishing:





- **Ushobora gushika ku mbuga zihambaye biciye kuri bookmarks zawe**:



Kuri service zihambaye (bijanye n'amabanki, ibijanye n'ikori, imeyiri, n'ibindi), no muri rusangi ku mbuga zose ukoresha ubudasiba, zigama URL yemewe muri bookmarks zawe kandi ntukigere ukoresha moteri y'ukurondera canke ihuza ryo hanze kugira ngo ushikeyo.



Woba wararonse ubutumwa kuri imeyiri buvuye ku biro vy'ikori burimwo ihuza? Nturifyondeko. Ahubwo, genda mu kibanza cawe bwite ukoresheje URL wabitse muri bookmarks zawe. Muri iki gihe, mucukumbuzi zose zigezweko ziratanga umurongo wa bookmarks ufise uburenganzira bwo gutunganya amahuzu yawe mu madosiye. Fata umwanya wo kubikora rimwe, usuzume neza URL n'icemezo ca SSL/TLS, uzoshobora kuronderera kurubuga ata nkomanzi.





- **Wubahirize imigenzo myiza yo kwemeza uwinjira**:



Ni ngombwa kandi gukurikiza imigenzo myiza yo kwemeza uwinjira kugira ngo ugabanye ingaruka zishobora guterwa na phishing. Amategeko abiri ahambaye cane ni ugukoresha amajambo y'ibanga yihariye kuri buri serivisi no gukoresha 2FA.



Reka dufate akarorero: iyo uwugutera ashoboye kuronka ijambo ry'ibanga rya konti yawe ya Steam, ariko ugakoresha ijambo ry'ibanga ritandukanye kuri buri konti yawe, ntazoshobora gushika ku bikorwa vy'agaciro nk'ivyo kuri imeyiri yawe canke banki. Kandi iyo wakoresheje ivyemezo bibiri mu kwimenyekanisha (2FA), rero n'aho woba ufise ijambo ry'ibanga, uwugutera ntazoshobora kwinjira, kuko atazoshobora gukoresha porogarame yawe ya TOTP (nka Authy, Google Authenticator...).



Uretse izo ngingo, gukoresha ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga bwiza nk'inyongera bushobozi ya mucukumbuzi na vyo nyene birashobora kugukingira imbuga z'ibinyoma. Muvy'ukuri kandi, nyinshi muri izo nyongera bushobozi zizobona URL iteye amakenga hanyuma zanke kwuzuza amakuru yawe, canke mbere zikumenyeshe, ivyo bizotuma udashobora gushikiriza amakuru yawe y'ukwinjira ataco wiyumviriye.





- **Suzuma ivyemezo vya SSL/TLS**:



igicapo c'igufuri kiri mu murongo wa aderese kigaragaza ko hariho uguhuza canke inzira inyegeje, ariko ntivyemeza ko urubuga rwemewe. Fyondako kugira ngo usuzume icemezo (ishirahamwe, urwego(domain), ubuyobozi bw'icemezo). ibi birashobora kugufasha nimba ufise amakenga ku bijanye na URL y'urubuga.



Phishing ikora gusa iyo ukanda ningoga cane. Kuri buri huza ryose uronka, nugire akamenyero ko kugenzura mu buryo butunganye, mbere no ku rubuga usanzwe uzi. Gufata umwanya wawe wo gusuzuma no kugenzura neza ama URL, mbere n'ayo umenyereye, ni kimwe mu bintu vyiza vyo kwikingira ubwo bwoko bw'igitero.



### Suzuma inyongera bushobozi (extensions) zashizweho



Inyongera bushobozi za mucukumbuzi ni ibice vyongerako ibintu (guhagarika amatangazo, guhindura ururimi, gufata amajambo, gucunga ijambo ry'ibanga, Bitcoin Wallets, n'ibindi). Bikora ubwonyene atakindi bisavye mu kibanza ca mucukumbuzi yawe kandi birashobora gushika ku mapaji yose canke igice cayo urondererako. Ivyo bituma zigira ububasha, ariko kandi zishobora gutera akaga.



Inyongera bushobozi mbi canke yahungabanijwe ushobora gufata amakuru yawe bwite, gusoma ibirimwo, gushiramwo kode kuri paji z'urubuga canke mbere gukora JavaScript mu nyuma. Hariho ama extensions aguma afise uburenganzira bwo Kwugurura ama tab canke amateka y'ivyo warondera muri kahise, birenze kure y'ibikenewe kugira ngo zikore.



Kugira ngo ugabanye ivyo bibazo, shiramwo gusa inyongera bushobozi ziva ku masoko yemewe (Mozilla Add-ons), wame usuzuma uruhusha rusabwa, kandi ugumize igitigiri cazo ku rugero rutoyi cane. Sukura ama extensions utagikoresha, kandi wiyubare ama clones yazo.



Gusuzuma ubudasiba ama extensions yawe ni ikintu gihambaye mu kubungabunga mucukumbuzi yawe.



### Gutandukanya uko ukoresha urubuga



Kugabura ibikorwa ni umugenzo uhambaye wo kugabanya urugero rw'ivyago vy'uko urubuga rwo hungabanywa. Bigizwe n'ugutandukanya mu buryo bw'ubuhinga imikoreshereze yawe itandukanye ya interineti: Kurondera ku giti cawe, ku bijanye n'umwuga, mw'ibanga canke ivy'amabanga akomeye.



Intumbero iroroshe: gukingira ikintu gifitaniye isano n'igikorwa kinaka (nk'ugusohoka kwa cookies, igitero canke ubusuma bw'ibiganiro) ibintu vyo humanya ikibanza cawe cose c'ubuhinga bwa none. Uburyo bwinshi burashobora gukoreshwa, bwonyene canke bufatanye n'ibindi:





- **Koresha mucukumbuzi nyinshi zitandukanye**: nk'akarorero, Firefox ku bikorwa vy'umuntu ku giti ciwe, Tor canke Mullvad ku bikorwa bihambaye, na Chromium ku bikorwa vy'umwuga. Buri mucukumbuzi ikoresha ububiko bwayo bwite, butandukanya rwose cookies, ibiganiro na extensions. Ivyo kandi biragufasha guhindura imiterere ya mucukumbuzi bivanye n'ivyo uyikoresha.





- **Rema imirongo y'ibikorwa(profiles) myinshi muri mucukumbuzi imwe**: mucukumbuzi zimwe zimwe ziraguha uburenganzira bwo kurema imirongo y'ibikorwa yigenga, imwe yose ifise amateka yayo, ibiganiro, extensions n'imiterere. Ivyo ni umuti udakomeye cane nko gukoresha mucukumbuzi nyinshi zitandukanye, ariko naho ari uko nta kintu kinini bimaze.





- **Koresha containers zubakiye muri mucukumbuzi**: Firefox itanga extension ya [Containers z'amakonti menshi](https://addons.mozilla.org/en-US/firefox/addon/multi-account-containers/), igufasha kw'ugurura amatab atandukanye, imwe yose ifise inzira yayo yo kwinjiramwo na cookies. Ushobora kandi gushiramwo ako kanya imbuga zimwe zimwe muri container kanaka, kugira ngo zigume zitandukanye igihe cose zuguruwe.



![Image](assets/fr/126.webp)





- **Koresha ikibanza ca sisiteme cihariye**: Ku bikorwa vy'agaciro cane, ushobora kandi gukoresha mucukumbuzi yawe mu mashini mpimbano canke muri container ya Docker, kugira ngo bigume bitandukanye rwose n'ikibanza cawe nyamukuru.



### Kugabanya impusha zihabwa imbuga



Mucukumbuzi zigezweko muri iki gihe bituma imbuga zishobora gusaba gukoresha uburyo bw'igikoresho cawe buhambaye, nk'ivyo gufata amasanamu, mikoro, aho umuntu ari canke imenyekanisha rya sisiteme. Ivyo bikoresho ni ngirakamaro kuri porogarame zimwe zimwe (videoconference, amakarata akora...), ariko kandi birafungura umuryango wo gukoresha nabi ubwo buryo iyo bigenzurwa nabi.



Iyo urubuga rugusavye gukoresha kimwe muri ivyo bintu, mucukumbuzi irakwereka ubwo busabe utegerezwa kwemera. Ariko rero, niwavyemera rimwe gusa utabizi, urwo ruhusha rushobora kuguma rukora ubudasiba mu gihe cose uzogenderera uru rubuga muri kazoza. Ivyo bisigura nk'akarorero ko urubuga rushobora kwongera gukoresha mikoro yawe canke kamera yawe ataco rukubajije, nimba utakuyeho ubwo burenganzira n'amaboko.



Kugira ngo wongere umutekano:




- Tanga nga uburenganzira gusa igihe bikenewe cane kubw'ikintu cemewe;
- Hitamwo uburyo bwo "kwemera rimwe" nimba buhari;
- Gukuraho n'amaboko uruhusha rwatanzwe biciye mu miterere ya mucukumbuzi ivyo wame ubikora.



![Image](assets/fr/125.webp)



### Suzuma inzira zirinzwe (HTTPS)



Igihe cose wohereje amakuru yawe bwite, ay'ibanga canke y'ubutunzi ku rubuga, yaba ijambo ry'ibanga, inomero y'ikarata y'inguzanyo canke ifomu isanzwe yo kw'iyandikisha, birahambaye ko ubona neza ko inzira hagati ya mucukumbuzi yawe n'urubuga inyegejwe.



Ivyo ni vyo vy'ukuri uruhara rwa HTTPS (*HyperText Transfer Protocol Secure*). Iri tegeko rishingiye ku buryo bwo kunyegeza amakuru bwa TLS (*Transport Layer Security*), butuma habaho:




- Kunyegeza amakuru ahanahanwa (nta n'umwe ashobora kuyasoma canke kuyahindura mu gihe ariko aragenda);
- kugenzura ukuri kwa server ya kure biciye ku cemezo c'ubuhinga bwa none ;
- gukingira ibitero vy'umuntu ari hagati, man-in-the-middle(MITM), bikunze kuboneka ku mihora rusangi canke imihora yahungabanijwe.



Mu majambo nyayo, urubuga rukoresha HTTPS rwerekanwa n'akagufuri kugaye mumurongo wa aderese muri mucukumbuzi yawe, akenshi hejuru ibubafu bwa interface. Gufyonda kuri aka kagufuri vyerekana amakuru yerekeye icemeza ca TLS c'urubuga (Abatanza ico cemezo, itariki y'kizohererako, n'ibindi). Aderese y'urubuga nayo nyene itanguzwa na `https://`.



![Image](assets/fr/124.webp)



Ku rundi ruhande, iyo urubuga rugikoresha HTTP (ata "S"), iyo nzira ntiba inyegejwe. Amakuru yose yinjijwe arashobora rero gufatwa n'inkozi y'ikibi ari hagati yawe n'urubuga: abakozi b'umuhora, uwutanga uburenganzira bwo kuja kumuhora, ikibanza ca Wi-Fi gifise umutego wa booby (booby-trapped Wi-Fi hotspot), porogarame mbi yo mu karere, n'ibindi.



Mu vy'ukuri, ukwiye kwama usuzuma ayo makuru n'amaboko imbere y'uko winjiza amakuru ku rubuga. Mu bikorwa, mucukumbuzi nyinshi zigezweko zica zishirako ikimenyetso kagaragaza imbuga za HTTP nk'izidatekanye. Ushobora kandi gukoresha uburyo bwo guhatira gukoresha itegeko rya HTTPS mu miterere y'umutekano wa mucukumbuzi yawe, bikagufasha guhagarika imbuga zitarishigikiye.



Nkako, ni imbuga nke cane muri iki gihe zishobora gushikirwa biciye kuri HTTP gusa. Iryo tegeko ahanini ririko rirahebwa kubera HTTPS, atari kubera imvo zigaragara z'umutekano gusa, ariko kandi kubera ko rihabwa ibihano na moteri z'ukurondera kandi rigashirwa ko ikimenyetso ko rishobora gutera akaga na mucukumbuzi zigezweko, ivyo bikaba bidatuma rigirigwa icizere n'aba rondera.



### Guhitamwo moteri y'ukurondera



Nk'uko twamaze kubibona, birahambaye gutandukanya ibi bintu bibiri bikunda gutera amadidane: mucukumbuzi, ariyo porogarame ishizwe mu nyabwonko yawe (nka Firefox canke Brave) kandi ikoreshwa mu kwerekana amapaji y'urubuga, na moteri y'ukurondera, ariyo serivisi yo kuri interineti (nka Google) ariyo urungika ubusabe kugirango uronke inyishu. Ibi bintu bibiri birigenga, naho nyene mucukumbuzi akenshi zishiramwo moteri imwe ku buryo busanzwe.



![Image](assets/fr/122.webp)



Moteri y'ukurondera ukoresha mu kurondera iragira ico ikoze ata guca ku ruhande ku buzima bwawe bw'ibanga. Nkako, ivyo urondera vyose bishobora kuba :




- vyo fatanywa na aderese IP yawe nimba udakoresha Tor canke VPN ;
- bihuye ivyo winjirirako be n'ijambo ry'ibanga ryawe nimba uri kuri konti ;
- bibitswe kandi bigasuzumwa kugira ngo hakorwe urutonde rw'inyifato;
- bikoreshwa mu kwamamaza canke bikagurishwa ku bandi bantu.



Rero moteri nka Google itanga inyishu zihuta kandi zibereye (naho [inyigisho zimwe zimwe zivuga](https://consumerwatchdog.org/in-the-news/Wallet-hub-google-quality-issues-part-of-an-intentional-strategy/) ko Google iriko irasubira inyuma mukuba nziza no gukora kinyamwuga), kukiguzi co kugenzura ubusabe bwawe. Bing (Microsoft) na Yahoo zikorera mw'uwo murongo wo gukoranya ibikorwa vyawe vyo kuri interineti kugira ngo zigaburire imihora yabo yo kwamamaza.



Kugira ngo ugabanye uku gukurikiranwa, turagusavye guhitamwo moteri y'ukurondera yubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga itabika akaranga k'umuntu ku giti ciwe canke amateka y'ivyo urondera:




- [Startpage](https://www.startpage.com/);
- [Kagi Search](https://kagi.com/);
- [Qwant](https://www.qwant.com/);
- [Mojeek](https://www.mojeek.com/);
- [SearXNG](https://docs.searxng.org/) (ushobora kwitunganiriza).



![Image](assets/fr/123.webp)



Muri mucukumbuzi nyinshi, urashobora guhindura n'amaboko moteri y'ukurondera mu miterere yayo. Ivyo bigufasha kwirinda Google udahinduye mucukumbuzi yawe.



Imigenzo myiza twabonye muri iki gice ni yo shingiro y'ukuronedera mu buryo butekanye kandi bufise ubusegaba. Niwabikorerako ubudasiba, uzogabanya cane ukuntu ushobora gushikirwa n'ibintu bivyoguhungabanya.



Ubu ko twabonye ingene mucukumbuzi n'inyabwonko bikoreshwa, mu gice gikurikira turaza kuraba ingene twosubira kugenzura terefone yacu.






# Gusubirana ububasha kuri terefone yawe


<partId>5f0ef9ad-5701-4620-89bf-eb6937adccac</partId>


## Sisiteme ya terefone ngendanwa: Gutahura ingorane


<chapterId>020329e9-a2cb-464b-bb4c-ee4f0e5346c6</chapterId>


Kugeza ubu, twashize umutima canecane ku gukingira no gukoresha inyabwonko yawe. Ariko rero, ku bantu benshi, ubu terefone ngendanwa ni co gikoresho gikoreshwa cane mu buzima bwa misi yose.


Mu buryo butandukanye n'inyabwonko, amaterefone ngendanwa muri rusangi akoresha sisiteme zugaye, zigenzurwa cane n'abazikora. Ni co gituma muri iki gisata, ndasaba ko twosuzuma ingorane zidasanzwe zijanye na sisiteme ya terefone ngendanwa.


### Android: Kuva kuri open-source gushika ku bugenzuzi bwa Google


#### Incamake y'amateka ya Android


Android ubu ni yo itwara isoko ry'amaterefone ngendanwa kw'isi yose, ikaba ifise hafi 72% vy'ibikoresho bikoreshwa. Iterambere ryayo ryatanguye mu mwaka w'2003 aho hashirwa ko Android Inc. hamwe na Andy Rubin, Rich Miner, Nick Sears na Chris White. Intumbero yabo ya mbere yari iyo guhingura uburyo bwo gukoresha kuma kamera y'ubuhinga bwa none.


Inyuma yo kwankwa kenshi n'abashoramari, Android Inc. yahisemwo guhindura umugambi wayo mu guhingura sisiteme ya terefone ngendanwa. Kugira ngo tubone ivyo, mu myaka ya 2003-2004, isoko rya terefone ngendanwa ryari ririko riratera imbere cane, ahanini ryari riganzwa n'abahinguzi nka Nokia, Motorola, Sony Ericsson na Samsung. Ivyinshi mu bikoresho vyari "amaterefone y'ikibanza", bifise ama keyboards afadika, imboneshamashusho ntoyi z'amabara, rimwe na rimwe na kamera y'isanzwe. terefone ngendanwa zari zisanzwe zihari, ariko ahanini zari zigenewe abahinga babanyamwuga, kandi zitwarwa n'amashirahamwe nka BlackBerry.


Google yaguze Android Inc. mu mwaka w'2005 ku mahera ashika ku miriyoni 50 z'amadorari. Hagati y'umwaka wa 2005 n'uwa 2007, iyo sosiyete yarateguye sisiteme yayo imbere, ata nibakora verisiyo ya rusangi. Muri ico kiringo, hariho ibihuha vy'uko Google yariko irakora terefone ngendanwa, bishoboka ko yafashe ivyiyumviro kuri BlackBerry, ico gihe yariko irakundwa cane.


Ariko muri nzero 2007, hari ikintu cahinduye cane amateka ya terefone ngendanwa: Steve Jobs yashize ahabona iPhone y'uruvyaro rwa mbere. Iciyumviro rusangi c'uko keyboard yari ngombwa cane caracitsemwo ibice. iPhone yashizeho igikoresho cagenewe gukoreshwa mu gukora ku kumboneshamashusho(touch), ico gikoresho kimwe gusa cahinduye ivyo isoko ryiteze.


Kubera iyo mpinduka, Google yaciye itegekwa gusubira kwiyumvira inzira y'umugambi wayo wa Android kugira ngo ushobore gukorana na interface ya touch. Mu nyuma mu mwaka w'2007, Google yaratanguje ku mugaragaro Android nk'umugambi wa open-source ushingiye kuri kernel ya Linux yahinduwe, mw'izina *Android open-source Project (AOSP)* canke umugambi wa Android w'isoko y'uguruye.


Igikoresho cambere gikoreshwa na Android cashitse kw'isoko, HTC Dream, casohotse mu 2008. Yatanga ikibanza cari kikiri mu ntango, ariko cuguruye: abahinguzi n'abakoresha bashobora guhindura sisiteme mu mwidegemvyo kuvyo bakeneye, mu gihe abahinguzi bashobora kurema no gukwiragiza porogarame ata kubanza kugira ivyo bemererwa mbere. Ubwo buryo bwaciye bwihuta gutsindira abantu benshi kandi bwatumye abahinguzi benshi bakoresha cane Android.


![Image](assets/fr/131.webp)


*Isoko : [Na Akela NDE - Ibikorwa vyiwe bwite](https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?curid=6680413), CC BY-SA 3.0*


Ariko rero, ukwo kwuguruka kwa mbere kuzogenda kugabanywa na Google. Hamwe na kode ya open-source ya AOSP, iyo sosiyete iriko irategura urutonde rwa porogarame n'ama APIs, bihurijwe hamwe mw'izina *Google Mobile Services (GMS)*. Ivyo bizogenda bizamwo Play Store, Ikarata ya Google, YouTube, Google Play Services, Gmail, Chrome n'Umufasha w'Ijwi(Voice Assistance). Kugira ngo abahinguzi bashobore gushiramwo imbere y'igihe Play Store, ubu bategerezwa gusinyana amasezerano y'uruhusha na Google no kwemeza ko ibikoresho vyabo bihuye n'ingingo ngenderwako za GMS, ivyo bikaba bigabanya cane ubushobozi bwabo bwo guhindura ibintu nk'uko bashaka.


Android yarateye imbere cane: yarengeye iOS mw'isoko kuva mu ntango za Mukakaro 2011, hanyuma iba sisiteme yambere ihambaye ya terefone ngendanwa muri Ruheshi 2012, inyuma y'aho SymbianOS isenyukiye bukwi na bukwi inyuma y'aho Nokia iyihevye ikaja kuri Windows Phone. Android kuva ico gihe yagumye ari yo irongoye isoko ry'amaterefone ngendanwa ata n'umwe ahakana, kandi uno musi yo na iOS nizo zihariye isoko.


![Image](assets/fr/130.webp)


#### Open-source na Google


Umugambi wa Android ushingiye ku miterere y'ububiri. Ku ruhande rumwe, AOSP (*Android open-source Project*) iserukira urufatiro rw'isoko yuguruye rwa sisiteme: harimwo kernel ya Linux, ikirundo ca porogarame za sisiteme, interface y'ibicapo yoroheje n'umugwi w'ama APIs. Uru rufatiro rwagiye ahagaragara ku ruhusha rwa Apache 2.0, kandi iguma ishobora gushikirwa na bose. Ku rundi ruhande, ikibanza mu vy'ukuri gikoreshwa n'abantu benshi bakoresha Android bishimikije hafi vyose ku bihimba vy'ubuhinga vyakozwe na Google: *Google Mobile Services* (GMS).


Ivyo bice si open-source: ntibishobora gusuzumwa n'abanyagihugu mu mwidegemvyo, canke ngo bisubirizwe mu buryo bworoshe. Kugira ngo bashobore kubishira ku bikoresho vyabo mu buryo butegekanijwe n'amategeko, ababikora bategerezwa gusinya amasezerano y'uruhusha na Google kandi bagakurikiza ibisabwa bikomeye vy'ubuhinga n'ubudandaji. Ivyo bisabwa birimwo:



- ubufatanye nk'itegeko bwa porogarame nyinshi za Google nka porogarame za sisiteme zidashobora gukurwamwo
- gushira ahabona porogarame zimwe na zimwe (Google Search, Play Store, Gemini, n'ibindi) ahabanza
- ikoreshwa ryihariye rya APIs za Google ku bikorwa bihambaye nk'uguhuza, gusunika amatangazo n'aho umuntu ari


![Image](assets/fr/132.webp)


Ivyo biriko biratuma buhoro buhoro abahinguzi ba terefone ngendanwa bagira ivyo bakoresha butabaha kwigenda, kandi bikaba bituma ugutanga amakuru y'abantu ku ma seriveri ya Google biba bidashoboka ko vyohagarikwa kuba koresha terefone ngendanwa. Izo serivisi zigamije gutuma umuntu akoresha neza, ariko kandi akagira ibikorwa bihambaye nk'ugucungera backup y'amakuru, gucungera aho umuntu ari, canke kwemeza umuntu nihoraho biciye ku konti ya Google (kenshi bisabwa kugira ngo umuntu akoreshe neza igikoresho ciwe).


Naho Android iguma, mu vyiyumviro, sisiteme ya open-source mu ntumbero yayo, amaterefone menshi ya Android agurishwa kw'isi yose akoresha verisiyo yahinduwe kandi ikomezwa na Google. Muri iyi verisiyo, igice ca open-source ahanini kirihishije, utopfa ushoboye kwinjirira.


Kugira ngo vy'ukuri usubirane ububasha bwo kugenzura, ni ngombwa rero guhindukira ukaja ku bundi buryo nk'ama ROM y'ubuntu (GrapheneOS, CalyxOS, n'ibindi), ivyo tuzobiraba mu nyuma muri iki cigwa.


### iOS: umutekano mwinshi, ariko ni uburyo bwugaye


#### Incamake y'amateka ya iOS


iOS ni uburyo bwo gukoresha bwakozwe na Apple ku materefone yayo, bwashizweho na iPhone ya mbere mu 2007 (ico gihe yitwa "*iPhone OS*"). Kuva mu ntango, Apple yarafashe ubuhinga bwo gukorana n'ibindi vyose mu buryo buhagaze(vertical integration): ibikoresho, porogarame, sisiteme, serivisi zo kuri interineti n'ububiko bwa porogarame vyose birateguwe, bigenzurwa kandi bikabungabungwa na Apple. Mu ntango, porogarame z'umwimerere zitasohowe na Apple mbere ntizari zishigikiwe. Ubwo buryo buratandukanye cane n'ubwa Android, kuko ikibanza cayo cari gifise ibice vyinshi kuva mu ntango, kandi n'ubu biracariho.


![Image](assets/fr/133.webp)


iOS mu ntango yari ishingiye kuri sisiteme yakoreshwa na Mac: OS X. Ikoresha kernel y'ikivange iva kuri Darwin, ubwawo ikava kuri BSD Unix na Mach microkernel. Uyu mushinge w'ubuhinga ushoboza iOS kuragwa igitigiri c'ubukomezi n'ugushikama kw'imiterere yihariye kuri sisiteme za Unix. sisiteme rero yateguwe bishingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako zikomeye z'umutekano, harimwo:



- sandboxing ikwiye ya porogarame, kubuza porogarame imwe kuronka amakuru y'iyindi canke imigenderanire y'iyindi
- umukono w'itegeko kuri kode za porogarama, yemeza ubutungane bwa binaries n'inkomoko yavyo (App Store gusa)
- kunyegeza amakuru y'ibikoresho kuri chip, biciye kuri *Secure Enclave*, igikoresho co kunyegeza amakuru (cryptographic coprocessor) gitandukanijwe n'ibindi bice vya sisiteme
- gushira kugihe vyihuse amakuru y'umutekano, bishirwaho ubwonyene na Apple ku bikoresho vyose, ata n'umwe yitambika


Ubu buhinga bwimyubakire bwugaye burashoboza Apple gutanga uburyo bwogukoresha bugenda neza kandi butekanye. Iterambere ry'imbere na ryo nyene rituma habaho uguhindura neza ibikoresho n'ama porogarame, ata guhinduka kunini hagati y'ubwoko, bitandukanye na Android. iOS rero ifatwa nk'imwe muri sisiteme zitekanye cane ku bitero vy'inyabwonko.


#### Ibibi vyo kwugara iOS


Ariko rero, uwo mutekano ushingiye ku kwugara cane uwukoresha igikoresho ciwe, kuko ata bubasha afise bwo kugenzura igikoresho ciwe. Ntibishoboka gushiramwo izindi porogarame atari izi ciye kuri App Store, kiretse biciye kuri *jailbreak*, igikorwa gikomeye, giteye amakenga kandi kenshi kidashikamye gikuraho warranty kandi kigatuma umutekano wa sisiteme uhungabana. Iryo hame kandi rica hejuru ubuhinga bwa Apple bwo gukora ubucuruzi, busaba agashimwe ku bikorwa bikorwa na porogarame z'abandi.


Guhindura ibintu nk'uko umuntu abishaka na vyo nyene biragoye cane. Ntibishoboka guhindura cane inyifato ya sisiteme, guhindura mu mwidegemvyo ikibanza c'igihe co gukora, canke gushika ku madosiye ya sisiteme. Rero, mu bikorwa, iyo terefone iguma ari iya Apple, mbere n'inyuma yo kuyigura, kuko nta bubasha bwose bwokuyigenzura ufise.


![Image](assets/fr/134.webp)


Ikindi, ugushiramwo iCloud kw'tegeko muri serivisi nyinshi (gukora backups, guhanahana ubutumwa, amafoto, ahantu, Siri...) bituma abakoresha bashobora gushiramwo amakuru yabo bwite. Naho Apple ivuga ko ifise uburyo bwo kwubahiriza ubuzima bw'ibanga (kandi, bitandukanye na Google, uburyo bwayo bwo gukora ubucuruzi ntibushingiye ku gukoresha nabi amakuru y'umuntu ku giti ciwe), hariho imipaka myinshi igumaho:



- ibintu bimwe bimwe (nka metadata z'inzira, ibisabwa na Siri canke inyandiko z'amakosa) bica ku maseriveri ya Apple.
- uburyo bwo gusesangura inyifato ku vyiyumviro bishingiye ku vyo umuntu abona, gusubiramwo App Store canke kuyungurura ubutumwa bikoresha uburyo butagenzurwa
- gukoresha serivisi nka iCloud bisobanura kwizigira ibikorwa na Apple, ataco ugenzura kijanye n'aho canke igihe amakuru abikwa


Ubwa nyuma, ku bijanye n'ubusegaba muvy'ubuhinga bwa none, iOS igereranya ikibanza cugaye: nta butegetsi bwo hanze (yaba uwukoresha canke ishirahamwe ryigenga) bushobora kugenzura canke guhindura uko ikora. Abakoresha rero bategerezwa kwizigira Apple ku rwego rwose: ibikoresho, porogarame, umuhora...


### Ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha bwa open-source na Android


Nk'uko twabibonye, ​​ubuhinga bwa Android busanzwe, bugenzurwa na Google, bushingiye kuri verisiyo ya sisiteme y'isoko yuguruye (AOSP) bufise ibintu bimwe bimwe bigenzurwa (GMS). Imigambi myinshi y'isoko yuguruye iriko irakoresha neza AOSP kugira ngo itange ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha bwubaha cane ubuzima bw'ibanga, ata n'ibintu bishobora kwinjiramwo, kandi n'uburyo bwiza bwo guha ububasha bwokugenzura uwukoresha. Izo sisiteme zindi zirashobora gushirwamwo kugira ngo zisubirire sisiteme yari ihasanzwe, mu buryo bwa ROMs zihinduwe. Bigufasha gusubira kuronka ububasha kuri porogarame, ariko kandi bisaba ububasha bukeyi ku bikoresho,  kuko bihuye n'ibikoresho bikeyi gusa.


#### Ibisabwa ku bikoresho n'imburi


Imbere yo gushiramwo, birahambaye ko usuzuma ko terefone yawe ihuye na ROM wahisemwo. Vyinshi muri iyo migambi bishigikira urutonde rw'ibigereranyo bibujijwe. Akenshi, uzokenera gukoresha amaterefone ya Google Pixel, kubera ubufasha bwayo bwo kw'ugurura bootloader na drivers za rusangi.


Gushiramwo bisaba Kwugurura bootloader, igikorwa gituma ishusho nshasha ya sisiteme yandikwa, ariko kigafuta burundu ibiri mu gikoresho bihasanwe. Izindi serivisi nka, F-Droid canke Aurora Store vy'ama porogarame, na vyo nyene bizobwirizwa gushirwamwo n'amaboko.


Hari abahinguzi babuza canke bagatera ingorane ikigikorwa, canke mbere bagahagarika ibikorwa bimwe bimwe (camera, sensors, n'ibindi) igihe habayeho guhindura sisiteme. Ni vyiza rero guhitamwo terefone ihuye (kenshi ni Google Pixel).


![Image](assets/fr/135.webp)


#### GrafeneOS


[GrapheneOS](https://grapheneos.org/) ni ROM ya AOSP iteye imbere, yateguriwe gutanga umutekano wo kurugero rwo hejuru kuruta Android isanzwe. Itegurwa n'umugwi wigenga kandi igenzurwa n'abahinga. Graphene ishira mu ngiro uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano buteye imbere, harimwo:



- kugabanya cane amahirwe yo gushikirwa n'ibitero: guhagarika ibikorwa vyinshi (NFC, Bluetooth, n'ibindi), kwugara ports za USB iyo igikoresho kitariko kirakoreshwa, kugenzura neza pogo pin, n'ibindi.
- sandbox ya Android ikomeye
- uburinzi bw'uburyo bw'ibikoresho(nka memory) buteye imbere
- ubugenzuzi bw'uruhusha
- kunyegezwa kw'amakuru y'ibikoresho kudafise aho guhiye na Google
- n'ibindi.


![Image](assets/fr/136.webp)


GrapheneOS nta bihimba bigenzurwa ishiramwo. Ufise umwidegemvyo wo kwongerako ibikorwa vya Google canke ukareka, ariko ivyo biri ukwavyo (bishizwe muri sandbox mu mirongo y'ibikorwa yihariye). Ivyo bituma iyo sisiteme ishobora cane guhangana n'ibitero vyo mu karere no gukoresha intege nye za sisiteme.


Graphene ihuye gusa n'ubwoko buherutse gusohoka bwa Google Pixel(Pixel 6, 7, 8 na 9).


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/grapheneos-08d43d7a-0b22-4638-a151-578d48d32d88

#### CalyxOS


[CalyxOS](https://calyxos.org/) ni sisiteme yo hagati igamije guhuza ubuzima bw'ibanga, umutekano n'uguhuza n'ikoreshwa rya misi yose. Ishingiye kandi kuri AOSP, ifise ivyiza vy'umutekano. Ikintu kidasanzwe ni ugushiramwo MicroG, uburyo busubirira serivisi za Google kubuntu. Ivyo bituma bishoboka gukoresha porogarame nyinshi za Android zishingiye ku bikorwa vya Google, utarinze guca muri binaries zigenzurwa zemewe.


CalyxOS kandi itanga porogarame zashizweho mbere bizanana (Signal, F-Droid, Aurora store, VPN yashizwemo imbere...), na interface nziza. Biroroshe kuyishiramwo biciye ku gikoresho ca interface y'ibicapo ku bakoresha Pixel. Calyx ahanini ikorana na Google Pixels, ariko kandi na bumwe mubwoko bwa Fairphone na Motorola.


![Image](assets/fr/137.webp)


#### LineageOS


[LineageOS](https://lineageos.org/), samuragwa wa CyanogenMod, ni ROM y'ubundi buryo ihuye cane. Ishigikira amajana menshi y'ibigereranyo, ibi tubikesha umuryango munini w'abatanga inkunga. Ishingiye kuri AOSP, ishimika ku guhindura ibintu nk'uko umuntu abishaka, ku kworosha no ku kwidegemvya mu gukoresha.


LineageOS iguha sisiteme ya Android idafise aho ihuriye na bahinguzi, ata bloatware, ubutunganyirizo bw'uburenganzira bwuzuye, gushira kugihe vyoroshe na interface itunganye. Ushobora kwongerako serivisi za Google canke ugahitamwo kuyikoresha ijana kw'ijana mu mwidegemvyo.


Ariko ku bijanye n'umutekano, LineageOS ntishiramwo uburinzi bumwe bumwe bw'ibikoresho canke ubukomezi bwa memory buboneka muri GrapheneOS na CalyxOS. Gushirwa kugihe kwayo kugenwa n'umuryango wayo, bishobora gutuma habaho ugucerezwa mu bice vy'umutekano.


![Image](assets/fr/138.webp)


### Ni OS iyihe ya smartphone yo gukoresha iki?


Igihe uhitamwo sisiteme ya terefone yawe, urakeneye kumenya ivyerekeye umutekano, ubuzima bw'ibanga, ukworoha gukoresha n'uguhuza n'ibikorwa. Buri muti wose ufise ibintu vy'ubuhinga vyihariye bizogira ico bikoze ata guca ku ruhande ku bumenyi ufise ku musi ku musi, ubushobozi bwawe bwo kugenzura, n'ukuntu ushobora gushikirwa n'ugucungerwa canke gushikirwa n'ingorane.


Android isanzwe (ifise GMS) iguma ari umuti ukwiragiye cane muri iki gihe. Itanga ubushobozi bwo gukorana na porogarame zose za Android, ukworoherezwa mugukoresha no guca ubona serivise zizwi cane (Play Store, Maps, Gmail...). Ariko rero, ukwo kworoha gukoresha bishingiye ku gufatanya gukomeye kwa serivisi za Google, n'ugukorakoranya amakuru mu buryo butunganye: GPS, amateka y'ivyo urondera, metadata zifatwa igihe uhamagaye, ivyo ukunda mu kwamamaza... Rero ni amahitamwo mabi nimba uhangayikishijwe n'ubusegaba bwawe muvy'ubuhinga bwa none canke ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe.


Sisitme ya iOS ya Apple irafise umutekano mwinshi cane. Ariko rero, uwo mutekano ujana n'ukwugarwa cane kw'ikibanza: Uwukoresha ntashobora gushiramwo porogarame hanze ya App Store (kiretse mu bihe vy'inyuma), ntashobora guhindura inyifato za sisiteme, kandi yizigira Apple ku bijanye n'ugucungera ibikoresho, ububiko bwo mu gicu(cloud) n'uguhuza. Ni ikibanza ciza kandi gikomeye, ariko ikigomwa ikintu icarico cose kijanye no kugir ico uhindura canke kwigenga.


GrapheneOS igenewe cane imirongo y'ibikorwa isaba umutekano n'ibanga. Urugero rw'umutekano wayo, ariko, rurashiraho inzitizi zimwe zimwe: ibikoresho bikeyi bihuye (ibigereranyo vya Google Pixel biherutse gusa), nta kwinjira kwihuta kwa serivisi za porogarame z'abandi, n'ugukenera gutunganya n'amaboko ibindi bikoresho vyo gushira kugihe, store canke imenyekanisha. Nimba ubuzima bw'ibanga n'umutekano ari vyo ushira imbere, biragaragara ko ari yo mahitamwo meza kuruta ayandi yose.


CalyxOS itanga uburinganire bushimishije. Ubumenyi bw'abakoresha buguma hafi y'ivya Android isanzwe, ariko ata kugenzura kwa Google. Ishigikira igitigiri kibereye c'ibigereranyo (cane cane Google Pixel), kandi ishobora gushirwako ata bumenyi buhanitse bw'ubuhinga. Ku bakoresha bashaka umutekano wo hejuru ataco batakaje ku bijanye n'uguhuza porogarame, CalyxOS ni umuti ukora, uringaniye.


Ubwa nyuma, LineageOS ni distribution ya AOSP ku bakoresha bashaka guhinduranya no kugenzura. Ihuye n'igitigiri kinini c'ibikoresho, mbere n'ivya kera, iremera guhindura uko umuntu ashaka sisiteme, kandi itanga ubundi buryo buremurutse bwa OEM overlays. Ariko rero, ntiyinjiza mu buryo bw'umwimerere ivyiza vy'umutekano biteye imbere biboneka muri GrapheneOS canke CalyxOS, kandi ntiyama yungukira ku gushirakugihe bihoraho ku bigereranyo vyose. LineageOS rero isaba indero kanaka y'abakoresha kugira ngo igume itekanye mu gihe kirekire.


| Sisiteme   | Umutekano | Ubuzima bw'ibanga | Uguhuza | Guhindura uko ushaka |
| ---------- | --------- | ----------------- | ------- | -------------------- |
| Android    | 🟡       | 🔴                | 🟢     | 🟢                   |
| iOS        | 🟢       | 🟡                | 🟡     | 🔴                   |
| GrapheneOS | 🟢       | 🟢                | 🟡     | 🟡                   |
| CalyxOS    | 🟡       | 🟢                | 🟡     | 🟡                   |
| LineageOS  | 🟡       | 🟡                | 🟢     | 🟢                   |

Tutitaye ku mahitamwo yawe ya sisiteme ya terefone ngendanwa, mu gice gikurikira turaza kuraba imigenzo myiza ushobora gukurikiza kugira ngo ukingire neza terefone yawe no kubungabunga ikibanza ciza vy'ubuhinga bwa none.


## Gukingira terefone yawe muvyo uyikoresha umusi ku musi


<chapterId>37b9499e-32cf-42c3-8715-15c6884d2ec7</chapterId>


Mu gice giheruka, twasuzumye ingorane zijanye na sisiteme za terefone ngendanwa, hanyuma turaba uburyo butandukanye bwo kuronka ububasha bwinshi kuri terefone yawe. Ariko guhitamwo sisiteme nziza ntibihagije: kugira ngo ubone umutekano nyawo n'ibanga, birahambaye ko ukorera ku migenzo imwe imwe myiza mu gukoresha kwawe kwa misi yose.


Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba intambwe ku yindi impanuro zimwe zimwe z'ishimikiro zikora Kuri sisiteme iyariyo yose ya terephone ngendanwa.


### Amakuru yo gushira kugihe


Ngira nsubiremwo ivyo nari navuze, ariko buri mkakuru mashasha asohorwa n'abahinguzi ashobora kuba arimwo ibintu bihambaye vy'umutekano. Ikindi, amaterefone ngendanwa ashobora gushikirwa n'ingorane nyinshi kubera ubunini bwa attack surface: Biciye ku mihorora ya ngendanwa, kuri porogarame z'abandi, ku guhanahana amakuru ata nsinga (Wi-Fi, Bluetooth, NFC, n'ibindi).


Kutemeza ivyo shirwa kugihe muri sisiteme bisigura gusiga n'ibigirankana ubugoyagoye buzwi ugasiga integenke ataco zikozweko, zanditswe ku mugaragaro mu bitabo vy'amakuru nka CVE (*Common Vulnerabilities and Exposures*). Ayomakosa abayarakozwe rimwe na rimwe aca akoreshwa n'ibikoresho biri kuri interineti, mbere ata n'ubuhinga buhanitse bisaba. Ivyo bituma terefone ya kera iba ikintu ciza cane co gutera, mbere no ku bitero vyinshi vy'ubuhinga bwa none.


![Image](assets/fr/139.webp)


Ni ngombwa rero ko wemeza ishirwa kugihe rya sisiteme utarinze kubigiramwo uruhara mu mitunganyirize ya sisiteme yawe, kandi ugasuzuma n'amaboko buri ndwi ko igikoresho cawe gishobora gushirwa kugihe kikaronka bishasha vy'umutekano. Kuri Android, ivyo bikorwa kenshi uciye  `Settings > Security > System Update`, no kuri iOS uciye `Settings > General > Software Update`.


#### Ubufasha mu gushirwa kugihe


Si amaterefone ngendanwa yose yaremwe kimwe iyo bishitse ku bijanye n'ugufasha porogarame. Ibikoresho vyinshi vyo mu rwego rwo kwinjira n'ivyo hagati birahagarika kwakira amakuru mashasha ahambaye inyuma y'imyaka ibiri canke itatu gusa, ivyo bikaba bigutera ingorane zikomeye cane.


Ariko rero, hariho amashirahamwe afise ubuhinga bwiza cane bwo gufasha, cane cane Google (imyaka 7), Fairphone (imyaka 5 gushika kuri 7), Samsung (imyaka 5 gushika kuri 7) na Apple (imyaka 5 gushika kuri 7). Ico kigereranyo ni ikintu gihambaye cane igihe ugura terefone nshasha: Igikoresho kiramvye ni co mbere na mbere igikoresho kibungabungwa.


#### Koresha amaduka(stores) yizewe ya porogarame


porogarame zo kuri terefone ngendanwa ni zo zitera ingorane nyinshi: Ni zo zicamwo ama porogarame menshi mabi agezweho ya Android. Gushiramwo porogarame biciye kuri dosiye ya `.apk` yavuye ku rubuga rutazwi, canke kw'iduka ritemewe, bisigura kwishira mu kaga ko gushiramwo porogarame igira ububi n'ibigirankana, canke ihinduwe kugira ngo ishiremwo ibikorwa vy'ubutasi canke vy'ukwiba amakuru.


No ku maduka yemewe nka Google Play canke Apple App Store, urakeneye kuguma uri maso. Naho hari uburyo bwo kuyungurura, porogarame mbi zirashobora kugerageza kwinjira mu buryo budasanzwe. Nk'akarorero, porogarame za "Sparrow wallet" zirashobora rimwe na rimwe kubonwa kuri Play Store, kandi tuzineza ko iyo porogarame ikora kuma PCs gusa: Nta gukekeranya iyo iba ari porogarame y'ububeshi.


Imbere yo gushiramwo, fata umwanya wo gusuzuma ibintu bikeyi: uburenganzira busabwa, igitigiri c'ivyo uvoma, igiharuro muri rusangi ca rating, itariki ya nyuma yashizwe kugihe n'ivyo abakoresha bandi bavuga.


Kuri Android, amaduka y'ubundi buryo ya open-source nka [F-Droid](https://f-droid.org/) atanga umuti w'inyifato runtu kandi kenshi utekanye: porogarame yose ikoranirizwa hamwe ivuye mu masoko y'ubuntu, kandi igasuzumwa n'amaboko. Ku ma porogarame y'umuntu akenewe, ibikoresho nka [Aurora store](https://auroraoss.com/) bituma umuntu ashobora kwinjira muri Play Store ata konti ya Google, ivyo bikaba bigabanya amakuru yokorakoranywa.


![Image](assets/fr/140.webp)


Uretse sisiteme, porogarame zishizwe kuri terefone ngendanwa yawe na zo nyene zirakeneye kuguma zishirwa ku gihe. Ushobora gushiraho uburyo bwo gushira kugihe ata ruhara ubigizemwo biciye mu mitunganyirize y'iduka ryawe rya porogarame, hanyuma ukagira akamenyero ko gukorera isuzuma ry'amaboko n'imiburiburi rimwe mu ndwi.


Kuri Android, iyo ushizemwo porogarame biciye ku madosiye `.apk`, uzokenera gucunga ivyahinduwe n'amaboko kugira uyishire kugihe. Muvy'ukuri, izo porogarame zishirwamo zivuye hanze y'imihora yemewe nta buryo bwo kwishira kugihe zigira. Rero uzokenera gusuzuma ubudasiba verisiyo zasohowe n'abahinguzi kuri GitHub canke ku rubuga rwabo rwemewe.


### Gucungera uburenganzira rwa porogarame


Kuri terefone ngendanwa, porogarame iyo ari yo yose irashobora gusaba gushika ku bintu bihambaye: Mikoro, kamera, ikibanza nyaco, igitabu ca aderese, amadosiye, SMS, sensors za motion, n'ibindi. Uburenganzira bwo gushika kurivyo ntiwbaze ko arikintu gisanzwe: Muvy'ubuhinga, iyo uburenganzira butanzwe, porogarame ishobora kubukoresha mbere naho utabona, bikabandanya uko, rimwe na rimwe ntumenyeshwe ibiriko biraba. Ni co gituma bihambaye gukurikiza Ihame ry'uburenganzira buke: guha buri porogarame uburenganzira bwa ngombwa gusa kugira ibashe gukora neza.


![Image](assets/fr/141.webp)


Nk'akarorero, porogarame y'itara ntikeneye gushika ku bantu muvugana canke aho uri. Porogaramwe y'igena bihe ishobora gukorana n'uguhindura aho umuntu ari, ata GPS ishobora gukoresha. porogarame yo gusoma PDF ntikeneye gukoresha mikoro canke SMS. Nimba ufise amakenga, wame wanka ku buryo busanzwe, hanyuma wongere usuzume nimba iyo porogarame itariko irakora neza. Kuri sisiteme zimwe zimwe, birashoboka kandi gutanga uburenganzira mu gihe gito gusa: haba ku gukoreshwa rimwe, canke igihe gusa porogarame iriko irakora. Ivyo bibuza porogarame gukoresha uburenganzira bumwe bumwe buri ituguruye ataco ubiziko.


Android na iOS ubu zitanga uburenganzira bwo kugenzura. Ushobora kubicungera ugendeye  kuri porogarame canke ku bwoko bw'uburenganzira busabwa. Fata umwanya, rimwe mu kwezi nk'akarorero, kugira ngo usuzume uburenganzira buriko burakoresha biciye ku miterere ya terefone yawe.


Hariho kandi sisiteme zimwe zimwe zishobora kuguha uburenganzira bwo gukuraho uburenganzira bwatanzwe kuri porogarame inyuma y'ikiringo butagikoreshwa. Ivyo bigabanya ingorane iyo wibagiwe gukuramwo porogarame utakiyikeneye.


### Uburyo bwo kugara ngendanwa


Umutekano wo wa terefone ngendanwa utangurana n'uburyo bwo kuyugara. Iyi ni yo nzitizi ya mbere iri hagati y'umuntu ashobora kugutera n'ukuronka amakuru yawe bwite. Uburyo bwo kwizigirwa cane buracari kode ya PIN canke ijambo ry'ibanga rigoye.


Ku rundi ruhande, uburyo bwo Kwugurura nk'imigero y'ibicapo(graphical schemes) burabujijwe cane. Mwene iyo migero y'ibicapo isiga ibimenyetso biboneka kumboneshamashusho yawe, biroroshe gufata mu mutwe ku wundi muntu ariko arihweza ikimenyetso cawe, kandi ntabwo ari kenshi iba igoye bihagije.


Uburyo bwa biometric (gukoresha isura canke gukoresha ibikumwe) butanga uburyo bugaragara ko bworohereza abakoresha, ariko bukwiye gukoreshwa n'ubwenge. Iyo umuntu ahuye ingorane zigaragara (ubusuma, agashigwa kunkeke n'abapolisi, n'ibindi), igikumwe canke isura yiwe birashobora gukoreshwa kunguvu. Mu bihugu bimwe bimwe, gukoresha ubuhinga bwa biometric ntibigukingira nk'uko ijambo ry'ibanga rikingira.


Ku rundi ruhande, uburyo bwa biometric burashobora gukingira (canke bushobora kuba muri kazoza) hakoreshejwe ubuhinga nk'ugusubiramwo isura canke gusubirana ibimenyetso vy'intoke vyihishije ku kintu. Ukwizigirwa kwavyo na kwo nyene kuva cane ku rugero rw'umutekano w'igikoresho cawe: Nk'akarorero, ubuhinga bwa Apple bwo kumenya isura y'umuntu bukoresheje Face ID burakomeye cane kuruta ubw'amaterefone amwe amwe yo mu rwego rwo kwinjira.


Mu guca irya n'ino, ng'uru urutonde kuva ku buryo bwiza bwo kwugara terefone ngendanwa gushika ku bubi kuruta ubundi:



- Ijambo ry'ibanga ry'indome n'ibiharuro
- Kode ya PIN
- Biometric
- Ibicapo
- Nta kwugara


![Image](assets/fr/142.webp)


Ku bikoresho bikomeye, umuti mwiza ni ijambo ry'ibanga rifatanijwe n'uguhagarika biometric, n'uKwugurura n'amaboko gusa. Ivyo vyoshobora gusa n'ibibuza, ariko ni uburyo bwiza bwo kwirinda. Biragaragara, ko ku bijanye na Kode ya PIN canke ijambo ry'ibanga ry'indome n'ibiharuro, uko bigenda biba birerire kandi bikagenda bivangitiranya ni ko bigenda neza. Bitegerezwa kandi guhangana n'ibitero vy'inguvu z'agahomerabunwa.


### Gukoresha no gushira amakuru mu kibanza c'ihariye


Nk'uko twabibonye mu bice vyabanje, gushira amakuru mu kibanza c'ihariye ni umugenzo uhambaye wo kugabanya ingorane iyo habaye guhungabana kw'igice kimwe ca sisiteme. Mu kurema ibibanza bitandukanye vy'ibikorwa vyawe bitandukanye, urabuza igitero canke amakuru asohoka mu gice kimwe guhumanye igikoresho cawe cose. Kuri Android, uyu mukenyuro ushobora gushirwa mu ngiro biciye ku buryo butari bukoranye na sisiteme.


#### Koresha umurongo w'ibikorwa vy'umwuga utandukanye


*Work Profile* ni ubryo busanzwe buri muri Android (kuva kuri Android 5.0), bugufasha gukora igice ca porogarame gitandukanye muri terefone imwe. Mu buryo bw'ivyokorwa, uwo murongo w'ibikorwa ukora nk'ikintu kiri ukwaco: ama porogarame, amakonti n'amakuru abitswe muri iki kibanza ntibishobora gukorana n'ivyo mu murongo w'ibikorwa bwite. Ukwo gutandukanya bibuza amakuru gusohoka hagati y'ibibanza bibiri, kandi bikagabanya uburenganzira bwa porogarame. Ubwo buryo akenshi bucungirwa imbere mu masosiyete, ariko kandi hari uburyo bwo kubukoresha ku giti cawe kugira ngo utandukanye porogarame ibikorwa.


![Image](assets/fr/143.webp)


Igikoresho ca Shelter ni porogarame ya open-source ikoresha iyi ubu buryo bwa *Work Profile* bwa sisiteme ya Android kugira ngo ihe abakoresha batari abahinga uburyo bworoshe bwo guhingura ikibanza kiri ukwaco. Shelter ishobora gukoreshwa mu gushiramwo no gukoresha porogarame zihambaye mu kibanza kirinzwe, bikagabanya cane ukuntu zishobora gushikirwa n'izindi porogarame zishizwe kuri terefone.


![Image](assets/fr/144.webp)


#### Koresha amaterefone menshi atandukanye


Kugira ngo ugutandukanya imikoreshereze bigere mbere kure, birashoboka guhitamwo gukoresha ibikoresho vyinshi, kimwe cose kikaba kigenewe ubwoko butandukanye bw'igikorwa (c'umuntu ku giti ciwe, c'umwuga canke gihambaye). Ukwo gutandukanya gutuma igikorwa kija ukwaco, bikaba bikomeye cane kuruta ugutandukanya biciye kuri porogarame, kubera ko terefone imwe imwe yose ikora yigenga.


Iyo terefone ngendanwa imwe ihungabanijwe, izindi ziguma uko z'ari ataco zibaye. Ukwo kugabura nakwo nyene kurafise akamaro ko kworohereza imitunganirize yo gushika ku makuru n'uburenganzira kuri buri gikoresho cose, kandi bikagabanya ukuntu muri rusangi umuntu ashobora gushikirwa n'ibintu bishobora kumutera ingorane.


### Kugenzura uruja n'uruza rw'amakuru yawe


Terefone yawe ngendanwa iguma itumanako n'isi yo hanze, haba biciye kuri Wi-Fi, Bluetooth, NFC, GPS canke ku mihora y'amaterefone ngendanwa. Imwe yose muri izo nzira irashobora kuba attack surface. Gutahura ingene zikora no kuzikingira rero ni ngirakamaro kugira ngo umuntu agabanye amahirwe yo guhura ingorane.


#### Wi-Fi ya rusangi


Imihora ya Wi-Fi ya rusangi, nk'iyo mu bibanza bafatiramwo ibinyobwa, mu ma hotels canke mu miduga itwara abantu rusangi, usange arigake iba itekanye. Naho bisaba ijambo ry'ibanga, akenshi riba rizwi na benshi, kandi rimwe na rimwe ijambo ry'ibanga rikoreshwa urashobora kurimenya bitagoranye bitagoranye. Uwugutera yamaze kwinjira ku muhora uriko arashobora gufata packets zawe, gufata amakuru y'ibanga canke akagutera ibintu bibi biciye ku bitero vya Man-in-the-Middle.


Kugira ngo wikingire, irinde gusa gukoresha iyo mihora ya rusangi, canke ukoreshe VPN, izotuma habaho inzira inyegeje hagati y'igikoresho cawe na seriveri iri kure. Iyo nzira inyegeza amakuru yawe, bikaba bigoye cane kuyafata canke kuyahindura.

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mozilla-vpn-f55903d4-aece-4d59-b193-2eb073e59b67

Naho ku bijanye n'umuhora wa wi-Fi wo muhira, ivyo tuzobivuga mu gice ca nyuma c'iki cigwa ca SCU202.



#### Bluetooth, NFC na GPS


Bluetooth (umurongo w'ivy'itumanako rya hafi na hafi munzira itaboneka), NFC (Near Field Communication) na GPS (amakuru y'aho uri biciye ku cogajuru) birakoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe ku materefone menshi ngendanwa. Iryo koranabuhanga rishobora gukoreshwa nk'irembo ry'ibitero vyo mu karere: Gushitsa kode uri kure, gushika aho utemerewe, gukurikirana aho umuntu ari, mbere no gufata amakuru y'itumanako iyo ari Bluetooth (nk'akarorero, ubugoyagoye bwa BlueBorne).


Kugira ngo ugabanye ivyo bibazo, wama uzimya ivyo bikoresho igihe utariko urabikoresha. Ivyo bigabanya cane attack surface kandi bikagukingira ko umuntu agerageza kukwinjirira.


#### Imihora y'amaterefone ngendanwa


Amaterefone ngendanwa aguma atumanako n'ibibanza vy'abanyene gutanga umuhora terefone ikoresha. Iri tumanako rishobora gufatwa na *IMSI Catchers* bashobora kwigana ibikorwa n'abaguha umuhora kugira ngo bafate amakuru yawe yo kuri terefone ngendanwa. Ivyo bitero bituma uwundi muntu ashobora kumenya igikoresho cawe, gukurikirana aho ugenda, rimwe na rimwe no gufata ibiganiro ugira kuri terefone n'ubutumwa.


![Image](assets/fr/145.webp)


Hariho porogarame zimwe zimwe, nka SnoopSnitch kuri Android, zishobora kumenya inyifato iteye amakenga mu vyo uhanahana n'urubuga. Ivyo bikoresho birasuzuma metadata y'ivy'itumanako ry'amaterefone ngendanwa kandi birashobora kukumenyesha iyo habaye impinduka mu bijanye n'imiterere y'iradiyo canke inyifato idasanzwe, ivyo bikaba bituma urushiriza kuba maso ku bijanye n'ukugerageza gufata amakuru.


Uburyo bwiza bwo gukingira itumanako ryawe ni ugukoresha porogarame z'itumanako zifise umutekkano ukwiye, haba igihe ukeneye guhamagara canke kwandika ubutumwa. Izo porogarame ntizikoresha umuhora wa terefone ngendanwa, kandi zikora vyose kugira ngo amakuru ahanahanwa anyegezwe mu buryo bubereye. Ivyo tuzobiraba mu buryo buziguye mu gice gikurikira.


### Gukingira igikoresho cawe ngendanwa


#### Porogarame ikingira umugera nyabwonko kuri terefone ngendanwa (Antivirus)


Akamaro ka antivirus kuri ngendanwa akenshi gafatwa nkikintu kidasanzwe, ahanini bivuye ku masekeza yo kwamamaza akomeye. Akaga nyako kuri terefone ngendanwa, cane cane kuri Android, muri rusangi kava ku mu gushiramwo porogarame mbi zivuye mu bibanza bitemewe. Ku gikoresho gihora gishirwa kugihe, gitunganijwe neza (cane cane mu bijanye n'uburenganzira), kandi gikoresha gusa amakuru yemewe canke yagenzuwe, ingorane zo kwandura ni nkeyi cane.


Kandi, ibikoresho vya Android bisanzwe bifise Google Play Protect, ikora nka antivirus. Abo bandi bagurisha antivirus za terephone nabonyene bakoresha ubwo burya Google Play Protect, Ntakindi zikora usivye gusubiramwo. Mu vy'ukuri rero, antivirus yo kuri terefone ngendanwa nta co itanga, yaba kuri Android canke kuri iOS.


Ikindi kandi, izo porogarame zirashobora gutuma abazikoresha bumva ko bafise umutekano gusa ico ni ikinyoma, bigatuma bemera ko barinzwe rwose ibitero, mu gihe mu vy'ukuri zitanga uburinzi nubundi buba buhasanzwe. Nta n'imwe itanga uburinzi ku bijanye na phishing, canke uburenganzira bwinshi buhabwa porogarame, kandi nyene bizwi neza ko ibitero vya terefone ngendanwa biva kuri izo nzira nyene.


Akamaro kavyo nyakuri rero ni gato cane, kandi izo porogarame rimwe na rimwe ziratwara amahera menshi, zikaba kandi zitwa umucanwa n'uburyo bwinshi vya terefone yawe ata ni co bimaze. Ni vyiza ko tutazikoresha, kandi gusa ugafata imigenzo myiza washikirijwe muri iki gice.


### Suzuma inzira zisohoka


Hariho kandi porogarame za firewall kuri terefone gendanwa, nka NetGuard canke RethinkDNS, zikora nka firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro) yo mu karere ku gikoresho cawe. Bakoresha VPN API ya Android kugira ngo bafate amakuru yose asohoka, bidasavye ko baca kuri root.


Mu bikorwa, ivyo bisigura ko umuntu ku giti ciwe ashobora guhagarika gukoresha interineti ku ma porogarame amwe namwe, gutyo bikagabanya cane ingorane zo gukorakoranya amakuru bidakenewe canke guhanahana amakuru muburyo butemewe.


NetGuard, nk'akarorero, iragufasha gucunga uburyo bwo gukoresha interineti ku buryo bubereye porogarame kuri porogarame, ku makuru ya Wi-Fi n'ayo kuri terefone ngendanwa. RethinkDNS kandi itanga ibintu biteye imbere nk'ukuyungurura DNS, guhagarika amatangazo n'ugusuzuma DNS queries kugira ngo umenye ibishobora gusohoka.


![Image](assets/fr/146.webp)


### Gushirako backup n'ubucungerezi burinzwe mugihe co gutakaza


#### Kunyegeza backup zawe


Gukora buri munsi backup y'amakuru yawe ari kuri terefone ngendanwa yawe ni ikintu gihambaye cane ku mutekano wawe. Ariko iyo backup itegerezwa kuba inyegejwe, kugira ngo amakuru yawe y'agaciro ntabonwe n'umuntu wese yoba ashoboye gushitsa ibiganza vyiwe ku bikoresho vyawe vy'ububiko. Ivyo birajanye n'amafoto, inyandiko n'amakuru ya porogarame.


Kugira ngo ubishikeko, ushobora gukoresha imiti yo mukarere yo kunyegeza amakuru, nka disk ya hanze canke urufunguzo rwa USB runyegeza amakuru ajako (nk'akarorero na Veracrypt). Ivyo bidakunze, inyishu za cloud zo kwitunganiriza nka *Syncthing* canke *Nextcloud* ziguha uburenganzira bwo gucungera amakuru yawe kuri seriveri y'umuntu ku giti ciwe, mu gihe uguma ugenzura vyose ku bijanye no kuyaronka n'ibanga. mu buryo butandukanye na serivisi za cloud z'ubudandaji (Google Drive, iCloud...), iyo miti igabanya cane amahirwe y'uko amakuru yawe ashika ku bandi bantu.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/veracrypt-d5ed4c83-7c1c-4181-95ea-963fdf2d83c5

#### Gufuta vyose uri kure


terefone ngendanwa yazimiye canke yibwe irashobora kuba isoko y'amakuru menshi ku muntu atera: Amakuru y'umuntu ku giti ciwe, amateka y'ivyo yarondera, amakonti arimwo, n'ibindi. Birumvikana rero ko ari ngombwa ko dutunganya uburyo bw'umwimerere bwo kuraba aho iri kw'ikarata, kwugara no gufuta vyose kugikoresho caweuri kure.


Kuri Android, ushobora gukoresha *Find My Device* uciye mu miterere ya Google. Kuri iOS, *Find My iPhone* irafise uruhara nk'urwo nyene, ushobora kuyironka ukoresheje iCloud. Ivyo bikoresho biratuma ushobora guca ufunga uburenganzira bwo gukoresha, ugahamagara igikoresho kugira ngo ubone aho kiri, canke nk'uburyo bwa nyuma, ugafuta amakuru yose uri kure. Hariho kandi ibikorwa bisa n'ivyo bitunganywa n'abahinguzi, nka *SmartThings Find* ya Samsung.


![Image](assets/fr/147.webp)


Ariko rero, ivyo bintu birashobora guteza ingorane zikomeye: Bishira hamwe amakuru yawe y'agaciro (aho uri, amakuru winjirirako, gukoresha urikure, n'ibindi) ku ma seriveri y'ishirahamwe ry'abikorera ku giti cabo, kandi bigasaba ko uguma ugaragaza aho uri.


Niwahitamwo kubishira mu ngiro uko biri kwose, gerageza ivyo bintu imbere y'igihe kugira ngo umenye neza ko bizokora neza ku musi uzoba ubikeneye vy'ukuri.


Canke rero, nimba ushaka kudakoresha izo serivice zo kugira ubu basha kuri telephone yawe uri kure yayo, ndagusaba cane ko uhora ukora backup y'amakuru yo kuri terefone yawe kugira ngo ntutakaze amakuru yawe iyo igikoresho cawe kizimiye canke cibwe. Kugira ngo uwutera ntashobore kuronka amakuru yawe, nushireho ijambo ry'ibanga rikomeye rya kwugara terefone yawe n'ikarata SIM yawe.


Twashitse ku mpera y'iki gice ku buryo bwiza bwo gukoresha terefone yawe ngendanwa. Mu gice gikurikira, nzokwereka inyishu zibereye cane zo gutuma tumanako n'abandi mu mutekano kandi mw'ibanga ukoresheje igikoresho cawe, haba mu guhamagara, guhana ubutumwa canke gucunga amatsinda yawe y'amakuru.


## Guhanahana amakuru ata wumva 


<chapterId>e60773c6-ee96-47b2-a9fa-08d1bdbd1108</chapterId>


Muri iyi si y'ubu ihurijwe hamwe, igice kinini c'ivyo duhanahana ku giti cacu, bihambaye kandi bijanye n'umwuga bibera mu butumwa bwo kuri interineti. Ariko rero, ibanga ry'uburyo bumwe ku bundi riratandukanye cane bivanye n'amategeko akoreshwa.


Muri iki gice, tuzogerageza gutahura ibibazo vy'ubuhinga n'ivy'ibikorwa bijanye no gukoresha ibikoresho vy'itumanako vy'ubuhinga bwa none, kugira ngo duhitemwo kandi dukoresha ivyo bitanga uburinzi nyakuri kuba tega amatwi no gucungerwa.


### Ni kuki ubutumwa bwa SMS butarinda ivyo muhanahana?


SMS (*Short Message Service*) mu mateka yarakunzwe cane mu guhanahana ubutumwa, ariko ishingiye ku nzira y'ubuhinga bwa kera kuva mu mpera z'imyaka y'1980. Iyi nzira, yinjijwe mu ngingo ngenderwako za GSM (*Global System for Mobile communications*), nta buryo bwo kunyegeza amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza kuyindi mpera itanga (end-to-end encryption). Mu bikorwa, ubutumwa bwose bwoherezwa burungikwa mu nyandiko zitomoye biciye ku nzira z'abatanga umuhora wa terefone ngendanwa (rimwe na rimwe burashobora kunyegezwa kuri interface y'iradio gusa, ariko ntibushobora gushika ku mpera kugeza kuyindi mpera). Ibi bisigura ko ubutumwa bushobora gufatwa munzego  nyinshi:



- na banyene umuhora
- n'inkozi y'amabi ifata uruja n'uruza rwa gendanwa yawe (nk'akarorero biciye kuri IMSI Catchers)
- canke n'inzego za Leta zifise uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ibitangwa n'umuhora mu buryo butegekanijwe n'amategeko canke butemewe n'amategeko .


Kubera ko ubutumwa bwa SMS bubikwa kuri serveri nyamukuru za banyene umuhora, be n'intege nye zo sisiteme yo kwemeza uwinjira (inomero ya terefone nk'ikimenyetso ca karanga cihariye), bituma ubutumwa bufatwa bitagoranye kandi bugashobora guterwa. SMS rero ntibereye rwose gutanga amakuru, haba mu bijanye n'umuntu ku giti ciwe, mu bijanye n'umwuga canke mu bijanye n'ibintu bikomeye.


Ivyo bipimo birakora no kuri MMS (*Multimedia Messaging Service*), ishingiye ku mishinge imwe y'ubuhinga, hakongerwako n'ibintu vyinshi (amafoto, amasanamu).


Mu myaka ya vuba, abakoresha n'abahinguzi bamwebamwe barashizeho RCS (*Rich Communication Services*), ni ukuvuga ubuhinga bwo guhindura ubutumwa bwo kuri terefone. RCS irashoboza kohereza ubutumwa butunganijwe (amashusho, amasanamu, ivyemezo vy'ukwakira, n'ibindi) kandi igashiramwo ubuhinga bwo Kwugurura amakuru (TLS), ariko ivyo biguma bivana na banyene umuhora kandi ntivyemeza ko ubutumwa buzoba bunyegejwe impera ku yindi mu bihe vyose. Ikindi, ugucika ibice kw'ishyirwa mu ngiro ryayo hagati ya banyene umuhoroa n'abakora amaterefone (hagati ya Android na iOS, nk'akarorero) biragabanya kwemerwa kwayo n'ukwizigirwa kwayo nyakuri.


Kuva muri 2021, Google Messages yatanguye gukoresha uburyo busanzwe bukoreshwa na Signal bwo kunyegeza amakuru impera ku yindi, ariko iyo nzira ishobora gukoreshwa gusa iyo abo bompi bakoresha Google Messages.


Muri Ntwarante 2025, ishirahamwe rya GSM ryasohoye *Universal Profile 3.0* (UP 3.0), ryashizeho noneho ingingo ngenderwako y'ugukorana n'abandi ku bijanye na kunyegeza amakuru impera ku yindi mucongereza end-to-end encryption (E2EE) muri RCS. Ivyo bituma mugihe habaye habaye guhanahana amakuru biciye kuri porogarame ifise RCS yubahiriza UP 3.0, amakuru ntashobora gusomwa na banyene umuhora be na IMSI-catcher. Google na Apple zatangaje ko zizoshigikira ubu buhinga (reka tubi hange amaso nimba ivyo bizokorana). Ariko rero, iyo porogarame imwe muri izo idahuye na RCS UP 3.0, canke iyo ata nzira ya IP iriho, ivy'uguhanahana amakuru bica bihindukira bikaja ku buryo busanzwe, butanyegeza SMS, ivyo bikaba bituma gufata amakuru bitagorana.


Ku ruhande rwa Apple, iMessage (yatangujwe mu 2011) itanga end-to-end encryption hagati y'abakoresha Apple, ariko ubu buryo buguma bwugaye kandi bugarukira ku bikoresho vya iOS/macOS. Iyo umuntu ahana ubutumwa n'abakoresha badafise ivyo bikoresho vya Apple, ubutumwa buca bukoresha inzira isanzwe, bugatakaza ibanga ryose. Encryption irashobora kandi gutakara iyo wewe canke uwo mugenzi wawe abitse ubutumwa muri iCloud atakoresheje *Advanced Data Protection*.


Muri make, nta SMS isanzwe, canke MMS, canke mbere RCS isanzwe ishobora gufatwa nk'imiti yo kwizigirwa, y'isi yose yo kuzigama ibanga ry'uguhanahana amakuru. Gukoresha ubutumwa bwa Google Messages, iMessage canke umurongo wa RCS UP 3.0 wo muri kazoza ni vyo vyonyene bishobora gutuma haba ibanga rikwiye, ivyo bikunda rero igihe cose bompi bafashe umurongo umwe wo kunyegeza amakuru. Kandi ni ho nyene umutego nyamukuru w'ubutumwa bwa SMS mu buryo bwagutse uri: Iyi porogarame yo gutanga ubutumwa, isanzwe iri ku materefone menshi, ihuriza hamwe amategeko atandukanye cane, kandi iyo uwo wandikira akoresha gusa amategeko ya SMS, ubutumwa bwawe buzorungikwa mu buryo butanyegeje, ataco ubiziko. Ni co gituma, gushika hashizweho ingingo ngenderwako yo kunyegeza amakuru impera ku yindi ntayegayezwa ya rusangi, ndaguhanura cane kudakoresha ubutumwa busanzwe, kuko uguma wizigira imirongo ngenderwako y'umutekano yuwo urungikiye ubutumwa kugira wumve utekanye.


Aho gukoresha SMS, noguhanura gukoresha porogarame z'ubutumwa za bigenewe zikoresha end-to-end encryption ntayegayezwwa kandi zigaakorera mu muco, zishobora gutuma umuntu ashobora guhanahana amakuru mu buryo butekanye kandi bw'ibanga.


### Ubutumwa butekanye: ni iyihe miti?


Kubera ko ubutumwa bwa SMS bwo kuri terefone bufise aho bugarukira, haradutse porogarame zitari nke zo muri iki gihe, zimwe zimwe ziba zifise ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru impera ku yindi. Ngiye incamake muburyo bw'ikigereranyo ya porogarame nyamukuru ziriho uno musi, kugira ngo bigufashe kumenya ivyo bihuye neza n'ivyo ukeneye mu bijanye n'umutekano n'ibanga.


#### Signal


Signal ni porogarame yo guhana hana ubutumwa yakozwe kugira ngo itange ibanga ryinshi n'umutekano. Ishingiye kuri *Signal Protocol*, ishobora gutuma ubutumwa bwose bunyegezwa impera kuyindi, ijwi canke amasanamu, hamwe n'ugusangira amadosiye. Iryo tegeko risubira gukoreshwa n'izindi serivisi nyinshi gutanga ubutumwa, nka WhatsApp, Facebook Messenger, Skype na Google Message (mu gushirwa mu ngiro kwayo kwa RCS).


![Image](assets/fr/148.webp)


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, ikiyago cose kiri muri Signal kirindwa n'uburyo bwo kunyegeza amakuru butaringaniye (asymmetrical) be n'ukumara igihe gito (ephemeral): Imfunguruzo z'ikiganiro ziraganirwako mu buryo bukomeye kandi zigasenyuka inyuma yo gukoreshwa, gutyo bikagabanya ingorane zo guhungabanywa. Ugukorera mumuco kw'iyi porogarame, kode yayo yose ikaba ari open-source ku ruhande rw'umukiriya n'urwa seriveri, bisigura ko umuhinga mu vy'umutekano canke umushakashatsi wese ashobora kugenzura ubutungane bwayo n'uko yubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako z'ubuhinga bwa cryptography zavuzwe.


Ariko rero, Signal irafise intege nke iyo bije ku bijanye no kutamenyekana: iyo porogarame isaba inomero ya terefone ibereye kugira ngo umuntu yiyandikishe kandi amenyekane. Naho iyo nomero itaboneka mu buryo butunganye ku bantu ushobora guhura na bo (ishobora guhishwa mw'izina rindi), ico gisabwa kirazana ukuntu umuntu yizigira terefone, bigatuma rero habaho ikinogo co gukurikiranwa.


Muri make, Signal ni umuti mwiza cane wo gutanga ubutumwa, ariko ikibabaje ni uko bisaba gufatanya n'inomero ya terefone.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/signal-8dfb5572-6962-4f1c-bfa5-3192da4e9a4e

#### WhatsApp


WhatsApp, ifiswe na Meta (yahora yitwa Facebook), nayo ikoresha *Signal Protocol* mu bijanye end-to-end encryption. Rero, mu vyiyumviro, ibiyago vyawe vya WhatsApp birakingirwa neza kugira ngo ntibifatwe. Ariko rero, si ngombwa ko ari vyo vyiza kuruta ibindi vyose mu bijanye n'ibanga nyaryo: iyo porogarame ikoranya amakuru menshi cane (ibiharuro, incuro umuntu ahinduranya, ahantu uri, abaantu bawe...), ibi bishobora gukoreshwa mu bucuruzi na Meta mu kwamamaza canke mu gusesangura.


Kandi, ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru bukoreshwa na WathsApp ntibushobora kugenzurwa, kuko kode yayo y'isoko ari iy'umuntu. Ni co gituma ntababwira ko mukoresha WhatsApp mu gihe ibanga n'umutekano w'ivyo muvugana ari ngirakamaro.


#### Telegram


Telegram ni serivisi y'ubutumwa izwi cane kubera ubuhinga bwayo n'ibintu biyikoresha (imirongo ya bose, ama bots, amatsinda manini...). Ariko rero, umutekano wayo uragabanutse cane ku buryo busanzwe: kiretse "secret exchange" gusa ni yo yungukira kuri end-to-end encryption. Ibindi biganiro vyose (ivyinshi mu biganiro abakoresha bavugana ku musi ku musi) bibikwa bitanyegejwe kuri seriveri ya Telegram.


![Image](assets/fr/149.webp)


Telegram rero irashobora mu buryo bw'ubuhinga gushika ku birimwo mu biyago vyinshi bitarinzwe mu buryo butomoye. Naho iyo sosiyete ifata ingingo ikomeye yo kudatanga amakuru ku butegetsi bwa Leta, Telegram si umuti mwiza wo guhanahana amakuru y'ibanga canke y'agaciro, kiretse ukoresheje uburyo butomoye "secret exchange" yayo, ariko ntaco bimaze cane ku musi ku musi.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/telegram-09ab3cf3-7625-4267-97a1-24e59a9e5943

#### Threema


Threema, yatangujwe mu Busuwisi mu 2012, itandukanye cane n'izindi serivisi z'ubutumwa nyinshi zirinzwe kubera uburyo bwayo bwo gukingira ubuzima bw'ibanga. Bitandukanye na Signal, WhatsApp canke Telegram, nta nomero ya terefone isabwa kugira ngo umuntu akore konti. Uwukoresha ashobora guhabwa ikimenyetso ca karanga kidasanzwe, kigatuma umuntu ashobora kwiyandikisha ata n'umwe amubona ata n'umwe ahuye n'akaranga nyakuri.


![Image](assets/fr/150.webp)


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, Threema itanga  ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuri impera ku yindi ku mirongo yose y'itumanaho: ubutumwa, guhamagara, amadosiye, amatsinda, n'ibindi bikorwa. Kuva mu mwaka w'2020, kode y'isoko ya porogarame ya terefone ngendanwa yarabaye open-source, bikaba vyatumye habaho igenzura ku muntu wese abishaka. Ku rundi ruhande, ikibanza na seriveri biguma ari vy'umuntu, naho nyene biri mu Busuwisi gusa, n'igihugu gifise amategeko meza ku bijanye no kurinda amakuru y'umuntu ku giti ciwe.


Iyi porogarame ihuye na Android na iOS, kandi itanga interface y'urubuga, hamwe na porogarame ya Windows, Linux na macOS. Ariko rero, kugira ngo utangure bisaba kuba ufise terefone ngendanwa.


Ikindi kintu gihambaye ca Threema ni ingingo y'ubucuruzi bwayo: iyo porogarame si ubuntu ahubwo ni iyo kugura (hafi €5.99). Aya mahitamwo arinda kwizigira ivyitegererezo bishingiye ku gukorakoranya amakuru canke kwamamaza. Kugira ngo umuntu ntamenyekane igihe agura, imfunguruzo zo gukoresha zishobora kugurwa muma bitcoins canke mu mafaranga ubwonyene kuri Threema Shop ya Android.


Ngira ngo uwo muti wo gutanga ubutumwa ni mwiza cane, ariko ikibazo cawo nyamukuru ni uko kode y'isoko ya seriveri yaboiguma ari iy'umuntu.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/threema-24382d25-df7b-4e96-b332-6968f748df74

#### SimpleX Chat


SimpleX Chat, yatangujwe mu 2021, irakuraho burundu iciyumviro ca karangamuntu y'ukoresha: nta nimero ya terefone, nta zina ry'iritazirano rya rusangi, nta rufunguzo rwa rusangi ruboneka. Uwukoresha wese amenyekana gusa biciye ku mahuza canke ku makode ya QR y'igihe gito. Uku kuntu y'ubatse bituma kumenyana hagati y'abakoresha budashoboka, bikaba vyemeza ko urugero rw'ibanga ruri hejuru cane.


![Image](assets/fr/151.webp)


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, ubutumwa buranyegezwa impera ku yindi bugaca ku muri seriveri. Izo seriveri nta bumenyi zifise ku bijanye n'uwurungitse, uwuronka canke imfunguruzo zabo. Ubutumwa bumaze gushikirizwa, buca bukurwaho kuri seriveri. SimpleX ikoresha ubuhinga butagiramwo ubufatanye, budashizwe ahantu hamwe: seriveri ntizisangira ububiko bwa rusangi, kandi umukoresha wese arashobora gushiramwo umurongo wiwe bwite. Ivyo bitandukanye n'imiti nka Matrix, aho abakozi bahuriye hamwe bakurikirana ivy'uguhinduranya.


Iryo tegeko ryose ni ry'isoko yuguruye: porogarame, seriveri na yandi mategeko urashobora kubigerako ukabasha ku bigenzura ku mugaragaro. SimpleX iboneka kuri Android, iOS, Linux, Windows na macOS, ifise ububiko bwo mu karere bunyegeza amakuru, bushobora gutwarwa, ku buryo imirongo y'ibikorwa ishobora kwimurirwa ahandi bitagombereye server nyamukuru. Buri muntu wese akoresha arashobora kandi gucunga imirongo y'ibikorwa myinshi yitandukanije, imwe yose ikaba ifise ivyayo, izina ry'ibanga n'ifoto. Ukwo guhinduranya bituma bishoboka gutandukanya neza ubuzima bw'ibanga, ubuzima bw'umwuga n'izina ry'iritazirano.


Abanyanyi bongerwako biciye ku mahuza y'igihe gito canke ama aderesi adahinduka (ibimenyetso bihoraho ariko bishobora gusubirwamwo). Ushobora kandi guhitamwo hagati yo itumanako ry'igihe gito canke uburyo bwa kera, bufise ubugenzuzi bwiza ku bijanye n'ukuboneka n'uburenganzira (nk'akarorero, guhisha izina ryawe ry'ukuri inyuma y'izina iryo ari ryo ryose, ry'iritazirano ryihariye kuri buri munyanywanyi wese).


Ku bijanye n'umutekano n'ibanga, SimpleX irarenga uburyo bwinshi bwo gutanga ubutumwa busanzweho, igabanya  metadata ku rugero rutoyi kandi igakuraho ukuntu umuntu yizigira ububiko bwa mbere canke ikimenyetso kidasanzwe. Ariko rero, uko kuntu yubatse birasaba ko habaho ibintu vyinshi bishobora gutuma umuntu ashobora gukoresha neza: rimwe na rimwe nta n'umwe ashobora gukoresha neza, bikenewe ko umuntu yiga gatoyi mu ntango, kandi bivana n'uko hariho ama seriveri y'ugutanga amakuru.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/simplex-chat-7a1efa11-4d0a-49c4-92aa-e18bf22c22b9

#### Session


Session, yatangujwe mu mwaka w'2020 n'ishirahamwe ryitwa Oxen Privacy Tech Foundation, ni porogarame yo guhanahana ubutumwa yagenewe gutanga ubuzima bw'ibanga n'uguhangara n'icungerwa. Session nta makuru y'umuntu ku giti ciwe isaba mu kwiyandikisha: nta nimero ya terefone, nta imeyiri, gusa imfunguruzo zibiri z'ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru (cryptographic keys) zivuye mu karere. Ivyo bituma umuntu ashobora kwemeza ko ari we atamenyekana.


![Image](assets/fr/152.webp)


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, Session ishira mu ngiro ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru impera ku yindi haba ku butumwa, amadosiye, amajwi guhamagara, hamwe n'imigwi (abashika ku 100). Ubutumwa burungikwa biciye ku muhora wigenga ushingiye ku bikoresho vya seriveri ya node vy'isunga ubwubatsi bwa Tor's Onion. Ubwo buryo buratanga uburinzi buteye imbere kubijanye nogucungerwa ku muhora, harimwo n'aba ISP n'abakozi ba Leta.


Porogarama ya session na seriveri ni open-source. Iyi porogarame iboneka kuri Android, iOS, Windows, macOS na Linux, ikaba ifise uburyo bwo gukorana hagati y'ibikoresho biciye ku majambo Mnemonic asa n'ayo akoreshwa mu ngondo za Bitcoin. Iri jambo riha uwuriko arakoresha ububasha bwo gucungera amakuru yiwe, ariko kandi ritanga inshingano ikomeye mu bijanye no gukora backup.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/session-b0e3193c-2129-4f1b-9013-c211210724c3

#### Keet


Keet, yatangujwe mu 2022 na Holepunch (isosiyete ishigikiwe na Tether na Bitfinex), iratandukanye cane mu buryo bwayo bwo kwegereza abantu bose: Ivy'uguhanahana amakuru vyose (ubutumwa, guhamagara n'amasanamu, uguhanahana amadosiye, n'ibindi) biba hagati y'abakoresha, bitagombereye guca kuri seriveri n'imwe. Ububuryo y'ubatse mwo bwa P2P bukurako abahuza kandi bugatuma iyo sisiteme igira ibanga kandi ikaba ishobora gukomera.
