![Image](assets/fr/153.webp)


Keet ipfuka ivy'itumanako vyose kuva ku mpera kugeza ku yindi. Ukwiyandikisha ntibimenyekana rwose: nta nomero ya terefone, imeyiri aderese canke ikimenyetso kigaragaza umuntu bisabwa. Ivyo bituma haba ibanga ryinshi kuva igihe iyo serivisi itanguye gukora. Guhamagara na masanamu vy'agaciro kanini cane, kandi ukwohereza amadosiye nta n'aho bigarukira, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kubikoresha mu buryo bw'umwuga no mu buryo bwiwe bwite.


Ku rundi ruhande, naho ibice bimwe bimwe (cryptography n'ugukorana n'abandi) bisohorwa nka open-source kuri GitHub, interface ya porogarame ya ba kiriya ya Keet ntiyari yuguruye bimwe bishitse igihe SCU-202 yandikwa (Rusama 2025). Ariko rero, Holepunch yatangaje ko izosohora iyo kode yose muri kazoza.


Keet iboneka kuri Android, iOS, Windows, macOS na Linux, kandi ishobora guhurizwa hamwe hagati y'ibikoresho hakoreshejwe ijambo Mnemonic.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/keet-efdb759d-5e94-4bbf-b28c-5fa8669c809b

#### Olvid


Olvid, yatangujwe muri 2019, ni serivise y'ubutumwa bunyegejwe y'abafaransa. Iciyumviro cayo gikomeye: Ukwiyandikisha ata makuru y'umuntu ku giti ciwe. Imenyekanisha rishingiye ku guhana hana imfunguruzo z'ibanga hagati y'abakoresha.


![Image](assets/fr/154.webp)


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, ubutumwa buri kuri Olvid buranyegezwa impera ku yindi, hakoreshejwe uburyo bw'umunutu yashizeko bwihariye bwagenewe gukingira atari ibiri mu butumwa gusa, ariko na metadata: Nta n'umwe, harimwo na seriveri, ashobora kumenya uwuriko aravugana n'uwundi, canke ryari. Ico kigereranyo kigabanya cane ingorane zo gukora ubutasi no gucungera abantu.


Ariko rero, seriveri n'ivyo bikorana biguma ari ivy'umuntu kandi bikaba bishizwe hamwe, bibunga bungwa na AWS (*Amazon Web Services*). Kode ya porogarame imaze imyaka myinshi ari open-source, ariko kode ya seriveri ntisohorwa, ivyo bikaba bigabanya ugukorera mu muco kw'ubuhinga bwa sisiteme.


Icegereranyo c'umutekano ca Olvid gishingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako ihambaye: Ugukuraho burundu uyundi muntu yizigirwa mu gushinga akaranga k'ubuhinga bwa none. Aho bitandukanira ubundi buryo bwinshi bwo gutanga ubutumwa bunyegeza amakuru, bwishingikiriza ku bubiko bumwe kugira ngo bucunge akaranga k'abakoresha, Olvid ntiyizigira ibikorwa na serivisi vyose vy'ubuhinga bwo guhanahana amakuru kugira ngo bimenyeshe ubutungane bw'itumanako. Ubu buryo vyubatse burakuraho ingorane zijanye n'uguhungabanya ububiko.


Olvid ikoresha seriveri yo gukwiragiza ubutumwa hagati, ariko uruhara rwayo ni urw'ivy'ubuhinga bwo kurungika no kwakira: Ikora ivy'ugutanga ubutumwa bushizwe mu buryo butajanye n'igihe kandi bunyegejwe. Iyi seriveri nta ntambwe iyo ari yo yose igira mu nzira yo gushiramwo amakuru, kandi ntizi akaranga nyakuri k'abakoresha, canke ibirimwo canke amakuru y'ubutumwa (uretse urufunguzo rwa rusangi rw'uwuronka, rukenewe kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gutanga inzira). Bishobora rero gufatwa nk'agasho ku buryo busanzwe, ataco bihungabanya ku mutekano muri rusangi. Naho yoba yahungabanijwe, ntiyo kwemera ko umuntu wese ashobora kuronka ibirimwo mu bimenyetso vy'itumanako. Olvid rero yiyumvira ko ubutumwa buzokwiragizwa hamwe (kubera imvo z'ubushobozi n'uburyo bw'ibikorwa), mu gihe yizeza umutekano udashingiye kuri ivyo bikorwa na serivisi.


Olvid itanga amaverisiyo abiri:



- Verisiyo y'ubuntu, itanga ibikorwa vyose kiretse guhamagara amajwi n'amasanamu (kwakira gusa) no gukorana n'ibikoresho vyinshi
- Verisiyo yishurwa ku €4.99 ku kwezi ifungura ibiranga vyose


Iyi porogarame yemejwe na ANSSI (*Agence Nationale de la Sécurité des Systèmes d'Information*) Ikigo c'Igihugu c'Umutekano wa Sisiteme y'Amakuru.


Olvid ikorana na Android, iOS, Windows, macOS na Linux. Ivy'ubuhinga bwayo biguma vyoroshe kandi bishoboka. Iyo porogarame irafise kandi uburyo bwo gukora backup z'amakuru anyegejwe z'imfunguruzo n'abanywanyi ushobora kugaruro konti yawe ku gikoresho gishasha.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/olvid-05038dc1-62c0-4a47-be4e-3d23c6155bfd

### Porogarame z'ubutumwa zo kwirinda


Porogarame zizwi cane z'ubutumwa nka WhatsApp, WeChat, Facebook Messenger, Instagram Direct Message, Snapchat na LINE zirakoreshwa ku musi ku musi. Ariko rero, mu vy'ubuhinga, izo nzira ntizihuye n'ingingo ngenderwako z'umutekano zo muri iki gihe zibereye gukoreshwa mu guhanahana amakuru ku giti cawe.


Muri rusangi, ibintu bibiri vy'ishimikiro umuntu akwiye kwitwararika igihe ahitamwo serivisi yo gutanga ubutumwa ni ibi: Yoba itanga ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru impera ku yindi(end-to-end encryption), kandi kode yayo ikaba ari open-source? Hanyuma hariho n'ibindi bishobora gushimisha umuntu, nk'ukwiyandikisha ata mazina canke gukoresha imihora itagira aho igenzurirwa hamwe, ariko ivyo bibiri vya mbere ni vyo vy'ishimikiro. Ukunyegeza amakuru bituma ivyo muhana hana biguma ari ibanga, mu gihe Kwugurura kode y'isoko bigufasha kugenzura ko ukunyegeza amakuru vyashizwe mu ngiro ata nkomanzi.


Gukoresha serivisi zidashobora gushitsa ivyo bisabwa bibiri ni nk'uguha burundu uburinzi bw'amafaranga yawe abakinnyi b'ubudandaji inyungu zabo z'ubutunzi akenshi zivana no kuyakoresha.


Nguru urutonde rw'incamake y'ibikoresho nyamukuru vyo gutanga ubutumwa biriho n'ibiranga, nk'uko bimeze mu gihe c'ukwandika iki cigwa (Rusama 2025):


| Porogarame           | E2EE 1:1         | E2EE amatsina gusa | Kwiyandikisha utamenyekanye | Porogarame y'uruhusha rwa open-source | Seriveri y'uruhusha rwa open-source | Seriveri ikwiragiye | Umwaka ya sohotse |
| -------------------- | ---------------- | ------------------ | --------------------------- | ------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------- | ------------------- | ----------------- |
| WhatsApp             | ✅              | ✅                 | ❌                         | ❌                                    | ❌                                 | ❌                  | 2009              |
| WeChat               | ❌              | ❌                 | ❌                         | ❌                                    | ❌                                 | ❌                  | 2011              |
| Facebook Messenger   | ✅              | 🟡 (ubishatse)     | ❌                         | ❌                                    | ❌                                 | ❌                  | 2011              |
| Telegram             | 🟡 (ubishatse)  | ❌                 | 🟡                         | ✅                                    | ❌                                 | ❌                  | 2013              |
| LINE                 | ✅              | ✅                 | ❌                         | ❌                                    | ❌                                 | ❌                  | 2011              |
| Signal               | ✅              | ✅                 | ❌                         | ✅                                    | ✅                                 | ❌                  | 2014              |
| Threema              | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | ❌                                 | ❌                  | 2012              |
| Element (Matrix)     | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | ✅                                 | 🟡 (federated)      | 2016              |
| Delta Chat           | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | N/A                                | 🟡 (via imeyiri)    | 2017              |
| Conversations (XMPP) | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | ✅                                 | 🟡 (federated)      | 2014              |
| Session              | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | ✅                                 | ✅                  | 2020              |
| SimpleX              | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | ✅                                 | ✅                  | 2021              |
| Olvid                | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | ❌                                 | 🟡(no directory)    | 2019              |
| Keet                 | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ❌                                    | N/A                                | ✅                   | 2022             |
| Jami                 | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | N/A                                | ✅                   | 2005             |
| Briar                | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | N/A                                | ✅                   | 2018             |
| Tox                  | ✅              | ✅                 | ✅                         | ✅                                    | N/A                                | ✅                   | 2013             |

*E2EE = End-to-end encryption* ubuhinga bwo kunyegeza amakuru impera n'impera


Umutekano w'ivy'itumanako ryawe ry'ubuhinga bwa none uvana canecane no guhitamwo ubuhinga bwiza no kwemera uburyo bwiza bwo kubikoresha. Gutahura uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano bushingiyeko, kumenya amakosa ari mu mirongo ngenderwako isanzwe no guhitamwo uburyo bwo kwizigirwa ni vyo bishingiyeko canecane kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kuvugana n'abandi ata wumva.


Kugeza ubu, twasuzumye ingene wokingira terefone yawe n'ingene wohitamwo porogarame yo gutanga ubutumwa yizigiwe. Mu gice gikurikira, ndasaba kwagura iyi nyigisho ku miryango yose ikomeye y'ama porogarame y'amaterefone ngendanwa, kugira ngo uronke uburyo bundi bwo gukoresha ama porogarame ukunda cane. Yaba ari imeyiri, ububiko bw'amadosiye, ikarata, amasanamu canke umuziki, ni ibihe bikoresho vy'isoko yuguruye ushobora gukoresha?


## Porogarame z'isoko yuguruye: ubundi buryo bwiza


<chapterId>9c0e056c-45ce-407c-b4b6-f648bbc1f7d5</chapterId>


Uretse porogarame zo gutumanako, birahambaye kwibuka ko izindi porogarame ziri kuri terefone yawe zishobora gukoresha amakuru yawe mu ntumbero z'ubudandaji. Ikintu ciza, hariho uburyo bundi bwo gukoresha bwa open-source bwubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe. Ivyo nivyo nshaka kubamenyesha muri iki gice.


Sinzosubira ku bijanye n'ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha amamucukumbuzi na porogarame z'itumanako muri gice, nk'uko twamaze kubivuga mu buryo buziguye mu bice vyabanje.


### Imeyiri z'abaguzi


imeyiri iguma ari igikoresho gihambaye co guhanahana amakuru, ariko porogarame zizwi cane, nka Gmail canke Outlook, zitera ibibazo vyinshi ku buzima bw'ibanga. Izo serivisi akenshi zisesangura ubutumwa bwawe, zibika metadata kandi zikagira uruhara mu kurema imirongo y'ibikorwa vyo kwamamaza.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [FairEmail](https://email.faircode.eu/)


FairEmail ni porogarame ya Android yikwije, ishingiye ku mutekano. Ishigikira IMAP/SMTP, amakuru anyegezwa hifashishijwe OpenPGP, ibuza amashusho ya kure (akoreshwa nk'abikurikirana), kandi serivisi nimwe yabandi ikoresha. Biguha ububasha bwose ku nzira, imenyekanisha n'inyifato yo guhuza.


![Image](assets/fr/155.webp)



- [K-9 Mail](https://k9mail.app)


K-9 Mail ni porogarame open-source ya Android y'ubutumwa bwa imeyiri, iherutse gushirwa muri ThunderBird ya Mozilla. Yemera ama konti menshi, PGP encryption biciye kuri OpenKeychain, kandi ikora bitagombereye seriveri iri hagati.


![Image](assets/fr/156.webp)



- [Thunderbird Mobile](https://www.thunderbird.net/mobile/)


Thunderbird Mobile ni verisiyo ya terephone ngendanwa ya porogarame open-source y'ubutumwa bwa imeyiri yateguwe na Mozilla Foundation. Nkuko firozofiya y'umugambi iteye, iyo porogarame ishimika ku bijanye n'ibanga, kode iciye mu muco no kutagira ubuhinga bwo gupima bwa telemetry. Thunderbird Mobile ishingiye kuri porogarame ya K-9 Mail, ariyo ikurikira ku mugaragaro kuri Android. Irafise uburongozi buteye imbere bwa konti za IMAP na POP, kunyegeza ubutumwa bwa imeyiri (biciye kuri OpenPGP), na interface yoroshe kandi ikora neza.


![Image](assets/fr/157.webp)


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/thunderbird-91d02325-0361-4641-b152-8975890284a8

- [Tuta](https://tuta.com/)


Tuta (yahora yitwa "*Tutanota*") itanga umuti wuzuye w'ubutumwa bwa imeyiri bunyegeje impera ku yindi, ariko porogarame yayo ya terefone ngendanwa yemera gusa amakonti ya Tuta. Ntikorana n'izindi serivisi z'ubutumwa bwa imeyiri. interface igezweko kandi nta n'ibintu vyinshi biriho, kandi kwiyandikisha ntibisaba amakuru y'umuntu ku giti ciwe.


![Image](assets/fr/158.webp)



- [Proton Mail](https://proton.me/mail)


Proton Mail ni serivise y'ubutumwa bwa imeyiri butekanye iva mu Busuwisi itanga muburyo bw'umwimerere bwo nyegeza amakuru impera ku yindi hagati y'abakoresha Proton. Iyi porogarame yo kuri terefone ngendanwa ni open-source, nta vyo kwamamaza igira kandi nta makuru bwite y'umuntu ikorakoranya mukwiyandikisha. Proton Mail yemera gusa amakonti ya Proton, ariko yemera kohereza amakuru anyegejwe kuri aderese yohanze hakoreshejwe ijambo ry'ibanga.


![Image](assets/fr/159.webp)


Uburyo bwa imeyiri bushingiye ku bice 2 bitandukanye: Uwutanga serivisi ya imeyiri (nka Gmail, Tuta canke Proton Mail), akora ivyo kwakira, kohereza no kubika ubutumwa biciye ku ma seriveri; na porogarame ya imeyiri (client), ari yo porogarame ikoreshwa mu kuraba no kwandika imeyiri zawe (nk'iporogarame ya Gmail, Outlook, K-9 Mail canke Thunderbird). Umukiriya ashobora kwihuza n'abatang serivisi badatandukanye biciye kumategeko ngenderwa ko nka IMAP canke SMTP.


Birashoboka rero gukoresha client ya open-source yubahiriza ubuzima bw'ibanga mu gihe mu sanzwe uriko ukoresha konti itangwa na serivisi zisanzwe. Hariho porogarame zimwe zimwe, nka Gmail, Proton Mail canke Tuta, zitanga clients zikoranye uburyo bwo guhanahana ubutumwa, gutyo bagatanga umuti wuzuye ushizemwo interface yogusoma n'ukurungika/kwakira imeyiri.


Ngibi ivyiyumviro bike, aho uriko uhitamwo uwuguha serivisi za imeyiri:



- [Proton Mail](https://proton.me/mail)
- [Tuta](https://tuta.com/)
- [Mailbox](https://mailbox.org/)
- [Disroot](https://disroot.org/)
- [Mailfence](https://mailfence.com/)


### Gukora ikarata no kurondera


Ivyinshi mu bikoresho vya kera vyo gukora ikarata, nka Google Maps, Waze canke Citymapper, bikusanya amakuru menshi y'umuntu ku giti ciwe. Barandika aho wimuka, ivyo urondera be n'ingeso zawe, bakabikoresha mu vy'ubudandaji.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Organic Maps](https://organicmaps.app/)


Organic Maps ni porogarame y'ubuntu yo kugendera ku nzira. Ishingiye ku makuru ava muri [OpenStreetMap](https://www.openstreetmap.org), urutonde rw'amakuru rwuguruye. Uca uvoma amakarata y'uturere ushaka, hanyuma ukagendagenda bitagombereye umuhora.


Nta kwamamaza, gukurikirana canke gukorakoranya amakuru birimwo. Iyi porogarame irabereye cane cane mu ngendo z'amaguru, kwikinga canke mu muduga, ifise interface yoroshe, yihuta kandi idasamaza.


![Image](assets/fr/160.webp)



- [OsmAnd](https://osmand.net/)


OsmAnd (*OpenStreetMap Automated Navigation Directions*) ni indi porogarame y'ikarata y'isoko yuguruye. Itanga uburyo bwo kugenderamwo na GPS bitagombereye interineti,amakarata agaragaza neza ido n'ido ry'ahantu (harimwo ubutaka, inzira za makinga, utunyuro), n'uguhindura vyinshi.


Ushobora gukoresha ibice bitandukanye (ibice vy'abagenda n'amaguru, ivy'ugutwara abantu rusangi, n'ibindi), gusobanura imburi z'umuvuduko canke gushiramwo amakarata yihariye nk'ayo gutembera mu misozi canke inzira zo mu mazi.


Verisiyo y'ubuntu irimwo vyose ukkeneye, kandi verisiyo irihwa iragufasha Kwugurura mbere n'ibindi bikoresho be no gushigikira umugambi.


![Image](assets/fr/161.webp)


### Ibiro n'inyandiko


Ibikoresho vya kera vy'ibiro nka Google Docs canke Microsoft Office birakora cane, ariko biratera ingorane zikomeye mubijanye n'ibanga. Inyandiko zibikwa kuri seriveri zazo, zigasuzumwa, rimwe na rimwe zigakoreshwa mu kwamamaza canke mu gutoza ibigereranyo vy'ubwenge bw'ubukorano(AI models).


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Collabora Office](https://www.collaboraoffice.com/)


Collabora Office ni verisiyo ya LibreOffice yagenewe terefone ngendanwa, ikorana na terefone ngendanwa be na tablets za Android na iOS. Iragufasha gukora, guhindura no gusangiza inyandiko z'ibiro utazokwigera uva ku gikoresho cawe canke mu gicu(cloud) cawe bwite.


Porogarame ishigikira guhindura mu bufatanye iyo ihuye na Nextcloud n'inyongera bushobozi ya Collabora kuri interineti. Ibi bituma bishoboka kwigana Google Docs, ariko mu kwakira amadosiye yawe wewe nyene.


![Image](assets/fr/162.webp)



- [ONLYOFFICE](https://www.onlyoffice.com/)


ONLYOFFICE ni office suite ya open-source. Iragufasha Kwugurura no guhindura inyandiko za Word, Excel na PowerPoint ukoresheje terefone yawe ngendanwa, mbere nigihe utari kuri interineti. Ushobora kandi kuyifatanya na serivisi zitandukanye za cloud kugira ngo habeho kwihuza, nka Nextcloud.


![Image](assets/fr/163.webp)


### ubutunganyirizo bwa dosiye n'igicu(cloud)


Servisi nka Google Drive canke Dropbox zibika amadosiye yawe ku ma seriveri ya kure y'amashirahamwe yigenga. Amakuru yawe arashobora rero kurabwa maze agakoreshwa mu kwamamaza canke mu gukora ivyegeranyo. Ikindi kandi, ukeneye interineti be n'iyindi konti y'itunganywa n'abandi kugira ngo ushobore kubironka.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Nextcloud](https://nextcloud.com/)


Nextcloud ni umuti wa cloud w'isoko yuguruye w'umuntu ku giti ciwe ushobora kwitunganiriza wewe nyene canke ukawukoresha biciye kuri serivisi wizigirwa. Iragufasha kwihuza na cloud, gusangiza no guhindura amadosiye yawe ukoresheje terefone yawe, mu gihe uguma ugenzura vyose vyawe ku bubiko bwayo.


Kuri Android, urashobora gushiramwo porogarame yemewe ya Nextcloud kugira ngo ushikire igicu cawe bwite aho uri hose. Ushobora kandi kwongerako ibikorwa nk'ugucungera amafoto, ibiro, ikirangamisi n'ubutumwa.


![Image](assets/fr/164.webp)



- [Material Files](https://github.com/zhanghai/MaterialFiles)


Material Files ni ubutunganyirizo bwa dosiye bw'isoko yuguruye buremurutse kandi butagiramwo ibintu vyinshi. Buragufasha kurondera, kwimura, gukopiya canke gufuta amadosiye mu karere kawe ku gikoresho cawe ca Android.


porogarame nta kwamamaza canke gukurikiranwa, kandi nta burenganzira bw'ikirenga isaba. Ni uburyo bushimishije bundi busa n'ubutangwa na Google, akenshi yinjizwa mu zindi serivisi z'igicu zifise banyenezo.


![Image](assets/fr/165.webp)


### Ikirangamisi / Igitabo


Abantu benshi bakoresha porogarame nka Google Calendar canke Outlook Calendar kugira ngo bashobore gucunga amasaha yabo. Nyamaze izo serivisi zihuye n'amakonti yo kuri interineti ahuriye hamwe akorakoranya amakuru yerekeye ingeso zawe, ama nama n'ingene ukora.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Etar](https://github.com/Etar-Group/Etar-Calendar)


Etar ni ikirangamisi coroshe, gikora neza kandi ca open-source rwose. Gishobora gukora mu karere ata interineti, ariko kandi kiremera guhuza na cloud biciye kuri CalDAV, umurongo usanzwe wo guhuza ikirangamisi na serivise ziharanira ubuzima bw'ibanga (nka Nextcloud canke EteSync).


![Image](assets/fr/166.webp)



- [Simple Calendar](https://simplemobiletools.com/simplecalendar/)


Iyi porogarame iri mu bigize suite ya "*Simple Mobile Tools*". Nta konti canke kwibjira mu muhuhora bisaba, ivyo bikaba bituma ushobora gukora utari kuri interineti. Ushobora kwongerako amakuru y'ibizoba muri kazoza, gushirako ivyibutsa no gutunganya ivyerekanwa ku musi, ku ndwi canke ku kwezi. Cokimwe n'ibindi bice vyo muri suite, Simple Calendar nta kwamamaza, nta gukurikiranwa kandi 100% ni isoko yuguruye.


![Image](assets/fr/167.webp)



- [Tuta Calendar](https://tuta.com/calendar)


Tuta Calendar, yateguwe n'umugwi uri inyuma ya Tuta Mail, ni ikirangamisi kinyegeza amakuru impera kuyindi muburyo bukwiye cakorewe gutuma ibintu vyawe bib'ibanga. Ikora kuri Android, iOS ndetse biciye ku mukiriya w'urubuga(web client). Mbere n'amazina, ubusobanuro na metadata z'amakuru y'ibizoba muri kazoza vyose biranyegejwe, kugira ngo ntihaze hagire uwundi muntu, harimwo na Tuta, ashobora gushika ku makuru yawe.


![Image](assets/fr/168.webp)



- [Proton Calendar](https://proton.me/calendar)


Ikirangamisi ca Proton kandi gitanga uburyo bw'umwimerere bwo kunyegeza amakuru yawe impera kuyindi be na metadata zayo. Gishobora gukoreshwa kuri terefone ngendanwa (Android, iOS) no ku rubuga(web client), Gifise interface igaragara kandi ikora neza. Iyi serivisi irashoboza gukora ibirangamisi vyinshi, kwinjiza/gusohora ibintu n'uburyo bwo gusangiza. Umukiriya w'urubuga(web client) ni open-source, ariko porogarame zo kuri terefone ngendanwa ntiziraba open-source neza.


![Image](assets/fr/169.webp)


### Kwandika ivyiyumviro


porogarame nka Evernote, Google Keep canke OneNote zikoreshwa mu gufata ivyiyumviro, gutunganya ibikorwa canke kubika urutonde. Ariko rero, zose zizigira serivisi zo kuri interineti z'ifise banyezo, ivyo bikaba bishira amakuru yawe ku ma seriveri yabo kandi akenshi zigasuzuma ibirimwo kugira ngo bikoreshe mu bucuruzi.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Quillpad](https://quillpad.github.io/)


Quillpad ni porogarame iremurutse cane yagenewe canecane gufata ivyiyumviro hakoreshejwe Markdown. Bigufasha kunyegeza ivyiyumviro vyawe, gutunganya ibintu vyawe hakurikijwe ibimenyetso n'amabara, no kwongerako inyibutsa. Ivyo vyose birakora ata konti canke inzira bikenwe, kandi amakuru aguma abitswe ku gikoresho cawe. Bishobora kandi kubikwa mu buryo bunyegejwe kuri pCloud.


![Image](assets/fr/170.webp)



- [Joplin](https://joplinapp.org/)


Joplin ni umuti wikwije, utanga uguhuza ivyiyumviro vyawe binyegejwe na serivisi bihura nka Nextcloud, Dropbox canke WebDAV. Ushobora gucunga ivyiyumviro bisanzwe canke bitunganijwe (muri Markdown), gushira mu mice inyandiko zawe, mbere no kwinjiza amadosiye nivyo bifatanywa.


Interface yayo iragoye gatoyi kuruta iya QuillNote, ariko iracari nziza cane kuri terefone ngendanwa, kandi irabereye gukoreshwa ku giti cawe no ku kazi.


![Image](assets/fr/171.webp)


### ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga


Abakoresha benshi bareka mucukumbuzi zabo zikabika amajambo y'ibanga yabo biciye ku miti nka Google Password Manager. Naho bibereye, ubwo bwoko bw'uburongozi buhurikiye hamwe ntibutanga ububiko bunyegejwe impera kuyindi bugenzurwa n'ukoresha, kandi bushira ahabona amakuru yawe y'ibanga iyo konti yawe ya Google ishobora guhungabanywa. Kugira ngo ushobore gucunga amajambo y'ibanga yawe mu buryo butekanye kandi bubereye, hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo gukoresha.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Bitwarden](https://bitwarden.com/)


Bitwarden ni bumwe mu butunganirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga bw'isoko yuguruye bwinshi buriho uyu musi. bu nyegeza amakuru yawe yose yokwinjira aho nyene mu karere, bukaguha amajambo y'ibanga akomeye ya kozwe, kandi bugatanga uguhuza kunyegejwe hagati y'ibikoresho.


Ushobora gukoresha ama seriveri ya Bitwarden, canke ukitunganiriza wewe nyene nimba ushaka kuronka ububasha bwose bwo kugenzura. Interface ya terefone ngendanwa ira bona neza iratomoye kandi iragenda neza, ikaba ishobora gukorana neza na sisiteme ya Android canke iOS.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9


- [KeePassDX](https://www.keepassdx.com/)


KeePass ni ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga bw'amateka bushingiye ku madosiye anyegejwe yaho mu karere. Ku ri ngendanwa, KeePassDX ni uburyo bwiza cane bwo gukoresha kuri Android, bujanye n'urutonde rw'amakuru urwo ari rwo rwose rwa KeePass. Ikora bitagombereye ko uba uri kuri interineti, ata gicu, bikaba ari umuti mwiza ku bashaka ko amakuru yabo aguma ari 100% yo mu karere.


![Image](assets/fr/172.webp)


Hariho kandi [KeePassium](https://keepassium.com/) ya iOS, porogarame yinjijwe neza mu bikoresho vya Apple, ihuye n'uburyo bwa KeePass n'isoko yuguruye. Ubundi buro bwa iOS bw'umukiriya wa KeePass ni Strongbox, ariko iyi porogarame imaze imyaka myinshi itari open-source.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246


- [Proton Pass](https://proton.me/pass)


Yatangujwe n'umugwi wa Proton (uzwi cane kubera Proton Mail na Proton Drive, n'ibindi), Proton Pass ihuriza hamwe ukworohereza gukoresha, kunyegeza amakuru impera kuyindi be n'ibikorwavy'Ubusuwisi bifasha kubijanye n'ubuzima bw'ibanga. porogarame yo kuri terefone ngendanwa ntigoye, iratuma wongerako amajambo y'umutekano, kandi iremera auto-completion(ira kwuzuriza mugihe ugerageza kwandika). Ni uburyo bwiza cane ku bashaka umuti mpindura mateka, udafite ikibazo ku bijanye no gutunganya ivy'ubuhinga.


![Image](assets/fr/173.webp)


### VPN


VPNs (*Virtual Private Network*) zigufasha kunyegeza uruja n'uruza rwa interineti yawe  maze rukarungikwa kuri seriveri iri hagati ya kure. Ivyo binyegeza aderese IP yawe, bigakingira inzira yawe ku mihora ya rusangi (Wi-Fi kubibuga vy'indege, ama café...) kandi bikakurinda uburyo bumwe bumwe bwo gucungerwa.


Ariko rero, si VPN zose zaremwe zingana. Serivisi zikunzwe cane nka NordVPN canke ExpressVPN zikora neza, ariko uburyo bwazo bw'ibanda ku rundandazwa, n'ikigereranyo gishingiye ku gukurikirana abakoresha kugira ngo ubucuruzi bwazo bube bwiza. Bisaba kandi gukora konti kandi kenshi zikorakoranya amakuru menshi gusumvya.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Mullvad VPN](https://mullvad.net/)


Mullvad ni imwe mu VPN nziza cane mu bijanye no kurinda ubuzima bw'ibanga. Nta imeyiri canke ijambo ry'ibanga bisaba: Konti yawe ihuye n'igiharuro icarico cose. Kuriha bishobora gukorwa hifashishijwe bitcoins canke mu mafaranga. Client ya terefone ngendanwa ni open-source, iroroshe gukoresha kandi ifise ububasha budasanzwe. Mullvad nta makuru y'ivyabaye ibika, ntikurikirana abayikoresha, kandi ihora isohora igenzurwa ry'umutekano ryigenga.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8


- [IVPN](https://www.ivpn.net/)


IVPN ni ubundi buryo bwiza cane bwibanda ku buzima bw'ibanga. Itanga interface yoroheje kandi ikora neza, nta makuru y'ivyabaye ishobora gukorakoranya, kandi biremewe kwiyandikisha ata makuru yawe utanze. Ushobora kandi kwishura mu ma bitcoins. Iyi porogarame irimwo firewall (uruhome rw'umuriro) ruzibira uruja n'uruza rwose rutari urwa VPN, rushobora kuba ingirakamaro cane kuri terefone ngendanwa. Clients zose ni open-source.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68


- [Proton VPN](https://protonvpn.com/)


Iyi VPN yateguwe n'umugwi wa Proton, itanga umugambi w'ubuntu, ata kwamamaza. Proton VPN ikorera mu Busuwisi, ikurikiza amategeko akomeye agenga ivy'ubuzima bw'ibanga, kandi itangaza igenzurwa ryayo kenshi. Clients nazo nyene ni open-source.


![Image](assets/fr/174.webp)


### Ivyemezo bibiri 2FA


Ivyemezo bibiri (2FA) ni ubundi buryo bw'inyongera bw'umutekano hanyuma y'ijambo ry'ibanga ryawe. Akenshi bishingiye kuri kode y'igihe gito ikorwa buri misegonda 30 na porogarame zo kwemeza. Iyi kode ishingiye kw'ibanga risangiwe hagati y'igikoresho cawe na serivisi yo kuri interineti, hakurikijwe umurongo wa TOTP (*Time-based One-Time Password*). porogarame izwi cane ni Google Authenticator, ariko ntabwo ari open-source kandi ivyo bigatuma wizigira ikibikoresho vya Google.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Aegis Authenticator](https://getaegis.app/)


Aegis ni porogarame y'isoko yuguruye yuzuye. Inyegeza urutonde rwawe rwa 2FA n'ijambo ry'ibanga, itanga backup zishobora kwoherezwa hanze (kandi nyene zinyegejwe), kandi ikagufasha kurobanura amakonti yawe hakurikijwe ububiko. interface iratomoye, igezweko kandi yoroshe gusubirazamwo ku gikoresho gishasha, igihe cose ufise dosiye ya backup n'ijambo ry'ibanga rijanye na yo.


![Image](assets/fr/175.webp)



- [Ente Auth](https://ente.io/auth/)


Ente Auth ni umuti ugezweko, wa open-source, ukoreshwa ku mbuga nyinshi ufise backup zinyegejwe impera kuyindi. Uragufasha gukoranya amakode yawe ya 2FA mu buryo butekanye kuri terefone ngendanwa, ku nyabwonko no ku rubuga. Ushobora kandi kuyikoresha utari kuri interineti, hadakenewe ko ugira cloud backup canke kurema konti.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/ente-auth-1928e65a-3b43-40f3-9efd-457ee2d79bb9
Ente Auth itanga ibintu vyinshi vy'inyongera: Gutunganya hakurikijwe ibimenyetso, ibicapo vya serivisi zose, ivyiyumviro, ivyo ukunda, ubushakashatsi buhuriweko, gusangira kode n'umugwi bitekanye.


![Image](assets/fr/176.webp)



- [Authy](https://www.authy.com/)


Authy itanga uburyo bwa 2FA bwoguhuza ku bikoresho vyinshi, bishobora kuba vyiza, ariko porogarame ntabwo ari open-source kandi isaba inomero ya terefone kugira ngo umuntu yiyandikishe. Ariko rero, ku batangura, iratunganye kuruta Google Authenticator, cane cane kubera igikorwa cayo ca cloud backup.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/authy-a76ab26b-71b0-473c-aa7c-c49153705eb7

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/proton-authenticator-047ca2eb-a922-4e0e-8f75-1b89d23951ae
Nimba wifuza kumenya vyinshi ku bijanye n'ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga, kwemeza na 2FA na VPNs, ndagusaba gusoma ibice bijanye n'ivyo vy'icigwa ca SCU-101:


https://planb.academy/courses/99c46148-7080-4915-a7e0-9df0e145cd47

### Ikirere


Porogarame za kera z'ikirere nka AccuWeather canke Météo France akenshi zikusanya amakuru y'ibanga, harimwo n'aho uri nyaho, ingeso rimwe na rimwe mbere n'ibimenyetso vy'ibikoresho, ku ntumbero z'ubucuruzi canke zo kwamamaza. Izo serivisi kandi zishingiye ku ma API zicungirwa hamwe kandi zifise ba nyenezo, bigabanya ububasha ufise ku makuru yerekanwa canke arungikwa.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Geometric Weather](https://github.com/WangDaYeeeeee/GeometricWeather)


Geometric Weather itanga iteganyagihe riziguye n'ibikoresho bishobora guhindurwa, vyose ata kwamamaza canke gukorakoranya amakuru. Kode yayo ni open-source. Iyo porogarame ikorana na serivisi nyinshi zikora ivy'iteganyabihe.


![Image](assets/fr/177.webp)



[Prognoza](https://github.com/davidtakac/prognoza)


Prognoza ni porogarame yoroheje irasa ku  ntego: Kwerekana ibihe biriko n'iteganyagihe. Itanga ibikoresho vyinshi. Prognoza nta kwamamaza igira, nta n'ugukurikirana kandi nta burenganzira bw'ikirenga isaba.


![Image](assets/fr/178.webp)



- [Forecastie](https://github.com/martykan/forecastie)


Porogarame y'ikirere yoroheje, ishingiye kuri OpenWeatherMap, ni open-source, ishobora guhindurwa, ifise ibikoresho vy'utuntu n'utundi.


![Image](assets/fr/179.webp)


Muri rusangi, kuri porogarame z'ikirere, ni vyiza gutunganya n'amaboko ahantu ushaka kuruta gukoresha uburyo bwishirako bwo kugaragaza aho uri.


### Streaming amajwi/amasanamu


Imbuga zikundwa cane nka Spotify canke YouTube zitanga uburyo bwiza bwogukoresha, ariko ivyo bikaba bifise igiciro c'uguhungabanya ubuzima bw'ibanga. Izo serivisi ziguma zegeranya yerekeye inyifato: Amateka yo kuraba canke kwumviriza, umwanya umaze, ivyo ukunda, igikoresho ukoresha. Aya makuru akenshi akoreshwa mu gutanga urutonde canke mu gutora abantu.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [LibreTube](https://libretube.dev/)


LibreTube ni porogarame ya Android ishobora kugufasha kuraba amasanamu ya YouTube ata Google igukurikirana. Ivyo usaba vyose birungikwa biciye ku nzira ya seriveri ya proxy, iyo na yo ikaba ituma umuntu adashobora kumenyekana igihe ashika ku masanamu. Ifise interface igezweko, iranyaruka kandi nta kwamamaza igira. porogarame nta konti ya Google isaba, kandi iragufasha kwiyandikisha ku mihora canke gukora urutonde rw'indirimbo zo mu karere.


![Image](assets/fr/180.webp)



- [NewPipe](https://newpipe.net/)


NewPipe ni uwundi mukiriya wa YouTube. Iraremurutse, nta kwamamaza, nta gukurikiranwa kandi yose ni open-source, iragufasha kuraba, kuvoma canke kwumviriza amasanamu kuri YouTube (n'izindi mbuga nk SoundCloud canke PeerTube) mu nyuma. Nta guhuza na Google bikenewe. NewPipe ikora yigenga ntaho ihuriye na porogarame ya YouTube, kandi ntibisaba serivisi za Google kugira ngo ikore.



- [VLC Android](https://www.videolan.org/vlc/download-android.html)


Igikoresho gikundwa cane ca VLC kiraboneka no kuri Android. Ishigikira uburyo bwinshi bw'amajwi n'amasanamu, kandi iragufasha gukina amadosiye mu karere canke ku rubuga, vyose ata kwamamaza canke gukorakoranya amakuru. Ni umuti mwiza cane wo gucunga ububiko bwawe bwite bwa multimedia mu karere, ata guhuza na serivisi y'uwundi muntu.


![Image](assets/fr/181.webp)



- [Funkwhale](https://funkwhale.audio/):


Funkwhale ni urubuga rwigenga rwo gusangira no kwumviriza umuziki, na clients zihuye.


### Keyboard


Keyboard mpimbano nka Gboard ya Google canke SwiftKey ya Microsoft biri hose kuri terefone ngendanwa. Ariko rero, biratera ingorane zikomeye mu buzima bw'ibanga: Urudome rwose rwanditswe rurashobora kwandikwa, gusesangurwa canke kurungikwa kuri seriveri za kure. Naho ayo mashirahamwe yovuga ko atamenyekanisha ayo makuru, gukorakoranya amakuru birashoboka.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [OpenBoard](https://github.com/dslul/openboard)


OpenBoard ni keyboard ya Android ya open-source, ishingiye kuri keyboard ya AOSP (*Android open-source Project*). Nta bintu birimwo vy'abantu canke ugukurikiranwa, kandi ntivugana na seriveri ya kure. Gukosora, kuzuza n'inkoranyamajambo y'umuntu ku giti ciwe bikora aho mu karere gusa.



- [FlorisBoard](https://florisboard.org/)


FlorisBoard itanga uburyo bugezweko, bw'ibice bice. Kandi ni open-source, ihuriza hamwe ibikorwa biteye imbere nk'ugushiramwo ibimenyetso, ugushiraho uburyo bw'ihariye bw'idome n'ugucungera indimi nyinshi. Ibikorwa vyose vyerekeye amakuru bikorerwa aho nyene, bitagombereye interineti ata guhuza n'ama seriveri yo hanze. FlorisBoard iracariko irategurwa, ariko irakoreshwa neza ku musi ku musi ku bashaka keyboard ikomeye badatakaje ubuzima bw'ibanga bwabo.


![Image](assets/fr/182.webp)


### Calculator


Porogarame ya Google Calculator, naho ikora neza, iracari igicuruzwa ca Google kandi izana n'ingorane zisanzwe zijanye n'ugukorakoranya amakuru no kwizigira ikibanza kihurikiye hamwe.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [OpenCalc](https://github.com/Darkempire78/OpenCalc)


OpenCalc ni calculator yihuta kandi yoroshe gukoresha, gihuye neza n'ivyo umuntu akeneye buri musi. Nta makuru akorakoranywa kandi ikora bitagombereye interineti, nta kwamamaza canke kwizigira serivisi iyo ari yo yose yo hanze.


![Image](assets/fr/183.webp)


### Iduka rya porogarame


Iduka rya Google Play ni ryo soko ry'ama porogarame ku materefone menshi ya Android. Ariko rero, ifatanye cane na serivisi za Google kandi ijana n'ugukorakoranya amakuru mu buryo butunganye, mbere no mu gihe co kurondera canke gushira kugihe ibintu vyoroshe.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [F-Cold](https://f-droid.org/)


F-Droid ni urutonde rwa porogarame z'isoko y'uguruye gusa. porogarame zose ziriho zirashobora gusuzumwa no gukurwako ku buntu, ata kwamamaza, gukurikiranwa canke kwizigira serivisi za Google. porogarame ya F-Droid ubwayo nta konti y'ukoresha isaba.


![Image](assets/fr/184.webp)



- [Aurora Store](https://auroraoss.com/)


Iduka rya Aurora rigufasha gushika ku rutonde rw'iduka rya Google Play utamenyekanye, ata konti ya Google. Ni client y'ubuntu ikorana na seriveri za Google, mu gihe inyegeza akaranga kawe biciye kuri konti rusangi. Ni umuti w'agaciro wo kubandanya ukoresha ibintu bimwe bimwe bikenewe vy'umuntu: porogarame, mu gihe wirinda Google Play telemetry.


### Amakuru


Porogarame ya Google News, naho ikora kandi igenewe umuntu, yizigiye kugusuzuma neza ivyo ukunda, amateka y'ivyo urondera n'ingeso zo gusoma kugira ngo itunganye impanuro iguha. Ivyo birimwo kwegeranya amakuru menshi yerekeye umuntu, akenshi akoreshwa mu kwamamaza.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [News](https://github.com/bubelov/news)


Porogarame ya *News*, yateguwe na Bubelov, itanga uburyo butandukanye cane. Ni RSS reader yoroheje, yagenewe kurondera amakuru ata gukurikiranwa kubayeko, kwamamaza canke ubuhinga bwo gutanga impanuro butaboneka. Ushobora guhitamwo n'amaboko amasoko yawe (itangazamakuru, ama blogs, podcasts, ibinyamakuru vyigenga, n'ibindi), bikaguha gusoma ataco winona, mw'ibanga. Yubatse neza ntabintu vyinshi biriko, ibivugwa kumakuru biza birishira ku gihe, kandi nta makuru ashikirizwa abandi.


### Porogarame y'abanywanyi


Google Contacts, nk'ibindi bikoresho vyinshi bikoreshwa kuri Android, bihuza ibitabu vyawe vya aderese za banywanyi bawe n'seriveri za Google. Ivyo bisigura ko amakuru yose y'abantu ushobora guhamagara (amazina, inomero, ubutumwa bwo kuri interineti, rimwe na rimwe ama aderesi y'iposita canke amafoto) abikwa kuri interineti kandi afitaniye isano na konti yawe. Ukwo gushirahamwe bifasha gukora ububiko bw'inyongera no guhuza, ariko bivyura ibibazo bikomeye vy'ubuzima bw'ibanga.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Connect You](https://github.com/you-apps/ConnectYou)


Connect You ni uburyo bundi buremurutse, butagiramwo ibintu vyinshi, kandi buri open-source bugenewe abashaka gucunga abanywanyi babo, bitagombereye interinet nta gukorakoranya amakuru canke gukorana n'igicu c'uwundi muntu (third-party cloud) ku nguvu. Itanga interface yoroshe, ituma vyoroha gurobanura, kurondera no guhindura ivyo winjije, kandi ishobora gukorana na serivisi ya CalDAV nimba uriko ukoresha seriveri yabanywanyi witunganirije (biciye muri Nextcloud, nk'akarorero).


### ubutunganyirizo bw'amafoto


Google photo ni meza cane mu kubika amashusho mu gicu, kuyatunganya canke kuyaronka biciye mu kumenya isura. Ariko ukwo kworoha guhisha uburyo amakuru yawe akoreshwa mu buryo bubereye: Ishusho yose irasesangurwa, igashirwa mu rutonde kandi igahuzwa n'ayandi makuru yawe ya Google. Amafoto yawe arashobora kuba isoko y'inyongera y'amakuru, akoreshwa mu vy'ubudandaji.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Simple Gallery](https://github.com/SimpleMobileTools/Simple-Gallery)


Simple Gallery ni porogarame yoroheje y'isoko yuguruye ikora bitagombereye interineti. Ni kimwe mu bigize *Simple Mobile Tools*. Iragufasha gucunga, kurobanura, kuraba no guhindura amashusho yawe ata makuru ava ku gikoresho cawe. Irafise kandi retouching, gukingira ijambo ry'ibanga nahaja ivya fuswe. Nta gukurikiranwa, nta guhuza ku nguvu: Amafoto yawe agumana nawe.



- [Aves](https://github.com/deckerst/aves)


Aves ni ubundi buryo bufise interface igezweko. Itanga uburyo bwo kugendagenda neza mu migwi ya amafoto(album) n'imitunganirize iteye imbere (ibimenyetso, utuyunguruzo, kurobanura, n'ibindi). Nta nzira ya interineti isabwa kugira ngo ikore, kandi nta makuru y'abayikoresha yegeranywa.


![Image](assets/fr/185.webp)



- [Ente Photos](https://ente.io/)


Ente Photos ni serivisi y'isoko yuguruye (clients + seriveri) igufasha kurema backup zinyegejwe impera kuyindi ubwayo bidasavye ko ugira ico ukoze. Amashusho yawe aranyegezwa ku gikoresho imbere y'uko yoherezwa, kugira ngo mbere na seriveri za Ente ntizishobore kuyaronka. Ente kandi itanga verisiyo aho ushobora kwitunganiriza ku bakoresha binzobere.


![Image](assets/fr/186.webp)



- [Stingle Photos](https://stingle.org/)


Stingle ni ikibanza co gushiramwo amafoto ikaba na porogarame ya kamera, bifatanijwe na serivise zigufasha gukora backup zinyegejwe. Cokimwe na Ente, amafoto arakingirwa na end-to-end encryption(E2EE). Ushobora gukoresha serivisi yabo ya cloud batanga (1 GB ku buntu) canke ukitunganiriza seriveri ya Stingle yawe kugira ngo uronko ubu basha bukwiye bwo kuyigenzure yose. interface iroroshe, nta n'amatangazo canke gukurikiranwa biriko.


![Image](assets/fr/187.webp)


### Umusomyi wa PDF


**Uburyo bundi**:


Adobe Acrobat Reader, ikoreshwa cane mu gusoma canke gutanga insiguro ku nyandiko za PDF, izana n'ibikorwa vyinshi vyo kuri interineti bishobora gushikiriza amakuru yawe: Telemetry ikora, guhuza n'igicu kwegeranya amakuru ku madosiye yawe canke ingeso zo gusoma.



- [MuPDF Viewer](https://f-droid.org/en/packages/com.artifex.mupdf.viewer.app/)


MuPDF Viewer ni igikoresho co gusoma PDF kiremurutse cane, cihuta kandi ca open-source. Ikoresha uburyo bukeyi bwa sisiteme. Naho idatanga ibintu bihambaye cane nko gushirako insiguro canke gusinya, ikora akazi kayo neza cane: Kwerekan'inyandiko zawe, ata gutatwa.



- [MJ PDF Reader](https://gitlab.com/mudlej_android/mj_pdf_reader)


MJ PDF Reader ni porogarame yoroheje, ya open-source, ituma ushobora gusoma amadosiye ya PDF ata kwamamaza canke gufatanya na konti yo kuri interineti.


### Terefone


Porogarame ya Google yitwa Phone, ishirwa ku materefone menshi y'ubuhinga bwa Android, ikora neza ariko ikorakoranya amakuru menshi y'ukungene ikoreshwa.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Koler](https://github.com/Chooloo/koler)


Koler ni porogarame y'amaterefone ya open-source yakozwe kugira ngo ibe isa neza, yoroshe gukoresha kandi ikubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga. Itanga interface igenda neza kandi ishobora gukoreshwa neza mu gucunga uko uhamagara, ata gukurikiranwa canke gusesangura amakuru y'umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ariko rero, ubu ntabwo harimwo ukuyungurura guteye imbere igihe uhamagara canke gufatanya na serivise z'abandi.


![Image](assets/fr/188.webp)


### Guhindura indimi


Google Translate ni co kigereranyo mu guhindura indimi, ariko uko ikoresha mu buryo butegekanijwe birimwo kohereza ibibazo vyawe vyose kuri Google, n'ugukurikirana kwubakiyemwo n'ugukorakoranya amakuru y'agaciro (Ivyanditswe vyahinduwe, amateka, n'ibindi).


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [TranslateYou](https://github.com/you-apps/TranslateYou)


TranslateYou ni porogarame ya open-source y'ubahiriza ubuzima bw'ibanga bw'abayikoresha. Ikora nka interface ya moteri zitandukanye z'uguhindura indimi (LibreTranslate, LingvaTranslate, Mozhi, DeepL, n'ibindi), kandi ikagufasha guhitamwo serivice idakoresha nabi amakuru yawe.


Nta kwamamaza, nta gukurikirana, interface yoroshe gukoresha bituma TranslateYou iba ubundi buryo bwiza kuri Google Translate.


![Image](assets/fr/189.webp)


### Igikoresho co gupima mu buryo bw'ifoto igicuruzwa


Yuka ikoreshwa cane mu gupima ibifungurwa n'ibintu vyo kwisiga bijanye n'ubwiza no gusuzuma umwimerere wavyo, ariko ishingiye ku kigereranyo kitaboneka, gifise ingingo ngenderwako ziteye amakenga, igice c'urutonde rw'amakuru c'umuntu kandi ikaba itari open-source. Ikindi, ibikorwa vyayo bisaba guhuzwa na seriveri, n'ubushobozi bwo gukorakoranya amakuru y'ikoreshwa.


**Uburyo bundi**:



 [OpenFoodFacts](https://world.openfoodfacts.org/open-food-facts-mobile-app)


OpenFoodFacts ni uburyo bundi bukorera mu muco kandi kandi bushira imbere ubuzima bw'ibanga. Uyu mugambi w'ubufatanye w'isoko yuguruye utanga urutonde rw'amakuru kw'isi yose, rugaburirwa n'intererano z'abakoresha. Amakuru yerekeye ingaburo, ibirungo n'ibimenyetso bishobora gushikirizwa mu buryo buciye mu muco, ata gukorakoranya amakuru muburyo butaribwo.


Porogarame ya terefone ngendanwa ituma ushobora gupima amakode y'imirongo, ugaca ubona amakuru ajanye nico gicuruzwa, kandi nawe ubwawe ugatanga umusanzu ku rutonde rw'amakuru. Ni ubuntu gukoresha, ata kwamamaza canke gukurikiranwa.


### Gusangira hafi


Ibikorwa nka Quick Share (Android) canke AirDrop (iOS/macOS) bigufasha kohereza amadosiye hagati y'ibikoresho biri hafi biciye ku Bluetooth no kuri Wi-Fi ako kanya, bitagombereye interineti. Birakora, ariko bishingiye ku ma sisiteme yugaye, rimwe na rimwe ihuye n'amakonti ya Google, Samsung canke Apple.


Quick Share ubu ni umuringo ngenderwako kuri Android. Iyi porogarame, yashizweho ubwa mbere na Samsung, yashizwe hamwe mu mwaka w'2024 na Nearby Share ya Google, bituma haba porogarame imwe yo gusangira amadosiye kuri Android.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Snapdrop](https://github.com/SnapDrop/snapdrop)


Snapdrop ni uburyo bundi bwa open-source kandi ku buntu bidakenewe ko urinda kuyishiramwo. Igufasha gusangira amadosiye hagati y'ibikoresho bihuriye ku muhora umwe, biciye kuri mucukumbuzi. Kurungika no kwakira ni ako kanya (peer-to-peer) kandi amakuru ntashobora guca kuri server iri kure.


Iyindi nzira iryoshe cane ni [PairDrop](https://github.com/schlagmichdoch/pairdrop) (Fork ya Snapdrop), itanga ibintu bikeyi vy'inyongera.



- [Warpinator](https://github.com/linuxmint/warpinator)


Warpinator, yakozwe na Linux Mint, ituma vyoroha gutanga amadosiye hagati y'ibikoresho bihuriye ku muhora umwe wa Wi-Fi. Ikora peer-to-peer, bitagombereye cloud canke seriveri y'abandi, ifise interface yoroshe. Hariho uburyo bwa Android, butuma amadosiye ashobora guhererekanwa hagati ya terefone n'inyabwonko.



- [LocalSend](https://localsend.org/)


LocalSend ni ubundi buryo bwo ku buntu, bufise ubushobozi bwose bufise interface isanzwe. Iyi porogarame yose ni open-source, ishobora gutuma habaho uburyo bukwiragijwe bwo kunyegeza impera ku yindi amadosiye ashobora guhererekanwa hagati y'ibikoresho bihuriye ku muhora umwe wo mu karere. Nta serveri zo hagati zikoreshwa, kugira ngo amakuru yawe ntazokwigera ava ku muhora wawe wo muhira.


![Image](assets/fr/190.webp)


### Books


Ama porogarame nka Goodreads, naho akoreshwa cane, aravyura ibibazo bikomeye vy'ubuzima bw'ibanga. Uru rubuga nufiswe na Amazon, ikoranya amakuru atari make ku vyo usoma, ivyo ukunda, ivyo ubona n'ivyo usubiramwo. Ikindi, interface yizigira cane gukurikirana abakoresha no gusuzuma inyifato yabo ku ntumbero z'ubucuruzi.


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Openreads](https://github.com/mateusz-bak/openreads)


Openreads ni uburyo bw'uguruye bwo gukurikirana ibisomwa bw'ubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga. Iyi porogarame iragufasha gukora ububiko bw'ibitabu bwawe bwite, gukurikirana ingene usoma, gupima no gutanga ivyiyumviro ku bitabu, no kuronka impanuro zishingiye ku ngingo zawe bwite, ata gusuzuma canke gukurikiranira hamwe. Amakuru yose aguma ku gikoresho cawe canke ahuzwa biciye kuri serivisi zo kwitunganyiriza.


### Isaha, inkengeri n'ingengabihe


**Uburyo bundi**:



- [Chrono](https://github.com/vicolo-dev/chrono)


Iboneka kuri F-Droid kandi ikaba ari open-source, Chrono itanga interface igezweko, idafise ibintu vyinshi, ata kwamamaza canke gukorakoranya amakuru. Bigufasha gushirako inyibutsa y'inkengeri uko ubishaka: Izokwisubiramwo hakurikijwe imisi canke amatariki yihariye, guhitamwo ijwi, umwanya izomara, canke mbere ibikorwa vyo gukora kugira ngo inkengeri izimye (Gutorera umuti igiharuro, gusubira gusoma icanditswe, n'ibindi).


Iyo porogarame ifise igenabihe n'isaha ihagarara (timer na stopwatch), n'ugufata ikiringo c'ibihe, ivyegeranyo, kugereranya igihe n'ugucungera ibihe bigiye bitandukanye. Ushobora gutunganya amasaha menshi, ugahindura uko igaragara (amabara, imiterere, amashusho), mbere ugatunganya inkengeri zawe n'igenabihe vyawe bifise ibimenyetso.


Kugira ngo ushobore gutohoza neza ivy'iyi nsanganya matsiko, ndagusaba kugenderera uru rubuga [*Ubuzima bw'ibanga buhebuje*](https://awesome-privacy.xyz/), rufise urutonde rw'ibintu vyiza kuruta ibindi vyose bishobora gukoreshwa mu gukingira ubuzima bw'ibanga kuruta porogarame ukoresha ku musi ku musi.

___


⚠️ ***Niwiyubare**: Naho uburyo bundi buvugwa muri iki gice ahanini ari ubw'isoko y'uguruye kandi bushingiye ku kubahiriza ubuzima bw'ibanga, si ukuvugako butagira aho bugarukira canke ingorane. Bumwe bwoshobora kuba butakibungabungwa, bukagira integenke canke utunenge tutavuzwe, bukazoteba bukaba ubw'umuntu canke mbere, hakazoziramwo porogarame mbi. bimwe bimwe vyoshobora kandi kuba bitemewe n'amategeko mu karere iwanyu. Nanditse iki gice muri Ruheshi 2025, ariko birashobora kuba vyarahindutse kuva ico gihe.*


Ikindi kandi, jewe ubwanje sinasuzumye kode ya buri gikoresho cose cavuzwe, kandi impanuro zanje ntizikwiye na gato gufatwa nk'ivyemezo vy'ukuri. Ni ngombwa rero ko umuntu wese akora ubushakashatsi bwiwe bwite imbere yo gukoresha izo porogarame.


___


# Gukingira umuhora wawe wo mu karere(aho hagufi)


<partId>23e49e48-34c9-435c-a36f-1c86b0254275</partId>


## Gutahura neza umuhora wawe wo muhira


<chapterId>8a7577e0-4a27-4331-a6d9-7a4c838fa720</chapterId>


Umutekano w'ubuhinga bwa none akenshi utangurana n'ukumenya neza umuhora wawe wo muhira. Igikoresho cawe co muhira ni co kintu ca mbere interineti yinjiramwo mugushika mu kibanza cawe bwite, kandi ni co gitera ingorane nyinshi umutekano wawe n'ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe.


Gutahura ingene umuhora wawe wo mu karere ukora, ingene amakuru yawe agenda n'ibikoresho bijejwe gucunga ayo makuru ni ikintu gihambaye cane ku busegaba bwawe bw'ubuhinga bwa none.


Muri iki gice, tuzokwihweza buhoro buhoro ivyiyumviro vy'ishimikiro vy'gukoresha umuhoro wo muhira, kuva ku nsiguro y'ico interineti ari co gushika ku bintu vy'ukuri nk'ugutanga ama aderesi IP yo mu karere n'uruhara rwa router. Intumbero ni ugusubira ku vyiyumviro vy'ishimikiro bihambaye kugira ngo umuntu atahure neza igice gikurikira, kizovuga ku bintu vyinshi vyo gukora n'amaboko.


### Interineti


#### Incamake ku mateka ya interineti


Amateka ya interineti asubira mu mpera z'imyaka y'1960, mu gihe c'ubushakashatsi bwa siyansi n'ubw'igisirikare. Umugambi wa mbere, witwa "ARPANET", watangujwe n'ishirahamwe ry'Abanyamerika ARPA (ubu ryitwa DARPA) kugira ngo bahuze ibibanza vyinshi vy'ubushakashatsi, kugirango bashobore gusangira uburyo n'ibikoresho.


![Image](assets/fr/191.webp)


Intumbero yari kandi iyo guhingura umuhora ushobora gukomera, ushobora kubandanya ukora naho igice kimwe cawo coba casambutse (ivyo vyari bikenewe hagati mu ntambara ya y'ubutita canke Cold War). ARPANET ni yo yatumye habaho uguhanahana amakuru kwa mbere hagati y'inyabwonko ziri kure na kure mu 1969.


![Image](assets/fr/192.webp)


Mu myaka icumi irenga, uwo mugambi waragutse, cane cane mu gutuma amategeko ya TCP/IP ashirwa ku rugero rumwe akaba ngenderwako mu 1983, ivyo bikaba vyacitse umushinge w'ubuhinga rusangi wa interineti yose. Mu myaka y'1990, ukuza kwa *World Wide Web*, twavuganye mu gice ca banje, kwatumye abantu bose bashobora gukoresha interineti mu kworohereza abantu kuronka inyandiko biciye kuri mucukumbuzi. Iyo mpinduka ikomeye yahinduye interineti mwo igikoresho co gutumatumanako no kuronka amakuru kubantu bose.


#### interineti ni iki?


interineti, bisobanura "umuhora ufatanye" (interconnected network), ni ibikorwa n'ibikoresho vyo kw'isi yose bishoboza ama miriyaridi y'ibikoresho guhanahana amakuru. Si serivisi imwe, canke ahantu kanaka, ahubwo ni ihuriro ry'imihora y'inyabwonko rusangi n'iy'abikorera ku giti cabo, ihuye ku rugero rw'imibumbe. Buri mukinyi (umuntu ku giti ciwe, ishirahamwe, ubutegetsi bwa Leta, n'ibindi) arashobora gufatanya umuhora wiwe n'isi yose, igihe gusa yubahiriza amategeko amwamwe y'ubuhinga agezweko atuma ibikoresho bishobora gutahurana.


Ibikorwa n'ibikoresho vya interineti bishingiye ahanini ku masezerano abiri:



- **IP** (*Internet protocol*) Akaranga ka buri gikoresho cose kiri ku muhora kandi kirungika packets y'amakuru.
- **TCP** (*Transmission Control Protocol*) Icamwo ibice uruja n'uruza, igenzura amakosa maze igasubiza ibice mu murongo uko vyagomvye gukurikirana.


→ Ku bikorwa vy'igihe nyaco aho ukwizigirwa ata gaciro kanini bifise kuruta kurindiriza (VoIP, DNS, streaming, n'ibindi), akenshi hakoreshwa uwundi murongo wo gutwara  aho gukoresha TCP: UDP (*User Datagram Protocol*).


Ayo mategeko abiri arakorana kugira ngo ubutumwa bwoherezwa buva ahantu hamwe buja ahandi bushike bushitse kandi bukurikirana kumurongo.


Mu majambo nyayo, iyo ugendereye urubuga, nk'akarorero mu kwandika aderese muri mucukumbuzi yawe, ibikorwa vyinshi biratangura inyuma. Ubwa mbere, inyabwonko yawe canke terefone yawe ngendanwa itegerezwa guhindura aderese isomwa (nk'iyitwa `planb.network`) ikayigira aderese IP, ikoresheje igikorwa citwa DNS (*Domain Name System*). Iyo aderese IP ya seriveri y'urubuga imaze kwononekara, ayo makuru arashobora kwoherezwa aho aja.


Ayo makuru rero akaca akurikira inzira igoye. Ubwa mbere, ica muri router yawe yo mu muhira na modem, imbere y'uko ishika ku bikorwa n'ibikoresho vya ISP yawe. avuye ngaho, arashobora kujabuka imihora myinshi iri hagati (rimwe na rimwe intsinga zica mu nyanja, ama routeur y'inzira, aha hana hanirwa amakuru ya interineti, n'ibindi) imbere y'uko ashika aho aja: Seriveri y'urubuga wipfuza kugenderera. Nayo nyene ica irungika amakuru (ibirigize rubuga) mu cerekezo kinyuranye.


![Image](assets/fr/193.webp)


Interineti rero irashobora gusobanurwa mu ncamake nk'umuhora munini cane uri mu migwi yigenga, ushingiye ku mategeko rusangi, aho igikoresho cose gishobora kuvugana n'ikindi, aho coba kiri hose kw'isi. Ariko naho ukwo Kwuguruka gutuma habaho uguhanahana amakuru y'ubuhinga bwa none, bisaba kandi ko ufata ingingo yo kwiyubara: Igikorwa cose ukora kuri interineti gica mu bikorwa n'ibikoresho udashobora kugenzura, kandi ibanga ry'uguhanahana amakuru yawe rivana n'ingene utunganya ivyo bikoresho no kubikoresha.


### Uruhara rwa modem na router


Mu mihana myinshi yo muri iki gihe, umuntu ashobora gukoresha interineti biciye ku gikoresho co hagati gikora nka modem na router. Izina ry'iki gikoresho ritandukanye ku gihugu ku kindi (mu Bufaransa, citwa "Interineti Box"). Ico gikoresho gikora vyinshi gitangwa na ISP ni co kiguhuza n'ibindi bikoresho vyo kuri interineti.


→ *ISP = Internet Service Provider canke mukirundi abatanga serivisi za interineti.*


Iki gikoresho gihuza ibikorwa 2 nyamukuru:



- **Uruhara rwa modem**


Modem (mu ncamake "*modulator-demodulator*") ni co gice gihuza umuhora wa ISP yawe n'inzu yawe. Ihindura sinyare ziza nkumuyagankuba canke nk'urumuri zakiriwe (biciye mu nzira ya fiber optic, coaxial, ADSL canke umuhora wa terefone ngendanwa) mwo sinyare y'ubuhinga bwa none ishobora gutahurwa n'ibikoresho vyawe. Ku rundi ruhande, ihindura amakuru ava mu bikoresho vyawe mu buryo bushobora gutuma aca mu bikorwa n'ibikoresho vy'uwuguha umuhora. Iyo ntambwe ni ngirakamaro nimba umuhora wawe wo muhira uzovugana na interineti.



- **Uruhara rwa router**


Router ni umutima w'umuhora wawe wo mu karere. Itanga inzira ishika kuri interineti ku bikoresho vyawe vyose: inyabwonko, amaterefone ngendanwa, ibikoresho bihuye, amacapiro, n'ibindi. Iha kimwe cose muri vyo aderese (Itandukanye n'IP yawe ya rusangi iboneka kuri interineti). Router ica itunganya uruja n'uruza, kugira ngo amakuru ashike ku gikoresho nyaco. Ishobora kandi kuba ifise firewall, ikayungurura packets z'umuhora canke gucunga amategeko ya port forwarding. NAT inyegeza umuhora wawe wo mu karere kuri interineti, ikoresheje aderese IP imwe ya rusangi kugira ngo iserukire ibikoresho vyawe vyose. Router yonyene ni yo izi igikoresho co mu karere catanguje igisabwa.


Mu bihugu bimwe bimwe, ivyo bikorwa bibiri rimwe na rimwe biragabanywa hagati y'ibikoresho bibiri bitandukanye: Modem na router.


Mu bikorwa, routeur ya modem igezweko akenshi irimwo ibindi bikorwa vy'inyongera: Wi-Fi access point, switch ya Ethernet, interface y'uburongozi, rimwe na rimwe mbere na seriveri y'amadosiye n'ibindi.


Gutahura uruhara rwa router-modem ni ikintu nyamukuru mu gukingira umuhora wawe wo mu karere. Mu buryo, ico gikoresho gikora urubibi hagati y'isi yo hanze (interineti) n'ikibanza cawe c'ibanga c'ubuhinga bwa none. Gutunganya nabi, amajambo y'ibanga agoyagoya canke sisiteme itagikoreshwa bishobora guhindura iri rembo rikaba ikinogo cuguruye. Ku rundi ruhande, modem-router itunganijwe neza iba uruhome rwo gukingira abayitera.


Mu gice gikurikira, turaza kuraba ingene twotuma iyo ntunganyo igenda neza, tukamenya utunenge two kwitwararika, maze tugasubirana ubu basha bwo kugenzura iki gikoresha.


### Umuhora wo mu karere (LAN)


Umuhora wo mu karere, canke "LAN" (*Local Area Network*), ni amahuriro yose y'ubuhinga bwa none ari mu nzu yawe. Harimwo ibikoresho vyose bihabwa inzira na router yawe: inyabwonko, amaterefone ngendanwa, tablets, amacapiro, n'ibindi.


Aho bitandukaniye na interineti, nuko yo ari umuhora wo kw'isi yose, umuhora wa bose, umuhora wo mu karere ni ikibanza c'ibanga, igice kimwe kiri ukwaco, gigenewe gutuma ibikoresho bishobora kuvugana, ata guhanahana kwavyo kuva mu nzu yawe. Nk'akarorero, iyo urungitse dosiye ku nyabwonko yawe ku capiro iri kuri Wi-Fi, canke ugacungera itara riri ku muhora biciye kuri terefone yawe, iryo tumanako ribera aho hantu gusa, bitagombereye guca kuri seriveri iri kure.


![Image](assets/fr/194.webp)


Ibi bishingiye ku mugwi w'ingingo ngende rwako z'ikoranabuhanga n'amategeko, igihambaye murivyo ni itegeko rya IP. Igikoresho cose kiri ku muhora wawe wo mu karere gihabwa aderese IP yo mu karere (kenshi mu buryo `192.168.x.x`), ikoreshwa nk'akaranga kaco kihariye muri uwo muhora. Iyi aderese ntiboneka kuri interineti. Kiretse aderese IP yawe ya rusangi, isangiwe n'ibikoresho vyose biciye kuri modem, ni yo yonyene igaragara hanze y'inzu yawe.


Ariko ivyo bisa n'ukwitandukanya n'abandi ntibikwiye kuguha icizere c'ikinyoma y'uko ufise umutekano. Umuhora wo mu karere utunganijwe nabi ushobora kuba irembo ry'ibitero, cane cane mu bihe bikurikira:



- Nimba serivise z'uguruye (nk'ugusangira amadosiye canke interface y'uburongozi) zishobora gushikwako biciye kuri interineti .
- Nimba Wi-Fi idatekanye (ijambo ry'ibanga rigoyagoya canke uburyo bwo kunyegeza amakuru butagikoreshwa)
- Nimba ibintu bimwe bimwe biri ku muhora bivugana n'isi yo hanze mu nyandiko zitomoye canke bigasiga ivyuho vyuguruye


Ni ngombwa rero gutahura ingene umuhora wawe ugenda imbere, no kugenzura ibikoresho bishobora gukorana, hagati yavyo canke n'isi yo hanze.


### Wi-Fi


Wi-Fi (mu ncamake "*Wireless Fidelity*") ni ubuhinga bwo guhanahana amakuru ata nsinga bushobora gutuma uhuza ibikoresho vyawe n'umuhora wawe wo mu karere, ata n'urutsinga rukeneye. Iri koranabuhanga rishingiye ku gutanga amakuru biciye ku mirongo ya radiyo, muri rusangi mu mirongo y'incuro 2,4 GHz na 5 GHz (canke mbere 6 GHz ku nzira za Wi-Fi 6E na Wi-Fi 7).


Ariko ukwo kworoherwa mu gukoreshwa bizanana n'ingaruka zavyo. mu buryo butandukanye n'inzira zihuza n'insnga (nk'ivyo bita Ethernet), sinyare za Wi-Fi zica mu mpome kandi zishobora gutorwa iri ku metero amajana n'amajana. Ivyo bisigura ko abantu bari hanze y'inzu yawe (mu nzira, mu nyubakwa iri hafi, mbere n'abavuye mu miduga ihagaze hafi) bashobora kugerageza kumenya umuhora wawe maze bakawujako mugihe woba utarinzwe neza.


![Image](assets/fr/195.webp)


Uwutera afise uburenganzira bwo gukoresha umuhora wawe wa Wi-Fi yoshobora rero:



- Gufata amakuru atanyegejwe arengana ku rubuga (nk'igisabwa ca DNS canke uruja n'uruza rwa HTTP)
- Kugera kuri dosiye zawe canke ibikoresho vyawe nimba bitarinzwe neza
- Kwinjiza ibintu bibi muri mucukumbuzi yawe
- Gukoresha inzira yawe ya interineti ataco uzi, canke mbere agakora ibitero vyo kuri interineti akoresheje aderese IP yawe ya rusangi.


Kugira ngo wirinde ivyo bintu, urakeneye gukingira umuhora wawe wa Wi-Fi. Tuzorabira hamwe ingene ivyo twobikora mu bice bikeyi bikurikira.


### Aderesi IP zo mu karere


Iyo uhuje igikoresho n'umuhora wawe wo muhira, kironka aderese IP yo mu karere. Iyi aderese igizwe n'ibiharuro bine bitandukanijwe n'utuburungu (nk'akarorero `192.168.1.14`). Ikoreshwa nk'akaranga k'ihariye k'igikoresho cose kiri ku muhora wawe wo mu karere. Ni kubera iyo aderese kuba router yawe ishobora kumenya igikoresho co koherezako amakuru (nk'akarorero, paji y'urubuga canke amasanamu wasavye).


Ni vyiza gutahura ko izo aderese IP zo mu karere zitaboneka kuri interineti. Ziri mu migwi yaziganijwe, bigenwa n'ingingo ngenderwako mpuzamakungu, idashobora gukoreshwa ku rubuga rwa rusangi. Imigwi itatu ikunze gukoreshwa ya aderese IP yo mukarere ni:



- `192.168.0.0` kugeza `192.168.255.255` (muri rusangi ku bakoresha b'ibanga)
- `10.0.0.0` kugeza kuri `10.255.255.255` (muri rusangi ku masosiyete)
- `172.16.0.0` kugeza `172.31.255.255`


Igikoresho kimwe nyene gishobora kugira aderese IP nka `192.168.1.42` muhira, mu gihe uwundi akoresha wo mu kindi gihugu azogira ikindi gikoresho gifise iyo aderese IP ku muhora waco bwite wo mu karere, ata n'umwe yigeze agira amakimbirane, kuko ayo ma aderesi ntava ku rubuga rwo muhira. Ni router itanga uruja n'uruza hagati y'umuhora wawe wo muhira n'umuhora wa rusangi, igahindura izo aderesi biciye ku buryo bwitwa "NAT" (*Network Address Translation*).


Aderesi IP zo mu karere muri rusangi zitangwa mu buryo buhinduka, hakoreshejwe DHCP (*Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol*). Iyo uhuje igikoresho gishasha n'umuhora, kirungika ubusabe bwa DHCP bwa aderese, maze router ikagiha aderese imwe muzihari zategekanijwe. Iyi aderese ishobora guhinduka uko igihe kigenda kirarenga.


Ariko rero, birashoboka gutunganya ama aderesi IP adahinduka y'ibikoresho bimwe bimwe. Ivyo bisigura kubika aderese yihariye ku gikoresho kinaka, ku buryo buhoraho. Ivyo ni ngirakamaro mu bihe bimwe bimwe, nk'akarorero:



- Kugira ngo ushobore gushika kuri seriveri y'umuntu ku giti ciwe canke NAS ukoresheje ikindi gikoresho
- Kugira ngo usohore impapuro ku capiro iri ku muhora uri kure bitagombereye ko urondera aderese yayo
- Kugira ngo ureme amategeko yo kuyungurura canke port forwarding muri router yawe


### Ivyambu (ports) vy'umuhora 


Kugira ngo utahure ingene umuhora wo mu karere ukora, ukwiye kumenya ko aderese IP yose (yaba iyo mu karere canke iya rusangi ) ifatanye n'urutonde rw'ivyambu vy'ibiharuro, bifise ibiharuro kuva kuri `0` gushika kuri `65535`. Ivyo vyambu si ibigaragara: Ni ibibanza mbimbano vyo kwinjirirako canke vy'ugusohokerako bituma porogarame na serivisi bishobora gutumanako ku rubuga rwose.


Igihe cose igikoresho gitumanako biciye kuri interineti canke ku muhora wo mu karere, kibigira mu gufatanya IP aderese n'igiharuro c'icambu. Ivyo bituma umuntu ashobora kumenya igikoresho co kurungikako amakuru gusa, ariko kandi akamenya na porogarame canke serivise biri kuri ico gikoresho. Nk'akarorero:



- Icambu `80` gikoreshwa mu gushika ku mapaji y'urubuga akoresha HTTP
- Icambu `443` gikoreshwa mu gushika ku mapaji y'urubuga akoresha HTTPS (inzira inyegeje)
- Icambu `22` gikoreshwa ku nzira ya SSH
- Ivyambu `25`, `465` na `587` bikoreshwa mu kohereza ubutumwa bwa imeyiri kuri interineti (SMTP)
- Icambu `110` gikoreshwa mu gusoma ubutumwa kuri interineti biciye kw'itegeko rya POP3
- Icambu `143` gikoreshwa mu gusoma ubutumwa kuri interineti biciye kw'itegekomasezerano ya IMAP
- Icambu `21` gikoreshwa mu gutanga dosiye biciye kw'itegeko rya FTP
- Icambu `53` gikoreshwa ku bisabwa vya DNS...


Ivyo vyambu bikoreshwa kandi mu ma sisiteme nka Bitcoin canke Tor, aho ivyambu vyihariye bikoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe ku bijanye n'ugutumatumanako hagati y'umuntu n'uyundi(peer-to-peer) kuyobora uruja n'uruza:



- Icambu `8333` gikoreshwa ku nzira ya P2P kuri Bitcoin Mainnet
- Icambu `18333` gikoreshwa ku nzira ya P2P kuri Bitcoin Testnet
- Icambu `8332` gikoreshwa kuri interface RPC y'igihimba ca Bitcoin (node)
- Icambu `9050` gikoreshwa na proxy ya Tor SOCKS5
- Icambu `9150` gikoreshwa na mucukumbuzi ya Tor


Mu yandi majambo, icambu kimeze nk'umuryango wihariye. Iyo ugendereye urubuga, inyabwonko yawe yugurura icyambu c'isoko maze ikarungika ubusabe kuri aderese IP y'urubuga rwa kure, bugenewe icambu `443` nimba ari inzira inyegejwe. Seriveri iri kure ica igarura inyishu biciye ku muhora umwe. Kur router, iki ciyumviro c'ivyambu ni ikintu gihambaye: IKeneye kumenya igikoresho n'icambu co mu karere kugira ibe ariho uringika amakuru ya packets y'injiye.


Ariko ubwo bushobozi bwo Kwugurura ivyambu na bwo burazana ingorane z'umutekano. Icambu gisigaye cuguruye bidakenewe gishobora kumenyekana biciye kubikoresh vyo gupima umuhora maze kigakoreshwa n'abatera iyo gifitaniye isano na serivisi ishobora guhungabanywa canke itunganijwe nabi. Ni nk'umuryango wuguruye. Ariko ivyo tuzobivugako mu nyuma.


Gutahura rero ingene umuhora wawe wo muhira ukora ni ikintu gihambaye cane. Gutahura neza ivy'ishimikiro vya modem yawe, Wi-Fi, routers, aderese IP zo mu karere n'ama ports(ivyambu) biragufasha kumenya ingorane zishobora gushika maze ukagira ico ukoze kur'ivyo kugira ngo ukomeze umutekano wawe w'ubuhinga bwa none.


Muri iki gice, twavuze ivyiyumviro bihambaye bijanye n'umuhora wawe wo muhira. Mu gice gikurikira, turaza kuraba ingene wokingira ibikorwa n'ibikoresho vya interineti vyo mu karere kawe turaba ingene bikorwa, n'ingene wotunganya neza Wi-Fi yawe kugira ngo umutekano wawe ubungabungwe.


## Gukingira umuhora wawe wo muhira mu ntambwe nkeyi


<chapterId>d5577b2e-5247-4d10-8685-4906391e2cc1</chapterId>


Nk'uko twabibonye mu gice ca banje, gukingira umuhora wawe wo muhira ni ikintu gihambaye cane kugira ngo ukingire ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe, amakuru yawe bwite, no kugira ngo ushobore gukingira ubusegaba bwawe muvy'ubuhinga bwa none.


Umaze gusubiramwo ivyiyumviro vy'ishimikiro, iki gice kizokuyobora mu ntambwe zitomoye, zivyo gukora kandi neza zo kwongereza umutekano w'umuhora wawe wo mu karere.


*Ibuka: Amakuru atangwa ngaha ni muri rusangi, nkuko Plan ₿ Academy igenewe abantu bo kw'isi yose. Bivanye n'ivyo mu karere iwanyu be n'ivyo ISP yawe ikora, hari imigenzo myiza wokora imwe imwe ishobora kutavugwa ngaha, canke ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo butandukanye.*


### Guhitamwo no kurinda ibikoresho vyawe vy'umuhora


Umutekano w'umuhora wawe wo muhira utangurana n'uguhitamwo neza ibikoresho: router, canke mu bihe bimwe bimwe router ya modem. Ico gikoresho kiratanga uruja n'uruza hagati y'umuhora wawe wo mu karere na interineti. Ni co gituma gifise uruhara runini mu kurinda amakuru yawe.


Ni vyiza guhitamwo ibikoresho vya none, bibungabungwa n'uwabikoze, kandi bihuye n'ingingo ngenderwako z'umutekano ziherutse gushirwaho. Uyu musi (Ruheshi 2025), birakenewe ko umuntu ahitamwo igikoresho gihuye n'itegeko ryo kunyegeza amakuru rya WPA3 (*Wi-Fi Protected Access 3*), ikaba yaraje gusubirira WPA2 kandi igakosora amakosa menshi. Cane cane, WPA3 iratuma umuntu ashobora guhangana n'ibitero vy'inguvu z'agahomerabunwa (brute-force attacks) ku majambo y'ibanga ya Wi-Fi, kandi igatuma habaho ukwitandukanya neza hagati ya clients kumuhora.


Router ihuye na Wi-Fi 6, Wi-Fi 6E canke Wi-Fi 7 izoguha umuvuduko mwiza kandi, ikiruta vyose, ubufasha bw'akavukire bw'ikoranabuhanga bwo gucungera umutekano bugezwe ko. Ku rundi ruhande, ibikoresho vya kera cane, cane cane ivyo bitagishobora gushirwa kugihe, vyoshobora kuba birimwo utunenge tuzwi kandi tutarakosorwa. Bikururira ingorane umuhora wawe wose, naho woba ubitunganije neza. Ugereranije n'amaterefone ngendanwa canke inyabwonko, ama router ni ibikoresho dukunda gukoresha imyaka myinshi. Ariko rero, vyoshobora kuba vyiza ko ubisubiriza kenshi, kugira ngo wungukire ku bwoko busha kandi buguha umutekano.

**Ntiwitonde**: Nk'itegeko rusangi, router zitangwa naba ISPs zirashobora kutagira uburyo bwo gushirwa kugihe bukenewe, kimwe n'ubushobozi bwo guyihindura uko ushaka. Mu bindi bihe, ISPs boshobora no kugira uburyo uburenganzira bwo kwinjira mu muhora wawe w'imbere.

Rero urabe ko hari uburyo wo shira kugihe sisiteme ya router yawe buryo bubereye. Ivyo bishasha bikosora ubugoyagoye, vyongerako ibintu bishasha kandi bikongera ugushikama kwa sisiteme muri rusangi. Hari abahinguzi bahita baguha ubwonyene ibishasha muburyo bwihuse, ariko mu bihe bimwe bimwe uzokenera kuvyisuzumira n'amaboko biciye kuri interface y'umuyobozi ya router yawe. Nk'uko biri kuri terefone yawe, inyabwonko, sisiteme na porogarame, birahambaye ko uhora ushira kugihe router yawe. Ushobora kubishira muri gahunda zawe zaburi ndwi - Nk'akarorero, buri musi w'Imana - mu gukora urutonde rw'ibintu vyose ukeneye kugenzura no guhsira kugihe.


Ubundi buryo kandi, urashobora gukoresha 'auto-updates' canke n'imiburi buri ugakoresha 'auto-scan' kugira ngo urabe ko hari ivyo woshira kugihe muri firmware (sisiteme) mugihe kuvyikorera ari vyo ukunze. N'aho uburyo bwo kuvugurura bwikora bushobora gukomeza kuba bwa teza ingorane y'umutekano, kutavugurura firmware ya router yawe kenshi bizoshira mu kaga umuhora wawe wo mu karere kubera ko izo negenke ziba zamaze kumenyekana.

**Akarorero**: Iyo ugura router yawe, bishobora kuba vyiza gushaka amasosiyete yamenyekanye mu ruganda amaze igihe kirekire atanga routers kw'isoko. Akarorero, routers ya 'Fritz!Box' yamenyekanye canke nk'ibikoresho vya plug-and-play, bikwiriye gukoreshwa haba mu muryango canke mu masosiyete mato. Poritike yabo yo gushira kugihe sisiteme yabo ikunze kumara imyaka myinshi.

Nimba router yawe itaki bungabungwa ariko igikora neza ku bijanye na igikoresho ubwaco, woshobora gushiramwo indi firmware ya open-source, nka:



- OpenWrt, ni distribution ya Linux yihariye mu bijanye n'ama router, itanga uburyo bwinshi bwo guhindura ibintu no gushira kugihe vyamako
- pfSense na OPNsense, ni sisiteme zibiri zishingiye kuri FreeBSD (zimeze nka Unix) za firewall zikorera ku myubakire ya x86 be na ma routers


**Iciyumviro**: Bamwe mu batanga serivisi za interineti (ISP) batanga kuba kiriya babo routers nyinshi zakozwe na sosiyete imwe ikorana naba ISPs batandukanye bo kw'isi yose. Ushobora gusanga kugira ngo ushyiremo imwe mu zindi firmware zo gusubiriza iyo bizanana na router, abandi bashobora kuba barabonye uko babikora, n'ubwo baba bari ku rundi ruhande rw'isi.

![Image](assets/fr/196.webp)



https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/opnsense-90c2785d-a0d7-4981-be8d-d290bbeb8263

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/pfsense-24eea96a-2fdc-42a6-a77b-89bc29149864

Izo sisiteme zituma umuntu ashobora kugenzura neza amategeko agenga firewall, inzira zinjira n'izisohoka, gucamw'ibice umuhora (VLANs) n'ugucungera DNS, ariko rereo zigenewe cane abakoresha b'inzobere.


**Mu ncamake, ndabagira inama yo**:



- Guhitamwo router nshasha zigezweko
- Kwama ushira sisiteme yawe ku gihe
- kwiyumvira iyindi firmware wokoresha igihe bikenewe


### Guhindura amakuru asanzwe yo kwinjira n'amajambo y'ibanga


Amwe mu makosa asanzwe akorwa (kandi ashobora gutera akaga) ni ukugumizako amakuru yo kwinjira yatanzwe n'uwakoze router, canke gukoresha ijambo ry'ibanga ry'ridakomeye.


Mu mateka, amakuru yo kwinjira ya router yari afise umutekano muke cane kandi kenshi yari asa ku bakoresha bose, ibizwi cane ni `admin/admin`. Ayo makuru yo kwinjira asanzwe ashirwa ahagaraga, vyanditswe mu bitabu vy'abakoresha kandi vyanditswe cane mu rutonde ry'amakuru ya batera. Muri ico gihe, umuntu wese abona ko router yawe iriho yoshobora kugerageza kwinjira muburyo butemewe mu kugerageza gushiramwo ayo makuru asanzwe azwi.


Muri iki gihe, benshi mu bahinguzi bibi bikoresho baha ijambo ry'ibanga ry'umwihariko kandi rikomeye kuri router yose. Ariko rero, no muri ico gihe, ndabahimiriza guhindura ayo makuru asanzwe ariho. Ivyo bigabanya ingorane za supply chain, kandi bikabuza gukoresha ijambo ry'ibanga rizanana n'igikoresho (rimwe na rimwe usanga ryanditsi ku ga papuro kari kuri router) guhungabanya umutekano wawe.


Ni ngombwa rero ko uhindura ayo makuru ubwo nyene umaze gushiramwo router yawe:



- Izina ry'ukoresha (nimba ririho) rya interface y'ubuyobozi
- Kandi ikiruta vyose, ijambo ry'ibanga ry'ubuyobozi, ririnda gushika ku miterere yose y'umuhora, hamwe n'ijambo ry'ibanga rya Wi-Fi.


Iryo jambo ry'ibanga ritegerezwa kuba rirerire (indome 40), rigoye (ibiharuro, indome nto, indome nini n'ibimenyetso), ridasanzwe (ritazosubira gukoreshwa ahandi), kandi ridasanzwe. Ndagusaba ko mukurema ukoresha ubutunganyirizo bw'ijambo ry'ibanga no kubika neza ayo makuru.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

Imburi: ntiwitaranye ijambo ry'ibanga ry'uburongozi bwa router (rikingira ukuntu umuntu ashobora gushika ku ntunganyo zayo) n'ijambo ry'ibanga rya Wi-Fi (rituma ushobora kwifatanya n'umuhora wa wireless). Ivyo ni ibintu bibiri bitandukanye, kandi vyompi bikeneye guhindurwa.


Ubwa nyuma, ama routeurs amwe amwe yo muri iki gihe arafise uburyo bubiri bwo gucunga: Interface y'urubuga rwo mu karere (rushobora gushikwako biciye kuri aderese nka `192.168.1.1`) na interface ya cloud (igushoboza gucungera igikoresho uri kure biciye kuri interineti). Nimba ubwo buryo bwa nyuma bukoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe, ndaguhanura ko woyizimya nimba utariko urayikoresha, canke ukomeze umutekano wayo ukoresheje ijambo ry'ibanga rikomeye kandi bishoboka ukoreshe kwemeza uwinjira n'ivyemezo bibiri (2FA) ubwo buryo buriho.


### Gutunganya imiterere ya router


Router ni umutima w'umuhora wawe wo muhira. Ivyo ikora birafise uruhara runini mu gucungera umutekano w'ibikoresho vyose biri ku muhora. Ikibabaje ni uko vyinshi mu bikorwa bikoreshwa kuri ivyo bikoresho bishobora gutuma umuhora wawe uterwa n'abantu bo hanze ataco ubiziko. Ni co gituma bihambaye gukora isuzuma ryuzuye ry'amahitamwo yakoreshejwe, no guhagarika ivyo bidakenewe cane bivanye n'ivyo ukeneye.


Hari ibiranga bikwiye kwirindwa canke gukurwaho mu buryo butegekanijwe:



- **UPnP (*Universal Plug and Play*)**:


Ivyo bituma ibikoresho biri ku muhora wawe bisaba router Kwugurura ivyambu ubwavyo. Naho ivyo vyorosha gukoresha ibintu bimwe bimwe (imikino yo kuri interineti, amakamera ari ku muhora, n'ibindi), birafungura kandi umuryango w'ibikoresho bibi bishobora guhindura imiterere y'umuhora ata ruhusha rwawe. UPnP ni kimwe mu bituma serivisi z'indani zija ahagaragara uta bigambiriye.



- **WPS (*Wi-Fi Protected Setup*)**:


Mu ntango, ibwo buryo bwari bugenewe kworohereza abantu kuja kuri Wi-Fi ata jambo ry'ibanga winjije, iyi sisiteme ikaba ishingiye kuri kode ya PIN akenshi igoyagoya kandi ishobora guhungabanywa n'ibitero vy'inguvu z'agahomerabunwa. Ndaguhanura ku yizimya.



**Gukorera kure (*Gutunganya imikoreshereze ya kure*)**:


Hariho ama routeurs ashobora kuguha uburenganzira bwo kwinjira muri interface  y'ubuyobozi bwayo uri hanze y'umuhora wo mukarere, biciye kuri interineti. Ivyo biha amahirwe menshi yo gutegwa router yawe. Bizimye burundu, kiretse igihe ubikeneye ivyo gutunganya imikoreshereze ya kure  muburyo bumwe canke ubundi. Naho ari ukwo, wampe ukoresha VPN.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/tailscale-9acbd7de-04d9-40f6-ab80-35f0dfedb632


- **Amategeko ya kera atagikoreshwa canke adatekanye**:


Hagarika serivisi y'ubuyobozi iyo ari yo yose ikoresha amategeko agaragara mu nyandiko rusangi nka Telnet, FTP, HTTP zitanyegejwe canke SMBv1. Aya mategeko ntatuma amakuru ahanahanwa aba ibanga canke ngo akwize ubutungane, kandi akenshi araterwa n'ibintu bibi. Nimba ukeneye gushika ku nzira yo mu karere canke kure, koresha gusa inzira ziciye kuri HTTPS (Interface inyegejwe), SSH canke SFTP, nk'uko bikwiye.



- **Ping WAN / ICMP**:


Hariho ama router yishura ku vyo ICMP isaba ku buryo busanzwe bivuye hanze (ibwirizwa rya `ping`). Ivyo bituma uwugutera ashobora kugenzura ko umuhora wawe ukora kandi ko ushobora gushikirwa. Nimba atavyo ukeneye, hagarika izo nyishu muri firewall ya router.


Ubwa nyuma, wibuke gutanga uburenganzira bwo gukoresha interface y'uburongozi bwa router ku bikoresho vyizigirwa gusa, ugahagarika uburenganzira bwo kuyikoresha ku ma aderesi IP amwe amwe, nimba interface ibikwemerera. Hariho porogarame zimwe zimwe, nka OpenWrt, zitanga ubugenzuzi bwiza cane kuri ivyo bintu.


### Gukomeza umutekano w'umuhora wa wi-Fi


Akenshi umuhora wa wi-Fi niho hantu ho kwinjirira kugira ngo umuntu yinjire mu kibanza cawe we co muhira. Ntiboneka n'amaso ariko ikaba ishobora gushikwako n'abari hanze y'impome z'inzu yawe, hariho amahirwe menshi yo kuyishikako kumuntu wese ari hafi.


Intambwe ya mbere ihambaye ni uguhitamwo amategeko meza ajyenga ivyo kunyegeza amakuru. Igihe cose wame ukoresha "*WPA3-Personal*", umurongo ngenderwa ko ugezwe ko kandi utekanye. Ntibikingira gusa amakuru ahanahanwa, ariko kandi biragukingira ibitero bimwe bimwe bizwi.


Izina ry'umuhora wawe wa Wi-Fi, ryitwa "SSID" (*Service Set Identifier*), rikwiye kuguma ritagira aho ribogamiye. Irinde gushiramwo izina ryawe, aderese canke izina ry router. Izina nka `MaisonDupont_WiFi6` aho uba utanze amakuru menshi cane ku muntu ashobora ku gutera. Hitamwo izina rusangi, ritagira insiguro yihariye. Ivyo bigabanya amakuru aboneka kumuntu agukurikirane canke akoreshe ikibantu.


Ikindi kintu ciza ni ugukora umuhora w'abashitsi utandukanye n'umuhora wawe nyamukuru. Uwo muhora wundi, akenshi utangwa mu buryo busanzwe buzanana na router zigezweko, uragufasha guha abashitsi bawe inzira ya interineti bitagombereye ko bashika ku bindi bikoresho vyawe (ordinateri, amacapiro, NAS, n'ibindi). Bisigura kandi ko udategerezwa kubaha ijambo ry'ibanga ry'umuhora wawe nyamukuru. Kugira ngo ugende kure yivyo, nushireho uburyo bwo kwitandukanya n'abandi kuri uyu muhora w'abashitsi: Ivyo bizotuma kandi abashitsi badashobora kuvugana, bigabanye n'ingorane zijanye n'ibikoresho bishobora gukoreshwa nabi.


Ubwa nyuma, nuhindure ubushobozi bwo gutanga sinyare bw'igikoresha gitanga Wi-Fi. Kubisanzwe, ama router menshi atanga sinyare ikomeye cane, rimwe na rimwe ikaba ishika kure cane y'impome zawe. Ivyo bituma urushirizaho gushikirwa n'ikibi. Mu miterere iteye imbere ya router yawe, nugabanye ubushobozi bwo gutanga sinyare ku rugero rutoyi rukenewe kugira ngo inzu yawe ikwize. Nimba router yawe ibikwemerera, urashobora kandi guhindura ugashira ho uburyo bwo kuzimya Wi-Fi mugihe ata wuriko arayikoresha.


### Ugucamwo ibice umuhora


Imwe mu nzira nziza zo gukomeza umutekano w'umuhora wo muhira ni ukuwucamwo ibice. Ivyo birimwo kugabura mwo umuhora wo mu karere imihora mito yigenga yitwa "VLANs" (*Virtual Local Area Networks*). Izo VLAN zituma bishoboka gutandukanya ubwoko butandukanye bw'ibikoresho canke ikoreshwa, naho nyene zikoresha ibikoresho bimwe (router, insinga, terminal ya Wi-Fi, n'ibindi).


VLAN yose ikora nk'umuhora mutoyi, wigenga ufise amategeko yawo yo gutumatumanako . Guhanahana amakuru hagati ya VLANs birabujijwe ku bisanzwe canke bikagenzurwa ku rugero rwo hejuru cane. Ivyo birabuza nk'akarorero tereviziyo ya hungabanijwe gushika ku nyabwonko yawe bwite canke kuri NAS. Ubwo buryo bushingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako 2 z'ishimikiro z'umutekano wo kuri interineti twamaze kwiga mu bice vyabanje: Kugabura kwihariye n'uburenganzira buke.


![Image](assets/fr/197.webp)


Mu majambo nyayo, ngutu uturorero tumwe tumwe two kugabura woshobora gukoresha:



- VLAN y'umuntu ku giti ciwe: Ku bikoresho vyawe wizigira nk'inyabwonko, amaterefone ngendanwa canke ama seriveri y'umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ico ni co gice nyamukuru aho amakuru yawe y'agaciro agendagenda.



- IoT VLAN: Ku bintu bihuye (amatara, inyakiramajwi, ama kamera, amatereviziyo y'ubuhinga bwa none, n'ibindi). Ivyo bikoresho kenshi ntibitekanye, ntibishigwa kugihe, kandi ni vyo bikunda guterwa. Kubitandukanya nibindi biragabanya cane ingorane zo kuba inzira yo kwinjira mu muhora wawe.



- VLAN y'umushyitsi: Igenewe abagenzi bawe canke umuryango wawe iyo baje kubana nawe. Itanga uburyo bwo gukoresha interineti, ariko nta buryo bwo gukoresha ibikoresho vyawe vy'ibanga itanga.


Ubwa nyuma, ubu buryo buratanga kandi inyungu mu bijanye n'ubushobozi bwo gukora neza n'ugucungera: Bugufasha gushira imbere ubwoko bumwe bumwe bw'uruja n'uruza, gukoresha amategeko yihariye y'umutekano bivanye na VLAN (firewall, kugabanya umuvuduko, DNS filtering, n'ibindi), no kugenzura neza inyifato idasanzwe y'umuhora. Ni akamenyero ndabashimira cane.


### Gutunganya DNS muburyo buteye imbere


DNS (*Domain Name System*) ni serivisi ya interineti ihindura ama aderesi y'umuhora atahurwa n'abantu (nk'akarorero `planb.network`) mu ma aderesi IP atahurwa n'inyabwonko. Iyo igikoresho kiri ku muhora wawe gishaka kugenderera urubuga, kirabaza seriveri ya DNS kugira ngo kironke aderese ya serivieri iriko urwo rubuga.
