Kubera ko mubisanzwe ivyo bisabwa vya DNS akenshi birungikwa mu nyandiko zitomoye (zitanyegejwe) kuri ba ISP bawe, bikabashoboza (canke abandi nka leta) kubona imbuga zose ugenderera, naho amakuru y'izo mbuga yoba anyegejwe biciye kuri HTTPS.


Kugira ngo ukaze ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe bwo kurondera ku mbuga kandi ubuze ibintu bimwe bimwe udashaka kuva ku muzi, urashobora gufata ububasha ku bijanye n'uko DNS ikora ku muhora wawe wo muhira. Tangira mu gusubiriza ama serveri ya DNS asanzwe arimwo n'uburyo bundi bwubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga nka :



- [Quad9](https://quad9.net/): Harimwo urutonde rwo kubuza imbuga mbi kandi ntizigama amazina igihe kirekire



- [Cloudflare DNS](https://www.cloudflare.com/application-services/products/dns/): Irihuta kandi yiyemeje gukurikiza ingingo ngenderwako zikomeye zo kutabika amazina y'imbuga



- [NextDNS](https://nextdns.io/): Ishobora guhindurwa cane, ifise ubuhinga bwo kuyungurura n'ivyegeranyo biteye imbere



- [AdGuard DNS](https://adguard-dns.io/): Yoroshe gutunganya, n'amahitamwo yo guhagarika amatangazo n'ugukurikiranwa


![Image](assets/fr/199.webp)


Inyuma y'aho, ugurura itegeko ryo kunyegeza ibisabwa nk'uburyo bwo kwirinda ko ivyo bisabwa vya DNS vyofatwa canke ngo bikurikiranwe. Hariho amategeko 2 nyamukuru yo gukora ivyo:



- DoH (**DNS over HTTPS**): Inyegeza ibisabwa vya DNS mu mategeko ya HTTPS, bikaba bituma bidashoboka ko wotandukanya ibi bisabwa n'uruja n'uruza rw'umuhora runyegejwe



- DoT (**DNS over TLS**): Irema inzira yihariye inyegejwe icishwamo amakuru hagati y'igikoresho cawe na serveri ya DNS



- DoQ (**DNS over QUIC**): Itwara ibisabwa vya DNS biciye ku nzira ya QUIC ishingiye kuri UDP


Mu bikorwa, kunyegeza amakuru ya DNS n'uguhindura seriveri bishobora gushirwa mu ngiro ku nzego zitandukanye:



- Ku rugero rwa porogarame: Porogarame zimwe zimwe, nka mucukumbuzi ya Firefox, biguha uburenganzira bwo gutunganya amategeko yo kunyegeza ya DNS, nka DoH, ataco uhinduye. Ariko rero, uwo muti ukingira gusa ivyo usaba biciye kuri iyo porogarame, nturinda ibindi ukora ku nyabwonko yawe.


![Image](assets/fr/198.webp)

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/firefox-11814cec-3415-4ed9-a06e-f6fda5c9510f

- Ku rugero rwa sisiteme: OS zimwe zimwe zishiramwo ubufasha bwa DNS zinyegejwe (DoT canke DoH), bucungera ibisabwa vyose vya DNS bica mu rutonde rw'umuhora wa sisiteme. Ariko rero, ivyo ntibishobora gukingira inyabwonko yose canke terefone yose: Ama porogarame arashobora kudaca muri iyo nzira iyo atunganijwe gukoresha uburyo butandukanye bwo gukorana na DNS canke amategeko.



- Ku rugero rw'umuhora: Ukunyegeza amakuru ya DNS gushobora gukoreshwa ku muhora wose wo mu karere biciye ku gutunganya router. Na none, router itunganijwe kuri DoH/DoT ibona gusa uruja n'uruza rwoherezwa kuri yo vy'ukuri. Rero mucukumbuzi yatunganijwe kugira ngo ikorane niyindi DNS ya kure ishobora kurengana ubwo bugenzuzure. Kugira ngo ugabanye ivyo utwo twasamutwe, ukeneye guhagarika port 53 mu nyandiko zitomoye no kubuza aho DoH/DoT ija bitemewe biciye kuri firewall ya router.


Kandi, ama routeurs ya modem atangwa na ISP ntabwo yama ashigikira ivyo bintu. Iyo router ifise aho igarukira, hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo kuyikoresha. Ushobora gushiramwo client ya DNS inyegeza amakuru n'amaboko kuri buri gikoresho, urashobora kandi kongerako router yawe ku giti cawe inyuma y'iya ISP (ishobora kwemera kunyegeza ibisabwa vya DNS) canke ugashiraho seriveri ya DNS yo mu karere (nk'akarorero, kuri Raspberry Pi) ijejwe kunyegeza ibisabwa vya DNS no kubirungika kur seriveri ya DNS irinzwe.



Kugira ngo ibintu bigende imbere, urashobora kandi gushinga umuti wo kuyungurura DNS wo mu karere nka Pi-hole canke AdGuard Home.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/pi-hole-46a735c5-8af3-4cc3-a2c2-1d4f6a7dc428

Ivyo bikoresho bikora nka seriveri ntoyi ya DNS iri mu muhora wawe, bikabuza ibisabwa ku mbuga zizwi ko zakira amatangazo, ibikurikirana mucukumbuzi, phishing canke imbuga mbi. Ivyo bikoresho kandi biragufasha kwikorera urutonde rwawe rwo kubuza canke guhindura ukuyungurura bivanye n'ibikoresho birikumurongo.


![Image](assets/fr/200.webp)


### Ukwinjirira kure biciye kuri VPN


Mu bihe bimwe bimwe, birakenewe ko ushobora gushika ku muhora wawe wo muhira igihe uriko uragenda: Kuraba amadosiye kuri NAS, gukoreshe igihimba (node) ca Bitcoin na Lightning, ushikire seriveri witunganirije, canke urongore umuhora wawe. Ariko rero, iyo nzira yo guhuza uri kure itegerezwa kuba itekanye.


Impanuro ya mbere ni ukutazokwigera ufungura icambu kuri router yawe kugira ngo ushikire igikoresho (nk'akarorero biciye kuri RDP, SSH canke FTP), kuko ivyo bica bigaragaza iyo serivisi kuri interineti yose, ivyo bikaba ari ubugoyagoye. Ibitero vy'ubuhinga bwa none bitera ivyambu vyuguruye ni vyinshi.


Umuti ndababwira ni ugukoresha VPN (*Virtual Private Network*), ni ukuvuga inzira inyegeje hagati y'igikoresho cawe ca kure (inyabwonko, terefone ngendanwa, n'ibindi) n'umuhora wawe wo mu karere. Iyo umaze kwifatanya na VPN, urashobora gushika ku bintu vyo mu nzu yawe nk'aho woba uri ng'aho mu karere, kandi mu buryo butekanye.


Inyishu zibiri nyamukuru ku bakiriya b'abikorera ku giti cabo ni:



- WireGuard: Igezweko, irihuta kandi iraremurutse
- OpenVPN: Niya kera, ariko irakuze cane kandi ishobora gutunganywa kuburyo butomoye
  

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/wireguard-81fdd0db-b2bd-4a6c-a082-2de269e26779

Aha niho hari inyigisho yuzuye kuri Tailscale, umuti woroshe gutunganya VPN ukoresha WireGuard:


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/tailscale-9acbd7de-04d9-40f6-ab80-35f0dfedb632

Ushobora kwakira iyo VPN ataco uhinduye kuri router bihuye, ku nyabwonko ntoyi (nk'iya Raspberry Pi) canke kuri seriveri yihariye muhira. Ushobora kandi kuyishiramwo nka client ataco uhinduye ku gikoresho ico ari co cose.


Ariko VPN si iyo gukoresha kure gusa. Ushobora kandi gukoresha client ya VPN wa kera ku bikoresho vyawe kugira ngo unyegeza amakuru yawe yose asohoka, mbere n'igihe uri kure yo muhira (Wi-Fi ya bose, hoteli, kaminuza, n'ibindi). Muri ico gihe, igikoresho cawe gifatanya na seriveri ya VPN y'uwundi muntu (y'ubudandaji canke iyo witunganirije), iyo seriveri igaca irungika amakuru yawe kuri interineti. Ivyo bihisha aderese IP yawe nyayo kuba ISP, bikarinda amakuru yawe ubutasi bwo mu karere kandi bikarinda uburyo bumwe bumwe bwo gucengera.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

Ubwa nyuma, birashoboka kandi gushinga VPN ataco uhinduye kuri router yawe, bikagufasha kurinda ibikoresho vyose vy'iwawe muhira ataco ukeneye gushiramwo umu client wa VPN kuri kimwe cose muri bitagombereye ko ushira VPN client kuri buri gikoresho.


### Gukurikirana no kumenya


Igihe umuhora wawe watunganijwe neza kandi waciwemwo ibice, birahambaye ko urenga kure umutekano usanzwe. Gukurikirana neza umuhora wawe wo mu karere birashobora gutuma umenya inyifato idasanzwe, amahuzu atemewe canke ibimenyetso vy'ukwinjirigwa. Intumbero ni ukumenya ingorane hakiri kare, imbere y'uko zitera akaga.


Intambwe ya mbere ni ugushira hamwe inyandiko z'umutekano. Igikoresho cose gifatanye n'umuhora kiratanga amakuru harimwo amakuru yerekeye amahuza, amakosa canke igikorwa giteye amakenga. Aho kurondera izo nyandiko imwe kuri imwe, ndabagira inama yo kubirungika kuri seriveri ishobora kubishira mu migwi, kubirobanura no kubisuzuma. Imiti nka Graylog canke Elastic Stack (ELK) igufasha gukoranya izo nyandiko muri interface y'igicapo aho ushobora kurondera ibintu vyihariye, gukora imburi canke kubona ibikorwa vy'umuhora.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/graylog-3a7f0377-1d95-4446-abe0-d7866a551455

Hanyuma rero, fata umusi ku musi ibipimo vy'umuhora wawe, nk'akarorero na Nmap. Ivyo bizokuronsa incamake y'ibikoresho vyose biri ku muhora wawe, n'ivyambu vyuguruye. Iyo ubonye igikoresho kitazwi canke igikorwa kidasanzwe, ivyo vyoshobora kuba ikimenyetso c'igitero.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/communication/nmap-862300d7-6dfb-4660-970d-f56a9f58f60d

Kugira ngo ugende mbere n'imbere, urashobora gushiramwo IDS (*Intrusion Detection System*), canke mbere IPS (*Intrusion Prevention System*). Ivyo bikoresho, nka Suricata canke Snort, bigenzura uruja n'uruza rw'umuhora mu gihe nyaco kandi bikamenya imikono y'ibitero bizwi (ugupima ivyambu, injections, amahuzu ateye amakenga, n'ibindi). IDS iragabisha, mu gihe IPS ishobora guhagarika ibikorwa bimwe bimwe.


Ubwa nyuma, gukurikirana ukuntu umuvuduko ukoreshwa na vyo nyene ni ikimenyetso ciza c'ibikorwa bidasanzwe. Iyo igikoresho gikoresheje umuvuduko udasanzwe mu buryo butunguranye ata mvo igaragara, ivyo vyoshobora kwerekana ko hoba hariko ikuntu kiriko kira vomwa muburyo butemewe, ko amakuru yasohotse canke mbere ko igikoresho coshobora guhungabanywa. Ibikoresho nka ntopng canke vnStat bigufasha kubona ivyinjira n'ibisohoka ku gikoresho.


https://planb.academy/tutorials/computer-security/data/ntopng-77435bd3-674a-4f35-81d9-0a5325bbdcbd

### Ububiko bw'inyongera (Backup) Gusubiza inyuma no kwihangana


Naho woba ufise umuhora utekanye, ukwononekara kw'ibikoresho, amakosa yo gutunganya canke ibintu bitateguwe (ugucika kw'umuyagankuba , isanganya, ukwononekara kwa hard disk, n'ibindi) birashobora gutuma amakuru atakara canke serivisi zawe zigahagarara. Kugira ngo ushobore gukomeza ikibanza cawe c'ubuhinga bwa none no kwirinda gutangura uhereye ku ntango iyo habaye ingorane, birahambaye ko ushira mu ngiro ubuhinga bwa backup no kwihanganira ingaruka z'isanganya.


Tangurana n'ugukora backup y'intunganyo(imiterere) y'ibikoresho vy'umuhora wawe, cane cane router. Izo dosiye z'imiterere zishobora kurungikwa hanze biciye kuri interface y'ubuyobozi. Kubika kopi biratuma ushobora gusubizaho ningoga sisiteme yawe ikwiye iyo igikoresho gitangujwe canke kigasubirizwa. Ndabagira inama kandi yo kunyegeza iyi backup.


Ubwa nyuma, kugira ngo umuhora wawe ushobore guhangana n'ugucika kw'umuyagankuba gura UPS. Ico gikoresho kiratanga backup y'umuyagankuba iminota mikeyi iyo umucanwa wacitse, kikagufasha kubandanya ukoresha interineti canke ukamenya neza ko ibikoresho bihambaye (NAS, router, Wi-Fi access point, n'ibindi) bifungwa neza. Hari n'ibikoresho bimwe bimwe bishobora kohereza ibwirizwa ryo kuzimya ubwavyo ku bikoresho bihuye iyo bibonye ko umucanwa ubaye muke.


Niwakurikiza izi ntambwe nke, uzoba wubatse umuhora ukomeye kandi utekanye wubaha ubuzima bw'ibanga bwawe.
